### [1] [From raw data to neutrino candidates: a neural-network pipeline for Baikal-GVD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11176)
*A. Matseiko,G. Plotnikov,I. Kharuk*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于神经网络的Baikal-GVD数据处理流水线，利用Transformer架构和域适应（domain adaptation）技术，显著提升事件重建质量和候选事件筛选速度，支持近实时分类与多信使天文学应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提升Baikal-GVD中微子望远镜的事件重建质量，并加速中微子候选事件的选择过程，以支持近实时多信使（multi-messenger）预警系统和弥散中微子通量测量。

Method: 设计了三阶段神经网络流水线：快速抑制广延大气簇射（extensive air shower）事件、抑制噪声光学模块激活、提取高置信度中微子候选事件。三个阶段均采用Transformer架构，通过注意力机制（attention mechanism）利用hit间关联。通过域适应（domain adaptation）技术处理蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）模拟与实验数据之间的域偏移（domain shift）。

Result: 流水线相比标准重建链实现了数个数量级的加速。噪声抑制神经网络在精度上超越了传统算法，并能提供信号hit的时间残差估计，有助于识别径迹状（track-like）hit。域适应技术改善了模拟与实验数据之间的一致性。

Conclusion: 该框架实现了近实时事件分类，可直接应用于多信使预警系统和弥散中微子通量测量，证明基于Transformer的深度学习流水线在中微子望远镜数据处理中具有显著优势。

Abstract: We present a neural-network-based data processing pipeline for Baikal-GVD, designed to improve event reconstruction quality and accelerate neutrino candidates selection. The pipeline comprises three stages: fast suppression of extensive air shower events, suppression of noise optical modules activations, and extraction of high confidence neutrino candidates. All three networks employ a transformer architecture that exploits inter-hit correlations through the attention mechanism. Applied sequentially, the pipeline achieves orders-of-magnitude speedup over the standard reconstruction chain. Moreover, noise suppression neural network surpasses the accuracy of algorithmic noise suppression algorithms and provides estimate for time residuals of the signal hits, which is crucial for identification of track-like hits. We address the domain shift between Monte Carlo simulations and experimental data by incorporating a domain adaptation technique, demonstrating improved agreement between the two domains. The resulting framework enables near-real-time event classification, with direct applications to multi-messenger alert systems and diffuse neutrino flux measurements.

</details>


### [2] [An agentic framework for gravitational-wave counterpart association in the multi-messenger era](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10584)
*Yiming Dong,Yacheng Kang,Junjie Zhao,Xinyuan Zhu,Ziming Wang,Lijing Shao*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了GW-Eyes，一个基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体框架，首次在下一代引力波与电磁波探测器时代实现引力波信号与候选电磁对应体的自主关联，并支持自然语言交互以辅助人工专家完成多信使天文学中的多项任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着引力波（gravitational waves, GWs）的探测，多信使天文学（multi-messenger astronomy）为理解天体物理、致密物质、引力和宇宙学提供了新窗口。然而，下一代引力波和电磁（electromagnetic, EM）探测器将带来事件数量的急剧增长，对现有数据分析范式构成巨大挑战。

Method: 开发了GW-Eyes，一个由大语言模型（large language models, LLMs）驱动的智能体框架，首次集成了领域专用工具，能够自主执行引力波信号与候选电磁事件之间的对应体关联任务。该框架还支持自然语言交互，辅助人类完成星表管理、天区图（skymap）可视化和快速验证等辅助任务。

Result: GW-Eyes利用了大语言模型的复杂决策能力与可追溯推理过程，能够自主完成GW-EM对应体关联任务，并通过自然语言交互为人工专家提供辅助支持。

Conclusion: 该框架为多信使天文学提供了一种新的研究视角，有望有效应对下一代探测器时代的数据分析挑战。

Abstract: With the detection of gravitational waves (GWs), multi-messenger astronomy has opened a new window for advancing our understanding of astrophysics, dense matter, gravitation, and cosmology. The GW sources detected to date are from mergers of compact object binaries, which possess the potential to generate detectable electromagnetic (EM) counterparts. Searching for associations between GW signals and their EM counterparts is an essential step toward enabling subsequent multi-messenger studies. In the era of next-generation GW and EM detectors, the rapid increase in the number of events brings not only unprecedented scientific opportunities, but also substantial challenges to the existing data analysis paradigm. To help address these challenges, we develop GW-Eyes, an agentic framework powered by large language models (LLMs). For the first time, GW-Eyes integrates domain-specific tools and autonomously performs counterpart association tasks between GW and candidate EM events. It supports natural language interaction to assist human experts with auxiliary tasks such as catalog management, skymap visualization, and rapid verification. Our framework leverages the complex decision-making capabilities of LLMs and their traceable reasoning processes, offering a new perspective to the multi-messenger astronomy.

</details>

# nlin.CD [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Stochastically perturbed billiards: fingerprints of chaos and universality classes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11849)
*Roberto Artuso,Matteo Burlo*

Main category: nlin.CD

TL;DR: 本文研究随机微扰（stochastic perturbation）对弹性反射定律的影响，发现混沌台球（chaotic billiards）的关键统计特征保持不变，而可积台球（integrable billiards）在极小扰动下行为发生根本性变化，可关联至Evans随机台球模型，其空间平稳测度（spatial stationary measure）沿边界非均匀分布，区别于混沌台球。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典（及量子）台球桌因形状不同呈现出从强混沌到可积的丰富动力学特征。本文旨在探究随机微扰对弹性反射定律的作用如何改变不同类别台球系统的统计行为，特别是可积台球在微扰下的独特响应。

Method: 对弹性反射定律引入随机微扰（stochastic perturbation），分析混沌台球与可积台球在该扰动下的行为差异。对于极小扰动情形，将可积台球的行为与Evans随机台球模型（Evans stochastic billiard）建立联系，后者在每次碰撞时反射角为$(-π/2,π/2)$上的均匀分布随机变量。

Result: 混沌台球在随机微扰下保持其关键统计特征不变；可积台球在极小扰动下行为发生根本性变化，其空间平稳测度（spatial stationary measure）沿边界呈现典型的非均匀分布，与任何混沌台球桌均不同。

Conclusion: 随机微扰对混沌与可积台球系统的影响具有本质差异：混沌系统具有统计鲁棒性，而可积系统对微扰高度敏感，其平稳测度的边界非均匀性是区分两类系统的关键特征。

Abstract: Billiards tables - a minimal model for particles moving in a confined region - are known to present classical (and quantum) different features according to their shape, ranging from strongly chaotic to integrable dynamics. Here we consider the role of a stochastic perturbation of the elastic reflection law, and show that while chaotic billiards maintain their key statistical feature, the behaviour for integrable billiard tables is completely different: it can be linked, for tiny perturbations, to Evans stochastic billiard, where at each collision the reflected angle is a uniformly distributed stochastic variable on $(-π/2,π/2$). The resulting spatial stationary measure has peculiar aspects, like being typically non uniform along the boundary, differently from any chaotic billiard table.

</details>

# math.AG [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Theta functions for singular curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11152)
*Indranil Biswas,Jacques Hurtubise*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文将经典黎曼 theta 函数理论推广至不可约奇异黎曼曲面（irreducible singular Riemann surface）情形，通过构造广义雅可比簇（generalised Jacobian）紧化上的 theta 函数，并利用平移作用得到所有给定次数的线丛及其“万有截面”（universal section），从而建立了奇异情形下的黎曼经典结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典黎曼理论将 theta 函数与光滑黎曼曲面的线丛和 Abel 映射联系起来，但该理论在奇异黎曼曲面（singular Riemann surface）情形下尚不完整。本文旨在将此经典构造推广到不可约奇异黎曼曲面，填补这一理论空白。

Method: 设 $X$ 为不可约奇异黎曼曲面，$\widetilde X$ 为其解奇异化（desingularisation）。利用广义雅可比簇 $J(X)$ 到 $\widetilde X$ 的雅可比簇 $J(\widetilde X)$ 的纤维化结构，以及提升的 Abel 映射 $A: \widetilde X \to J(X)$，在广义雅可比簇 $J(X)$ 的紧化上构造 theta 函数（作为某个适当正线丛的截面）。随后借助 $J(X)$ 上的平移作用生成所有同次数的线丛，并将平移后的 theta 函数限制于 $A(\widetilde X)$ 上，得到 $X$ 上该次数线丛的“万有截面”。

Result: 成功在不可约奇异黎曼曲面情形下，构造了广义雅可比簇紧化上的 theta 函数，并利用该函数及其平移，统一描述了所有给定次数的线丛及其截面，实现了对经典黎曼结果的奇异推广。

Conclusion: 本文的结果将黎曼关于 theta 函数与线丛关系的经典理论从光滑曲面延伸到了不可约奇异黎曼曲面，为奇异代数几何中的 Abel 映射和线丛理论提供了统一的构造框架。

Abstract: Let $X$ be an irreducible singular Riemann surface, with desingularisation $\widetilde X$. The generalised Jacobian $J(X)$ of $X$ fibers over the Jacobian $J(\widetilde{X})$ of $\widetilde X$, and there is an Abel map $A$ of $\widetilde X$ to $J(X)$, lifting the Abel map to $J(\widetilde X)$. We build a theta function on a compactification of the generalised Jacobian $J(X)$ (giving a section of a suitable positive line bundle). The translation action on $J(X)$ then yields all line bundles of that degree, and the translates of the theta function, restricted to $A(\widetilde X)$, give a ``universal section'' of the line bundles of that degree over $X$. This extends to the singular case a classical result of Riemann.

</details>


### [5] [Positive Geometries from Cubic Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11909)
*Bernd Sturmfels,Simon Telen*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文从正几何（positive geometry）的新视角研究三次曲面（cubic surfaces），分别分析了二维（曲面减去27条直线）、三维（三维空间中的补集）和四维（模空间）情形下的正排列（positive arrangement）、组合秩（combinatorial rank）以及规范形式（canonical forms）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为正几何理论在代数几何中的应用提供新的研究对象，将三次曲面这一经典代数几何对象纳入正几何的分析框架。

Method: 从正几何视角出发，分别针对三次曲面的二维、三维和四维几何对象，分析其正排列结构、组合秩以及对应的规范形式。

Result: 在二维（曲面减去27条直线）、三维（三维空间中的补集）和四维（模空间）三种情形下，均获得了对应的正排列、组合秩和规范形式。

Conclusion: 正几何框架可以有效地应用于三次曲面的研究，为理解其几何与组合结构提供了新的统一视角。

Abstract: We present a study of cubic surfaces from the novel perspective of positive geometry. Our positive geometries have dimension two (the surface minus its 27 lines), dimension three (its complement in 3-space), and dimension four (the moduli space). In each case we explore the positive arrangement, its combinatorial rank, and the canonical forms.

</details>


<div id='math.DG'></div>

# math.DG [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [Convergence of Lorentzian spaces and curvature bounds for generalized cones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11271)
*Christian Ketterer*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文提出了洛伦兹预长度空间（Lorentzian pre-length spaces）的一种新收敛概念——$\ell$-收敛（$\ell$-convergence），证明了类时曲率（timelike curvature）和类时曲率-维度（timelike curvature-dimension）边界在该收敛下的稳定性，并将其应用于广义洛伦兹锥（generalized Lorentzian cones）以证明尖锐的曲率界和预紧性定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究在处理洛伦兹预长度空间的收敛问题时缺乏统一的、适用于广义洛伦兹锥的框架，且类时曲率与类时曲率-维度边界在收敛下的稳定性尚未得到充分证明。作者旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 作者首先定义了$\ell$-收敛（$\ell$-convergence）概念，以扩展此前该领域的收敛概念。随后，通过分析广义洛伦兹锥（generalized Lorentzian cones）的结构，证明了若底空间$I_i$与纤维$X_i$在Gromov-Hausdorff（GH）意义下收敛且函数$f_i$一致收敛，则对应的广义锥序列在$\ell$意义下收敛。

Result: 类时曲率（timelike curvature）和类时曲率-维度（timelike curvature-dimension）边界在（带测度的）$\ell$-收敛下保持稳定。广义洛伦兹锥在底空间与纤维的GH收敛及函数一致收敛条件下满足$\ell$-收敛，并由此获得尖锐的类时曲率与类时曲率-维度边界。此外，在具有全Ricci（或Riemann）曲率张量一致下界的平滑广义锥类中，$\ell$-收敛满足预紧性定理（pre-compactness theorem）。

Conclusion: 本文建立的$\ell$-收敛概念为洛伦兹预长度空间提供了统一且稳定的收敛框架，尤其适用于广义洛伦兹锥；所得预紧性定理为后续在更广泛的Lorentzian几何（Lorentzian geometry）背景下研究收敛性与曲率边界奠定了基础。

Abstract: The goal of this article is twofold. We introduce a notion of convergence for Lorentzian pre-length spaces, $\ell$-convergence, that extends previous convergence notions in this context. We show that timelike curvature and timelike curvature-dimension bounds are stable under (measured) $\ell$-convergence. Then, we show that $\ell$-convergence is well adapted for generalized Lorentzian cones: a sequence of generalized cones $-I_i\times_{f_i}X_i$ converges in $\ell$ sense if the base $I_i$ and the fiber $X_i$ converge in GH sense and the functions $f_i$ converge uniformly. We use this to show sharp timelike curvature and timelike curvature-dimension bounds for such cones. Finally, we obtain a pre-compactness theorem for $\ell$-convergence in the class of smooth generalized cones that have a uniform lower bound on the full Ricci (or Riemann) curvature tensor.

</details>


### [7] [A Comparison Theorem For the Mass of ALE and ALF Toric 4-Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12352)
*Aghil Alaee,Marcus Khuri,Hari Kunduri*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文针对具有非负标量曲率的完整ALE/ALF toric 4-流形，建立了质量的下界。该下界由对应引力瞬子的质量及其内部全测地2-球面的锥角缺陷决定，并推广至带锥形或轨形奇点的情况。同时证明了刚性：不等式取等当且仅当该流形是 Ricci 平坦的且与对应引力瞬子一致。结果可与正质量定理相关联，并提供了引力瞬子的变分刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论和几何分析中，正质量定理（positive mass theorem）表明在渐进平坦（asymptotically flat）背景下质量非负，但在ALE/ALF（asymptotically locally Euclidean / asymptotically locally flat）情形下，正性可能失效。本文旨在建立ALE/ALF toric 4-流形在非负标量曲率条件下的质量下界，并解释正性失效的原因。

Method: 通过将完整ALE/ALF toric 4-流形的质量与具有相同轨道空间（rod structure）结构的toric引力瞬子（gravitational instanton）的质量进行比较，并纳入引力瞬子内部作为第二同调群生成元的全测地2-球面（totally geodesic 2-spheres）的锥角缺陷（conical angle defects）所确定的表达式，构造下界不等式。该不等式还可推广至流形含有锥形奇点（conical singularities）或轨形奇点（orbifold singularities）的情形。

Result: 得到了ALE/ALF toric 4-流形质量的一个尖锐下界，该下界由对应toric引力瞬子的质量及其内部全测地2-球面的锥角缺陷之和给出。不等式在带奇点情形下也成立。刚性结果表明，不等式取等当且仅当该流形是Ricci平坦的（Ricci flat）且与对应引力瞬子一致。

Conclusion: 该结果可视为正质量定理在ALE/ALF背景下的推广，解释了正性在何种条件下可能失效。此外，主定理还可被解释为对相关toric引力瞬子的一种变分刻画（variational characterization）。

Abstract: We establish sharp lower bounds for the mass of asymptotically locally Euclidean (ALE) and asymptotically locally flat (ALF) toric 4-manifolds, in terms of equilibrium geometries consisting of gravitational instantons. More precisely, the mass of a complete ALE or ALF toric 4-manifold with nonnegative scalar curvature is bounded below by a sum comprised of the following quantities: the mass of the corresponding toric gravitational instanton having the same orbit space (rod) structure as the original ALE/ALF manifold, and an expression determined by the conical angle defects of totally geodesic 2-spheres within the instanton that serve as generators for its second homology. The inequality may be generalized to the situation in which the ALE/ALF manifold also possesses conical singularities as well as orbifold singularities, and it suggests a refined notion of `total mass' in which the result simply states that the total mass of the ALE/ALF manifold is not less than that of the corresponding gravitational instanton. Furthermore, we prove rigidity for these statements, namely the inequality is saturated only when the ALE/ALF manifold is Ricci flat and in fact agrees with the corresponding instanton. These results may be viewed in the context of positive mass theorems, providing an explanation of how positivity can fail in the ALE/ALF setting. Moreover, the main theorem may be interpreted as yielding a variational characterization of the relevant toric gravitational instantons.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.dis-nn'></div>

# cond-mat.dis-nn [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Context-Gated Associative Retrieval: From Theory to Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10970)
*Moulik Choraria,Argyrios Gerogiannis,Vidhata Jayaraman,Ankur Mani,Lav R. Varshney*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出一种两阶段联想记忆架构，通过上下文门控子电路重塑检索能量景观，从理论上证明其能指数级提升检索性能，并揭示该机制与大语言模型中上下文学习的内在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Hopfield网络及其推广将检索视为固定的查询到记忆的映射（query-to-memory mapping），忽略了外部上下文（external context）在回忆过程中的作用。本文旨在弥补这一缺失，引入上下文门控机制来建模上下文对记忆检索的调控。

Method: 提出一种两阶段联想记忆架构（two-stage associative memory architecture），包含一个上下文门控子电路（context-gate subcircuit），在检索前和检索过程中重塑能量景观（energy landscape）。通过理论分析证明上下文门控能增加记忆间距（inter-memory separation）并诱导稀疏性（sparsity），从而指数级提升检索性能。进一步在Llama-3上评估一阶近似，验证上下文学习（in-context learning）可作为上下文门控检索的实例。

Result: 理论上证明了系统存在唯一的自洽固定点（self-consistent fixed point），检索状态由直接上下文偏置（direct contextual bias）和二阶检索门控反馈回路（second-order retrieval-gate feedback loop）共同驱动。实验上，在Llama-3中观察到的原生动力学行为与理论一致：上下文局部化记忆子空间（context localizes a memory subspace），使零样本查询（zero-shot query）能够清晰区分记忆。

Conclusion: 该框架在联想记忆理论（associative memory theory）与大语言模型现象学（LLM phenomenology）之间建立了机制性联系，为理解上下文学习提供了底层理论基础。

Abstract: Hopfield networks and their generalizations have established deep connections among biological associative memories, statistical physics, and transformers. Yet most models treat retrieval as a fixed query-to-memory mapping, ignoring the role of external context in recall. In this work, we propose a two-stage associative memory architecture, wherein a context-gate subcircuit reshapes the retrieval energy landscape before and during recall. We show theoretically that context gating increases inter-memory separation while inducing sparsity, translating into exponential improvements in retrieval. Crucially, we prove that the system admits a unique self-consistent fixed point, revealing that the resulting retrieval state is driven by both a direct contextual bias and a second-order retrieval-gate feedback loop. We then bridge this theory to transformers; specifically, we evaluate a first-order approximation on Llama-3, confirming that in-context learning acts as context-gated retrieval. Native dynamics mirror our theory: context localizes a memory subspace, enabling the zero-shot query to cleanly discriminate. Ultimately, this framework provides a mechanistic link between associative memory theory and LLM phenomenology.

</details>

### [9] [Dependence of the nonlinear Schr{ö}dinger flow upon the nonlinearity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11643)
*Rémi Carles,Quentin Chauleur,Guillaume Ferriere*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究能量次临界情形下散焦非线性薛定谔方程（defocusing nonlinear Schrödinger equation）的解对非线性幂次（power of nonlinearity）的依赖性，重点关注全局时间描述。按难度递减顺序，讨论了总幂次趋近于1时的极限及其与对数薛定谔方程（logarithmic Schrödinger equation）的联系、长程效应（long range effects）可能存在的描述，以及短程情形（short range case）下散射算子（scattering operator）的连续性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非线性薛定谔方程的解如何依赖于非线性项的幂次，特别是参数趋近临界值时的行为，以及不同作用程（range）下的动力学特征。

Method: 采用理论分析框架，针对能量次临界（energy-subcritical）的散焦非线性薛定谔方程，从三个递进难度的问题出发进行系统性研究。

Result: 总幂次趋近于1时的极限行为与对数薛定谔方程存在联系；对长程效应和短程情形分别给出了解的动力学描述和散射算子的连续性结果。

Conclusion: 非线性薛定谔方程的解对非线性幂次具有敏感依赖性，极限情形与对数薛定谔方程自然衔接，不同作用程下解的全局行为呈现不同特征。

Abstract: We consider the defocusing nonlinear Schr{ö}dinger equation in the energy-subcritical case, and investigate the dependence of the solution upon the power of the nonlinearity. Special attention is paid to the global in time description. The main three aspects addressed, in the decreasing order of difficulty, are the limit when the total power tends to one, along with the connection with the logarithmic Schr{ö}dinger equation, the description when long range effects may be present, and the continuity of the scattering operator in the short range case. This text resumes the presentation given by the first author at {É}cole polytechnique for the Laurent Schwartz seminar, in May 2026.

### [10] [The unified transform for Burgers' equation: Application to unsaturated flow in finite interval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11788)
*Konstantinos Kalimeris,Leonidas Mindrinos,Athanasios Paraskevopoulos*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对一维垂直入渗问题，在恒定扩散系数和二次水力传导率假设下，将Richards方程简化为Burgers方程，通过Hopf-Cole变换线性化后，利用统一变换方法（Unified Transform Method / Fokas方法）求解有限区间上的扩散方程，得到显式积分表示解，数值结果与经典Fourier级数解一致，但收敛性和稳定性更优，并考察了两个水文应用实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Richards方程（Richards' equation）的求解通常因非线性而面临挑战，尤其是在一维垂直入渗（one-dimensional vertical infiltration）问题中，需要更高效、稳定的解析或半解析方法。

Method: 在恒定扩散系数（constant diffusivity）和水力传导率（hydraulic conductivity）与含水量（water content）呈二次关系的假设下，将Richards方程简化为Burgers方程；通过Hopf-Cole变换（Hopf-Cole transformation）将其线性化为有限区间上的扩散方程（diffusion equation），并带有混合边界条件（mixed boundary conditions）；随后利用统一变换方法（Unified Transform Method / Fokas method）求解该初边值问题。

Result: 该方法给出了解的显式积分表示（explicit integral representation）。数值评估结果与经典Fourier级数（Fourier series）解完全一致，但在收敛性（convergence）和稳定性（stability）方面表现更优。

Conclusion: 统一变换方法为求解简化的Richards方程提供了一种有效的替代方案，尤其在水文应用（hydrological applications）的两个实例中得到了验证，展示了该方法在实际问题中的适用性。

Abstract: In this paper, we focus on one-dimensional vertical infiltration, assuming constant diffusivity and a quadratic relationship between hydraulic conductivity and water content. Under these assumptions, Richards' equation reduces to Burgers' equation, which we then linearize via the Hopf-Cole transformation. This turns the initial boundary value problem into a diffusion equation on a finite interval with mixed boundary conditions. To solve it, we use the Unified Transform Method (also known as the Fokas method). This approach gives an explicit integral representation of the solution, and when evaluated numerically, the results match classical Fourier series solutions exactly, but with better convergence and stability. Two examples from hydrological applications are examined.

</details>

### [11] [Strain-controlled crossover between Majorana and Andreev bound states in disordered superconductor-semiconductor heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11066)
*Shubhanshu Karoliya,Ekta,Gargee Sharma*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过紧束缚 Bogoliubov–de Gennes 模拟，研究了半导体纳米线和石墨烯纳米带中非均匀应变对低能态的控制与转换作用，发现应变能有效调节 Majorana 边界态与部分分离的 Andreev 束缚态之间的相互转化，并建立了基于位置依赖拓扑质量的解析框架，为在无序系统中区分和稳定 Majorana 模式提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑 Majorana 边界态（MBS）在超导杂化系统中被微扰低能激发所掩盖，特别是部分分离的 Andreev 束缚态（psABS）可模拟 Majorana 特征，导致明确识别困难，亟需一种系统性的调控手段来区分和稳定 MBS。

Method: 采用紧束缚 Bogoliubov–de Gennes（BdG）模拟，研究一维半导体纳米线和石墨烯纳米带系统，其中涉及超导性、Rashba 自旋轨道耦合、Zeeman 场和无序效应，同时引入空间非均匀应变，并结合基于位置依赖拓扑质量的解析框架分析应变驱动的畴壁运动机制。

Result: 弱应变可通过修正有效能带参数和重新分布波函数权重，定性重塑低能谱；在纳米线中，应变调节 Majorana 分量的空间重叠并移动拓扑相边界，实现从平庸态到 psABS 再到拓扑 MBS 的可控交叉；在石墨烯纳米带中，应变抑制子带混合、解除简并并稳定边界局域模式；无序诱导的 psABS 可通过应变增强的非局域性转化为分离良好的鲁棒 MBS。

Conclusion: 应变是一种有效的调控参数，可用于在现实的无序系统中区分和稳定拓扑 MBS，为拓扑量子计算中复杂杂化结构的 Majorana 模式控制与识别提供了实验上可行的途径。

Abstract: The unambiguous identification of topological Majorana-bound states (MBSs) in superconducting hybrid systems is hindered by trivial low-energy excitations, especially partially separated Andreev bound states (psABSs), which can mimic Majorana signatures. Here we show that spatially nonuniform strain offers a systematic route to control and interconvert these low-energy states. Using tight-binding Bogoliubov--de Gennes simulations, we study one-dimensional semiconductor nanowires and graphene nanoribbons with superconductivity, Rashba spin-orbit coupling, Zeeman fields, and disorder. We find that even weak strain can qualitatively reshape the low-energy spectrum by modifying effective band parameters and redistributing wavefunction weight. In nanowires, strain tunes the spatial overlap of Majorana components and shifts the topological phase boundary, enabling controlled crossovers between trivial states, psABSs, and topological MBSs. In graphene nanoribbons, where multiband effects and edge states produce a dense, hybridized low-energy spectrum, strain suppresses subband mixing, lifts degeneracies, and stabilizes boundary-localized modes. In both platforms, we identify regimes where disorder-induced psABSs are converted into well-separated and robust MBSs through strain-enhanced nonlocality. We further develop an analytical framework based on a position-dependent topological mass and strain-driven domain-wall motion, which captures the physical mechanism of these crossovers and yields a real-space criterion for the emergence and stability of Majorana modes. Our results establish strain as an effective tuning parameter for distinguishing and stabilizing topological MBSs in realistic disordered systems, and suggest an experimentally relevant pathway toward improved control and identification of Majorana modes in complex hybrid structures relevant to topological quantum computation.

</details>


### [12] [The Algebra of Free Fermions: Classifying Spaces, Hamiltonians, and Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11655)
*Tian Yuan,Yang Qi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过引入 $\mathbb{Z}_2$-分次代数 $A_{\mathrm{sym}}^V$ 和 $\mathbb{Z}_2$-分次 Wedderburn-Artin 分解，将具有一般对称性（包括反线性对称、反对称、投影表示和点群对称）的自由费米子系统分类问题转化为表示论中的扩张问题，证明其构成一个 $G$-$Ω$-谱，并开发了 GAP 程序包实现自动计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑物相（topological phases of matter）是现代凝聚态物理（condensed matter physics）的核心研究领域。尽管自由费米子系统（free fermion systems）如拓扑绝缘体和超导体已通过“十重分类法（Tenfold Way）”和 K-理论（K-theory）得到研究，但对于包含反线性对称、反对称、投影表示和点群对称等一般对称性的系统，仍缺乏统一的分类框架和计算方法。

Method: 在 Kitaev 的 $Ω$-谱（$Ω$-spectrum）和分类空间（classifying space）思想以及 Freed-Moore 的 K-理论基础上，证明自由费米子系统构成一个 $G$-$Ω$-谱（genuine $G$-$Ω$-spectrum）并与物理文献中的多种分类方案建立联系。引入 $\mathbb{Z}_2$-分次代数（$\mathbb{Z}_2$-graded algebra）$A_{\mathrm{sym}}^V$，将一般对称性分类问题转化为表示论（representation theory）中的扩张问题（extension problem）；为此发展了 $\mathbb{Z}_2$-分次 Wedderburn-Artin 分解（$\mathbb{Z}_2$-graded Wedderburn-Artin decomposition）的计算方法，并开发了 GAP 程序包实现自动化。

Result: $\mathbb{Z}_2$-分次 Wedderburn-Artin 分解不仅能给出分类结果，还能显式构造对应的 Dirac 哈密顿量（Dirac Hamiltonian）。基于该分解开发的 GAP 程序包可实现相关计算的自动化。

Conclusion: 本文为具有一般对称性的自由费米子系统提供了一个统一的数学分类框架，并通过代数分解方法将分类与哈密顿量显式构造相结合，为拓扑物相的理论计算提供了实用的自动化工具。

Abstract: Research on topological phases of matter is a core field in modern condensed matter physics. Free fermion systems, such as topological insulators and superconductors, have been studied using the "Tenfold Way" and K-theory. Building on Kitaev's idea of $Ω$-spectrum and classifying space, as well as Freed-Moore's K-theory, this work demonstrates that free fermionic systems form a genuine $G$-$Ω$-spectrum and clarifies its connection to several distinct classification schemes appearing in the physical literature. By introducing the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-graded algebra $A_{\mathrm{sym}}^V$, the classification problem for systems with general symmetries, including antilinear symmetries, antisymmetries, projective representations, and point group symmetries, is turned into an extension problem in representation theory. To solve this, a computational method for the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-graded Wedderburn-Artin decomposition of $A_{\mathrm{sym}}^V$ is developed. This decomposition not only yields a classification but also enables the explicit construction of the corresponding Dirac Hamiltonian. Furthermore, a GAP programming package has been developed to automate these calculations.

</details>


### [13] [Valley-Controlled Viscosity of Two-Dimensional Dirac Fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11069)
*Alexey Ermakov,Alessandro Principi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文研究了弱杂化小角度扭曲双层石墨烯中谷不平衡（valley imbalance）对二维狄拉克流体（Dirac fluids）粘度的调控作用，发现谷能级分裂可产生非单调的粘性响应，并对比分析了单层石墨烯（MLG）和二维电子气（2DEG）的粘度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受近期弱杂化小角度扭曲双层石墨烯实验的启发，作者希望探索谷不平衡（valley imbalance）如何影响二维狄拉克流体（Dirac fluids）的粘性，从而为调控流体动力学输运提供新的自由度。

Method: 通过理论分析，研究两个低能狄拉克锥（Dirac cones）相对位移对电子流体粘度的控制作用；计算单层石墨烯（MLG）和二维电子气（2DEG）的粘度作为对比基准。

Result: 增大谷能级分裂会导致系统依次经历谷耗尽（valley depletion）、电荷中性交叉（charge-neutrality crossover）和电子-空穴散射（electron-hole scattering）等不同输运区间，产生显著的非单调粘性响应。单层石墨烯的运动粘度（kinematic viscosity）因其惯性质量密（inertial mass density）对温度的强依赖而呈单调递减函数。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了谷控制（valley control）可作为调控狄拉克材料流体动力学输运的有效途径，并阐明了能带结构、散射相空间（scattering phase space）和屏蔽效应（screening）在设定粘性响应中的相互作用。

Abstract: Motivated by recent experiments in weakly hybridized small-angle twisted bilayer graphene, we investigate how valley imbalance affects the viscosity of two-dimensional Dirac fluids. We show that shifting the two low-energy Dirac cones relative to one another provides a direct knob to control the viscosity of the electron fluid. As the splitting is increased, the system passes through distinct transport regimes associated with valley depletion, charge-neutrality crossover, and the onset of electron-hole scattering, producing a pronounced nonmonotonic response. To place this result in context, we also analyze the viscosity in monolayer graphene (MLG) and two-dimensional electron gas (2DEG). We show that, due to the strong dependence of its inertial mass density on temperature, the kinematic viscosity of MLG is a monotonically decreasing function of temperature. Our results identify valley control as a route to tuning hydrodynamic transport in Dirac materials and clarify the interplay between band structure, scattering phase space, and screening in setting the viscous response.

</details>


### [14] [Photon Momentum Enabled Symmetry Breaking and Nonlinear Photocurrents in the Centrosymmetric Dirac Semimetal PdTe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11113)
*Sambhu G Nath,Subhadip Manna,R K Gopal,Chiranjib Mitra*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明在中心对称狄拉克半金属（centrosymmetric Dirac semimetal）PdTe中，光子动量转移可作为动态对称性破缺机制，使名义上被体相对称性禁止的非线性光学响应得以实现，并系统区分了圆光生伏打效应（CPGE）、几何位移电流和光子拖曳过程的贡献，建立了厚度依赖的螺旋性光电流与量子几何张量之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中心对称狄拉克半金属中，时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）与中心反演对称性（inversion symmetry）的共存通常会禁止二阶非线性光电流（second order nonlinear photocurrent）。探索如何在保持体相对称性的同时，通过动态手段（而非静态结构破缺）来获取被禁阻的非线性光学响应，是本研究的核心动机。

Method: 采用偏振敏感测量（polarization sensitive measurements）技术，结合厚度依赖分析（thickness dependent analysis），对中心对称狄拉克半金属PdTe中光子动量转移引起的非线性光电流进行系统表征，区分不同微观机制的贡献。

Result: 螺旋性依赖的光电流在垂直入射时消失，随入射角变化而反转符号，表明光子与自旋极化表面态（spin polarized surface states）之间存在耦合。厚度依赖分析显示，螺旋性依赖光电流分量C随薄膜厚度线性标度，证明该响应来源于动量转移所启用的体相贡献（bulk contribution），而非仅来自表面态或应变。

Conclusion: 光学激发可以动态降低系统的有效对称性，从而实现对量子几何张量（quantum geometric tensor）的探测。这项工作确立了PdTe作为高对称拓扑材料中研究光子动量驱动的非平衡动力学（nonequilibrium dynamics）的有前景平台。

Abstract: In centrosymmetric Dirac semimetals, second order nonlinear photocurrents are forbidden by the coexistence of time-reversal and inversion symmetries. Here, we demonstrate that finite photon momentum transfer acts as a dynamic symmetry breaking mechanism in PdTe, enabling nonlinear optical responses that are nominally forbidden in the centrosymmetric bulk. Through polarization sensitive measurements, we resolve distinct contributions from the circular photogalvanic effect (CPGE), geometric shift currents, and photon drag mediated processes. We show that the helicity dependent current vanishes at normal incidence and reverses sign with the angle of incidence, reflecting the coupling between photons and spin polarized surface states. Crucially, thickness dependent analysis reveals that the helicity dependent photocurrent component C scales with film thickness, establishing a robust bulk contribution enabled by momentum transfer. This confirms that incident photons provide the directional axis required to probe interband quantum geometry, rather than the response originating solely from surface states or strain. Our results demonstrate that optical excitation can dynamically reduce the effective symmetry of the system, enabling access to quantum geometric tensors and establishing PdTe as a promising platform for exploring nonequilibrium dynamics governed by photon momentum in high symmetry topological materials.

</details>


### [15] [Bound States in Second-order Topological Graphitic Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11164)
*Haiyue Huang,Prineha Narang,Ioannis Petrides*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出基于二维石墨烯结构实现四极绝缘体（quadrupole insulators）的通用设计原则，通过调控之字形边缘（zigzag edges）的位置与连接识别出四种拓扑类别，发现拓扑保护的无质量角态（massless corner state）以及通过调节畴壁平滑度产生的具有非零角动量的有质量局域态（massive localized states），为实验可及的二次拓扑绝缘体（SOTIs）提供了实用框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 四极绝缘体作为一类二次拓扑绝缘体（second-order topological insulators, SOTIs），具有独特性质，但在实际电子材料平台上实现仍极为罕见，因此亟需提出通用的设计原理以推动其实验实现。

Method: 基于二维石墨烯结构，设计并调控之字形边缘（zigzag edges）的位置与连接方式，从而识别出四种拓扑类别；进一步通过调节畴壁（domain wall）的光滑程度来探索局域态的性质变化。

Result: 发现在不同拓扑类别畴的交界处出现拓扑保护的无质量角态（massless corner state）；通过调节畴壁平滑度，可额外产生具有非零角动量的有质量局域态（massive localized states）。

Conclusion: 该工作为实验上可实现的二次拓扑绝缘体（SOTIs）提供了实用框架，并揭示了二维体系中无质量与有质量束缚态共存的现象。

Abstract: Quadrupole insulators are a class of second-order topological insulators (SOTIs) that host zero-dimensional corner states within a two-dimensional bulk. Despite their unique properties, their realization in electronic systems on realistic material platforms remains rare. In this work, we present a general design principle to obtain quadrupole insulators based on two-dimensional graphitic structures. By engineering the positions and connections of zigzag edges, we identify four topological classes of graphitic structures. We show that topologically protected massless corner state emerge at the intersection of domains belonging to different topological classes. Crucially, by tuning the smoothness of the domain wall, we further demonstrate the appearance of additional massive localized states with non-zero angular momentum. Our results provide a practical framework for realizing experimentally accessible SOTIs and uncover the coexistence of both massless and massive bound states in two dimensions.

</details>


### [16] [Magnetic-field-tunable cyclotron hyperbolic polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11185)
*Zijian Zhou,Ran Jing,Heng Wang,Lukas Wehmeier,Mengkun Liu,Bing Cheng*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文预测了一类由磁场诱导载流子回旋运动（cyclotron motion）产生的新型双曲极化激元（hyperbolic polaritons），并建立了包含与其他集体激发耦合的理论框架，表明该模式可通过太赫兹近场纳米显微术（terahertz near-field nanoscopy）在实空间直接观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统双曲极化激元通常与结构各向异性或声子剩余射线带（Reststrahlen bands）相关，本文旨在探索由磁场诱导回旋运动作为双曲极化激元的新产生机制。

Method: 在高迁移率半金属（semimetals）中施加垂直磁场，利用回旋响应使面内介电函数在回旋共振频率以下从类金属转变为类绝缘体，而面外介电函数保持金属性，从而构建双曲介电环境并支持场可调双曲极化激元；同时建立了包含与其他集体激发耦合的理论框架。

Result: 该各向异性产生的双曲介电环境支持场可调（field-tunable）的双曲极化激元，且这些模式可通过太赫兹近场纳米显微术在实空间直接可视化。

Conclusion: 该工作将回旋运动确立为双曲极化激元的新产生路径，并为磁可编程纳米光子学（magnetically programmable nanophotonics）提供了一个多功能平台。

Abstract: Hyperbolic polaritons are conventionally associated with structural anisotropy or phononic Reststrahlen bands. Here, we predict a new class of hyperbolic polaritons arising from magnetic-field-induced cyclotron motion of charge carriers. When a perpendicular magnetic field is applied to high-mobility semimetals, the cyclotron response drives the in-plane dielectric function from metallic- to insulating-like below the cyclotron resonance frequency, while the out-of-plane response remains metallic. This anisotropy creates a hyperbolic dielectric environment that supports field-tunable hyperbolic polaritons. We develop a comprehensive theoretical framework incorporating coupling to other collective excitations and show that these modes can be directly visualized in real space via terahertz near-field nanoscopy. Our work identifies cyclotron motion as a new route to hyperbolic polaritons and establishes a versatile platform for magnetically programmable nanophotonics.

</details>


### [17] [Optical signatures of antiferromagnetic correlations in a strongly interacting quantum Hall MoSe2 monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11249)
*Jiho Sung,Pavel A. Volkov,Ilya Esterlis,Jue Wang,Luke N. Holtzmann,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Katayun Barmak,James Hone,Mikhail D. Lukin,Philip Kim,Hongkun Park*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过磁光光谱学（magneto-optical spectroscopy）实验，在MoSe2单层强关联电子液体中发现了非常规的量子霍尔态，该态倾向于零谷极化（zero valley polarization），表现出反铁磁相互作用（antiferromagnetic interactions），与传统量子霍尔铁磁体（quantum Hall ferromagnet）的自旋极化行为不一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强磁场下电子动能被淬灭形成朗道能级（Landau levels, LLs），弱相互作用即可驱动有序相，但零场下强电子-电子相互作用会改变这一图景，使预言态变得困难。本文旨在揭示强关联电子液体中磁场驱动的非常规量子霍尔态。

Method: 采用磁光光谱学（magneto-optical spectroscopy）手段，测量MoSe2单层中激子极化子（exciton polaron）能量随垂直磁场和电子密度的振荡行为，从而探测关联电子液体中朗道能级的形成以及不同谷（valley）间朗道能级的交叉。

Result: 降低朗道能级填充因子（filling factor）时，相互作用增强，交叉系统地展宽，表明完全极化谷简并朗道能级所需的塞曼能（Zeeman energy）增加。这些观测与反铁磁相互作用一致，倾向于零谷极化基态，与传统量子霍尔铁磁性不一致。

Conclusion: 该发现证明了强关联电子液体中存在性质不同的量子霍尔磁性形式，为理解磁场驱动的自旋非极化分数量子霍尔态（spin-unpolarized fractional quantum Hall states）及有序态提供了锚定点。

Abstract: Strong magnetic fields quench the kinetic energy of electrons, leading to the formation of flat energy bands, known as Landau levels (LLs). In this situation, even weak interactions can drive the emergence of various ordered phases. The simplest of such phases is a quantum Hall ferromagnet, where a spontaneous spin polarization emerges when LLs with opposite spins cross. The presence of strong electron-electron interaction at zero field changes this picture and makes the resulting states much harder to predict. Here we use magneto-optical spectroscopy to reveal quantum Hall states with unconventional correlations favouring an unpolarized state in the strongly correlated electron liquid in a MoSe2 monolayer. The oscillations of the exciton polaron energies as a function of perpendicular magnetic field and electron density demonstrate the emergence of LLs in a correlated electron liquid and density-dependent crossings between LLs of opposite valleys. On lowering the LL filling factor, where interactions within LLs are stronger, the crossings systematically broaden, indicating an increase in the Zeeman energy required to fully polarize the valley-degenerate LLs. These observations are shown to be consistent with antiferromagnetic interactions between LL electrons, favouring a ground state with zero valley polarization, and are therefore inconsistent with conventional quantum Hall ferromagnetism. This discovery demonstrates a qualitatively distinct form of quantum Hall magnetism in a strongly correlated electron liquid, establishing an anchoring point for understanding spin-unpolarized fractional and ordered states of correlated electrons driven by magnetic field.

### [18] [Laser-assisted tunneling in a static tungsten diselenide WSe$_2$ barrier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11737)
*Rachid El Aitouni,Mohammed El Azar,Clarence Cortes,Pablo Díaz,David Laroze,Ahmed Jellal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用Floquet形式理论研究单层WSe₂中狄拉克费米子（Dirac fermions）在静态静电势垒与线偏振激光场共同作用下的隧穿效应，发现激光场诱导丰富的Floquet边带结构，可有效抑制克莱因隧穿（Klein tunneling），并实现量子输运的动态光控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索光-物质相互作用对单层WSe₂中狄拉克费米子隧穿行为的调控机制，特别是克服克莱因隧穿限制、实现动态量子输运控制的可行性。

Method: 采用Floquet形式理论（Floquet formalism）处理时间周期驱动，推导系统三个区域的解析波函数；在界面处施加连续性条件得到透射和反射系数，并利用Büttiker方法计算电导（conductance）。

Result: 激光场诱导出丰富的Floquet边带结构（Floquet sideband structure），其数量和强度随驱动参数α增大而增强，导致透射显著抑制并有效克服克莱因隧穿。增大辐照区域宽度会增强费米子与外场的相互作用，引发能量重整化（energy renormalization）并形成类斯塔克束缚态（Stark-like confined states）。多个Floquet通道间的相互作用产生强干涉效应，进一步降低透射电流。

Conclusion: 光-物质相互作用可实现WSe₂材料中量子输运的动态控制，为可调谐量子滤波器（tunable quantum filters）和光控纳米尺度晶体管（light-controlled nanoscale transistors）等新型光电器件的开发提供技术支持。

Abstract: We study the tunneling effect of Dirac fermions in a monolayer WSe$_2$ subjected to a static electrostatic barrier and irradiated by a linearly polarized laser field. Within the Floquet formalism, the time-periodic driving is incorporated to derive analytical wave functions across the three regions of the system. By enforcing continuity conditions at the interfaces, we obtain the transmission and reflection coefficients, which are then used to evaluate the conductance via the Büttiker approach. Our results reveal that the laser field induces a rich Floquet sideband structure, whose number and strength increase with the driving parameter $α$. This leads to a significant suppression of transmission and provides an efficient mechanism to overcome Klein tunneling. Moreover, increasing the width of the irradiated region enhances the interaction between fermions and the external field, resulting in energy renormalization and the formation of Stark-like confined states. The interaction between several Floquet channels creates strong interference effects, which reduce the transmitted current even further. The results demonstrate that light-matter interaction allows for the dynamic control of quantum transport in WSe$_2$ materials. This technology allows for the development of new optoelectronic devices, including tunable quantum filters and light-controlled nanoscale transistors.

Method: 构建具有两个交替跳跃参数的一维六角元胞分子链模型，分别在周期性边界条件（periodic boundary condition）与开放边界条件（open boundary condition）下求解能谱，分析跳跃比（hopping ratio）对能隙及相变的影响。

Result: 系统呈现色散带（dispersive band）与平带（flat band）共存的丰富能谱结构；存在两种绝缘相，由跳跃比控制的能隙闭合（gap-closing transition）跃迁分隔；在跳跃比低于临界值的拓扑相（topological phase）中，有限链边界出现指数局域（exponentially localized）的边缘态（edge state）。

Conclusion: 跳跃比是调控体系从普通绝缘相到拓扑相的关键参数；边缘态的出现证实了该体系在特定参数下具有拓扑非平庸性质。

Abstract: We study the eigenspectrum properties of a one-dimensional molecular chain composed of hexagonal unit cells. The system features two alternating hopping parameters, resulting in a rich energy spectrum with both dispersive and flat bands. By analyzing the model under periodic and open boundary conditions, we identify two insulating phases separated by a gap-closing transition controlled by the ratio of hopping amplitudes. In the topological phase, realized when the hopping ratio falls below a critical value, edge states emerge that are exponentially localized at the boundaries of finite chains.

### [20] [Flow bistability in non-Newtonian electron fluid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12150)
*A. N. Afanasiev,P. S. Alekseev*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维导体中非牛顿电子流体的非线性流动，基于局部电子加热机制推导了非牛顿电子流体的简化动力学方程，揭示了窄通道几何中双稳态流动共存导致的S形电流-电压特性，并展示了电流开关与滞后现象的瞬态响应过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代低缺陷密度、强电子-电子散射的二维导体为粘性电子流体（viscous electron fluid）的形成提供了有利平台，其电荷输运处于流体动力学（hydrodynamic） regime，呈现诸多实验特征。本文旨在探究该体系在非牛顿（non-Newtonian）粘度依赖于流速梯度情况下的非线性流动行为，并分析其背后的局部电子加热（local electron heating）机制。

Method: 推导了非牛顿电子流体的简化动力学方程（simplified dynamic equations），考虑窄通道几何（narrow channel geometry）中的二维电子流体流动；进一步求解含时动力学方程（time-dependent dynamic equations），模拟纵向电压阶跃变化下的瞬态响应（transient response）。

Result: 在特定参数范围内，窄通道几何中存在两种稳态流动构型（steady-state flow configurations）共存，这种双稳态（bistability）导致电流-电压特性呈现S形（S-shaped current-voltage characteristic）。瞬态响应分析表明，非牛顿电子流体样品中会出现电流开关（current switching）与滞后（hysteresis）现象。

Conclusion: 局部电子加热可能是二维电子流体中非线性的主要机制之一；非牛顿效应导致的流动双稳态可解释相应的非线性输运行为，为理解二维导体的流体动力学现象提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Modern two dimensional conductors with low defect densities and strong electron-electron scattering are favorable platforms for formation of a viscous fluid of conduction electrons. Electric properties of these systems are determined by the hydrodynamic regime of charge transport distinguished by many experimental signatures: a decrease in sample resistance with increasing temperature (the Ghurzhi effect), strong negative magnetoresistance and others. Here we consider the flow of 2D electron fluid in the nonlinear regime characterized by non-Newtonian viscosity which depends on spatial gradients of hydrodynamic velocity. We derive a simplified version of the dynamic equations for the non-Newtonian electron fluid and consider the specific underlying mechanism associated with local electron heating. Recent works have demonstrated that this may be one of the main mechanisms for nonlinearity in 2D electron fluids. We show that in a certain range of parameters, the two steady-state flow configurations coexist for the narrow channel geometry, and this bistability leads to an S-shaped current-voltage characteristic. By solving the derived time-dependent dynamic equations, we trace the transient response to a step variation of the longitudinal voltage and demonstrate how the current switching and hysteresis occur in samples with the non-Newtonian electron fluid.

### [21] [Probing charge noise in bilayer graphene quantum dots by Landau-Zener-Stückelberg-Majorana spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12257)
*Katrin Hecker,Samuel Möller,Tobias Deußen,Hubert Dulisch,Luca Banszerus,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Christian Volk,Christoph Stampfer*

TL;DR: 该研究利用Landau-Zener-Stückelberg-Majorana（LZSM）干涉谱学技术，测量了双层石墨烯（BLG）双量子点中单粒子电荷量子比特在5–10 GHz频段的高频电荷噪声，提取的噪声谱密度$S_\varepsilon$约为0.5–0.9 neV/$\sqrt{\mathrm{Hz}}$，与III-V族半导体和硅平台相当。温度与频率依赖性表明，热（Johnson）噪声或电子-声子耦合是退相干的主导机制，而非二能级涨落子（two-level fluctuators）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电荷噪声是限制固态器件中量子比特相干性与弛豫的重要因素。在双层石墨烯（BLG）量子点——这一新兴的自旋和谷量子比特（spin- and valley-based qubits）平台中，电荷噪声的来源与大小尚未被充分探索。

Method: 采用Landau-Zener-Stückelberg-Majorana（LZSM）干涉谱学技术，对频率范围为5–10 GHz的单粒子电荷量子比特（single-particle charge qubit）进行高频电荷噪声测量。该量子比特形成于BLG双量子点（double quantum dot）中。

Result: 提取的噪声谱密度（noise spectral density）$S_\varepsilon$约为0.5–0.9 neV/$\sqrt{\mathrm{Hz}}$，与III-V族半导体和硅平台的报道值相当。温度与频率依赖性分析表明，电荷量子比特的退相干主要源于热（Johnson）噪声或电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling），而非二能级涨落子（two-level fluctuators）。

Conclusion: BLG量子点平台的电荷噪声水平与成熟的半导体量子比特平台相当，且其退相干机制由热噪声或电子-声子耦合主导。该结果为BLG量子点作为量子比特平台的可行性提供了噪声特性方面的定量依据。

Abstract: Charge noise is an important factor limiting qubit coherence and relaxation in solid-state devices. In bilayer graphene (BLG) quantum dots, recently established as a promising platform for spin- and valley-based qubits, both the origin and magnitude of charge noise remain largely unexplored. Here, we investigate high-frequency charge noise using Landau-Zener-Stückelberg-Majorana (LZSM) interference spectroscopy. We study a single-particle charge qubit formed in a BLG double quantum dot at frequencies between 5 and 10 GHz and extract a noise spectral density $S_\varepsilon$ on the order of 0.5-0.9 neV$/\sqrt{\mathrm{Hz}}$. This is comparable to values reported for III-V semiconductor platforms and silicon. From the temperature and frequency dependence of the charge qubit decoherence, we conclude that thermal (Johnson) noise or electron-phonon coupling dominates over two-level fluctuators.

</details>


### [22] [Magnon polaritons in a van der Waals ferromagnet coupled to a superconducting resonator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12298)
*Alvaro Bermejillo-Seco,Luuk J. van der Goot,Matteo Arfini,Yaroslav M. Blanter,Gary A. Steele,Herre S. J. van der Zant*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁振子-光子杂化（magnon-photon hybridization）在微波波段对集成磁性激发与超导电路至关重要，但该现象已在块体磁系统中广泛验证，在二维范德瓦尔斯（van der Waals）材料中因磁体积减小和耗散增加而尚未实现。

Method: 采用低阻抗超导谐振腔设计，对剥离的范德瓦尔斯铁磁体Cr₂Ge₂Te₆薄片（厚度低至30纳米）进行微波测量，通过六个器件中可重复的避免交叉（avoided crossings）来表征磁振子极化激元（magnon polaritons）杂化态。

Result: 在六个独立的Cr₂Ge₂Te₆器件中均观测到可重复的避免交叉，证实了磁振子-光子杂化的存在；耦合强度随厚度呈平方根依赖关系（square-root dependence），符合预期规律。

Conclusion: 基于耦合强度对厚度的平方根依赖关系进行外推，表明在单层极限（monolayer limit）下实现磁振子-光子杂化是可行的，为二维磁性材料与超导量子电路的集成铺平了道路。

Abstract: Achieving magnon-photon hybridization in the microwave regime is essential for integrating magnetic excitations with superconducting circuits. While this has been extensively demonstrated in bulk magnetic systems, realizing it in two-dimensional van der Waals materials remains challenging due to their reduced magnetic volume and increased dissipation. Here, magnon-photon hybridization is observed in exfoliated flakes of the van der Waals ferromagnet Cr$_2$Ge$_2$Te$_6$, with thicknesses down to 30 nm. The resulting magnon polaritons-hybrid excitations of cavity photons and magnons-are evidenced by reproducible avoided crossings across six devices, enabled by a low-impedance superconducting resonator design. The coupling strength follows the expected square-root dependence on thickness, and extrapolation of this scaling indicates that hybridization in the monolayer limit is within reach.

### [23] [Optical Response of a screw dislocated GaAs Quantum Wire: Temperature and Pressure Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12371)
*Vinod Kumar,Shweta Kumari,Surender Pratap*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了在温度、静水压力和轴向磁场的共同作用下，螺位错（screw dislocation）对抛物型GaAs圆柱形量子线（cylindrical quantum wire）光学响应的影响。通过扭转修正度规（torsion-modified metric）和与压力、温度相关的有效质量与介电常数，得到含Whittaker函数的薛定谔方程解析解。结果显示，螺位错引起的对称性破缺导致不同跃迁呈现相反的红移/蓝移行为，温度、压力和磁场对光学吸收系数和折射率变化具有可调谐效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索螺位错这一结构缺陷对低维半导体量子线光学性质的影响，以及外场（温度、压力、磁场）的协同调控机制，为量子器件的设计与优化提供理论依据。

Method: 采用扭转修正度规描述螺位错几何效应，结合随压力与温度变化的有效质量与介电常数，求解含抛物限制势的薛定谔方程，获得以Whittaker函数表示的精确解；基于本征态计算线性与三阶非线性光学吸收系数及对应的折射率变化。

Result: 增大螺位错参数导致m=0→+1跃迁出现明显红移并抑制共振振幅，而m=0→-1跃迁则呈现蓝移且峰值增强。升温使共振向高光子能方向移动并增强振幅，静水压力则引起红移并降低峰值强度。磁场增强光学响应并导致m=0→+1跃迁蓝移，而m=0→-1跃迁相反。

Conclusion: 螺位错通过k_z依赖的耦合破缺角动量态m与-m的对称性，使不同跃迁对缺陷参数呈现非对称响应；温度、压力和磁场可作为有效的外部调控手段，可调谐量子线的光学吸收与折射率特性。

Abstract: We investigate the influence of a screw dislocation, characterized by the dislocation parameter, on the optical response of a parabolic GaAs cylindrical quantum wire under the combined effects of temperature, hydrostatic pressure, and the axial magnetic field. Using a torsion-modified metric together with pressure- and temperature-dependent material properties, namely the effective mass and dielectric permittivity, we obtain exact solutions of the Schrödinger equation in terms of Whittaker functions. The screw dislocation introduces a \(k_z\)-dependent coupling that breaks the symmetry between the angular momentum states \(m\) and \(-m\) and modifies the centrifugal term in the effective potential. Based on the resulting eigenstates, we evaluate the linear and third-order nonlinear optical absorption coefficients, as well as the corresponding refractive index changes, for the dipole-allowed transitions \(m = 0 \to +1\) and \(m = 0 \to -1\). Our results show that increasing the dislocation parameter produces a pronounced redshift and suppresses the resonance amplitude for the \(m = 0 \to +1\) transition, whereas the \(m = 0 \to -1\) transition exhibits a blueshift accompanied by peak enhancement. We further find that increasing temperature shifts the resonances toward higher photon energies and enhances their amplitudes, while hydrostatic pressure causes a redshift and reduces the peak intensity for both transitions. In addition, the magnetic field strengthens the optical response and induces a blueshift for the \(m = 0 \to +1\) transition, whereas the opposite behavior is obtained for the \(m = 0 \to -1\) transition. We have also examined the behavior of the refractive index changes, which exhibit analogous asymmetric dependence on the dislocation parameter.

</details>

### [24] [Electronic Direct Detection of Light Dark Matter with Intermediate-Mass Mediators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11063)
*Connor Stratman,Tanner Trickle*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了电子基直接探测实验对亚GeV暗物质（dark matter）与中间质量媒介子（intermediate-mass mediator）相互作用的灵敏度，发现轻、重媒介子质量极限之间可相差多达三个数量级，并公开了相关计算代码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来电子基直接探测实验灵敏度显著提升，但传统分析仅考虑轻、重媒介子质量极限这两个端点情形，忽略了中间质量区域的灵敏度变化，无法准确刻画实验的实际探测能力。

Method: 在Si和Ge靶材料中计算无背景（background-free）灵敏度，并投影DAMIC-M实验对亚GeV暗物质模型的灵敏度；同时结合暗物质通过冻入（freeze-in）机制产生遗存丰度（relic abundance）的条件，确定电子基直接探测实验对媒介子质量的敏感范围。

Result: 轻、重媒介子质量极限之间并非由单一标度分隔，而是存在多达三个数量级的媒介子质量区间，电子基直接探测实验对亚GeV暗物质在该“中间质量”区间内具有显著灵敏度。

Conclusion: 电子基直接探测实验对亚GeV暗物质探测的媒介子质量敏感范围远大于此前预期，相关计算结果已公开集成至EXCEED-DM代码中供社区使用。

Abstract: Recent years have seen dramatic improvements in the sensitivity of electron-based direct detection experiments. Typically, the sensitivity to dark matter scattering is determined in the light and heavy mediator mass limits. In this paper we show that the light and heavy mediator mass limits are not separated by a single scale, but instead can be separated by up to three orders of magnitude in mediator mass for sub-GeV mass dark matter. We calculate the background-free sensitivity in Si and Ge targets, and a projected DAMIC-M sensitivity, to sub-GeV mass dark matter models with ``intermediate-mass" mediators between the light and heavy mediator limits. This allows us to determine the precise range of mediator masses that electron-based direct detection experiments are sensitive to when the dark matter relic abundance is generated via freeze-in. We make the calculations presented here publicly available in an updated release of EXCEED-DM (https://github.com/tanner-trickle/EXCEED-DM).

</details>


### [25] [Time-dependent signals of new physics at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11071)
*Max H. Fieg,Patrick J. Fox,Jinbo Zhang,Aishik Ghosh,Virat Varada,Daniel Whiteson*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用超轻暗物质（ultralight dark matter）与振荡背景场耦合所引起的时间变化（time variation）信号，在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上区分新物理与标准模型（Standard Model）背景，并证明引入时间信息的搜索灵敏度可比不含时间信息的搜索提升至多两倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型强子对撞机（LHC）通过缺失能量和共振搜索等多种渠道探测超出标准模型（Standard Model）的新物理信号。传统搜索假设新物理和标准模型背景在时间上不变（仅考虑系统误差），但若新物理存在时间变化（time variation），则可提供额外维度用于分离信号与背景。

Method: 论文考虑暗物质（dark matter）与夸克（quarks）以及一个额外重粒子（heavy particle）之间的相互作用，利用超轻暗物质（ultralight dark matter）耦合振荡背景场（oscillating background field）所产生的时间变化特征，在LHC上使用时间信息（timing information）进行信号搜索。

Result: 使用时间信息的搜索灵敏度（sensitivity）可比不使用时间信息的搜索提升至多两倍（a factor of two stronger）。

Conclusion: 在LHC搜索中引入时间信息可以显著增强对暗物质相关新物理信号的探测能力，提供一种超越传统时间不变假设的新搜索策略。

Abstract: The Large Hadron Collider (LHC) is sensitive to signals of beyond the Standard Model physics through a variety of channels including missing energy and resonance searches. In most searches, the new physics and the Standard Model backgrounds are assumed to be invariant in time, up to systematic effects from the experiment. However, new physics with a time variation would provide an additional handle to separate signal from background. Such a time variation may come from ultralight dark matter coupling to an oscillating background field. In this paper, we consider an interaction of dark matter with quarks and an additional heavy particle, and show that the sensitivity of a search that uses timing information at the LHC can be up to a factor of two stronger compared to one that does not use time information.

</details>


### [26] [An ultra-broadband axion dark matter experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11078)
*Angelo Esposito,Kin Chung Fong,Lam Hui*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种全新的宽带搜索轴子（axion）策略，利用轴子场平方（axion field squared）控制的观测量，通过将直流超导量子干涉仪（dc SQUID）工作在磁通甜点（flux sweet spot）并使用锁相调制（lock-in modulation）技术，实现对轴子-光子耦合（axion-photon coupling）的探测。该方案超宽带（ultra-broadband），覆盖轴子质量超过15个数量级，灵敏度可达 |g_{aγγ}| ≳ 10^{-16} GeV^{-1}，比现有约束好数个数量级，且基本不依赖于轴子质量。文章还讨论了系统背景来源及消零技术（nulling technique），并指出该策略可推广至轴子-费米子耦合（axion-fermion coupling）及其他暗物质候选者如暗光子（dark photon）的探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有轴子探测方案在质量覆盖范围或灵敏度上存在局限，亟需一种超宽带、高质量无关且高灵敏度的新策略，以更全面地搜索轴子及其他暗物质候选者。

Method: 利用轴子场平方控制的观测量来搜索轴子，具体实现是将直流超导量子干涉仪（dc SQUID）偏置于磁通甜点（flux sweet spot），此时电压与磁通量成二次方关系，并通过锁相调制（lock-in modulation）技术规避低频噪声。

Result: 该方案超宽带（ultra-broadband），覆盖轴子质量超过15个数量级，且可进一步扩展。投影灵敏度为 |g_{aγγ}| ≳ 10^{-16} GeV^{-1}，比当前约束优数个数量级，且基本不依赖于轴子质量。

Conclusion: 讨论了系统背景的来源及消零技术（nulling technique）以将其降至可接受水平，并指出该策略可扩展至轴子-费米子耦合（axion-fermion coupling）及其他暗物质候选者（如暗光子 dark photon）的探测。

Abstract: We propose a novel broadband strategy to search for axions by leveraging observables controlled by the axion field squared. We present a practical implementation of this concept for probing the axion--photon coupling. This is done by operating a dc SQUID at the flux sweet spot, where the voltage depends quadratically on the magnetic flux, and using lock-in modulation to evade low-frequency noise. The proposed setup is ultra-broadband, spanning over 15 orders of magnitude in axion mass, with further expansion of the mass range possible. The projected sensitivity is $|g_{aγγ}| \gtrsim 10^{-16} \text{ GeV}^{-1}$, orders of magnitude better than current bounds, and largely independent of axion mass. We discuss the sources of systematic background and a nulling technique to reduce them to an acceptable level. We also discuss how our strategy could be adapted to probe the axion-fermion coupling, as well as to detect other dark matter candidates such as dark photons.

The ALPs are assumed to originate from $D^\pm$-meson decays in association with a charged pion. We perform both truth-level and detector-level Monte Carlo simulations and obtain the expected sensitivity reach to the mixing parameter between the HNL and the electron neutrino, $|V_{eN}|^2$, with a displaced-vertex search at STCF. We find that STCF can probe values of $|V_{eN}|^2$ about one-to-two orders of magnitude beyond the existing bounds. We also perform an approximate reinterpretation of a search for HNLs at the CHARM experiment, which is subject to model-dependent assumptions on the production and kinematic distributions, and find that beam-dump experiments may provide strong complementary constraints.

### [28] [SMEFT everywhere: a NLO study of $\boldsymbol{pp \to t\bar{t}H}$ with decaying tops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11747)
*Giuseppe Bevilacqua,Minos Reinartz,Malgorzata Worek*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文计算了大型强子对撞机（LHC）双轻子道 $pp\to t\bar{t}H+X$ 过程的次领头阶 QCD 修正，并包含标准模型有效场论（Standard Model Effective Field Theory, SMEFT）中四个维度-6算符的贡献。研究发现，运动学截断、高阶效应以及SMEFT算符在顶夸克衰变中的贡献应当一致地加以考虑，因为它们显著影响了 LHC 上该过程的标准观测量形状。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 计算了 LHC 双轻子道 $pp\to t\bar{t}H+X$ 过程的次领头阶（next-to-leading order, NLO）QCD 修正，并一致地纳入了 SMEFT 中四个维度-6算符（${\cal O}_{tφ}$, ${\cal O}_{φG}$, ${\cal O}_{tG}$, ${\cal O}_{tW}$）的贡献。高阶修正和有效算符同时包含在过程的产生部分和顶夸克衰变中，并考虑了重整化群（renormalization group, RG）效应和线性、交叉及二次贡献的不确定性。

Result: 在 LHC Run III 质心能量 $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV 下给出了积分（integrated）和微分（differential）截面层次的预测。比较了稳定顶夸克假设与从衰变产物重建顶夸克两种方案的结果，并展示了运动学截断、高阶效应和 SMEFT 算符对标准观测量形状的显著影响。

Conclusion: 运动学截断、高阶 QCD 修正以及 SMEFT 维度-6算符在顶夸克衰变中的贡献不可忽略，应当在未来的精确理论预言和实验分析中一致地加以考虑。

Abstract: We present the computation of the next-to-leading order QCD corrections to the $pp\to t\bar{t} H+X$ process in the di-lepton channel at the LHC, including relevant dimension-6 operators $({\cal O}_{tφ}, \, {\cal O}_{φG},\, {\cal O}_{tG}, \, {\cal O}_{tW})$ from the Standard Model Effective Field Theory. In our studies, higher-order corrections and effective operators are consistently included in the production part of the process as well as in the top-quark decays. We perform a detailed study of linear, cross, and quadratic contributions and their uncertainties, including renormalisation group effects. Our findings are presented at the integrated and differential cross-section level for the LHC Run III center-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV. Finally, we provide predictions for $pp\to t\bar{t} H+X$ with stable top quarks and compare them with the results in which top quarks are reconstructed from their decay products. We show that kinematic cuts, as well as higher-order effects and SMEFT operators in top-quark decays, are important and should be consistently considered together, because they have a significant impact on the shape of the standard observables measured for the $pp\to t\bar{t}H+X$ process at the LHC.

Abstract: The photoproduction of $J/Ψ$ in peripheral Oxygen - Oxygen ($OO$) collisions at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) is investigated considering distinct assumptions for the modeling of the nuclear photon flux, overlap function and dipole - proton scattering amplitude. Predictions for the associated rapidity distributions and total cross - sections are presented. Our results indicate that the experimental study of the photoproduction of $J/Ψ$ in peripheral $OO$ collisions is, in principle, feasible. In addition, they point out that the combination of the results for this final state in $OO$ collisions with those obtained for $PbPb$ collisions will allow us to derive important constraints on the description of photon - induced process at peripheral collisions.

Abstract: We compute the graviton absorption and emission rates by hydrogen atoms in line with the results obtained by Weinberg, Gould, Dyson and other authors. The spontaneous emission of gravitons by the hydrogen atoms has a tiny undetectable rate, while the absorption rate of gravitons is much higher and is proportional to the number of hydrogen atoms and to the graviton luminosity. The graviton luminosity of Sun, or a typical star, is induced by the scattering of electrons and protons in a completely ionised hydrogen plasma at the core of the Sun and their energies are in the eV to keV range. We suggest measuring the excess in the ratio of the photon luminosities from interstellar hydrogen atoms that is induced due to the absorption of gravitons. ### [32] [Reviving primordial black hole formation in slow first-order phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11332)
*Wen-Yuan Ai,Ke-Pan Xie*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文论证了在慢速一级相变（slow first-order phase transitions）中产生的大曲率扰动仍可作为原初黑洞（primordial black holes）的有效起源：过冷相变后的缓慢再加热（reheating）会导致宇宙进入早期物质主导时期（early matter-dominated era），即使较小的过密度也能增长并坍缩为原初黑洞，且此类黑洞具有较大自旋。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期分析指出，若在同一规范（gauge）下评估密度对比（density contrast）与形成阈值（formation threshold），慢速一级相变产生原初黑洞的机制似乎被排除。本文旨在证明该机制仍然可行。

Method: 在超冷相变（supercooled transition）后，研究人员引入了缓慢再加热过程，使得宇宙进入一个早期物质主导时期。在该时期内，即使较小的过密度也能增长并坍缩。

Result: 该机制在考虑缓慢再加热及物质主导时期后仍然有效，且产生的原初黑洞具有一个有趣特征——大自旋（large spins）。

Conclusion: 慢速一级相变产生原初黑洞的机制并非被排除，在过冷相变后缓慢再加热导致早期物质主导时期的情景下，该机制依然可行，并能产生具有大自旋的黑洞。

Abstract: Large curvature perturbations generated during slow first-order phase transitions are a promising source of primordial black holes. However, recent analyses suggested that the mechanism is ruled out once the density contrast and the formation threshold are evaluated in the same gauge. In this work, we show that this mechanism remains viable: after a supercooled transition, reheating can be sufficiently slow that the Universe enters an early matter-dominated era, during which even small overdensities grow and collapse into primordial black holes. An interesting feature of this scenario is that the black holes are produced with large spins.

### [33] [Probing the small-scale primordial power spectrum via relic neutrinos and acoustic reheating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11956)

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明中微子退耦后的扩散阻尼会降低中微子温度，从而减少 relic 中微子丰度，且该丰度受原初曲率功率谱的积分控制。未来 PTOLEMY 实验可对原初曲率功率谱在小尺度上设定上限 ∼ O(0.1)，与 BBN、谱畸变、脉冲星计时阵及 21-cm 观测互补。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索中微子退耦后小尺度涨落通过扩散阻尼（diffusion damping）耗散对 relic 中微子（relic neutrino）温度及丰度的影响，并评估未来实验对原初曲率功率谱（primordial curvature power spectrum）的约束能力。

Method: 通过解析扩散阻尼对中微子温度的影响，将 relic 中微子丰度的改变与原初曲率功率谱 Δ²_ℛ(k) 的积分联系起来，并基于 PTOLEMY 探测器的灵敏度推导对功率谱幅度的限制。

Result: 发现 PTOLEMY 可在尺度 k ≲ 3×10⁵ Mpc⁻¹ 上设定 Δ²_ℛ(k) ≲ O(0.1) 的上限，该限制与大爆炸核合成（Big Bang Nucleosynthesis）、谱畸变（spectral distortions）、脉冲星计时阵（pulsar timing arrays）及未来暗时代 21-cm 观测（dark ages 21-cm observations）互补。

Conclusion: 小尺度扩散阻尼效应可改变 relic 中微子丰度，为原初曲率功率谱在小尺度上提供新的探测途径，PTOLEMY 的实验结果可填补现有约束的空白区域。

Abstract: We show that the dissipation of small-scale perturbations through diffusion damping after neutrino decoupling lowers the present-day neutrino temperature compared to the expected value of $1.96\,{\text{K}}$. This reduces the relic neutrino abundance by an amount controlled by the integral of the primordial curvature power spectrum $Δ_{\cal R}^2(k)$. We find that a relic neutrino detection by PTOLEMY can set limits $Δ_{\cal R}^2(k) \lesssim {\cal O}(0.1)$ on scales $k \lesssim 3 \times 10^5\,{\text{Mpc}^{-1}}$, complementary to limits from Big Bang Nucleosynthesis, spectral distortions, pulsar timing arrays, and future dark ages 21-cm observations.

</details>


### [34] [Toward Charge-Dependent Tests of the Equivalence Principle: A Phenomenological Parameter and an Unexplored Frontier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12246)
*Renato Vieira dos Santos*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文引入了一个现象学参数 κ（定义为 Δa/g = κ·Δ(q/m)），用于量化电荷与引力加速度之间的潜在线性耦合。通过综合现有精密等价原理实验数据，首次给出了该耦合的有效灵敏度估计：|κ| < 2.1×10⁻⁴ kg/C（95%置信水平）。该约束比成分依赖的等价原理违背（composition-dependent violations）弱约11个数量级，表明电磁轴（electromagnetic axis）仍是经验引力中未被充分探索的前沿。论文将 κ 与标准模型扩展（Standard-Model Extension, SME）及 THεμ 形式主义（THεμ formalism）等已有框架联系起来，并指出其处于现有高精度测试未触及的参数空间区域。有效场论（EFT）分析表明，将曲率直接耦合到电磁场强度的量纲-6算子（dimension-six operators）由于地空时曲率极小（G_N ρ_⊕ ∼ 10⁻⁵⁵ GeV²）而在现象学上无关。因此，未来在可及水平上测量 κ 不会探测最小几何耦合（minimal geometric couplings），而是将指示超越最小引力EFT的新物理，例如爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论（Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton theory）中由轻标量场介导的相互作用。文章还分析了Schiff-Barnhill效应（Schiff-Barnhill effect）这一主要系统背景，并展示了如何将其与真实信号分离，最后概述了以最大化荷质比差异（charge-to-mass ratio differences）为核心的实验策略，以将这一被忽视的轴转化为探测新物理的目标工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有精密等价原理实验主要探测成分依赖的违背，但电荷与引力加速度之间的直接线性耦合（即“电磁轴”）尚未被系统定量约束。本文旨在填补这一空白，为引力检验开辟一个被忽视的新方向。

Method: 定义现象学参数 κ（Δa/g = κ·Δ(q/m)）以量化电荷-引力耦合；综合已有精密等价原理实验数据给出 κ 的置信上限；将 κ 与标准模型扩展及 THεμ 形式主义等理论框架建立联系；进行有效场论分析，评估最小引力EFT中量纲-6算子的可观测性；研究 Schiff-Barnhill 效应作为系统背景的分离方法。

Result: 首次给出 κ 的定量约束：|κ| < 2.1×10⁻⁴ kg/C（95%置信水平），比常见成分依赖的等价原理违背约束弱约11个数量级。量纲-6算子在最小引力EFT中被地空时曲率的极小量值压制，无现象学意义，因此未来对 κ 的测量将指向超越最小引力EFT的新物理，如轻标量场介导的相互作用。

Conclusion: 电磁轴是经验引力中尚未被有效约束的前沿方向；未来实验应以最大化荷质比差异为核心策略，区分 Schiff-Barnhill 效应与真实信号，从而将 κ 的测量转化为探测新物理的灵敏探针。

Abstract: We introduce and define the phenomenological parameter $κ$, defined by $Δa/g = κ\, Δ(q/m)$, to quantify potential linear coupling between electric charge and gravitational acceleration. A synthesis of existing precision equivalence principle experiments yields the first quantitative estimate of the effective sensitivity to this coupling: $|κ| < 2.1 \times 10^{-4}~\si{\kilo\gram\per\coulomb}$ at 95\% confidence level. This constraint is approximately eleven orders of magnitude less stringent than corresponding bounds on composition-dependent violations, revealing that the electromagnetic axis remains a largely underexplored frontier in empirical gravity. We connect $κ$ to established frameworks -- the Standard-Model Extension and the $THεμ$ formalism -- showing that it occupies a region of parameter space untouched by existing high-precision tests. An effective field theory analysis shows that dimension-six operators that couple curvature directly to the electromagnetic field strength are suppressed by the minuscule terrestrial spacetime curvature ($G_N ρ_\oplus \sim 10^{-55}~\text{GeV}^2$) and are therefore phenomenologically irrelevant. Consequently, a future measurement of $κ$ at an accessible level would not probe minimal geometric couplings but would signal physics beyond minimal gravitational EFT, such as mediation by light scalar fields as in Einstein-Maxwell-Dilaton theory. We examine the Schiff-Barnhill effect, the primary systematic background for any such measurement, and show how it can be separated from a genuine signal. We outline the necessary experimental strategy, focused on maximizing charge-to-mass ratio differences, to transform this overlooked axis into a targeted probe for new physics.

</details>

### [35] [Power Studies For Two-Sample and Goodness-of-Fit Methods For Multivariate Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12089)
*Wolfgang Rolke*

Main category: stat.ME

TL;DR: 基于大规模模拟研究，系统评估了多变量数据中多种拟合优度检验（goodness-of-fit test）和双样本非参数检验（non-parametric two-sample test）的统计检验力（power），发现单一方法难以在所有情形下保持高效，并据此推荐了一组能在不同原假设（null hypothesis）与备择假设（alternative）组合下均表现良好的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多变量（multivariate）数据的拟合优度和双样本检验在统计实践中至关重要，但各类方法在不同原假设与备择假设组合下的检验力表现缺乏系统性比较，难以指导实践者选择合适的方法。

Method: 开展大规模模拟研究（simulation studies），涵盖二维（2D）连续数据与离散数据，以及更高维度的连续数据；使用R包MD2sample和MDgof进行所有计算。

Result: 没有任何单一方法能在所有情形下提供稳定的检验力；某些方法在特定原假设与备择假设组合下表现良好，但在其他组合下可能严重失效。基于研究结果，筛选出一组数量较少的方法，确保在所考察的案例中至少有一种方法具有较高的检验力。

Conclusion: 多变量检验中不应依赖单一方法，建议根据问题特点从推荐的方法集合中选取合适的检验方式。相关R包（MD2sample和MDgof）已在CRAN上公开发布，便于学界复现与使用。

Abstract: We present the results of a large number of simulation studies regarding the power of various goodness-of-fit as well as non-parametric two-sample tests for multivariate data. In two dimensions this includes both continuous and discrete data, in higher dimensions continuous data only. In general no single method can be relied upon to provide good power, any one method may be quite good for some combination of null hypothesis and alternative and may fail badly for another. Based on the results of these studies we propose a fairly small number of methods chosen such that for any of the case studies included here at least one of the methods has good power. The studies were carried out using the R packages MD2sample and MDgof, available from CRAN.

</details>

### [36] [The Meissner effect does not require radial charge flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10945)
*A. V. Nikulov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文指出超导迈斯纳效应（Meissner effect）中持续电流（persistent current）的出现源于Cooper对的角动量量子化（quantization of angular momentum），而非Lorentz力驱动的径向电荷流（radial charge flow）；作者认为量子化不仅是传统超导理论的主张，更是实验事实，因此反对替代理论所要求的径向电荷流解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对Jorge Hirsch提出的空穴超导电性（hole superconductivity）替代理论——该理论认为迈斯纳效应中的持续电流由Lorentz力作用于径向电荷流产生，而非量子化——本文旨在指出该观点与实验事实相矛盾，并论证量子化解释的充分性。

Method: 文章通过对比传统超导理论（conventional theory of superconductivity）与空穴超导电性替代理论对迈斯纳效应中持续电流起源的两种解释——角动量量子化 vs. Lorentz力作用下的径向电荷流——进行理论辨析，并援引实验事实作为评判依据。

Result: 作者论证，持续电流源于量子化不仅是传统理论的主张，更是已被实验验证的事实，无法用Lorentz力加以解释；因此，迈斯纳效应的解释不需要径向电荷流。

Conclusion: 迈斯纳效应的解释不需要径向电荷流，传统超导理论中基于Cooper对角动量量子化的解释与实验事实一致，足以说明该效应。

Abstract: The Meissner effect is the expulsion of magnetic flux from the interior of a bulk superconductor in the presence of the constant critical magnetic field by the persistent current circulating near the surface of the superconductor. The conventional theory of superconductivity explains the appearance of the persistent current in the Meissner effect and other macroscopic quantum phenomena observed in superconductors as a consequence of the quantization of angular momentum of Cooper pairs. According to the alternative theory of hole superconductivity the persistent current appears due to the Lorentz force acting on a radial charge flow rather than due to quantization. Therefore, the author of this theory, Jorge Hirsch, argues in his numerous publications that a radial charge flow is required to explain the Meissner effect. This article draws attention to the fact that the appearance of the persistent current because of quantization is not only the statement of the conventional theory of superconductivity, but first of all the experimental fact that cannot be explained using the Lorentz force. Therefore, the explanation of the Meissner effect does not require radial charge flow.

</details>


### [37] [Geometry-enabled magnetic resilience in superconducting nanowire single-photon detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10968)
*Marinus C. van der Maas,Lin Jin,Ilhan Tunç,Raymond Vermeulen,Henri Ervasti,Ravi Gopie,Jan Riegelmeyer,Marco Colangelo,Ryoichi Ishihara,Carlos Errando-Herranz*

TL;DR: 本文系统表征了NbTiN超导纳米线单光子探测器（SNSPD）在磁场下的性能，发现磁场会在低偏置电流下提升本征探测效率（IDE），在高偏置电流下抑制IDE，并导致饱和平台退化。研究表明退化程度高度依赖纳米线宽度，通过优化宽度可在应用相关磁场下实现宽光子能量范围的饱和IDE。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对NbTiN SNSPD在不同磁场下进行系统性能表征，测量本征探测效率（IDE）随偏置电流的变化，并考察不同纳米线宽度对磁场诱导退化的影响。

Result: 磁场在低偏置电流下增强IDE，在高偏置电流下抑制IDE，导致饱和平台退化；退化程度与纳米线宽度高度相关，通过优化宽度可在应用相关磁场下实现宽光子能量范围的饱和IDE。

Conclusion: 最小化超导器件在磁场下的退化，能够支持探测器集成的自旋-光学和原子量子处理器、高灵敏度磁力测量以及量子转导等应用。

Abstract: While magnetic fields and superconductors are both central to classical and quantum technologies, their combined use is often challenging, as magnetic fields significantly affect superconducting device performance. In superconducting nanowire single-photon detectors (SNSPDs), magnetic fields drastically reduce detection efficiencies, hampering their application in magnetically-active classical and quantum photonics. Here, we systematically characterize the performance of NbTiN SNSPDs under magnetic fields and show the enhancement of their intrinsic detection efficiency (IDE) at lower bias currents and its suppression at higher currents. This leads to SNSPD performance degradation through reduced or disappearing saturation plateaus. We show that the magnitude of this degradation is highly dependent on nanowire width and demonstrate width-optimized SNSPDs with saturating IDE for a wide range of photon energies under application-relevant magnetic fields. Minimizing degradation in superconducting devices under magnetic fields enables applications like detector-integrated spin-optic and atomic quantum processors, high-sensitivity magnetometry, and quantum transduction.

### [38] [First-principles real-space embedding theory of the superconducting proximity effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11211)
*Nicolas Baù,Mitra Dowlatabadi,Tommaso Chiarotti,Massimo Capone,Antimo Marrazzo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种基于实空间动力学嵌入（real-space dynamical embedding）的格林函数（Green's function）框架，实现了对介观系统中超导近邻效应（superconducting proximity effect）的从头算（first-principles）模拟。该框架通过正常和反常嵌入自能（normal/anomalous embedding self-energies）的图解形式化描述，能够计算跨越数百纳米的局域谱函数和近邻长度，并在紧束缚模型和基于密度泛函理论（DFT）与最大局域瓦尼尔函数（MLWFs）的NbSe₂/CrBr₃异质结构上进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管超导近邻效应在量子材料、超导器件和拓扑平台中具有核心作用，但目前尚缺乏一种从头算的预测性框架来描述实际界面处的近邻效应，现有的计算代价过高，阻碍了第一性原理（first-principles）描述的可行性。

Method: 提出了基于实空间动力学嵌入的格林函数框架，将超导近邻效应以正常和反常嵌入自能的形式进行图解化表述，从而解耦并量化由超导库（superconducting bath）耦合产生的不同重整化机制（renormalization mechanisms）；结合递归方案（recursive schemes）实现大尺度计算。

Result: 在Qi-Hughes-Zhang和Fu-Kane-Mele紧束缚模型中分析了拓扑绝缘体经s波超导体邻近化后的混合宇称超导（mixed-parity superconductivity）；在基于DFT和MLWFs的NbSe₂/CrBr₃异质结构上进行了第一性原理模拟，结果可与扫描隧道谱（scanning tunneling spectroscopy, STS）实验直接对比。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个可扩展且概念统一的框架，弥合了微观电子结构与介观尺度近邻物理之间的鸿沟，实现了超导界面的可预测原子级模拟。

Abstract: When a superconductor is placed in contact with a normal material, Cooper pairs penetrate the latter and induce superconductivity via the proximity effect. Despite its central role in quantum materials, superconducting devices and topological platforms, a predictive first-principles description of the proximity effect at realistic interfaces has remained computationally prohibitive so far. Here, we fill this gap by developing a Green's-function framework based on real-space dynamical embedding that enables first-principles simulations of superconducting proximity in mesoscopic systems. We show that the proximity effect admits a transparent diagrammatic formulation in terms of normal and anomalous embedding self-energies, which disentangle and quantify the distinct renormalization mechanisms generated by coupling to a superconducting bath. By combining this formalism with recursive schemes, we compute local spectral functions and proximity lengths extending over hundreds of nanometers into the bulk without resorting to thick interface slabs. We deploy the approach on tight-binding models (Qi-Hughes-Zhang and Fu-Kane-Mele), where we analyze mixed-parity superconductivity in topological insulators proximitized by $s$-wave superconductors, and on first-principles simulations of NbSe$_2$/CrBr$_3$ heterostructures based on density-functional theory and maximally-localized Wannier functions, the latter enabling direct comparison with scanning tunneling spectroscopy experiments. Our work provides a scalable and conceptually unified framework that bridges microscopic electronic structure and mesoscale proximity physics, enabling predictive atomistic simulations of superconducting interfaces.

### [39] [Discovery of a nonsymmorphic superconductor with spontaneous rotational symmetry breaking and nontrivial zero modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11395)
*Hui Guo,Zhixuan Li,Senhao Lv,Tianqi Gao,Zihao Huang,Kuanrong Hao,Lizhi Zhang,Ke Zhu,Siyu Li,Xianghe Han,Xiao Lin,Shengshan Qin,Wu Zhou,Haitao Yang,Hui Chen,Hong-Jun Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文发现非对称性（nonsymmorphic）化合物PtPb4是一种具有自发旋转对称性破缺和非平庸零能模（zero-energy modes）的超导平台，为拓扑超导（topological superconductivity）和马约拉纳束缚态（Majorana bound state）研究提供了新体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑超导对实现马约拉纳准粒子（Majorana quasiparticles）和容错量子计算（fault-tolerant quantum computation）具有重要意义，而非对称性超导体（nonsymmorphic superconductors）有望实现奇异的拓扑超导态，但实验实现仍然稀少。

Method: 结合面内与面外电阻率测量（resistivity measurements）以及扫描隧道显微镜/谱学（scanning tunneling microscopy/spectroscopy, STM/STS），对PtPb4的超导态和上临界场（upper critical field）进行表征。

Result: 观察到超导态和上临界场中显著的二重各向异性（twofold anisotropy），以及二重对称的磁涡旋（twofold-symmetric magnetic vortices），并发现鲁棒的非空间分裂零能涡旋束缚态（zero-energy vortex bound state），符合马约拉纳束缚态特征。

Conclusion: PtPb4展现出奇异的超导态，为探索拓扑超导和超导量子器件（superconducting quantum devices）提供了有前景的平台。

Abstract: Topological superconductivity has attracted great interest due to its fundamental significance for realizing Majorana quasiparticles and fault-tolerant quantum computation. Nonsymmorphic superconductors, with symmetry-protected nontrivial electronic structures, offer a promising route to exotic topological superconducting states, yet experimental realizations remain scarce. Here we identify nonsymmorphic compound PtPb4 as a robust platform hosting superconductivity with spontaneous rotational symmetry breaking and nontrivial zero-energy modes. PtPb4 crystallizes in a frustrated Shastry-Sutherland lattice and exhibits nontrivial band topology. By combining in-plane and out-of-plane resistivity measurements, pronounced twofold anisotropy is observed in both the superconducting state and the upper critical field, evidencing spontaneous rotational symmetry breaking. Scanning tunneling microscopy/spectroscopy further reveal twofold-symmetric magnetic vortices, providing direct real-space evidence for the symmetry-broken superconducting state. Notably, a robust zero-energy vortex bound state emerges and persists without spatial splitting over extended distances, consistent with the characteristics expected for Majorana bound state. These findings uncover an exotic superconducting state in PtPb4 and establish a promising platform for exploring topological superconductivity and superconducting quantum devices.

### [40] [Superconductivity Reinforces Charge-Density-Wave Phase Coherence across Cuprates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11401)
*H. Lee,C. -T. Kuo,M. Fujita,C. -C. Kao,J. -S. Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文发现高温超导铜氧化物（high-Tc cuprates）中，超导态（superconductivity）并非仅抑制电荷密度波（charge-density-wave, CDW）的幅度，而是同时增强其相位相干性（phase coherence），揭示了超导与CDW之间更复杂的双重竞争-增强关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，超导被认为通过降低CDW的幅度和空间范围来抑制其有序性。本文旨在检验这一图像是否完整，并探究超导对CDW相位相干性的影响。

Method: 采用共振软X射线散射（resonant soft x-ray scattering）结合对相干性敏感的动量廓线分析（coherence-sensitive momentum-profile analysis），在不同铜氧化物家族中系统测量CDW的相位相干性随温度的变化。

Result: 超导转变温度（Tc）以下，CDW的相位相干性呈现类似BCS（BCS-like）的增长，表现为CDW峰展宽（peak broadening）消失以及近乎完美的波矢锁定（wave-vector locking）。即使经过长期晶体老化造成的无序主导区域，这一增强效应仍然可见；在Bi-、Hg-、Y-和Nd基铜氧化物中均遵循共同趋势。

Conclusion: 超导通过两种截然不同的方式重塑CDW有序：抑制其幅度（amplitude）的同时增强其相位相干性（phase coherence），揭示了高温超导铜氧化物中还存在与晶格耦合（lattice coupling）相关的附加相位层次相互作用。

Abstract: For decades, superconductivity in high-Tc cuprates has been viewed as a competitor that suppresses charge-density-wave (CDW) order by reducing its amplitude and spatial extent. Here, we show that this picture is incomplete, as superconductivity is accompanied by a systematic enhancement of CDW phase coherence across multiple cuprate families. Using resonant soft x-ray scattering combined with a coherence-sensitive momentum-profile analysis, we uncover a BCS-like growth of phase coherence below Tc, which phenomenologically manifests as the absence of CDW peak broadening and near-perfect wave-vector locking. This enhancement remains visible even in a disorder-dominated regime created by long-term crystal aging and follows a common trend when compared with published data on Bi-, Hg-, Y-, and Nd-based cuprates. These results indicate that superconductivity reshapes CDW order in two distinct ways, suppressing its amplitude while strengthening its phase coherence, and reveal an additional phase-level interplay with lattice coupling in high-Tc cuprates.

</details>


### [41] [Experimental Progress in Ambient-Pressure Superconducting Bilayer Nickelate Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11584)
*Meng Zhang,Xi Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文综述了双层Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐薄膜在常压下的超导实验进展，重点讨论了合成方法、氧化学计量、衬底应变、正常态输运、超导性质、掺杂相图及动量分辨电子结构，并指出了若干未解问题及未来研究方向。
