  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双层Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐（bilayer Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates）在高压下展现出近80 K的超导电性，为非常规高温超导（unconventional high-temperature superconductivity）研究提供了新平台。近期常压超导RA₃Ni₂O₇薄膜的稳定制备改变了实验格局，使输运、谱学、显微及器件测量变得直接可行，因此有必要系统梳理该领域的实验进展与争议。

Method: 本文采用综述（Review）方法，系统总结常压超导双层镍酸盐薄膜的实验研究，涵盖合成路线（synthesis routes）、氧化学计量（oxygen stoichiometry）、衬底诱导应变（substrate-induced strain）、正常态输运（normal-state transport）、超导性质、掺杂相图（doping phase diagrams）及动量分辨电子结构（momentum-resolved electronic structure）等关键方面。

Result: 研究发现，外延应变（epitaxial strain）可以复现高压相的关键结构要素。同时，综述指出了多个尚未解决的问题，包括：纯相超薄薄膜的可重复性、两步超导转变（two-step superconducting transition）的微观起源、氧缺陷及衬底诱导掺杂的作用、Ni 3dz²衍生的γ能带（γ band）位置，以及配对对称性（pairing symmetry）。

Conclusion: 本文呼吁建立晶体结构、轨道重构（orbital reconstruction）与超导电性之间更定量的联系，并指明了未来实验方向以推动该领域的发展。

Abstract: Bilayer Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates display superconductivity near 80 K under high pressure, establishing a new nickelate platform for studying unconventional high-temperature superconductivity. The recent stabilization of superconducting RA3Ni2O7 (RA = rare earth or alkaline earth) films at ambient pressure has changed the experimental landscape: epitaxial strain can reproduce key structural ingredients of the high-pressure phase while making transport, spectroscopy, microscopy, and device-oriented measurements directly accessible. This Review summarizes the experimental progress on ambient-pressure superconducting bilayer nickelate films, with emphasis on synthesis routes, oxygen stoichiometry, substrate-induced strain, normal-state transport, superconducting properties, doping phase diagrams, and momentum-resolved electronic structure. We highlight several issues that remain unsettled, including the reproducibility of phase-pure ultrathin films, the microscopic origin of the two-step superconducting transition, the role of oxygen defects and substrate-derived doping, the position of the Ni 3dz2-derived γ band, and the pairing symmetry. We close by outlining experimental directions that could establish a more quantitative link among crystal structure, orbital reconstruction, and superconductivity in bilayer nickelate films.

</details>


### [42] [Euler Topology in Superconducting Honeycomb Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11587)
*Rasoul Ghadimi,Chiranjit Mondal,Bohm-Jung Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有时空反演对称性（IST symmetry）的超导蜂窝晶格中的欧勒拓扑（Euler topology），发现s波自旋单态（SWSS）和f波自旋三重态（FWST）超导配对分别导致谷-欧勒超导体和欧勒超导体，并揭示了镜面对称保护的螺旋畴壁模式以及FWST态中由非均匀跳跃诱导的狄拉克节点非阿贝尔编织。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索具有时空反演对称性（space-time inversion symmetry）系统中电子能带的非平凡欧勒拓扑（Euler topology）如何由超导电子不稳定性（superconducting electronic instabilities）自然实现，尤其是在狄拉克材料（Dirac materials）中。

Method: 以超导蜂窝晶格（superconducting honeycomb lattices）为研究对象，分别引入s波自旋单态（s-wave spin-singlet, SWSS）和f波自旋三重态（f-wave spin-triplet, FWST）超导配对，分析不同配对对称性下的能带拓扑结构及其物理后果。

Result: SWSS和FWST超导配对分别诱导出谷-欧勒超导体（valley-Euler superconductor）和欧勒超导体（Euler superconductor）；两种配对态的欧勒拓扑均产生受镜面对称保护的螺旋畴壁模式（helical domain-wall modes）；在FWST态中，引入非均匀跳跃（anisotropic hopping）可导致动量空间中狄拉克节点（Dirac nodes）的非阿贝尔编织（non-Abelian braiding）。


Conclusion: 超导电子不稳定性是在狄拉克材料中实现非平凡欧勒能带拓扑（nontrivial Euler band topology）的一种自然途径，为拓扑超导与欧勒拓扑的交叉研究提供了新方向。

Abstract: Electronic bands in systems with space-time inversion (IST) symmetry can host nontrivial Euler topology. Here, we investigate the band topology of IST-symmetric superconducting honeycomb lattices and demonstrate that s-wave spin-singlet (SWSS) and f-wave spin-triplet (FWST) superconducting pairings give rise to valley-Euler and Euler superconductors, respectively. We find that Euler topology in both pairing states gives rise to mirror-symmetry-protected helical domain-wall modes. Furthermore, we show that Euler topology in the FWST state induces non-Abelian braiding of Dirac nodes in momentum space when anisotropic hopping is introduced. Our work establishes superconducting electronic instabilities as a natural route to realizing nontrivial Euler band topology in Dirac materials.

### [43] [Nematicity in LaFeAsO single crystals studied by elastoresistance, high-resolution thermal expansion and shear-modulus measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11955)
*X. C. Hong,S. Sauerland,L. Wang,F. Scaravaggi,A. U. B. Wolter,R. Kappenberger,S. Aswartham,S. Wurmehl,S. Sykora,F. Caglieris,B. Büchner,C. Hess,R. Klingeler*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本论文通过高分辨率热膨胀、剪切模量和弹性电阻率测量，研究了LaFeAsO单晶中的向列相（nematicity），发现剪切模量软化与Curie-Weiss-like发散行为，证实了电子起源的向列相；但与BaFe$_2$As$_2$的对比显示出弹性电阻率行为的关键差异，挑战了现有的铁基超导体电阻各向异性理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究铁基超导体LaFeAsO中向列相（nematicity）的物理起源——究竟是电子自由度驱动还是晶格效应主导，并通过与BaFe$_2$As$_2$的对比，检验现有理论（如Landau理论）的普适性。

Method: 采用高分辨率热膨胀（high-resolution thermal expansion）、剪切模量（shear modulus $C_{\rm 66}$）和弹性电阻率（elastoresistivity）三种互补测量手段，从剪切模量和弹性电阻率数据中分别导出向列相磁化率（nematic susceptibilities）$χ^{sh}$与$χ^{er}$，并进行Curie-Weiss拟合分析。

Result: 在LaFeAsO中观察到剪切模量$C_{\rm 66}$在结构相变温度$T_{\rm S}$附近的软化，以及$χ^{sh}$和$χ^{er}$均呈现类似的Curie-Weiss-like发散行为；晶格与电子自由度耦合的特征能量约为30 K。与BaFe$_2$As$_2$的对比表明：两者剪切模量温度依赖性高度相似，但$χ^{er}$行为截然不同——BaFe$_2$As$_2$中$χ^{er}$与Landau理论预期一致，而LaFeAsO中$χ^{er}$和$χ^{sh}$的Weiss温度存在显著差异。

Conclusion: LaFeAsO中向列相具有电子起源（electronic origin），但其弹性电阻率行为与BaFe$_2$As$_2$及现有Landau理论预期存在显著偏差，表明铁基超导体中电阻各向异性（resistivity anisotropy）与电子向列相（electronic nematicity）的关联机制可能比现有理论更为复杂。

Abstract: Nematicity in LaFeAsO single crystals is studied by means of high-resolution thermal expansion, shear modulus, and elastoresistivity measurements. A softening of the shear modulus $C_{\rm 66}$ towards the structural phase transition at $T_{\rm S}$ is observed. In addition, a similar Curie-Weiss-like divergence of the nematic susceptibilities is found in the temperature dependence of both $χ^{sh}$ and $χ^{er}$, which are deduced from the shear modulus (sh) and the elastoresistivity (er) studies, respectively. These observations provide evidence for an electronic origin of nematicity in LaFeAsO. The characteristic energy of the coupling between the lattice and the electronic degrees of freedom is deduced to $\sim$30~K. The comparison to corresponding measurements on BaFe$_2$As$_2$ single crystals reveals a very similar temperature dependence of the shear modulus but yields contrasting results for $χ^{er}$ : In BaFe$_2$As$_2$, $χ^{er}$ diverges similarly as the uncoupled nematicity deduced from the shear modulus data as it is expected from the underlying Landau theory. In contrast, the Weiss temperatures of $χ^{er}$ and $χ^{sh}$ are significantly different in LaFeAsO. This difference is at odds with the commonly anticipated theories of resistivity anisotropy and electronic nematicity in iron pnictides.

</details>


### [44] [Phase-slip residual-order spin state in FeSe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12293)
*Zhixin Liu,Jiyu Fan,Lei Zhang,Ma Chunlan,Yanda Ji,Zhongqin Yang,Yan Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出残余序自旋态（residual-order spin state, ROSS）来解释FeSe中既存在强自旋涨落又缺乏静态长程磁有序的矛盾现象，通过混合交换关联计算和自旋结构因子模拟，证明该态来源于条纹磁序背景中嵌入的近简并相位滑移缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清磁性基态是分析非常规超导电性的前提，因微观磁序是自旋涨落配对理论的基本起点。FeSe表现出显著的条纹型和奈尔型自旋涨落（stripe- and Neel-type spin fluctuations），却缺少静态长程有序，这一长期未解的谜题需要新的理论解释。

Method: 采用PBE与r2SCAN混合交换关联计算（mixed exchange-correlation calculations），结合静态自旋结构因子S(q)的谱权重模拟，系统分析FeSe的磁性构型及其能量分布。

Result: FeSe并非由单一磁构型主导，而是由嵌入条纹背景中的近乎简并的相位滑移缺陷（phase-slip defects）集合控制。多种滑移构型被压缩在极窄的能量窗口内；非局域磁弹耦合通过晶格重新分布畴壁形成能，而竞争性磁相互作用将实空间相干长度截断至约十个磁矩的最优尺度。这些滑移态的加权叠加可同时再现非弹性中子散射观测到的条纹型和奈尔型自旋涨落的动量空间线形。

Conclusion: 提出残余序自旋态（ROSS）作为FeSe的磁性基态，该态保留局域条纹状反铁磁关联但因相位滑移而丧失长程相位相干。该结果为基于自旋涨落的超导模型提供了微观基础。

Abstract: Clarifying the magnetic ground state is essential for analysing unconventional superconductivity, because microscopic magnetic order provides one of the basic starting assumptions for spin-fluctuation pairing theories. FeSe exhibits pronounced stripe- and Neel-type spin fluctuations yet lacks static long-range order, posing a long-standing puzzle. By combining PBE and r2SCAN mixed exchange-correlation calculations with spectrally weighted simulations of the static spin structure factor S(q), we show that FeSe is not governed by a single magnetic configuration but by a nearly degenerate manifold of phase-slip defects embedded in a stripe background. We term this state a residual-order spin state (ROSS): a spin state that retains local stripe-like antiferromagnetic correlations but loses long-range phase coherence because of phase slips. Multiple slip configurations are compressed into an exceptionally narrow energy window. Non-local magneto-elastic coupling redistributes domain-wall formation energy through the lattice, whereas competing magnetic interactions truncate the real-space coherence length to an optimal scale of about ten moments. Weighted superpositions of these slip states reproduce the momentum-space line shapes of both stripe- and Neel-type spin fluctuations observed by inelastic neutron scattering, providing a microscopic basis for superconductivity models built on spin fluctuations.

</details>


### [45] [Anomalous spin-pumping behavior of half-metallic ferromagnet/d-wave superconductor heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12381)
*Hadi H. Hassan,Santiago J. Carreira,M. Cabero,F. Martinet,Alexander Buzdin,Jacobo Santamaria,Javier E. Villegas*

TL;DR: 本文通过铁磁共振实验研究了外延YBa2Cu3O7-d/La0.7Sr0.3MnO3异质结中d波超导体与半金属铁磁体配对时的自旋泵浦行为，发现(103)取向和c轴取向异质结呈现出截然不同的温度依赖Gilbert阻尼系数α(T)行为，分别由节点准粒子和界面束缚Andreev态主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导体/铁磁体异质结中的自旋泵浦实验揭示了复杂行为，但以往研究多集中于传统s波超导体与金属或绝缘铁磁体的组合，缺乏对d波超导体与半金属铁磁体配对体系的系统研究。

Method: 采用铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance, FMR）技术，测量外延生长在两种晶向（c轴取向与(103)方向）上的YBa2Cu3O7-d/La0.7Sr0.3MnO3异质结中随温度变化的Gilbert阻尼系数α。

Result: (103)取向异质结中α(T)在Tc以下先下降、后上升并超过正常态水平；c轴取向异质结中α(T)在Tc以下显著增强，在0.65-0.7Tc处达到峰值后衰减。

Conclusion: (103)取向行为可通过超导能隙打开与节点准粒子（nodal quasiparticles）主导的自旋输运解释；c轴取向的反常增强表明界面束缚Andreev态（interface-bound Andreev states）占主导，源于半金属LSMO邻近效应导致的超导序参量局部抑制。

Abstract: Spin-pumping experiments in superconductor/ferromagnet heterostructures, which probe spin-sinking by the superconductor, have revealed a variety of complex behaviors. Most studies have focused on conventional s-wave superconductors combined with metallic or insulating ferromagnets. Here, we study a d-wave superconductor paired with a half-metallic ferromagnet, in epitaxial YBa2Cu3O7-d/La0.7Sr0.3MnO3 heterostructures with two crystalline orientations: one in which YBCO is c-axis oriented, and the other in which YBCO grows along the (103) direction. Using ferromagnetic resonance (FMR), we probe the temperature-dependent Gilbert damping coefficient α. For (103) heterostructures, α(T) initially decreases below Tc, but then increases at lower temperatures, exceeding normal-state levels. This behavior can be understood in terms of the opening of the superconducting gap and spin transport via nodal quasiparticles, which dominate when the ab-plane of YBCO is exposed at the interface. In stark contrast, c-axis heterostructures exhibit a pronounced enhancement of α(T) below Tc, peaking at 0.65-0.7Tc before decaying. This anomaly suggests the dominance of interface-bound Andreev states, arising from a locally suppressed superconducting order parameter due to proximity effects with the half-metallic LSMO.

### [46] [Unique Gravitational-Wave Signals from Negative-Mass Binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10976)
*Oem Trivedi,Abraham Loeb*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个统一且可观测检验的理论框架，通过耦合层级（coupling level）与动力学探测（dynamical probes）来约束负质量（negative masses）；研究表明，负质量双星系统会产生反啁啾（anti-chirps）、弥散（dispersal）和逃逸运动（runaway motion）等异常信号，而这些信号在现有引力波观测中均未被探测到，从而在无需修改引力理论假设的前提下为排除负质量提供了强有力的排除通道。

Method: 同时采用耦合层级约束（如偶极辐射界限要求引力荷（gravitational charge）具有普适性）和动力学探测（如双星系统的运动学行为）两种途径，构建统一的检验框架。

Result: 负质量双星系统会引发反啁啾、弥散和逃逸运动等异常动力学特征，而当前引力波观测中并未出现这些信号。

Conclusion: 负质量双星的异常动力学特征提供了一条独立于修改引力理论假设的稳健排除通道，可用于约束负质量的存在。

Abstract: Negative masses have long been explored, but their observational viability remains unclear. In this work, we develop a unified, observationally testable framework to constrain negative masses using both coupling level and dynamical probes. We establish that while dipole radiation bounds require universality of gravitational charge, the intrinsic dynamics of negative mass binaries generically lead to anomalous behaviors such as anti-chirps, dispersal and runaway motion. These signatures are absent in current gravitational wave observations, providing a robust exclusion channel independent of modified gravity assumptions.

### [47] [Anisotropic Cosmology with interacting Dark Energy in f(R,T) Gravity: A Data-Constrained & independent Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10982)
*S. H. Shekh,N. Myrzakulov,Anirudh Pradhan,M. Zeyauddin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在$f(R,T)$引力框架下，结合Bianchi I型各向异性时空与变减速参数重建方案，利用哈勃数据和Pantheon+超新星样本约束模型参数，成功再现了从早期减速到当前加速膨胀的宇宙演化，并在晚期与$\Lambda$CDM模型高度一致。有效状态方程呈现类似于精粹（quintessence）的动力学子暗能量行为，但微扰稳定性分析揭示了经典不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在$f(R,T)$修正引力（modified gravity）的框架下研究各向异性宇宙（anisotropic Universe）的宇宙学动力学，以捕捉宇宙膨胀过程中可能偏离各向同性的演化特征。

Method: 采用Bianchi I型时空描述各向异性，并基于变减速参数（variable deceleration parameter）进行现象学重建，导出红移依赖的哈勃函数。通过联合观测哈勃数据（observational Hubble data）和Pantheon+ Ia型超新星样本（Type Ia supernova compilation）进行统计约束，确定模型自由参数。进一步利用状态finder诊断（statefinder diagnostics）和$O_m$诊断进行几何检验，并分析能量条件（energy conditions）与微扰稳定性（perturbative stability）。

Result: 参数空间被紧密限定，重建的膨胀历史与当前观测期望高度一致。模型成功再现了早期减速到当前加速的过渡，并渐近趋近于德西特（de Sitter）类 regime。状态finder和$O_m$诊断表明晚期与$\Lambda$CDM模型高度对应。有效状态方程（effective equation of state）呈现精粹类（quintessence-like）动力学演化。能量条件验证了模型的物理可接受性，但微扰分析揭示了经典不稳定性（classical instabilities）。

Conclusion: 该$f(R,T)$各向异性宇宙模型在背景层面与观测数据高度一致，并能自然描述宇宙的减速-加速转变，但在微扰层面存在经典不稳定性，限制了其完备有效性。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the cosmological dynamics of an anisotropic Universe within the framework of $f(R,T)$ gravity by incorporating pressureless dark matter and the dark energy models. The analysis is carried out in a Bianchi type-I space-time, allowing us to capture possible deviations from isotropy and their evolution during cosmic expansion. A phenomenological reconstruction scheme based on a variable deceleration parameter is adopted to derive a redshift-dependent Hubble function. To establish observational viability, we constrain the free parameters of the model using a comprehensive statistical analysis that combines observational Hubble data and the Pantheon+ Type Ia supernova compilation. The resulting parameter space is tightly bounded, and the reconstructed expansion history exhibits strong consistency with current observational expectations. The model successfully reproduces the transition from an early decelerating phase to the present accelerated epoch, while asymptotically approaching a de Sitter-like regime.
  Further we analyzed the geometrical diagnostics, including the statefinder and $O_m$ diagnostics, which indicate a close correspondence with the standard $Λ$CDM scenario at late times. The behavior of the effective equation of state suggests a dynamically evolving dark energy component consistent with a quintessence-like regime. Additionally, the analysis of energy conditions confirms the physical admissibility of the model, whereas the stability investigation reveals the presence of classical instabilities at the perturbative level.

</details>


### [48] [Photon Sphere and Shadow of a Perturbative Black Hole in $f(R,\mathcal{G})$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10992)
*G. G. L. Nashed*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在微扰 f(R, G) 引力框架下，通过构建史瓦西解的领头阶修正，分析了高曲率修正项对黑洞可观测量的影响，包括光子球半径、黑洞阴影、强引力透镜和准正则模，并指出高分辨率观测有望约束修正引力模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高曲率修正项作为广义相对论的高阶推广，其对黑洞可观测量的具体影响尚未被系统定量研究。本研究旨在揭示二次曲率不变量（quadratic curvature invariants）如何修正史瓦西黑洞周围的时空几何，并评估这些修正能否被未来的天文观测所检验。

Method: 在静态球对称时空背景下，基于微扰 f(R, G) 引力框架，将场方程在小耦合参数（与二次曲率不变量相关的）下展开，得到史瓦西解的领头阶偏离。通过渐近展开（asymptotic expansions）获得度规修正项，并用于分析零测地线（null geodesics）。

Result: 导出了光子球半径（photon-sphere radius）偏移的解析表达式，发现高曲率项会改变不稳定光子轨道的位置，且 Gauss-Bonnet 部分的贡献显著大于混合曲率项。这些修正进一步导致黑洞阴影半径（shadow radius）的变化，并区分了光子球位移与直接度规扰动对阴影大小的不同作用。

Conclusion: 强场可观测量的高曲率效应具有增强灵敏度，表明基于渐近微扰的处理方法能为估计广义相对论的领头阶偏离提供一致框架。极高分辨率观测（如甚长基线干涉测量和引力波探测）有望对修正引力模型施加约束。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of higher-curvature corrections on black-hole observables within a perturbative $f(R, G)$ gravity framework. Working in a static, spherically symmetric spacetime, we construct leading-order deviations from the Schwarzschild solution by expanding the field equations in small coupling parameters associated with quadratic curvature invariants. The resulting metric corrections are obtained as asymptotic expansions and used to analyze null geodesics. We derive analytic expressions for the shift in the photon-sphere radius and show that higher-curvature terms modify the location of unstable photon orbits, with the Gauss--Bonnet sector producing a more significant contribution than mixed curvature terms. These modifications propagate to observable quantities, leading to corrections in the black-hole shadow radius. We identify the distinct roles of photon-sphere displacement and direct metric perturbations in determining the shadow size. We further discuss the implications of these corrections for strong gravitational lensing and quasinormal modes, highlighting the enhanced sensitivity of strong-field observables to higher-curvature effects. While the present analysis is based on an asymptotic perturbative treatment, our results provide a consistent framework for estimating leading-order deviations from general relativity and suggest that high-resolution observations, including very-long-baseline interferometry and gravitational-wave measurements, may offer constraints on modified gravity models.

</details>


### [49] [Massive Scalar Quasinormal Modes, Greybody Factors, and Absorption Cross Section of a Parity-Symmetric Beyond-Horndeski Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11013)
*S. V. Bolokhov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了渐近平坦宇称对称超越Horndeski黑洞背景下有质量标量场的拟正规模、灰体因子和吸收截面，发现标量质量增大导致阻尼率显著下降（趋近长寿命准共振态），同时低频透射被抑制、吸收阈值向高频移动；时域演化显示从拟正规振铃到振荡晚期尾的转变，且大质量区振荡尾主导得较早，使得有质量标量场成为探测该黑洞几何形变与场质量竞争关系的灵敏探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索有质量标量场在超越Horndeski黑洞（beyond-Horndeski black hole）背景下的动力学与散射特性，理解标量质量与黑洞几何形变之间的竞争如何影响拟正规模谱、灰体因子（greybody factor）和吸收截面（absorption cross section）。

Method: 采用Padé改进的高阶WKB近似（Padé-improved high-order WKB calculations）结合时域演化（time-domain evolution），对标量场质量、几何偏离参数等代表性参数族进行计算与分析。

Result: 标量质量增大使有效势（effective potential）屏障峰消失且渐近水平抬升，导致阻尼率大幅下降，趋近长寿命准共振态（quasi-resonant states）；大质量区弱阻尼模式在时域中更难分离，振荡质量尾（oscillatory massive tails）在Koyama–Tomimatsu标度上早期主导；时域剖面显示从拟正规振铃（quasinormal ringing）向振荡晚期尾的过渡；标量质量增大抑制低频透射并将高效吸收阈值推向高频，而偏离Schwarzschild极限越大则吸收截面越大。

Conclusion: 长寿命模式与快速主导的质量尾之间的竞争，使得有质量标量场成为探测场质量与几何形变之间协同效应的精细且灵敏的探针。

Abstract: We study quasinormal modes, greybody factors, and the absorption cross section of a massive scalar field in the asymptotically flat parity-symmetric beyond-Horndeski black-hole background. The scalar mass raises the asymptotic level of the effective potential and can eliminate its barrier peak, thereby changing both the ringing spectrum and the scattering characteristics relative to the massless case. Using Padé-improved high-order WKB calculations together with time-domain evolution, we find that the damping rate decreases strongly as the field mass increases, indicating the approach to long-lived quasi-resonant states for representative parameter families. At the same time, in the large-mass regime these weakly damped modes become progressively harder to isolate in the time domain, because the oscillatory massive tails are expected to dominate on the Koyama--Tomimatsu scale $μ_s t\gg μ_s M$, which is comparatively early when $M=1$ and $μ_s$ is not small. The time-domain profiles also exhibit the transition from quasinormal ringing to an oscillatory late-time tail. Interpreting the same effective potential semiclassically, we show that increasing the scalar mass suppresses low-frequency transmission and shifts the onset of efficient absorption to higher frequencies, while larger deviations from the Schwarzschild limit enhance the absorption cross section. These results show that the competition between long-lived modes and rapidly dominant massive tails makes the massive sector an especially subtle and sensitive probe of the interplay between field mass and geometric deformation in this class of black holes.

</details>


### [50] [Quantum gravitational deflection of parallel matter wave beams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11035)
*Soham Sen,Vlatko Vedral*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）输出耦合产生两束平行原子激光（atom laser）的模型，发现除经典偏转外还存在由量子引力（quantum gravity）引起的潮汐偏转（tidal deflection），导致测地线分离（geodesic separation）中出现不可约噪声，并据此提出相应的实验探测方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知两束平行光子束在自身能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor）作用下不发生偏转，本文旨在探索物质波束（matter-wave beams）在此情形下是否会出现量子引力效应，并设计可探测该效应的实验模型。

Method: 通过将两个空间分离的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）进行输出耦合（outcoupling），产生两束平行的原子激光（atom laser）束，并分析其在量子引力作用下的测地线偏差。

Result: 发现除经典偏转外，还存在纯量子引力（quantum gravity）诱发的潮汐偏转，该偏转导致两束物质波测地线分离中产生不可约噪声。

Conclusion: 基于这一理论结果，提出了一个用于探测量子引力引起的两束平行物质波测地线分离标准差的实验模型。

Abstract: It is well known that two parallel photon beams do not deflect under the effect of their energy-momentum tensor. In this work, we propose a novel model where two spatially separated Bose-Einstein condensates are outcoupled to create two parallel atom laser beams. We find out that apart from the classical deflection, a purely quantum gravity induced tidal deflection is observed which results in an irreducible noise in the geodesic separation of the two beams. Based on this simple but novel theoretical outcome, we propose an experimental model for detecting this quantum gravity induced standard deviation in the geodesic separation of the two parallel matter-wave beams.

### [51] [Gauge-covariant Raychaudhuri dynamics for spin-nondegenerate Lorentz-violating congruences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11050)
*A. A. Araújo Filho,A. F. Santos,J. A. A. S. Reis,L. Lisboa-Santos,V. B. Bezerra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在最小电磁耦合下研究了带电自旋非简并洛伦兹破缺粒子汇（congruence）的Raychaudhuri动力学，推导了依赖于分支（branch）的电磁源项，并应用于b_μ、H_μν和d_μν扇区，进而拓展到准粒子束流领域，揭示了分支依赖的双折射效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Raychaudhuri方程推广到带电、自旋非简并且洛伦兹对称性破缺（Lorentz violation）的粒子汇，研究电磁耦合对汇聚焦（focusing）行为的影响。

Method: 通过规范协变动量P_μ=π_μ-qA_μ引入最小电磁耦合，保持分支色散关系的自由形式；利用分支的切向量（tangent）k^μ_(±)和动量Hessian M^(μν)_(±)导出协变加速度及Raychaudhuri方程中的电磁源项，并应用于具体洛伦兹破缺扇区。

Result: 在平直时空中，电磁场通过有效分支力的散度改变膨胀（expansion）；均匀场仅弯曲轨迹，局域聚焦需场梯度或与已变形汇的耦合。在准粒子束流中，能带Hessian充当有效电磁响应张量；对两分支系统，相反Hessian可导致一支聚焦、另一支散焦，实现分支依赖的双折射（birefringence）。

Conclusion: 建立了带电洛伦兹破缺粒子汇的Raychaudhuri动力学框架，揭示了分支依赖的电磁聚焦机制，并推广到准粒子体系，为理解凝聚态和引力系统中的分支双折射提供了几何统一描述。

Abstract: We investigate the Raychaudhuri dynamics of charged spin--nondegenerate Lorentz--violating particle congruences under minimal electromagnetic coupling. The coupling is introduced through the gauge--covariant momentum $P_μ=π_μ-qA_μ$, so that the branch dispersion relation keeps its free functional form, while the electromagnetic field enters through the evolution of $P_μ$. For a generic branch $\mathcal D^{(\pm)}(P)$, the tangent $k^μ_{(\pm)}$ and the momentum Hessian $M^{μν}_{(\pm)}$ determine the covariant acceleration, $a^μ_{(\pm)}=-qM^{μν}_{(\pm)}F_{νρ}k^ρ_{(\pm)}$. As a consequence, the Raychaudhuri equation acquires the branch-dependent electromagnetic source $-q\nabla_μ\!\left(M^{μν}_{(\pm)}F_{νρ}k^ρ_{(\pm)}\right)$. We apply this construction to the $b_μ$, $H_{μν}$, and $d_{μν}$ sectors, obtaining the corresponding branch tangents, Hessians, accelerations, and focusing equations. In flat spacetime, the electromagnetic field modifies the expansion through the divergence of the effective branch force. Therefore, uniform fields may bend the trajectories, whereas local focusing requires field gradients or, in the magnetic case, a coupling to an already deformed congruence. We also develop the analogous description for semiclassical quasiparticle beams, where the band Hessian plays the role of an effective electromagnetic response tensor. For anisotropic parabolic, Dirac--like, and Weyl--type dispersions, the same geometric structure relates electromagnetic textures to beam focusing. In two-branch systems, the opposite Hessians of the branches can produce focusing in one congruence and defocusing in the other, giving a quasiparticle realization of branch--dependent birefringence.

### [52] [Metric Reconstruction for Generic Black-Hole Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11080)
*Dongjun Li,Nicolás Yunes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 论文针对标准辐射规范（radiation gauge）在重建度规时要求无迹（tracefree）微扰、无法处理一般源（generic sources）的局限性，提出了一种含有迹（traceful）的辐射规范，用于佩特罗夫D型时空（Petrov type D spacetimes）的微扰重建。该方法通过两个一阶输运方程（transport equations）从应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）确定度规迹，其余分量则由纽曼-彭罗斯方程（Newman-Penrose equations）分层给出，并以施瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）及薄静态壳层为例验证了该框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准辐射规范下的度规重建（metric reconstruction）无法处理一般源（generic sources），因为它要求度规微扰（metric perturbation）必须是无迹的（tracefree）。本文旨在移除这一限制，使得佩特罗夫D型时空（Petrov type D spacetimes）的微扰重建能够兼容任意源分布。

Method: 引入一种含有迹的辐射规范（traceful radiation gauge）。通过两个一阶输运方程（transport equations）从应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）求解度规的迹（trace）；其余度规分量则基于纽曼-彭罗斯方程（Newman-Penrose equations）分层递推得到。

Result: 以施瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）带薄静态壳层（thin static shell）为例进行验证，展示了该方法可以处理包含源支撑的静态完备扇区（source-supported static completion sector）的情形。

Conclusion: 所提出的含迹辐射规范成功克服了标准辐射规范对一般源的限制，为佩特罗夫D型时空的度规微扰重建提供了一套完整的、分层可解的方法，并通过具体算例证实了其实用性。

Abstract: Standard (radiation-gauge) metric reconstruction excludes generic sources because it requires a tracefree metric perturbation. We remove this obstruction for perturbations of Petrov type D spacetimes by introducing a traceful radiation gauge. Two first-order transport equations determine the metric trace from the stress-energy tensor, and the remaining metric components follow hierarchically from the Newman-Penrose equations. We illustrate the method for a Schwarzschild black hole with a thin static shell, including a source-supported static completion sector.

</details>


### [53] [gwBenchmarks: Stress-Testing LLM Agents on High-Precision Gravitational Wave Astronomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11269)
*Tousif Islam,Digvijay Wadekar,Zihan Zhou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出 gwBenchmarks——一套基于引力波（gravitational wave）天文学中八项任务的基准测试，评估前沿大语言模型编码智能体（LLM coding agents）在端到端科学建模（end-to-end scientific modeling）中的表现。实验发现，现有智能体在简单任务上能达到基线水平，但在高精度需求任务上普遍存在指标误用、约束违规和结果伪造等系统性失败，性能距领域要求仍差1-2个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波天文学中的建模任务（如构建波形替代模型（waveform surrogate）、拟合并合残骸性质）需要高精度（相对误差≤10⁻⁴）且消耗大量计算资源（代表超10⁸核小时）。作者希望系统评估当前最先进的LLM编码智能体是否能独立完成这类需要严谨物理推理和高精度要求的端到端科学建模。

Method: gwBenchmarks包含八项任务，涵盖插值（interpolation）、回归（regression）和高维时间序列建模（high-dimensional time-series modeling），源于引力波解析计算（analytic calculations）和数值模拟（numerical simulations）。为避免智能体依赖代理指标（proxy metrics）或伪造结果完成任务，作者设计了外部预定义框架来客观衡量进展。实验评估了12种编码智能体。

Result: 在简单任务上，多个智能体均收敛到三次样条（cubic spline）解，其中一个智能体重新发现了文献中广泛使用的坐标变换。在较难的解析波形建模任务上，所有智能体性能均落后领域要求1-2个数量级，并表现出指标误用（metric misuse）、约束违规（constraint violation）和结果伪造（result fabrication）等系统性失败。12种智能体中没有一致的最优方案。

Conclusion: 当前最先进的LLM编码智能体在涉及高精度需求的引力波科学建模任务中能力严重不足，尚无法可靠替代人类专家在端到端建模中的工作，亟需进一步研究以提升其物理推理与数值精度控制能力。

Abstract: Modern gravitational wave astronomy relies on modeling tasks that often require months of graduate-level effort, including building fast waveform surrogates from expensive numerical relativity simulations, modeling orbital dynamics of black holes, fitting merger remnant properties and constructing template banks. These problems demand extreme precision to support detection and parameter inference, with state-of-the-art models achieving $\lesssim 10^{-4}$ relative error. We study whether state-of-the-art LLM coding agents can perform such end-to-end scientific modeling, where success requires constructing models with stringent accuracy criteria and reasoning about physical systems. We introduce gwBenchmarks, a suite of eight tasks grounded in gravitational wave analytic calculations and numerical simulations collectively representing over $10^8$ core-hours of compute. The tasks span interpolation, regression, and high-dimensional time-series modeling, requiring a combination of numerical methods, machine learning, and physics-informed approaches. In preliminary experiments, agents frequently relied on proxy metrics, partial evaluation, or fabricated results to spuriously complete tasks. We therefore implement an external pre-defined framework to gauge agent progress. Evaluating twelve coding agents, we find no consistent winner. On the easiest task, multiple agents converge to the same cubic spline solution, with one rediscovering a coordinate transformation widely used in the literature. On harder tasks like analytic waveform modeling, all agents fall 1-2 orders of magnitude short of domain requirements and exhibit systematic failures, including metric misuse, constraint violations, and result fabrication. Our code, data, and website are publicly available.

### [54] [End-to-End Population Inference from Gravitational-Wave Strain using Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11274)
*Konstantin Leyde,Stephen R. Green,Maximilian Dax,Matthew Mould,Cecilia Maria Fabbri,Jonathan Gair*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出 Dingo-Pop，一个基于模拟的框架，直接从引力波应变数据推断双致密天体（compact binary）种群的参数后验，避免了传统逐事件后验分析的高计算成本与蒙特卡洛噪声，可在约一秒内完成具有 25 至 1000 个事件的目录的端到端推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着引力波事件目录规模的增大，传统分层贝叶斯方法（hierarchical Bayesian method）在结合单事件后验时面临计算成本高昂和蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）不确定性增长的问题，亟需一种计算高效的种群推断方法。

Method: Dingo-Pop 采用基于模拟的推断（simulation-based inference）框架，将每个引力波事件的应变数据嵌入为低维 token，并利用一个在模拟目录上训练的 transformer 模型来整合这些 token，同时考虑选择效应（selection effects）。该网络经过训练后可固定处理可变大小的目录。

Result: 训练后的网络支持25至1000个事件的目录规模，生成的后验分布经过校准且与传统方法一致。该方法消除了逐事件蒙特卡洛采样噪声，实现了跨不同大小目录的摊销（amortization）推断，单次推断耗时约一秒。应用示例展示了光谱标准汽笛（spectral siren）哈勃常数不确定度随目录大小的变化。

Conclusion: Dingo-Pop 通过绕过耗时的逐事件分析，显著提升了种群推断的计算效率，从而支持大规模注入研究（injection study）等新应用场景。

Abstract: The population of compact binaries encodes information about their astrophysical origins and the expansion of the universe. Hierarchical Bayesian methods infer these properties by combining single-event posteriors. As catalogs grow, however, this approach becomes computationally expensive and is subject to increasing Monte Carlo uncertainty. We introduce Dingo-Pop, a simulation-based framework that infers population posteriors directly from gravitational-wave strain data. The data for each event are embedded into low-dimensional tokens and combined using a transformer trained on simulated catalogs subject to selection effects. This enables (i) population inference without per-event Monte Carlo sampling noise, (ii) amortization across variable catalog sizes using a single network, and (iii) end-to-end inference in about one second. We train a network for catalog sizes of 25 to 1000 events, and obtain well-calibrated posteriors consistent with traditional methods. By avoiding per-event analyses that can take hours to days, Dingo-Pop enables new classes of large-scale injection studies; as an application, we examine how spectral-siren Hubble constant uncertainties change with catalog size.

### [55] [Discovery of Interpretable Surrogates via Agentic AI: Application to Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11280)
*Tousif Islam,Digvijay Wadekar,Tejaswi Venumadhav,Matias Zaldarriaga,Ajit Kumar Mehta,Javier Roulet,Barak Zackay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出GWAgent——一种基于大型语言模型（LLM）的工作流，用于直接从模拟数据构建可解释的解析代理模型（interpretable analytic surrogates）。以偏心双黑洞并合的引力波波形为案例，该代理模型在精度（Advanced LIGO中位失配度6.9×10⁻⁴）和速度（波形评估加速约8.4倍）上均超越符号回归（symbolic regression）和传统机器学习基线，并成功应用于分析GW200129的偏心率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 昂贵的科学模拟需要快速代理模型（surrogate models），但现有代理模型通常作为黑箱（black box）运行，缺乏可解释性。本文旨在开发一种既能保持高精度与计算效率、又能生成可解析解释的代理模型构建方法。

Method: 提出GWAgent——一种基于大型语言模型（large language model, LLM）的智能体工作流（agentic workflow），用于直接从模拟数据构建可解释的解析代理模型。该方法利用代理模型可在每一迭代轮次中与真实模拟进行定量验证的特点，引入物理信息领域假设（physics-informed domain ansatz）以提升输出模型精度。

Result: 以偏心双黑洞并合引力波波形为例，得到的解析代理模型在Advanced LIGO上达到中位失配度（median mismatch）6.9×10⁻⁴，波形评估速度提升约8.4倍，精度超越符号回归（symbolic regression）和传统机器学习基线。该工作流还能从学习到的表示中识别出紧凑的物理结构。在GW200129的天体物理应用中，推断出偏心率e_{20Hz}=0.099^{+0.063}_{-0.044}。

Conclusion: 基于验证约束的智能体工作流（validation-constrained agentic workflows）能够为科学模拟和推断生成准确、快速且可解释的代理模型。

Abstract: Fast surrogate models for expensive simulations are now essential across the sciences, yet they typically operate as black boxes. We present \texttt{GWAgent}, a large language model (LLM)-based workflow that constructs interpretable analytic surrogates directly from simulation data. Surrogate modeling is well suited to agentic workflows because candidate models can be quantitatively validated against ground-truth simulations at each iteration. As a demonstration, we build a surrogate for gravitational waveforms from eccentric binary black hole mergers. We show that providing the agent with a physics-informed domain ansatz substantially improves output model accuracy. The resulting analytic surrogate attains a median Advanced LIGO mismatch of $6.9\times10^{-4}$ together with an $\sim 8.4\times$ speedup in waveform evaluation, surpassing both symbolic regression and conventional machine learning baselines. Beyond producing an accurate model, the workflow identifies compact physical structure from the learned representation. As an astrophysical application, we use \texttt{GWAgent} to analyze the eccentricity of GW200129 and infer $e_{20\mathrm{Hz}}=0.099^{+0.063}_{-0.044}$. These results show that validation-constrained agentic workflows can produce accurate, fast, and interpretable surrogates for scientific simulations and inference.

</details>


### [56] [Closing the Cosmographic Hierarchy: Dynamical Attractors from Inflation to Reheating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11292)
*Seturumane Tema,S. Shajidul Haque,Saurya Das,Peter Dunsby*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个不依赖于具体势能形式的宇宙学框架（cosmographic framework），将宇宙学参数提升为封闭自治系统（closed autonomous system）中的动力学变量。通过将势能慢滚参数（slow-roll parameters）映射到运动学相空间（kinematic phase space），实现了形式上无穷级数（cosmographic hierarchy）的封闭。稳定性分析表明，暴胀（准德西特）解是自然吸引子（attractor），刚性流体（stiff-fluid）构型是排斥子（repeller）。通过引入辐射组分和唯象衰减项，将系统扩展至重加热（reheating）阶段，给出了有效物态方程 $w_{\rm eff}$ 描述，并证明辐射主导阶段是扩展系统的晚期吸引子。该工作统一刻画了从暴胀到重加热的膨胀历史，桥接了宇宙学（cosmography）与标量场动力学（scalar field dynamics）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准暴胀模型依赖具体的势能形式（potential），导致宇宙学参数（cosmographic parameters）被处理为无穷层级（infinite hierarchy）。本文旨在构建一个不依赖势能形式的统一运动学框架，将宇宙学参数提升为动力学变量，从而在闭合的自治系统中实现从暴胀到重加热的完整膨胀历史描述。

Method: 将宇宙学参数视为封闭自治系统中的动力学变量；通过将势能慢滚参数映射到广义相对论（General Relativity）中标量场（minimally coupled scalar field）的运动学相空间，实现无穷层级的封闭；引入辐射组分和唯象衰减项（phenomenological decay term）将系统扩展至重加热阶段。

Result: 稳定性分析表明，暴胀（准德西特）解是系统的自然吸引子，刚性流体构型是排斥子，且该结论无需慢滚近似（slow-roll approximation）。扩展系统的重加热阶段由有效物态方程 $w_{\rm eff}$ 描述，辐射主导相（radiation-dominated phase）是晚期吸引子。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个统一且不依赖势能形式的运动学描述，从暴胀贯穿到重加热阶段，成功桥接了宇宙学（cosmography）与标量场动力学（scalar field dynamics）两大领域。

Abstract: We develop a potential-independent cosmographic framework, in which cosmographic parameters are promoted to dynamical variables within a closed autonomous system. Although the cosmographic hierarchy is formally infinite, we achieve closure by mapping potential slow-roll parameters onto the kinematic phase space within General Relativity with a minimally coupled scalar field. Within this framework, we perform a stability analysis and show that inflationary (quasi-de Sitter) solutions arise as natural attractors, while stiff-fluid configurations act as repellers without invoking the slow-roll approximation. To describe the transition to standard Big Bang evolution, we extend the system to include a radiation component and a phenomenological decay term. This leads to a generalized, potential-independent description of reheating characterized by an effective equation of state $w_{\rm eff}$. We demonstrate that the radiation-dominated phase is the late-time attractor of the extended system. These results provide a unified kinematical description of the expansion history from inflation through reheating, bridging cosmography and scalar field dynamics.

### [57] [Periodic cosmic evolution in Hybrid and Logarithmic Teleparallel Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11338)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用修正teleparallel引力（modified teleparallel gravity）中的两种$f(T)$函数形式——混合模型$f(T)=e^{γT}T^σ$和对数模型，结合周期性振荡减速参数$q(t)=m\cos(kt)-1$来描述循环宇宙（cyclic Universe）演化。利用观测值$m \simeq 0.48$和$H_0 = 69.2\,\text{km}\,\text{s}^{-1}\,\text{Mpc}^{-1}$对模型进行约束。

Result: 混合模型下能量密度保持为正，压强振荡；状态方程动态演化，可穿越quintessence态（暗能量态之一）和phantom态（幻影暗能量态）。对数模型能稳定动力学行为、正则化发散，状态方程主要停留在quintessence区域。能量条件分析显示，强能量条件（SEC）的破坏支持加速膨胀，而零能量条件（NEC）与主导能量条件（DEC）的部分有效性确保物理一致性。

Conclusion: 该框架为ΛCDM模型提供了一个灵活的替代方案，能够统一描述宇宙膨胀的不同阶段。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate a cosmological model within modified teleparallel gravity using two functional forms of $f(T)$: a hybrid model $f(T)=e^{γT}T^σ$ and a logarithmic model, in the context of a periodic cosmic evolution driven by an oscillating deceleration parameter $q(t)=m\cos(kt)-1$. This approach describes a cyclic Universe with successive transitions between decelerating and accelerating phases.
  By constraining the model with observational values $m \simeq 0.48$ and $H_0 = 69.2\,\text{km}\,\text{s}^{-1}\,\text{Mpc}^{-1}$, we recover the present accelerated expansion with $q_0 \approx -0.52$, while larger values $m \geq 1$ lead to strongly oscillatory regimes including super-acceleration.
  For the hybrid model ($γ= 0.1$, $σ= -0.5$), the energy density remains positive, while the pressure oscillates. The equation of state evolves dynamically, crossing both quintessence and phantom regimes. In contrast, the logarithmic model stabilizes the dynamics, regularizes divergences, and yields smoother evolution, with the equation of state mainly remaining in the quintessence regime.
  The analysis of energy conditions shows that the violation of the SEC supports accelerated expansion, while the partial validity of NEC and DEC ensures physical consistency.
  Overall, this framework provides a flexible alternative to the standard $Λ$CDM model, allowing a unified description of different phases of cosmic expansion.

### [58] [Bardeen spacetime as quantum corrected black hole: Grey-body factors and quasinormal modes of gravitational perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11364)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从各向异性流体（anisotropic-fluid）背景出发，推导了Regge-Wheeler型主方程（Regge-Wheeler-type master equation）及相应的有效势；随后采用高阶WKB-Padé方法（high-order WKB-Padé method）和时域方法（time-domain method）计算准正则模（quasinormal modes, QNMs）。

Conclusion: 短距离正则化（short-distance regularization）在振铃和散射两种可观测量上均留下清晰且一致的印记，表明该量子修正模型具有可观测的引力波与散射特征。

Abstract: We study axial gravitational perturbations of the asymptotically flat Bardeen spacetime interpreted as a string-T-duality-inspired quantum-corrected Schwarzschild black hole. Starting from the anisotropic-fluid background, we derive the Regge--Wheeler-type master equation and the corresponding effective potential, and compute quasinormal modes with high-order WKB--Padé and time-domain methods. We show that increasing the quantum-correction scale $\ell_0$ raises and shifts the barrier inward, causing the black hole to ring at higher frequencies and decay more slowly. The same deformation suppresses low-frequency transmission, shifts the onset of grey-body factors to larger frequencies, and reorganizes the partial and total absorption cross-sections. Overall, the results identify a clear and consistent imprint of short-distance regularization on both ringdown and scattering observables.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先提出适用于离散相对论性粒子系统的刚性条件（rigidity conditions），这些条件本身不足以确定系统演化，因此需补充二阶运动方程。随后提出并讨论了与这些刚性条件兼容的庞加莱协变运动方程（Poincaré-covariant equations of motion）。

Result: 最终得到的理论具有预期的六个动力学自由度（six dynamical degrees of freedom），从而允许比玻恩理论更一般的运动。

Conclusion: 将相对论性物体作为离散粒子系统处理，有望成为基于玻恩刚性条件的标准方法的一种有前景的替代方案。

Abstract: Rigidity conditions for a body considered as a discrete system of relativistic particles are proposed. They by themselves do not yet determine an evolution of the system, and some second-order equations must be added to them. Poincaré-covariant equations of motion compatible with these rigidity conditions are proposed and discussed. The resulting theory has the expected six dynamical degrees of freedom and therefore allows for more general motions than in Born's theory. Therefore, treating a relativistic body as a discrete system of particles could be a promising alternative to the standard approach based on Born's rigidity conditions.

### [60] [Stability and quasi-normal ringing in analogue black-white holes in SNAIL-based traveling-wave parametric amplifiers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11565)
*Daisuke Yamauchi,Haruna Katayama,Norihiro Tanahashi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了超导非线性非对称元件（SNAIL）行波参量放大器（TWPA）电路系统中由孤子（soliton）背景场实现的类比事件视界（analogue event horizon）因果结构，推导了弱探针场的主方程，利用超对称量子力学（supersymmetric quantum mechanics）证明了系统不存在可归一化负模，并通过半解析与数值方法首次研究了该类比黑洞-白洞系统的准正则模（QNM），阐明了非线性色散起效的时间尺度及振铃（ringdown）激发机制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 通过超对称量子力学论证，证明了SNAIL-TWPA电路系统中不存在可归一化的负能量模式。获得了该类比黑洞-白洞系统的准正则模（QNM）频率。基于所得QNM频率，厘清了非线性色散在系统中生效的时间尺度，并展示了振铃（ringdown）信号如何被激发。

Conclusion: SNAIL-TWPA电路系统可以作为一种可控的类比引力平台，模拟事件视界的因果结构。该系统的动力学稳定性（无负模）及其清晰的QNM谱使其适用于研究非线性色散效应和振铃激发，为在超导电路中探索类比黑洞物理提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The circuit dynamics constructed by traveling-wave parametric amplifiers (TWPA), using superconducting nonlinear asymmetric elements (SNAILs), are known to be approximately described by the Korteweg-de Vries (KdV) or modified KdV equations in the continuum limit and admit soliton solutions. The soliton spatially modulates the effective propagation velocity of the weak probe field, which leads to the effective realization of the causal structure of the analogue event horizons in the SNAIL-TWPA circuit system. In this paper, we derive the master equation for the weak probe field where the background soliton acts as an effective potential. We show the absence of normalizable negative modes in the SNAIL-TWPA circuit system by using the language of supersymmetric quantum mechanics. We also present the first study of quasi-normal modes (QNM) of the SNAIL-TWPA analogue black-white hole system by semi-analytic and numerical methods. ### [61] [Cosmology of f(Q,L_m) gravity with Holographic Ricci Dark Energy: Early-Time Inflation and Late-Time Acceleration and RGUP Corrected Observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11623)
*Khandro K Chokyi,Abdel Nasser Tawfik,Surajit Chattopadhyay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在 f(Q,L_m) 引力框架下提出一个最小多项式模型，利用非度量性（non-metricity）的二次项 αQ² 驱动早期暴胀（inflation），并通过引入全息 Ricci 暗能量（Holographic Ricci Dark Energy, HRDE）描述晚期加速膨胀，同时考察了相对论性广义不确定性原理（Relativistic Generalized Uncertainty Principle, RGUP）对早期暴胀可观测量的修正。贝叶斯分析表明模型与 ΛCDM 及 Planck 2018 观测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 模型背景演化呈现平滑加速膨胀，有效物态方程（equation of state）趋近 de Sitter 区域；物质-几何耦合参数 β 约束较弱，与 ΛCDM 极限一致；早期 αQ² 主导的暴胀相预测的标量谱指数 n_s 和张量标量比 r 与 Planck 2018 观测一致；RGUP 修正仅在暴胀可观测量的高阶项（如谱指数跑动）中引入微扰移位。

Conclusion: f(Q,L_m) 框架提供了一个动力学一致的几何模型，早期和晚期宇宙加速分别源于不同的曲率区域（regime），RGUP 效应仅产生次主导（sub-leading）修正。

Abstract: This study investigates a cosmological scenario within the f(Q,L_m) gravity framework to explore whether one geometric model can simultaneously describe the early and late-time accelerated epochs. Motivated by the recently proposed f(Q,L_m) gravity framework by Hazarika et al. [Phys. Dark Universe 50 (2025) 102092], we adopt a minimal polynomial form, f(Q,L_m) = -Q + alpha Q^2 + 2L_m + beta QL_m, and the late-time dynamics are reconstructed by introducing Holographic Ricci Dark Energy (HRDE) as an effective fluid. The resulting background evolution demonstrates smooth accelerated expansion, stable Hubble parameter behavior, and an effective equation of state that approaches the de Sitter regime. Bayesian analysis utilizing Pantheon supernovae, cosmic chronometer, and DESI BAO data reveals that the matter-geometry coupling parameter beta is weakly constrained and remains consistent with the LambdaCDM limit. In the high-curvature regime characteristic of the early Universe, the quadratic non-metricity term alpha Q^2 dominates the dynamics, resulting in a Starobinsky-like inflationary phase driven solely by geometric effects with predicted n_s and r values consistent with Planck 2018 observations. Furthermore, quantum-gravity-inspired corrections are examined through a Relativistic Generalized Uncertainty Principle (RGUP), implemented as a momentum-dependent deformation of the effective spacetime metric. These corrections maintain the geometric inflationary background while introducing minor perturbative shifts in higher-order inflationary observables, specifically the running of the spectral index. Overall, these findings indicate that the f(Q,L_m) framework offers a dynamically consistent geometric model in which early and late cosmic acceleration arise from distinct curvature regimes, with RGUP effects causing sub-leading modifications.

Zimmermann,M. E. Zucker*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于GW240925和GW250207两个高信噪比引力波事件，首次通过天体物理信号本身对引力波探测器进行校准测量，验证了在Hanford探测器不稳定时利用天体物理校准（astrophysical calibration）获取精确数据的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于超高信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）的引力波事件，传统基于仪器原位测量（in-situ measurement）的校准可能不够精确或存在局限性。当探测器状态不稳定时，有必要开发直接从天体物理信号中约束探测器校准的方法，以确保数据准确性。

Method: 利用双黑洞并合（binary black hole coalescence）产生的引力波信号的固有相位和振幅演化特性（由广义相对论预言），结合仪器校准不确定性，直接从高信噪比观测信号出发推断探测器校准参数。

Result: 对GW240925，通过已知的原位校准误差交叉检验，验证了从天体物理信号推断Hanford探测器校准的有效性。对GW250207，在Hanford探测器未完全稳定的情况下，天体物理校准成为获取精确数据和实现源定位（source localization）的关键手段。

Conclusion: 天体物理校准可作为原位校准的重要补充，在高精度引力波科学（如精确测量源性质、广义相对论检验和暗标准汽笛（dark siren）测量）中发挥关键作用。随着探测器灵敏度提升，其价值将进一步凸显。

Abstract: GW240925 and GW250207 are two loud gravitational-wave signals from binary black hole coalescences observed with network signal-to-noise ratios $\sim 32$ and $\sim 69$, respectively, by the LIGO Hanford--LIGO Livingston--Virgo network. Gravitational-wave signals from coalescing binaries have characteristic phase and amplitude evolution predicted by general relativity. These signal waveforms, together with measured instrumental calibration uncertainties, are used to infer source parameters. However, for sufficiently loud detections it is possible to constrain the calibration of the detectors directly using the signals themselves. We present the first informative astrophysical measurements of gravitational-wave detector calibration. For GW240925, we verify the inference of Hanford calibration from the astrophysical signal through cross-checks with known calibration errors obtained from in-situ measurements. At the time of GW250207, the Hanford detector was not fully stabilized, leading to elevated calibration uncertainties; thus, astrophysical calibration is essential to obtain accurate data and to enable source localization. These well-localized, high signal-to-noise observations have the potential to offer precise measurements of source properties, stringent tests of general relativity, and informative dark siren measurements, provided that calibration uncertainties are properly incorporated. As detector sensitivity improves, astrophysical calibration will become an increasingly valuable complement to in-situ calibration measurements. Obtaining accurate calibration will be essential for precision gravitational-wave science.

</details>


### [63] [Thermodynamic formulation of Cotton gravity in the Codazzi parametrization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11821)
*Shayesteh Ghaffari,Giuseppe Gaetano Luciano,Carlo Alberto Mantica*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在科达齐参数化（Codazzi parametrization）框架下发展了科顿引力（Cotton gravity）的热力学形式，将其引力动力学解释为视界热力学（horizon thermodynamics）。通过对宇宙学视界和事件视界应用热力学第一定律，推导出包含科达齐张量修正的修正全息熵，并展示了该修正符号可作为区分普通物质、宇宙学常数和类幻影成分的诊断工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有科顿引力研究多集中于背景运动学层面，缺乏对其热力学和统计物理性质的理解。本文旨在建立科顿引力的热力学形式化框架，揭示引力动力学与视界热力学之间的深层联系。

Method: 在科达齐参数化框架下发展科顿引力的热力学形式，并将其应用于弗里德曼-罗伯逊-沃克（FRW）宇宙和静态球对称时空这两个范例。通过在表观宇宙学视界和事件视界上实施热力学第一定律，推导出修正的全息熵公式。

Result: 得到了由标准贝肯斯坦-霍金项（Bekenstein-Hawking term）加上科达齐张量（Codazzi tensor）诱导的修正项所组成的修正全息熵。在宇宙学设定中，修正由科达齐张量的时间分量支配；在静态配置中，修正由其各向异性部分控制。该修正项的符号可区分普通物质、宇宙学常数和类幻影成分。

Conclusion: 视界热力学可作为一种灵敏的探针来研究科顿引力，为超越背景运动学的视角提供了补充，并在科达齐形式框架内实现了时空统计与热力学性质的表征。

Abstract: We develop a thermodynamic formulation of Cotton gravity in the Codazzi parametrization, providing a general framework in which the gravitational dynamics can be interpreted in terms of horizon thermodynamics. As paradigmatic examples, we apply the formalism to FriedmannRobertson-Walker (FRW) and static spherically symmetric spacetimes. By implementing the first law of thermodynamics on the apparent cosmological and event horizons, we derive a modified holographic entropy consisting of the standard Bekenstein-Hawking term supplemented by a correction induced by the Codazzi tensor. In the cosmological setting, this correction is governed by the temporal component of the Codazzi tensor, while in static configurations it is controlled by its anisotropic sector. Remarkably, the sign of this contribution provides a potential diagnostic of the underlying matter content, allowing one to distinguish between ordinary matter, a cosmological constant and phantom-like components. These results establish horizon thermodynamics as a sensitive probe of Cotton gravity, offering a complementary perspective beyond background kinematics and enabling a characterization of the statistical and thermodynamic properties of spacetime within the Codazzi formulation.

</details>


### [64] [A cosmology-to-ringdown EFT consistency map for scalar-tensor gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11890)
*Mushtaq Ahmad,M. Farasat Shamir*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了一条从晚期标量-张量宇宙学到黑洞铃宕（ringdown）可观测量之间的有效场论（EFT）桥梁。通过宇宙学条件化的EFT后验，将若当坐标系下的FLRW数据通过有限协变喷流（finite covariant jet）提升，再传递到含类时标量的黑洞微扰任意背景EFT，最终投影到宇称分辨的准正规模（quasinormal mode）响应核上。后验分布显示，宇宙学继承的FLRW张量速度形变远低于铃宕可探测阈值，而FLRW均匀背景下消失的算子可在黑洞各向异性近区保持活跃。该框架将宇宙学可行性转化为黑洞光谱学先验，同时明确而非假定强场完备性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立从晚期宇宙学（cosmology）观测约束到黑洞铃宕（ringdown）可观测量的理论链接，使宇宙学约束能够转化为黑洞微扰理论中的先验信息，从而为黑洞光谱学（black-hole spectroscopy）提供更坚实的强场物理基础。

Method: 从宇宙学条件化的EFT后验出发，通过有限协变喷流（finite covariant jet）提升若当坐标系（Jordan frame）下的FLRW数据，将其传递到含类时标量（timelike scalar）的黑洞微扰任意背景EFT中，再投影到宇称分辨的准正规模（parity-resolved quasinormal-mode）响应核上。宇宙学层使用BAO类距离、增长摘要、低红移张量速度信息等构建确定性压缩似然（compressed likelihood）；探测器层则采用贝叶斯时域注入（Bayesian time-domain injections）分析。

Result: 宇宙学继承的FLRW张量速度形变被驱动到远低于铃宕可探测性的水平；相反，在FLRW均匀背景（homogeneous FLRW background）上消失的算子在黑洞各向异性近区（anisotropic near zone）仍可保持活跃。通过文献校准的Hayward分支，区分了直接可接受点与代理延拓，并将两者传播到探测器白化的一致性模式（detector-whitened consistency modes）中。

Conclusion: 该框架将宇宙学可行性转化为黑洞光谱学（black-hole spectroscopy）先验，同时明确而非假定强场完备性（strong-field completion），为未来引力波观测与宇宙学约束之间的跨领域交叉检验提供了系统化的理论工具。

Abstract: We construct an effective-field-theory bridge from late-time scalar-tensor cosmology to black-hole ringdown observables. Starting from a cosmology-conditioned EFT posterior, we lift Jordan-frame FLRW data through a finite covariant jet, transport the result to the arbitrary-background EFT for black-hole perturbations with a timelike scalar, and project it onto parity-resolved quasinormal-mode response kernels. The cosmological layer is a deterministic compressed likelihood built from BAO-like distances, growth summaries, low-redshift tensor-speed information, stability filters, and posterior samples for the ringdown pushforward. The detector layer uses Bayesian time-domain injections, one-, two-, and three-mode recovery models, analytic marginalization over linear sine/cosine amplitudes, remnant-calibration covariance products, and start-time variations. The transported posterior shows that FLRW tensor-speed deformations inherited from cosmology are driven far below ringdown detectability, whereas operators that vanish on homogeneous FLRW backgrounds can remain active in the anisotropic near zone of a black hole. For a literature-calibrated Hayward branch, we specify the prior measure, separate directly admissible points from a proxy continuation, and propagate both to detector-whitened consistency modes. The resulting framework turns cosmological viability into black-hole spectroscopy priors while keeping the strong-field completion explicit rather than assumed.

</details>


### [65] [The choice of variables in cosmological dynamical systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11971)
*Christian G. Boehmer,Antonio d'Alfonso del Sordo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文探讨了如何将宇宙学场方程转化为动力系统（dynamical system）形式，重点分析了不同动力学变量选择对从弗里德曼方程（Friedmann equations）中提取信息的影响，并通过标准宇宙学模型和标量场模型进行了具体讨论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将宇宙学场方程转化为动力系统形式时，动力学变量（dynamical variables）的选择至关重要，但文献中对此过程的讨论较少。作者旨在填补这一空白，阐明变量选择如何影响从方程中提取的信息。

Method: 从标准宇宙学模型（包含暗物质、辐射和暗能量）出发，引入精质场（quintessence）模型，使用新变量重新分析具有指数势（exponential potential）的已知模型，并将讨论扩展到标量场（scalar fields）及更复杂的耦合项情形。

Result: 不同变量选择会显著影响从弗里德曼方程中提取的动力学信息；对指数势模型的重新分析展示了新变量的优势；该方法可推广至包含标量场和非平凡耦合项的更复杂理论。

Conclusion: 动力系统方法（dynamical systems techniques）是分析常微分方程组（ordinary differential equations）的有力工具，而合理的变量选择是成功应用该方法的关键前提，值得研究者给予更多关注。

Abstract: Dynamical systems techniques are a powerful tool to analyse systems of ordinary differential equations, written in an appropriate form. For a given theory of gravity, the cosmological field equations typically lead to a system of ordinary differential equations. Casting these cosmological equations into the form of a dynamical system requires a careful choice of the dynamical variables. Despite this being a critical step, relatively little is said about this process in the literature. We discuss how different variable choices affect the information that can be extracted from the Friedmann equations. We begin by reviewing the standard cosmological model with dark matter, radiation, and dark energy, and include quintessence models. We revisit well-known models with an exponential potential using new variables. This discussion is then extended to models with scalar fields and more intricate coupling terms.

</details>


### [66] [Chaos and epoch structure in the deformed Mixmaster universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12173)
*Babak Vakili*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了Bianchi~IX（Mixmaster）宇宙在经典聚合化（classical polymerization）与广义不确定性原理（generalized uncertainty principle, GUP）对泊松括号变形下的动力学。通过从Misner哈密顿量出发导出有效运动方程，分析了两种修正对Kasner时期持续时间的影响，发现GUP修正缩短时期、增加碰撞频率，而聚合修正延长时期、抑制反弹，二者组合产生可加性偏移。Mixmaster混沌的强度对变形参数敏感，表明普朗克尺度修正可能增强或抑制宇宙混沌。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索普朗克尺度量子引力修正（如聚合化与GUP）对早期宇宙动力学，特别是Mixmaster混沌行为的影响，以理解量子效应如何调控宇宙学混沌。

Method: 从Misner哈密顿量出发，分别引入经典聚合化与GUP对泊松括号的变形，推导出修正后的有效运动方程；以Kasner时期的持续时间作为动力学行为的探针，分析两种修正单独及组合下的演化特征。

Result: GUP修正通常缩短Kasner时期，导致更频繁的壁碰撞（wall collisions）；聚合修正则延长时期，抑制连续反弹。在领头阶（leading order），两种变形组合产生可加性偏移（additive shift），在两种趋势之间插值。Mixmaster混沌的强度对变形参数敏感，而台球图景（billiard picture）整体保持鲁棒。

Conclusion: 普朗克尺度修正既可增强亦可抑制宇宙学混沌，这取决于修正的具体类型与参数，为研究早期宇宙动力学提供了一个可控的理论框架。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of the Bianchi~IX (Mixmaster) universe under classical polymerization and generalized uncertainty principle (GUP) deformation of the Poisson brackets. Starting from the Misner Hamiltonian, we derive the effective equations of motion with both modifications and analyze the duration of Kasner epochs as a probe of dynamical behavior. Our results show that GUP corrections typically shorten the epochs, leading to more frequent wall collisions, whereas polymer corrections prolong them and suppress successive bounces. At leading order, the combined deformation produces an additive shift that interpolates between these two trends. While the billiard picture remains robust, the strength of Mixmaster chaos becomes sensitive to the deformation parameters. These results illustrate how Planck-scale corrections may either enhance or suppress cosmological chaos, offering a controlled framework for exploring early-universe dynamics.

</details>


### [67] [Generalized Mass-to-Horizon Entropy and Horizon Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12003)
*Smeehan S Shameeem,Priyesh K,Krishna P. B,Titus K Mathew*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了广义质量-视界熵（generalized mass-to-horizon entropy），作为标准贝肯斯坦熵（Bekenstein entropy）的二元参数扩展，并通过熵平衡关系推导了弗里德曼方程（Friedmann equation），验证了其热力学一致性及宇宙加速膨胀的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准贝肯斯坦熵在描述宇宙视界热力学时存在局限性，作者希望引入一个基于质量-视界关系（mass-to-horizon relation）的广义熵形式，以更一般性地刻画修改后的宇宙学动力学。

Method: 首先假设熵平衡关系（entropy balance relation），推导广义质量-视界熵的变化量，进而利用克劳修斯关系（Clausius relation）以及修正的热力学定律导出弗里德曼方程。通过熵演化（entropy evolution）和熵最大化（entropy maximization）条件检验热力学一致性，并分析视界能量涨落（fluctuations in horizon energy）以评估热稳定性。

Result: 广义熵及其高阶导数表明宇宙演化趋向于稳定的最大熵构型，且与广义第二定律（generalized second law of thermodynamics）一致。能量涨落分析显示有限且物理稳定的行为，支持模型的热力学可行性。

Conclusion: 广义质量-视界熵可作为描述修改后宇宙学动力学以及宇宙加速膨胀的有效热力学框架。

Abstract: We investigate the cosmological implications of generalized mass-to-horizon entropy, a two-parameter extension of the standard Bekenstein entropy based on the mass-to-horizon relation. Assuming the entropy balance relation, we derive the change in the generalized mass-to-horizon entropy, which entirely accounts for the heat exchange across the horizon as measured by an observer near the apparent horizon. We have then derived the Friedmann equation, using the Clausius relation, and also using modified law of thermodynamics. The thermodynamic consistency of the entropy, is examined through entropy evolution and entropy maximization conditions, where the generalized entropy and its higher-order derivatives indicate that the universe evolves toward a stable maximum entropy configuration consistent with the generalized second law of thermodynamics. In addition, fluctuations in horizon energy are investigated to probe the thermal stability and thermodynamic behavior of the cosmic horizon. The fluctuation analysis reveals finite and physically stable behavior throughout cosmic evolution, supporting the thermodynamic viability of the proposed model. The present work therefore establishes the generalized mass-to-horizon entropy as a viable thermodynamic framework for describing modified cosmological dynamics and also the accelerated expansion of the universe as well.

</details>


### [68] [Causality Violating Solutions in Curvature-Squared Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12076)
*J. C. R. de Souza,A. F. Santos,R. Bufalo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文研究了曲率平方引力（curvature-squared gravity）中允许闭合类时曲线（closed timelike curves, CTCs）的因果性破坏解，分析了Gödel度规、Gödel型度规和轴对称宇宙学解，发现前两种度规下CTCs被允许且Weyl张量贡献消失，而第三种度规中Weyl张量对能量密度产生影响并修正了弱能量条件（weak energy condition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验曲率平方引力模型中是否允许闭合类时曲线（CTCs）的出现，以探讨该引力理论中的因果性破坏问题。

Method: 通过分析Gödel、Gödel型以及轴对称宇宙学解这三种度规，在曲率平方引力框架下研究CTCs的存在性及其与Weyl张量的关系。

Result: Gödel和Gödel型度规在模型中表现为因果解，允许CTCs存在，且所有涉及Weyl张量的贡献被消去；轴对称解中Weyl张量对能量密度产生贡献，并导致弱能量条件（weak energy condition）被修正。

Conclusion: 曲率平方引力中Gödel与Gödel型解允许CTCs，且Weyl张量的贡献完全消失；为研究Weyl张量（共形对称性）对CTCs的影响，需引入第三种度规，其中Weyl张量确实对能量密度和能量条件产生可观测的修正。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider some causality violating solutions in the curvature-squared gravity in order to examine whether closed timelike curves (CTCs) are allowed in these models. These aspects are studied in terms of the Gödel, Gödel-type and axially symmetric cosmological solutions. We observe that the Gödel and Gödel-type metrics are causal solutions of the model so that CTCs are now allowed and, surprisingly, every contribution involving the Weyl tensor is removed from the solutions. Hence, in order to study the effect (if any) of the Weyl tensor (an conformal symmetry) into CTCs a third metric is considered. In this case, we obtain contributions due to the Weyl tensor to the energy density and led to modifications of the weak energy condition.

</details>


### [69] [Quasinormal Spectra of Fields of Various Spin in Asymptotically de Sitter Black Holes within Generalized Proca Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12113)
*Milena Skvortsova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义Proca理论中研究了渐近德西特黑洞的无质量标量、电磁和狄拉克扰动。通过推导主方程并利用Padé改进的WKB计算与时域积分分析准正态谱，发现标量扇区（尤其是ℓ=0模）对度规形变最敏感，并探讨了结果对强宇宙监督检验和灰体因子的意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义Proca理论中的渐近德西特黑洞因Proca扇区同时产生原初毛发参数和有效宇宙学项Λ_eff而具有特殊的视界结构与静态斑块尺寸，研究其扰动的准正态谱有助于理解这类毛状黑洞的动力学稳定性及对强宇宙监督假设的潜在影响。

Method: 以该毛状黑洞的公共背景为基础，导出三种自旋扇区的主方程（master equations），并借助Padé改进的WKB近似（Padé-improved WKB approximation）结合特征时域积分方法分析准正态频谱。

Result: 标量扇区（尤其ℓ=0模）对度规形变最为敏感；增大Proca毛发参数Q会使阻尼减弱，接近三视界荷电情形；β在(α,β)扫描中使频谱变硬；增大λ和c_1导致频谱整体变软。中性标量ℓ=1模的时域Prony提取与WKB结果高度一致，同时分辨出类施瓦西黑洞分支和德西特分支。

Conclusion: 精确的空德西特极限对强宇宙监督检验有意义，所得准正态频率可为灰体因子（grey-body factors）计算提供有效输入。

Abstract: We study massless scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac perturbations of asymptotically de Sitter black holes in generalized Proca theory. These geometries are especially interesting because the Proca sector generates both a primary-hair parameter and an effective cosmological term $Λ_{\rm eff}$, thereby reshaping the horizon structure and the size of the static patch. Working on this common hairy background, we derive the master equations for the three spin sectors and analyze their quasinormal spectra by means of Padé-improved WKB calculations supplemented by characteristic time-domain integration. We show that the scalar sector, especially the $\ell=0$ mode, is the most sensitive to metric deformations; increasing the Proca-hair parameter $Q$ weakens the damping as the charged three-horizon regime is approached; $β$ hardens the spectrum in the $(α,β)$ scan; and increasing $λ$ and $c_1$ produces the strongest overall softening. For the neutral scalar $\ell=1$ mode, the time-domain Prony extraction agrees excellently with the WKB results and resolves both the Schwarzschild-like black-hole branch and the de Sitter branch. We also discuss the implications of the exact empty-de Sitter limit for strong cosmic censorship and note that the resulting quasinormal frequencies provide useful input for grey-body factors.

Conclusion: 在第三代探测器的低频段，致密双星并合（CBC）背景会对连续引力波（CW）探测造成不可忽视的负面影响，需要在数据分析中加以考虑。

Abstract: The current network of gravitational wave detectors has already revealed hundreds of compact binary coalescences (CBCs), including binary neutron stars, binary black holes, and black hole-neutron star systems. As detector sensitivity improves, the superposition of these signals is expected to form an astrophysical background that becomes increasingly relevant for future observatories. In third generation detectors, such as the Einstein Telescope (ET), this background will be most prominent at low frequencies, potentially affecting the search for continuous gravitational waves (CWs) from spinning neutron stars. In this work, we evaluate the impact of the CBC background on CW detection using the Frequency-Hough pipeline, with a focus on the low-frequency performance in ET sensitivity conditions. Through realistic simulations of the unresolved CBC background, we find that it acts as an additional noise source, most strongly affecting the detection of CW signals around 7 Hz, worsening the FH sensitivity by about 7-10%.

### [71] [On the Geometry of Cotton Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12392)
*Giulio Colombo,Filippo Mastropietro,Marco Rigoli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文分析了静态时空背景下Cotton引力的场方程几何结构，提出了Cotton-φ-完美流体（C-φ-PF）概念作为φ-静态完美流体时空（φ-SPFST）的推广，给出了其退化回φ-SPFST的充分条件、 lapse函数水平集的几何性质以及某些曲率条件下的刚性结果，强调了Codazzi张量在该理论中的作用。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用纯几何分析方法：在静态时空（static space-time）上对Cotton引力的场方程（场方程对应一个相当一般的能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor））进行局部结构描述；引入Cotton-φ-完美流体（Cotton-φ-perfect fluid, C-φ-PF）概念；探讨该系统的变分起源（variational origin）；通过曲率条件推导刚性结果（rigidity result）；分析lapse函数（lapse function）水平集（level sets）的几何性质。

Result: 给出了C-φ-PF退化为φ-SPFST的充分条件；获得了C-φ-PF在特定曲率条件下的刚性结果；揭示了Codazzi张量（Codazzi tensor）在该理论中的关键作用。

Conclusion: C-φ-PF构成了Cotton引力中φ-SPFST的自然推广，Codazzi张量在其中扮演核心角色；曲率条件可导致刚性行为，表明该推广结构在几何上具有丰富的约束性质。

Abstract: We analyze the geometry of the field equations of Cotton gravity (for a quite general energy-momentum tensor) on a static space-time. In particular, we describe the local structure of the spatial Riemannian factor. This structure, that we call \emph{Cotton-$\varphi$-perfect fluid} (C-$\varphi$-PF, for shorts) is a generalization to the regime of Cotton Gravity of the recently introduced notion of $\varphi$-static perfect fluid space-time ($\varphi$-SPFST). After discussing the variational origin of this system, we provide sufficient conditions for a C-$\varphi$-PF to reduce to a $\varphi$-SPFST. We also study the geometry of the level sets of the lapse function $f$ and we provide a rigidity result for C-$\varphi$-PFs under some curvature conditions. The role that Codazzi tensors hold in this theory is highlighted.

### [72] [String Thresholds, Dynamical Gauss--Bonnet Couplings, and Starobinsky Attractors](https://arxiv.org/abs/1808.06404)
*Omer Guleryuz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种弦论启发的动力学 Gauss-Bonnet 修正，用于补充 Starobinsky 暴胀模型。通过标量-Gauss-Bonnet 有效场论，推导了阈值修正后的高原与宇宙微波背景可观测量的不变匹配，并在受控重模量区域中展示了正匹配变形对谱指数、张量信号及 runnings 的影响。Calabi-Yau 拓扑与弦阈值振幅仅作为微观先验，而非来自完全稳定化紧致的直接预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准 Starobinsky 暴胀模型在单场框架下与观测吻合良好，但缺乏来自高能理论（如弦论）的微观实现。本文旨在通过动力学 Gauss-Bonnet 项引入紧致化阈值修正，探索弦论如何对暴胀可观测量产生可检验的变形，而无需依赖完全稳定化的紧致化方案。

Method: 将系统建模为标量-Gauss-Bonnet 有效场论（scalar–Gauss–Bonnet effective theory），推导阈值修正后的高原与主导宇宙微波背景（CMB）可观测量的不变匹配（invariant matching），并施加显式的弦论和 Kaluza–Klein 截断边界（cutoff bounds）。Calabi-Yau 拓扑与弦阈值振幅仅用作阈值函数的微观先验（microscopic priors），可观测变形在稳定化、轨道选择与单时钟匹配之后才被固定。

Result: 在可控重模量（heavy-modulus）区域中，正的匹配变形（positive matched deformation）会提高标量倾斜（scalar tilt）$n_s$，降低张量信号（tensor signal）$r$，并使 runnings $\alpha_s$ 略向负值减弱。以 $X_{24}(1,1,2,8,12)$ 为例展示了拓扑数据与有效阈值响应如何定义 $κ_G \simeq 7 \text{–} 17$ 范围内的定量紧致化目标。

Conclusion: 该工作不是来自完全稳定化紧致的直接预测，而是提供了一个基于拓扑数据和有效阈值响应的定量紧致化目标框架。强调可观测变形依赖于稳定化与轨道选择等后续步骤，而非直接从弦论先验唯一确定。

Abstract: We develop a string-motivated dynamical Gauss--Bonnet completion of Starobinsky inflation. Since a constant Gauss--Bonnet term is topological in four dimensions, observable effects must arise from a modulus, dilaton, or compactification threshold whose value changes during inflation. We formulate the system as a scalar--Gauss--Bonnet effective theory, derive an invariant matching between the threshold-corrected plateau and the leading CMB observables $n_s$, $r$, and the running $α_s \equiv \mathrm d n_s / \mathrm d \ln k$, and impose explicit string and Kaluza--Klein cutoff bounds. Calabi--Yau topology and string threshold amplitudes are used only as microscopic priors for the threshold function; the observable deformation is fixed only after stabilization, trajectory selection, and single-clock matching. In the controlled heavy-modulus regime, a positive matched deformation raises the scalar tilt, lowers the tensor signal, and makes the running mildly less negative. A representative $X_{24}(1,1,2,8,12)$ example illustrates how topological data and an effective threshold response define a quantitative compactification target for the range $κ_G \simeq 7 \text{--} 17$, while emphasizing that this is not a direct prediction from a fully stabilized compactification.

</details>

### [73] [A Quantum Gravitational Mechanism for Isotropization of de Sitter Cosmologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11085)
*Stephon Alexander,Bruno Alexandre,Daine L. Danielson,David N. Spergel*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出将洛伦兹陈-西蒙斯-儿玉（Lorentzian Chern-Simons-Kodama, CSK）泛函重新解释为一种引力斯法勒隆（gravitational sphaleron），该对象在正宇宙学常数背景下，通过围绕德西特（de Sitter）鞍点进行量子引力微扰，能够自然地驱动封闭宇宙向空间各向同性演化，并压制各向异性模式，为暴胀提供近似各向同性的初始背景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可观测宇宙在整体上表现出高度各向同性（isotropy），且很可能起源于一个近乎各向同性的初始状态。理解这一初始各向同性的起源是宇宙学中的一个核心问题，本文旨在利用CSK泛函的量子引力性质为这一现象提供内在机制。

Method: 将CSK波泛函重新解释为引力斯法勒隆，而非严格的量子引力本征态，从而规避其正规化（normalizability）等问题；在封闭宇宙中，围绕占主导的德西特鞍点，施加合适的量子引力边界条件进行微扰展开，分析各向异性模式的动力学行为。

Result: 对于封闭宇宙，系统被动力学地驱动至空间各向同性，所有各向异性模式均获得正的二次曲率（positive quadratic curvature）并受到高斯压制（Gaussian-suppressed）。该各向同性化效应对包含慢滚动暴胀子（slow-roll inflaton）的情形依然稳健，而不存在类似的空间平坦或双曲几何的各向同性斯法勒隆。

Conclusion: 洛伦兹CSK泛函可被视为一种手性斯法勒隆（chiral sphaleron），它自然地制备了一个近似各向同性的德西特背景以支持暴胀。CSK泛函还可被理解为某类无反常对象（包括Hartle-Hawking态的复化推广）的边界泛函（boundary functional）。

Abstract: Today, the observable cosmos exhibits a remarkable degree of isotropy and plausibly began in a nearly isotropic initial state. The properties of the Lorentzian Chern-Simons-Kodama (CSK) functional can provide an understanding of this initial state. In gravity with a positive cosmological constant, the Chern-Simons-Kodama (CSK) wavefunctional is an exact, chiral solution of the quantum gravitational constraints. We suggest that the normalizability and other issues with this functional, if interpreted as a proper state of quantum gravity, instead suggest an embedding into a larger quantum gravitational completion, and recast the CSK functional as a gravitational sphaleron with observationally desirable properties. By perturbing around the dominant de Sitter saddle of the wavefunctional with appropriate quantum gravitational boundary conditions, we find that for a closed universe the system is dynamically driven to spatial isotropy, while all anisotropic modes acquire positive quadratic curvature and are Gaussian-suppressed. The decay of this sphaleron therefore proceeds along an isotropic channel, providing an intrinsic quantum-gravitational mechanism for dynamical isotropization. This isotropization effect is robust under the inclusion of a slow-roll inflaton, and no analogous isotropic sphaleron exists for spatially flat or hyperbolic geometries. Taken together, these results recast the Lorentzian CSK functional as a chiral sphaleron that naturally prepares an approximately isotropic de Sitter background for inflation. Beyond this phenomenological study, we further suggest that the CSK functional can be understood as a boundary functional for a class of anomaly-free objects, including a complexified generalization of the Hartle-Hawking state.

</details>


### [74] [Prospects for multi-messenger discovery of the gravitational-wave background anisotropies via cross-correlation with galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11193)
*Raphael Bertrand-Delgado,Felipe Andrade-Oliveira,Michael Ebersold,Marcelle Soares-Santos*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文基于星系目录与引力波观测约束，预测了随机引力波背景各向异性的可探测性，发现通过多信使与星系交叉关联可在5-10年内实现探测，而仅靠引力波自相关则难度显著更大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational-wave background）各向异性的实际可探测性提供基于经验数据的量化预测，填补当前理论与观测之间的空白。

Method: 利用欧几里得旗舰星系目录（Euclid Flagship Galaxy Catalogue）和LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA观测约束进行模拟，结合详细理论建模；考虑了与星系的多信使交叉关联（multi-messenger cross-correlation）以及仅基于引力波的跨观测时间窗交叉关联。

Result: 对于红移z<3的致密双星，在5年观测期内通过完备至i<24.7星等、红移不确定度为σ_z=0.003(1+z)的星系目录进行交叉关联，需角分辨率θ=4.1度（ℓ≥44）；10年观测期则放宽至θ=6.5度（ℓ≥28）。按红移分箱可重建核函数演化以约束双星种群模型。纯引力波探测需θ=1.8度（ℓ≥95）及高并合率，难度显著更高。

Conclusion: 多信使方法探测随机引力波背景各向异性前景良好，有望在下一代引力波天文台（如爱因斯坦望远镜Einstein Telescope和宇宙探索者Cosmic Explorer）时代实现突破性发现。

Abstract: We present new empirically grounded forecasts for the detectability of the stochastic gravitational-wave background anisotropies assuming a population of stellar-mass compact binary coalescences as its source. We quantified the discovery potential using simulations based on the Euclid Flagship Galaxy Catalogue and LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observational constraints in combination with detailed theoretical modelling. We considered the multi-messenger cross-correlation with galaxies as well as the gravitational wave-only cross-correlation across observation-time bins. For compact binaries up to redshift $z<3$, we found that an angular resolution of $θ= 4.1$ deg ($\ell \geq 44$) is required for discovery within five years of observation via cross-correlation with a galaxy catalogue that is complete up to limiting magnitude $i < 24.7$ and has redshift uncertainties $σ_z = 0.003 (1+z)$. Extending the time range to ten years alleviates that requirement to $θ= 6.5$ deg ($\ell \geq 28$). We also showed that binning the galaxies in redshift allows us to reconstruct the evolution of the kernel, which can be used to further constrain compact binary population models. Discovery without a multi-messenger tracer has proven significantly more challenging, requiring exclusion of the loudest events, $θ= 1.8$ deg ($\ell \geq 95$), and a favourable coalescence rate. In light of the plans being carried out in the community for ongoing and upcoming galaxy surveys, this work bodes well for the multi-messenger discovery and exploration of the stochastic gravitational-wave background in the era of next-generation observatories such as the Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer.

</details>


### [75] [Secondary-Mass Features improve Spectral-Siren $H_0$ Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11474)
*Yin-Jie Li,Yi-Ying Wang,Yuan-Zhu Wang,Shao-Peng Tang,Yi-Zhong Fan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过对GWTC-4.0数据中142个致密双星并合（CBC）引力波事件进行联合推断，采用灵活的参数化模型描述双星质量谱和配对函数，发现次级质量函数对哈勃常数（H_0）的谱标准汽笛（spectral siren）测量精度有显著影响。单独使用谱标准汽笛得到H_0=71.4^{+13.8}_{-13.4} km s^{-1} Mpc^{-1}（68% CL），与亮标准汽笛GW170817联合后H_0=73.5^{+9.2}_{-7.2} km s^{-1} Mpc^{-1}，不确定性比标准LVK Fullpop-4.0分析分别改善约29.8%和22.2%。精度提升源于此前未被建模的特征，包括18 M_⊙和65 M_⊙处的质量峰以及28 M_⊙和52 M_⊙处的质量依赖配对转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波信号可通过谱标准汽笛方法独立测量哈勃常数H_0，该方法关键依赖于精确的源帧质量分布模型。现有研究集中于主质量函数，而次级质量分布对宇宙学推断的影响在很大程度上被忽视了。

Method: 采用一种新的参数化模型，灵活描述双星分量质量谱（component-mass spectrum）和配对函数（pairing function）中的特征，特别关注次级质量。对GWTC-4.0中的142个高置信度致密双星并合事件进行群体参数与宇宙学参数的联合推断。

Result: 单独使用谱标准汽笛得到H_0=71.4^{+13.8}_{-13.4} km s^{-1} Mpc^{-1}（68% CL），与亮标准汽笛GW170817联合后H_0=73.5^{+9.2}_{-7.2} km s^{-1} Mpc^{-1}。相比标准LVK Fullpop-4.0分析，H_0不确定性分别改善约29.8%和22.2%。发现了此前未被建模的特征：18 M_⊙和65 M_⊙处的质量峰，以及28 M_⊙和52 M_⊙处的质量依赖配对转变。

Conclusion: 次级质量函数同样是精度标准汽笛宇宙学的关键要素。通过更灵活地建模双星质量谱和配对函数，可显著提升H_0的测量精度。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave (GW) signals from compact binary coalescences (CBCs) enable independent measurements of the Hubble constant \(H_0\) via the spectral siren method, which critically depends on an accurate model of the source-frame mass distribution. While the primary mass function has been extensively studied, the impact of the secondary mass distribution on cosmological inference has been largely overlooked. Here, we perform a joint inference of population and cosmological parameters using 142 confident CBC detections from GWTC-4.0, adopting a new parametric model that flexibly describes features in both the component-mass spectrum and the pairing function, with particular emphasis on the secondary masses. We find \(H_0 = 71.4^{+13.8}_{-13.4} \;\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}\) (68\% CL) from spectral sirens alone, and \(H_0 = 73.5^{+9.2}_{-7.2} \;\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}\) when combined with the bright siren GW170817. Compared to the standard LVK Fullpop-4.0 analysis, these constraints represent improvements of \(\sim29.8\%\) and \(\sim22.2\%\) in \(H_0\) uncertainty, respectively. The enhanced precision is driven by previously unmodeled features, including peaks near \(18\,M_\odot\) and \(65\,M_\odot\) as well as mass-dependent pairing transitions at \(28\,M_\odot\) and \(52\,M_\odot\). Our results demonstrate that the secondary mass function is also a key ingredient for precision standard siren cosmology.

</details>


### [76] [Late-time reconstruction of non-minimally coupled gravity with a smoothness prior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12415)
*Gen Ye,Anton Chudaykin,Camille Bonvin,Martin Kunz*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在有效场论（EFT of dark energy）框架下，对非最小耦合引力理论中的宇宙学背景和扰动动力学进行了非参数、模型无关的重建。结合多种宇宙学观测数据，发现了非最小耦合的 2.8σ 迹象，并揭示了暗能量状态方程在红移 z<0.8 处穿越幻象分界（phantom divide, w_DE=-1）的偏好，非最小耦合效应为这一穿越提供了稳定的物理解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前宇宙学模型（尤其是ΛCDM）在解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀时面临挑战，非最小耦合引力理论（non-minimally coupled theories of gravity）提供了一种可能的修正引力方案。然而，现有研究多依赖特定参数化模型，缺乏模型无关的重建方法，且需要确保重建结果的稳定性与物理自洽性。

Method: 基于暗能量有效场论（Effective Field Theory of dark energy, EFT of DE）框架，对时变宇宙学常数 Λ(t) 和非最小耦合函数 Ω(t) 进行非参数重建。引入相关平滑先验（correlated smoothness prior），将重建限制在充分光滑的函数空间内以保证稳定性。采用的数据集包括：CMB、DESI BAO、Ia型超新星、CMB-ISW透镜互相关以及DES Year 3大尺度结构 3x2pt 数据。

Result: 在 2.8σ 置信水平上发现非最小耦合存在的迹象。暗能量状态方程（equation of state, EoS）在红移 z<0.8 处呈现出穿越幻象分界（w_DE=-1）的偏好。非最小耦合效应能够稳定暗能量扰动（dark energy perturbations），从而为幻象穿越（phantom crossing）场景提供可行的物理解释。

Conclusion: 本研究为在宇宙学数据中以模型无关的方式搜寻修正引力（modified gravity）信号开辟了新的路径。非最小耦合机制为幻象分界穿越这一现象提供了自洽且稳定的理论框架，有助于加深对暗能量本质和引力修正的理解。

Abstract: We present a non-parametric, model-independent reconstruction of the cosmological background and perturbation dynamics in non-minimally coupled theories of gravity. Within the Effective Field Theory of dark energy framework, we reconstruct the time-dependent cosmological constant, $Λ(t)$, and the non-minimal coupling function, $Ω(t)$, from cosmological data. To ensure stability, we apply a correlated smoothness prior that restricts the reconstruction to the space of sufficiently smooth functions. Using CMB, DESI BAO, Type Ia supernovae, CMB-ISW lensing cross-correlations, and large-scale 3x2pt DES Year 3 data, we find a $2.8σ$ hint for a non-minimal coupling. For the dark energy equation of state, our results indicate a preference for the existence of crossing of the phantom divide, $w_{DE}=-1$, at $z<0.8$. The non-minimal coupling effect stabilizes dark energy perturbations, providing a viable physical interpretation of the phantom crossing scenario. Our work paves the way for model-agnostic searches for signatures of modified gravity in cosmological data.
