### [77] [Unveiling $f(R)$ Gravity with Void-Galaxy Cross-Correlation Multipoles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12482)
*Yue Nan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文针对Hu-Sawicki f(R)修改引力模型（MG），提出一种宇宙空洞-星系互相关函数在红移空间中的多极矩半解析计算方法，发现空洞尺度依赖的修改引力信号（单极偏差从小空洞+29.7%到大空洞+2.8%），且非线性演化将信号放大约4倍，使其能被DESI、Euclid等巡天探测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙空洞（cosmic void）为修改引力理论（如f(R)引力）所预言的标量第五力（scalar fifth force）提供低密度、屏蔽最弱的探测环境，是检验广义相对论（general relativity）的独特窗口。此前缺乏能同时考虑尺度依赖增长因子和非线性球壳动力学的半解析计算工具。

Method: 结合标量自由度（scalaron）的尺度依赖增长因子（scale-dependent growth factor）与非线性球壳动力学（nonlinear spherical shell dynamics），对Hu-Sawicki f(R)模型（n=1）红移空间中的空洞-星系互相关函数ξ^s(s,μ)进行单极、偶极和四极矩的半解析计算。该框架适用于任何能在准静态极限（quasi-static limit）下指定Geff(k,a)/G的度规f(R)理论。

Result: (1) 单极矩相对ΛCDM的偏差从大空洞（r_v=30 Mpc）的+2.8%增至小空洞（r_v=11.7 Mpc）的+29.7%（在|f_R0|=10^{-5}时），体现了与变色龙屏蔽（chameleon screening）相关的康普顿尺度标量响应（Compton-scale scalaron response），康普顿波长λ_C≈8 Mpc；(2) 非线性演化将修改引力信号放大约4倍（振幅因子𝒜_0≈4），使其落入DESI、Subaru PFS、Euclid、Roman Space Telescope等巡天的可探测范围；(3) 引力势包含有限范围汤川分量（finite-range Yukawa component），产生径向依赖的偶极特征；(4) 信号随红移减弱（标量康普顿波长收缩），但在第四阶段（Stage-IV）光谱空洞样本中仍可能被探测到。

Conclusion: 红移空间空洞-星系多极矩对空洞尺度的过渡响应、对密度/速度/第五力贡献的联合敏感性，以及空洞壳层周围的非线性放大效应，使其成为探测f(R)引力及相关非均匀暗能量（inhomogeneous dark energy）情景的有力半解析探针。

Abstract: Cosmic voids provide a low-density environment where the scalar fifth force predicted by $\fR$ modified gravity (MG) is least screened. We present a semi-analytical calculation of the monopole, dipole, and quadrupole of the void-galaxy cross-correlation function $ξ^{s}(s,μ)$ in redshift space for the Hu-Sawicki $\fR$ model ($n=1$), combining the scale-dependent growth factor from the scalaron degree of freedom with nonlinear spherical shell dynamics. The framework applies to any metric $\fR$ theory for which $\Geff(k,a)/G$ can be specified in the quasi-static limit. Our key results are: (1)~the monopole deviation from $\lcdm$ grows from $+2.8\%$ for large voids ($r_v = 30\;\Mpc$) to $+29.7\%$ for small voids ($r_v = 11.7\;\Mpc$) at $\fRz = 10^{-5}$ -- a distinctive size-dependent signature of the Compton-scale scalaron response associated with chameleon screening, with $λ_C \approx 8\;\Mpc$; (2)~nonlinear evolution amplifies the modified-gravity signal by $\mathcal{A}_0 \approx 4$, bringing it within reach of ongoing and upcoming wide-field spectroscopic surveys, such as DESI, Subaru PFS, Euclid, and the Roman Space Telescope; (3) the gravitational potential contains a finite-range Yukawa component, producing a radially dependent dipole signature that is complementary to the density and velocity multipoles; (4) the signal weakens with redshift as the scalaron Compton wavelength shrinks, but remains potentially detectable at Stage-IV spectroscopic void samples. We show that the void-scale transition in the modified-gravity response, the joint sensitivity to density, velocity, and fifth-force contributions, and the nonlinear amplification around void shells make redshift-space void-galaxy multipoles a powerful semi-analytical probe of f(R) gravity and related inhomogeneous dark energy scenarios.

### [78] [When Stochasticity Resolves into Certainty: Hidden Structure of Deterministic Motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11575)
*D. Y. Zhong*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明耗散系统中确定性运动是接触流（contact flow）的严格几何吸引子，而非统计近似；通过接触锁定定理（Contact Locking Theorem）揭示概率场指数梯度放大与刚度同步衰减之间的精确平衡，导致宏观-微观耦合指数消失，从而确定性动力学以普适时间尺度涌现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清耗散系统中确定性运动与统计描述之间的深层关系，证明确定性轨迹并非概率近似的极限结果，而是接触几何框架下的严格吸引子结构。

Method: 基于随机向量丛（stochastic vector bundles）的接触几何（contact geometry）构建含时接触势（time-dependent contact potentials），并引入精确闭包定理（exact closure theorem）确保主方程（master equation）在任意有限阶严格成立。

Result: 接触锁定定理证明概率场的指数梯度放大与刚度同步衰减精确抵消，导致有效宏观-微观耦合呈指数消失，确定性动力学以漂移场雅可比矩阵谱（drift-field Jacobian spectrum）决定的普适时间尺度涌现。受阻尼驱动的Duffing振子数值验证了该预测速率与指数收敛行为。

Conclusion: 耗散系统中的确定性运动本质上是接触流的一个严格几何吸引子，其涌现机制由接触几何的内在锁定机制而非统计近似所决定。

Abstract: We prove that deterministic motion in dissipative systems emerges as a strict geometric attractor of contact flow, not a statistical approximation. Building on the contact geometry of stochastic vector bundles, we develop time-dependent contact potentials with an exact closure theorem ensuring exact satisfaction of the master equation at any finite order. The Contact Locking Theorem shows that exponential gradient amplification of the probability field is precisely counterbalanced by synchronous stiffness decay, forcing the effective macroscopic-microscopic coupling to vanish exponentially. Deterministic dynamics therefore emerges through deterministic focusing with a universal timescale governed by the drift-field Jacobian spectrum. Validation of the damped-driven Duffing oscillator confirms the predicted rate and exponential convergence.

### [79] [A Feynman-Kac Formula for the Subcritical Ultraviolet-Renormalized Spin Boson Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11725)

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了自旋玻色子模型（spin boson Hamiltonian）的自能重整化（self-energy renormalized）版本满足费曼-卡茨公式（Feynman-Kac formula, FKF），从而将自旋处理为跳跃过程（jump process），并应用该公式证明了红外正则（infrared-regular）模型在紫外截断（ultraviolet cutoff）移除后基态（ground state）的存在性仍然保持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋玻色子模型描述了一个两态量子系统与玻色子量子场的线性耦合，是量子光学和凝聚态物理中的重要模型。此前类似FKF已被证明适用于Fröhlich极化子和Nelson模型，但自旋玻色子模型的自能重整化版本尚未建立相应的FKF，且紫外截断对基态存在性的影响需要严格分析。

Method: 通过证明自能重整化自旋玻色子哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）的费曼-卡茨公式，将自旋部分处理为跳跃过程，而玻色场仍保留在通常的玻色福克空间（Fock space）上处理。

Result: 成功建立了自能重整化自旋玻色子模型的FKF，并应用该公式证明了：对于红外正则模型，紫外截断移除后基态的存在性依然保持。

Conclusion: 该FKF为自旋玻色子系统提供了概率论处理框架，并论证了红外正则性足以保证基态在无紫外截断（no ultraviolet cutoff）极限下的存在性。

Abstract: We prove a Feynman-Kac formula (FKF) for the self-energy renormalized spin boson Hamiltonian, describing a two-state quantum system linearly coupled to a bosonic quantum field. Similar to recent FKFs for the Fröhlich polaron and the non- and semi-relativistic Nelson models, it yields a probabilistic treatment of the spin as a jump process, but treats the field on the usual bosonic Fock space. As an application, we prove that the existence of ground states for infrared-regular models persists the removal of an ultraviolet cutoff.

</details>


### [80] [A self-adjoint Fourier-type model for the iQuad wavefront sensor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11740)
*Victoria Laidlaw,Olivier Fauvarque,Alfred Miksch,Benoit Neichel,Ronny Ramlau*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了iQuad波前传感器（iQuad WFS）的完整数学框架，揭示了其与二维有限希尔伯特变换（2d finite Hilbert transform）的联系，证明了其线性算子的自伴性（self-adjoint），并提出了双iQuad结构（double iQuad WFS）以改进单一路径的缺陷，为基于模型的自适应光学（adaptive optics, AO）波前重建算法奠定理论基础。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 建立了包含前向模型（forward models）和基于Fréchet导数（Fréchet derivative）的线性化框架。揭示了iQuad WFS与二维有限希尔伯特变换之间的数学联系。提出双iQuad WFS双路径结构，结合两个旋转的iQuad WFS以抑制弱可见相位分量（poorly-seen phase components），并简化数学模型。还将调制概念（modulation）推广至iQuad WFS。

Result: 证明线性iQuad WFS算子具有自伴性，这是傅里叶型WFS中的独特性质。双iQuad结构能够有效抑制单iQuad WFS中不可见的相位分量。发现了iQuad WFS与金字塔波前传感器（pyramid wavefront sensor, PWFS）之间的相似性。

Conclusion: 该理论分析为iQuad WFS开发快速、鲁棒的基于模型波前重建算法奠定了基础，并为未来在自适应光学仪器中的应用铺平了道路。

Abstract: Advanced adaptive optics (AO) systems can use Fourier-type wavefront sensing to correct optical distortions encountered in ground-based telescopes, AO-assisted retinal imaging, and free-space optical communications (FSOC). Recently, a novel Fourier-type wavefront sensor (WFS) known as the iQuad WFS has been introduced. Its design features a focal plane tessellation with a four-quadrant phase mask (FQPM) that incorporates a $\pm π/2$ phase shift between adjacent quadrants.
  In this work, we establish a comprehensive mathematical framework for the iQuad WFS, including its forward models and linearizations based on the Fréchet derivative. We reveal a connection between the iQuad WFS and the 2d finite Hilbert transform and demonstrate that the linear iQuad WFS operator is self-adjoint - a unique property among Fourier-type WFSs. Additionally, we introduce the double iQuad WFS, a two-path configuration that combines two rotated iQuad WFSs. This design addresses the limitations of the single iQuad WFS by suppressing poorly-seen phase components. Moreover, the double setup simplifies the mathematical modeling. We also highlight iQuad similarities to the widely used pyramid wavefront sensor (PWFS). Finally, we extend the concept of modulation to the iQuad WFS, further enhancing its versatility.
  The theoretical analysis presented here lays the groundwork for the development of fast and robust model-based wavefront reconstruction algorithms for the iQuad WFS, paving the way for future applications in AO instruments.

</details>


### [81] [Local Topological Quantum Order and Spectral Gap Stability for the AKLT Models on the Hexagonal and Lieb Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12184)
*Amanda Young,Bruno Nachtergaele,Andrew Jackson*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了六角晶格（hexagonal lattice）和Lieb晶格上AKLT模型的基态满足局域拓扑量子序（LTQO）条件，进而得出在上述模型中基态之上的谱隙（spectral gap）在一般小扰动下保持稳定。这一结果建立在对Kennedy、Lieb和Tasaki提出的基态聚合物表示（polymer representation）的详细分析之上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证AKLT模型在特定晶格（六角晶格和Lieb晶格）上是否满足LTQO条件，这是理解拓扑序（topological order）稳定性的关键前提。

Method: 通过证明有限体积基态与唯一无限体积基态之间的不可区分性（indistinguishability）来建立LTQO性质。具体构建了一个递增且吸收的有限体积序列，使得任意有限体积基态期望值可被无限体积态以均匀指数速率逼近。研究基于Kennedy、Lieb和Tasaki的基态聚合物表示，并对其进行了必要修改以证明强形式的基态不可区分性。

Result: 证明了六角晶格和Lieb晶格上AKLT模型的基态满足LTQO条件；进而证明了这些模型基态之上的谱隙在一般小扰动下保持稳定。

Conclusion: AKLT模型在六角晶格和Lieb晶格上具有LTQO性质，这确保了谱隙在足够衰减的一般小扰动下具有稳定性。该方法基于对聚合物表示的精细化分析，为理解拓扑有序系统的鲁棒性提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We prove that the ground state of the AKLT models on the hexagonal lattice and the Lieb lattice satisfy the local topological quantum order (LTQO) condition. This will be a consequence of proving that the finite volume ground states are indistinguishable from a unique infinite volume ground state. Concretely, we identify a sequence of increasing and absorbing finite volumes for which any finite volume ground state expectation is well approximated by the infinite volume state with error decaying at a uniform exponential rate in the distance between the support of the observable and boundary of the finite volume. As a corollary to the LTQO property, we obtain that the spectral gap above the ground state in these models is stable under general small perturbations of sufficient decay. We prove these results by a detailed analysis of the polymer representation of the ground states state derived by Kennedy, Lieb and Tasaki (1988) with the necessary modifications required for proving the strong form of ground state indistinguishability needed for LTQO.

</details>


### [82] [Quasi-Sierpinski Structure for Uniform Load Distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12314)
*Javier Rodríguez-Cuadrado,Jesús San Martín*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种基于谢尔宾斯基三角形（Sierpinski triangle）的分形结构，通过实现基底均匀荷载分布，解决沿海城市填海造地（land reclamation）的生态破坏问题；该结构的关键在于支撑物需遵循高木函数类（Takagi class）垂直位移，从而使垂直变形与高木函数一致，水平变形与康托尔函数（Cantor function）相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 填海造地方法对现代沿海城市的开发不可或缺，但具有严重的生态破坏性。现有方法无法在支撑滨海结构的同时减轻对海洋生态系统的负面影响。

Method: 设计一种类似谢尔宾斯基三角形（Sierpinski triangle）的分形结构，依靠基底均匀荷载分布（uniform load distribution）直接坐落于海床之上。为实现均匀分布，结构的支撑物需按照高木函数类（Takagi class）中的任意函数进行垂直位移，从而使垂直变形遵循该函数类、水平变形与康托尔函数（Cantor function）相关。

Result: 该分形结构可实现基底均匀荷载分布，垂直变形与高木函数类一致，水平变形与康托尔函数相关。结构可兼容无限多种的面积与材料组合，为设计者提供高度建造灵活性（constructive flexibility）。

Conclusion: 提出的分形结构为填海造地的生态破坏问题提供了一种替代解决方案，兼顾力学性能与设计自由度。

Abstract: Land reclamation methods, indispensable for the proper development of modern coastal cities, are ecologically destructive. We present a fractal structure, similar to a Sierpinski triangle, which solves this problem by resting directly on the seabed thanks to the uniform load distribution we achieve on its base. To obtain this uniform distribution, we show that the supports of the structure must displace vertically following any function of the Takagi class. This causes the vertical deformations of the structure to follow this same class and the horizontal deformations to be related to the Cantor function. The structure works with an unlimited number of combinations of areas of its elements and materials, which gives designers a high degree of constructive flexibility.

</details>


### [83] [An analytical approach to calculating stationary PDFs for reflected random walks with an application to BESS-based ramp-rate control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12405)
*Carlos Colchero,Diego Jiménez-Arreguín,Álvaro Herrera,Jorge E. Pérez-García,Oliver Probst*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于现代概率论严格推导了反射随机游走的平稳概率密度函数（PDF）的Wiener-Hopf型积分方程，并将其应用于电池储能系统（BESS）的逆变器容量配置问题。通过构造马尔可夫核、推导第二类弗雷德霍姆积分方程并基于诺伊曼级数求解，得到了解析解；结果与数值方法及算法模拟结果一致。截断解析解可用于构建简化的工程设计规则，并为风能、太阳能等可变可再生能源（VRE）的爬坡率控制中储能系统逆变器选型提供了一般性洞见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为反射随机游走的平稳PDF建立严格的解析框架，并解决电池储能系统（battery energy storage systems, BESS）中逆变器容量配置这一实际工程问题，以支持可变可再生能源（variable renewable energy, VRE）的爬坡率控制。

Method: 包括三个步骤：(1) 构造马尔可夫核（Markov kernel）；(2) 推导BESS功率PDF的第二类弗雷德霍姆积分方程（Fredholm integral equation of the second kind）；(3) 基于诺伊曼级数（Neumann series）对该方程进行解析求解。解析结果与使用Nyström方法的数值解及基于模拟输入时间序列的算法仿真结果进行了对比验证。

Result: 解析解与Nyström数值解及算法仿真结果一致；截断解析解可用于构建简化的设计规则，为工程实践提供便利。

Conclusion: 该解析框架为BESS逆变器容量配置提供了理论依据和简化设计工具，适用于风能和太阳能等VRE源爬坡率控制场景下的储能系统选型决策。

Abstract: A Wiener-Hopf-type integral equation for the stationary PDF of a reflected random walk is derived rigorously based on modern probability theory, and an application to battery energy storage systems (BESS), specifically the sizing of the inverter, is discussed in depth. The methodological steps include the construction of a Markov kernel, the derivation of a Fredholm integral equation of the second kind for the PDF of the BESS power, and an analytical solution of the equation based on a Neumann series. The analytical results were compared against numerical solutions obtained with the Nystrom method, as well as against the results of an algorithmic simulation using simulated input time series. The use of truncated versions of the analytic solution allows for the construction of simplified design rules for the power systems practitioner. General insights into inverter sizing criteria of storage systems for ramp-rate control of variable renewable energy (VRE) sources such as wind and solar are provided.

### [84] [Large $N$ factorization of families of tensor trace-invariants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12468)
*Sylvain Carrozza,Johann Chevrier,Luca Lionni*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了大$N$极限下实高斯张量（real Gaussian tensor）与复随机张量（complex random tensor）的矩（moment）是否因子化（factorize）的问题。作者给出首个显式非因子化迹不变量（trace-invariant）例子，并建立了三个定理，刻画迹不变量在大$N$下因子化的充分条件与组合结构（树型主导配对，tree-like dominant pairings），最后将结果应用于多体量子纠缠理论中的Rényi纠缠熵（Rényi entanglement entropy）的典型期望值计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究发现，与矩阵情形不同，实高斯张量的矩在大$N$极限下一般不在连通分量（connected components）上因子化，但此前仅有非构造性证明且缺少显式反例。本文旨在填补这一空白，并系统性地探索哪些迹不变量（trace-invariant）在大量子数（large $N$）下仍然因子化，从而为量子信息等多体系统提供理论工具。

Method: 本文采用组合分析与随机张量理论相结合的方法，聚焦于Haar分布或高斯分布的复随机张量。通过构造显式反例展示非因子化行为，并提出基于树型主导配对（tree-like dominant pairings）的充分条件，进而证明满足该条件的迹不变量在大$N$下必定因子化。

Result: 主要得到三个定理：(1) 给出一个足够简单的组合上界（combinatorial bound），确保迹不变量在大$N$下因子化；(2) 证明任意兼容的迹不变量的期望值在大$N$下由树型结构主导；(3) 证明任何具有树型主导配对的迹不变量在大$N$下确实因子化。基于这些结果，证明文献中多类迹不变量满足因子化性质。

Conclusion: 本文不仅提供了首个显式非因子化复迹不变量例子，还建立了系统性的因子化判定框架。应用方面，该结果可用于计算均匀随机量子态下多体Rényi纠缠熵的典型期望值，对多体量子纠缠理论具有直接意义。

Abstract: It was recently proven that, in contrast to their matrix analogues, the moments of a real Gaussian tensor of size N do not in general factorize over their connected components in the asymptotic large N limit. While the original proof of this rather surprising result was not constructive, explicit examples of non-factorizing moments, which are expectation values of trace-invariants, have since then been discovered. We explore further aspects of this problem, with a focus on Haar-distributed (or Gaussian) complex random tensors, which are more directly relevant to quantum information. We start out by exhibiting an explicit example of non-factorizing trace-invariant, thereby filling a gap in the recent literature. We then turn to the opposite question: that of finding interesting families of trace-invariants that do in fact factorize at large N. We establish three main theorems in this regard. The first one provides a sufficient combinatorial bound ensuring large N factorization, that is also simple enough to be applicable to various cases of practical relevance. Our second main result shows that the expectation value of any compatible trace-invariant is dominated by certain tree-like combinatorial structures at large N, which we refer to as tree-like dominant pairings. Our third main theorem establishes that any trace-invariant admitting tree-like dominant pairings does actually factorize at large N. In this way, we are able to prove that various families of trace-invariants that have been previously studied in the literature do factorize at large N. We apply our findings to the theory of multipartite quantum entanglement: to any trace-invariant is associated a multipartite generalization of Rényi entanglement entropy, whose typical expectation value in the uniform random quantum state can be explicitly computed assuming large N factorization.

</details>

### [85] [The role of asymmetric time delay and its structure in 1D swarmalators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11713)
*Rommel Tchinda Djeudjo,Gourab Kumar Sar,Timoteo Carletti*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文研究带有非对称时间延迟的一维群聚振子（swarmalator）模型，揭示了延迟的**结构形式**（而非仅延迟大小）对空间-相位同步集体相图的决定性影响。非对称延迟会系统性地扩展活性π态，而对称延迟则更倾向于产生不稳定的无序态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 群聚振子（swarmalators）作为同时同步空间与相位的耦合振子类，时间延迟（time delay）普遍存在，但其结构为对称还是非对称的形式尚未得到充分关注。

Method: 研究采用一维群聚振子模型，将非对称时间延迟仅引入空间与相位动力学的自相互作用项中，从而打破了先前工作中的对称性假设。通过解析推导各集体态的稳定性边界，并结合数值模拟进行验证。

Result: 识别出异步态（async）、静态相位波（static phase wave）、静态π态（static π）和活性π态（active π）等多种集体态；推导出各态关于耦合参数和延迟的解析稳定性边界；发现非对称延迟会系统性地扩大活性π态而抑制其他有序态，与对称延迟模型相反。

Conclusion: 延迟的内部结构（非仅其大小）是决定群聚振子种群涌现集体行为的决定性因素。

Abstract: Swarmalators are a class of coupled oscillators that simultaneously synchronize in both space and phase, providing a minimal model for systems ranging from biological microswimmers to robotic swarms. Time delay is ubiquitous in such systems, arising from finite signal propagation speeds and sensory processing lags, yet its structural form, whether symmetric or asymmetric, has received little attention. Here, we study a one-dimensional swarmalator model with asymmetric time delay, in which the delay enters only the self-interaction terms of the spatial and phase dynamics, breaking the symmetry assumed in prior work. We identify various collective states such as async, static phase wave, static π, and active π, and derive analytical stability boundaries for each as a function of the coupling parameters and delay. Our analysis reveals that the asymmetric delay structure fundamentally reshapes the collective phase diagram: in particular, for the asymmetric delay models, increasing the delay systematically expands the active π state at the expense of other ordered states, in contrast to the symmetric delay model, which more strongly promotes the presence of unsteady states that are generally not well ordered. By providing closed-form stability conditions validated against numerical simulations, our work establishes that the internal structure of the delay, not merely its magnitude, is a decisive factor in determining the emergent collective behavior of swarmalator populations.

### [86] [Big Mysteries Survey: Physicists' Views on Cosmology, Black Holes, Quantum Mechanics, and Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11058)
*Niayesh Afshordi,Phil Halper,Matteo Rini,Michael Schirber*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于美国物理学会《物理杂志》开展的大规模调查“Big Mysteries Survey”，呈现了当代物理学家对宇宙学、黑洞物理、量子力学、量子引力和人择学等基本问题及争议性议题的看法。一个核心发现是，许多被公开描述为领域内“共识”的观点，在实际调查中仅得到较微弱的多数支持，或仅获相对多数而非绝对多数支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在系统性地了解当代物理学家对基础物理和争议性议题（如宇宙学、黑洞物理、量子力学、量子引力及人择巧合等）的真实看法，并检验公开宣称的“共识”与实际学界意见分布之间是否存在差距。

Method: 采用大规模问卷调查方法，通过美国物理学会（American Physical Society）的《物理杂志》（Physics Magazine）进行数据采集，调查内容涵盖宇宙学、黑洞物理、量子力学、量子引力及人择学等几个核心领域。

Result: 调查发现，若干常被公开描述为领域内“共识”（consensus）的观点，在实际数据中仅仅获得了较窄的多数支持（narrow majorities），甚至仅获得相对多数（pluralities）而非绝对多数支持。

Conclusion: 表明在当代物理学的一些基础性和争议性议题上，公开宣称的“共识”可能夸大了学界的实际一致程度，学界内部对这些问题的意见分布比通常认为的更加多元。

Abstract: We present results from the Big Mysteries Survey, a large-scale survey conducted through the American Physical Society's Physics Magazine on foundational and controversial topics in contemporary physics. The survey provides a snapshot of physicists' views on issues in cosmology, black-hole physics, quantum mechanics, quantum gravity, and anthropic coincidences. A central finding is that several positions often described publicly as field-wide ``consensus'' views are, in practice, supported by much narrower majorities or by pluralities rather than majorities.

### [87] [The mean-field theory of superfluid-superconducting vortex states in the outer core of neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11216)
*Dmitry Kobyakov*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 该论文扩展了已有的平均场（mean-field）理论，以研究在质子超导临界温度与中子超流临界温度不等（$T_{cp}\neq T_{cn}$）条件下的超流-超导涡旋态（superfluid-superconducting vortex states），发现中子涡旋的伦敦近似（London's approximation）在外核心区域完全失效，而质子涡旋的伦敦近似仅限于壳-核过渡附近区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在致密天体物理中，中子星内部的超流中子和超导质子共存，但两者的临界温度（$T_{c\alpha}$）通常不相等（$T_{cp}\neq T_{cn}$）。现有平均场理论未能处理这种不等温情形，因此需要发展更一般的理论框架来表征任意压强下的涡旋态。

Method: 将已有的平均场理论扩展至$T_{cp}\neq T_{cn}$的情形；基于有效手征场论（effective chiral field theory）定量建立配对能隙（pairing gap）$\Delta_{\alpha0}$随压强的依赖关系，并利用弱耦合结果$T_{c\alpha}\approx0.57\Delta_{\alpha0}$关联临界温度与能隙；类比纯超导体假定热力学磁场与约化温度$T/T_{cp}$呈二次关系；利用纯中子物质的多体近似推断能隙$\Delta_{\alpha T}$对$T/T_{c\alpha}$的依赖。

Result: 构建了一个经验性的$T/T_{c\alpha}$依赖关系以描述平均场中凝聚能与磁能的相互作用；发现超流熵引（superfluid entrainment）会增大中子涡旋核心尺寸并减小有效磁穿透深度（magnetic penetration depth）；中子涡旋核心的尺寸大于外核心区域的磁穿透深度。

Conclusion: 中子涡旋的伦敦近似在整个外核心区域均不成立，质子涡旋的伦敦近似仅适用于壳-核过渡附近；所发展的平均场理论为研究涡旋微观结构、角动量、磁化强度以及涡旋-磁通管相互作用能提供了理论途径。

Abstract: Purpose: Characterize superfluid-superconducting vortex states at arbitrary pressures with $T_{cp}\neq T_{cn}$, assuming both proton and neutron mean-fields are formed by spin-0 Cooper pairs.
  Method: The existing mean-field theory is extended to account for $T_{cp}\neq T_{cn}$. The pressure dependence of the pairing gap energy $Δ_{\alpha0}$ is quantitatively established on the basis of the effective chiral field theory. To link $T_{cα}$ with $Δ_{\alpha0}$, I use the weak-coupling result $T_{cα}\approx0.57Δ_{\alpha0}$. A quadratic scaled-temperature ($T/T_{cp}$) dependence of the thermodynamic magnetic field is postulated in analogy with pure superconductors. The $T/T_{cα}$-dependence of the gap $Δ_{αT}$ is inferred from the many-body approximations for the pure neutron matter.
  Results: An empirical $T/T_{cα}$-dependence for the mean-field is constructed to account for the interplay between the condensation and the magnetic energies. The superfluid entrainment is found to increase the size of the vortex core and to decrease the effective magnetic penetration depth. The size of the neutron vortex core is found to be larger than the magnetic penetration depth in the outer core.
  Conclusions: The usual approximation of infinitely thin vortex line (the London's approximation) for the neutron vortex is found to be irrelevant in the entire outer core and for the proton vortex is found to be limited to vicinity of the crust-core transition. The developed mean-field theory paves the way to study the vortex microscopic structure, the angular momentum, the magnetization and the vortex-fluxtube interaction energy.

### [88] [Time-dependent pore-network modelling of Ostwald ripening in porous media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10955)
*Ademola Isaac Adebimpe,Sajjad Foroughi,Branko Bijeljic,Martin J. Blunt*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个时间依赖的孔隙网络模型（pore-network model），耦合水相瞬态传质、毛细压力异质性和真实孔喉几何，以捕捉多孔介质中奥斯特瓦尔德熟化（Ostwald ripening）过程中气团的动态演化。模型应用于Bentheimer砂岩，再现了驱替与重排过程，并预测了残余气饱和度、相对渗透率和毛细压力，适用于氢气、天然气和二氧化碳的地下储存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多孔介质中残余气团的奥斯特瓦尔德熟化过程涉及复杂的气相演化，传统平衡渗流模型无法完整描述这一动态行为。本文旨在建立一个能够捕捉毛细压力非平衡演化、气团收缩与生长事件并存以及孔隙尺度流体构型变化的时间依赖模型。

Method: 构建了一个耦合水相瞬态传质、毛细压力异质性和真实孔喉几何的时间依赖孔隙网络模型。模型应用于Bentheimer砂岩，模拟吸水（imbibition）至残余气饱和度后的奥斯特瓦尔德熟化过程，追踪事件统计、毛细压力均衡、气团体积分布和空间饱和度剖面，持续48小时。

Result: 体积加权平均毛细压力保持恒定，但数加权平均气团压力快速下降，气团尺寸分布向数量更少、体积更大的气团（ganglia）演化。孔喉占据分析表明气体持续被困在较大的孔隙空间中。由于生长通过排水（drainage）进行，孔隙尺度流体构型与仅允许吸水事件的平衡无捕获渗流模型预测不同。

Conclusion: 该模型成功再现了实验室时间尺度下的驱替和气团重排过程，并可进一步预测现场尺度下的残余气饱和度、相对渗透率和毛细压力，为氢气、天然气和二氧化碳地下储存提供理论支持。

Abstract: We present a time-dependent pore-network model that couples transient mass transfer in the aqueous phase, capillary pressure heterogeneity, and realistic pore-throat geometries to capture the dynamic evolution of gas clusters during Ostwald ripening in porous media. The model is applied to Bentheimer sandstone to study Ostwald ripening after imbibition to residual gas saturation. Both imbibition (shrinkage) and drainage (growth) events occur as the local capillary pressure in trapped gas clusters approaches equilibrium. The model tracks event statistics, capillary pressure equilibration, cluster volume distributions, and spatial saturation profiles over 48 hours. While the volume-weighted average capillary pressure is constant, there is a rapid initial decline in average number-weighted cluster pressure and a shift in cluster size distributions toward fewer, larger ganglia, consistent with pore-scale imaging studies. Pore and throat occupancy analysis reveal persistent gas trapping in larger pore spaces. Since growth is by drainage, the pore-scale configuration of fluid is different from that predicted by an equilibrium percolation-without-trapping model that only allows imbibition events. The model reproduces displacement and ganglion rearrangement during time-limited laboratory experiments, and can then provide predictions of trapped saturation, relative permeability and capillary pressure under field-scale conditions with application to hydrogen, natural gas and carbon dioxide storage in the subsurface.

</details>


### [89] [A Guide to Fully Characterize the Fracture Properties of Cementitious Materials from Simple Experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10961)
*Subhrangsu Saha,Bruce J. Moore,Ben Manaugh,Jeffery R. Roesler,Oscar Lopez-Pamies*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一套由三个简单实验组成的测试方案，分别测量水泥基材料的弹性、强度和断裂韧性三个宏观材料属性，并验证这些参数足以预测任意结构在单调准静态加载下裂缝的成核与扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于弹性脆性材料断裂成核与扩展的最新理解，需要对水泥基材料中裂缝何时何地成核与扩展的三个宏观材料属性进行测量。

Method: 首先，通过圆柱试件的单轴压缩实验提取弹性模量（Young's modulus）和泊松比（Poisson's ratio）以及单轴抗压强度。其次，采用平板压头的巴西劈裂实验（Brazilian fracture test）确定单轴抗拉强度，进而通过插值（如Drucker-Prager拟合）估计材料的强度面。最后，通过带缺口立方体的楔形劈裂实验（wedge split test）获取断裂韧性（fracture toughness）。

Result: 通过将实验所得参数与3D打印砂浆梁的四点及三点弯曲实验（包括有缺口和无缺口）进行直接对比，验证了所提出的弹性、强度和韧性参数足以预测水泥基材料在任意单调准静态加载下裂缝的成核与扩展。

Conclusion: 该套简单实验获取的材料参数在尺度分离（separation of length scales）前提下，可推广用于任意水泥基材料结构在单调准静态加载条件下的断裂预测。

Abstract: Guided by recent advances in the understanding of nucleation and propagation of fracture in elastic brittle materials, this paper proposes a suite of three simple experiments that permit the measurement of the three macroscopic material properties governing when and where cracks nucleate and propagate in structures made of cementitious materials that are subjected to arbitrary monotonic quasi-static loading conditions. The first experiment is that of the uniaxial compression of a cylindrical specimen, which enables the extraction of the elastic properties -- namely, the Young's modulus and Poisson's ratio -- as well as the uniaxial compressive strength. The second experiment is the Brazilian fracture test, performed with flat platens on a material disk to determine the uniaxial tensile strength. Having knowledge of the uniaxial compressive and uniaxial tensile strengths then allows for the estimation of the strength surface of the material via interpolation (e.g., a Drucker-Prager fit). Finally, the third experiment is the wedge split test on a notched cube, which yields the fracture toughness. We demonstrate by means of direct comparisons with four-point and three-point bending tests on both unnotched and notched beams made of a 3D-printable mortar mixture that the elasticity, strength, and toughness properties obtained from the proposed tests are sufficient to predict the nucleation and propagation of fracture for any structure (granted separation of length scales) made of cementitious materials under any monotonic quasi-static loading condition.

</details>


### [90] [Nano-Clay-Stabilized Water-in-Oil Colloidal Pickering Emulsions as Thixotropic Lubricant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11004)
*Arun Kumar,Rahul Yadav,Yogesh M. Joshi,Manjesh K. Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

Method: 以葵花籽油为基液，采用纳米有机粘土（Garamite 1958）稳定制备触变性水包油Pickering乳液；系统考察该乳液体系的流变特性（屈服应力、剪切稀化、触变性）和摩擦学性能（钢-钢界面高接触压力下，对比干燥、水润滑和油润滑条件）。

Conclusion: 优异性能归因于触变性（thixotropy）、各向异性纳米粘土形貌（anisotropic nanoclay morphology）和稳定液滴包覆（stable droplet armoring）的协同效应，形成强健且自适应的界面膜。本研究通过关联微观结构与流变学及摩擦学性能，推进了对金属摩擦系统中Pickering乳液的理解，有助于设计高性能、智能且生态友好的金属润滑剂。

Abstract: The limitations of conventional mineral oil-based lubricants motivate the development of environmentally benign emulsions capable of providing lubrication and heat dissipation in demanding applications. In this study, nano-organoclay (Garamite 1958)-stabilized thixotropic water-in-oil Pickering emulsions are developed using sunflower oil as the base. The rheological and tribological properties of the emulsion system are systematically examined. Rheological findings reveal a pronounced increase in yield stress, shear thinning and thixotropic behavior on increasing Garamite loading percentage in the emulsion. The tribological performance is assessed against dry, water, and oil-lubricated conditions for a steel-steel interface under high contact pressure. The findings indicate that the tribological performance is significantly influenced by the microstructure and thixotropic behavior of the emulsions. The emulsion with the optimal nano-clay concentration demonstrates approximately 41\% and 84\% lower friction and approximately 80\% and 96\% lower wear than oil and water, respectively. The emulsion exhibits sensitivity to the sliding direction and displays load-responsive friction behavior with a memory effect owing to the reversible structuring of the clay-droplet network. This superior performance is attributed to the combined effects of thixotropy, anisotropic nanoclay morphology, and stable droplet armoring, which form a robust and adaptive interfacial film. This study advances the understanding of Pickering emulsions in metallic tribosystems by correlating the microstructure and rheology with tribological performance, thereby facilitating the design of high-performance, smart, and eco-conscious lubricants for metallic systems.

*Jacopo Bilotto,Arnav Singhal,Joaquin Garcia-Suarez,Gaëtan Cortes,Lucas Fourel,Jean-François Molinari*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于反向设计的摩擦学超界面（tribological metainterfaces）框架，通过结合可微接触力学引擎、神经网络和二次优化器，利用非标准形貌实现可编程的静态摩擦行为，仅需少量微凸起即可复现复杂摩擦定律，并经边界元法（BEM）严格验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 该框架仅需单元胞中的少量微凸起即可自动发现并生成能复现复杂目标摩擦定律的非标准表面形貌。预测的设计结果经高保真边界元法（Boundary Element Method, BEM）仿真严格验证，证实了其有效性和准确性。

Conclusion: 该框架桥接了数据驱动优化与严格物理建模，提供了一条尺度不变（scale-invariant）的路径，用于发现功能性摩擦学表面，为软体机器人、触觉及精密夹持等领域的界面摩擦编程开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Programming the static friction of mechanical interfaces is critical for soft robotics, haptics, and precision gripping. Static friction is governed by the real contact area, and standard rough surfaces exhibit a linear area-load scaling inherent to classical Archard and Greenwood-Williamson models, severely restricting their functional range. Here, we propose a framework for the inverse design of tribological metainterfaces engineered for programmable contact behaviors. By utilizing general axisymmetric asperities, we unlock nonlinear macroscopic responses unattainable by standard Hertzian contacts. To solve the inverse problem, we embed a fully differentiable contact mechanics engine within a neural network and a quadratic optimizer. We leverage regularized physical gradients to automatically discover non-standard topographies that reproduce complex target friction laws, with only a few asperities in unit cells. The predicted designs are strictly validated against high-fidelity Boundary Element Method (BEM) simulations. This framework bridges data-driven optimization and rigorous physics, offering a scale-invariant pathway for discovering functional tribological surfaces.

Abstract: The rheology of phase-separated condensates plays a central role in applications spanning advanced materials design and cellular processes, yet quantitative characterization of their viscoelasticity remains challenging due to the limitations of existing microrheological methods that require tracer particles or mechanical contact. Here, we establish tracer-free and contactless acoustic microrheometry as a versatile platform for quantifying the frequency-dependent complex shear modulus of single microscale condensates over 0.01-10 Hz. Using spatiotemporally controlled acoustic radiation force generated within a micro-acoustic resonator, this method deforms condensates for creep-recovery and oscillatory viscoelastic measurements.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: A paradigm for the study of wrinkling in elastic sheet is the Lamé configuration, in which azimuthal wrinkles form in an annular sheet subjected to tensile loads at both edges. Since wrinkles are spatially extended, this instability provides a mechanism for stress transmission over long distances. A natural extension of this problem is wrinkling in sheets with multiple holes or broken symmetry. Here, we investigate tension-induced wrinkling in thin elastic sheets containing two circular holes by combining analytical modeling and experiments. The pre-buckled state is solved analytically using bipolar coordinates, enabling identification of the wrinkling threshold as a function of the distance between the two holes. Near-threshold wrinkling and interactions between wrinkles are analyzed, and we validate our theoretical predictions against experimental observations obtained through video imaging of spin-coated polystyrene sheets floating on liquid surfaces with controlled surface tension. Our results demonstrate that geometric symmetry breaking, such as the presence of a second hole, strongly influences wrinkle nucleation, orientation, and spatial extent. Beyond mechanics, these findings might provide a simple mechanism for cellular mechanosensing, where force transmission is amplified by mechanical instabilities.

Here we combine solid-state NMR and Small Angle Neutron Scattering to unravel the structure and dynamics of PEGDA hydrogels containing added PEG chains of various concentrations. When plotting the sample permeability, K, as a function the specific surface of the PEGDA heterogeneities we obtain a master curve, showing that the heterogeneity of the PEGDA matrix controls the permeability of the sample. ### [95] [Cell divisions suppress dynamical correlations in solid tissues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12109)
*Ali Tahaei,Ahandeep Manna,Marko Popović*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过二维弹塑性模型（elastoplastic model）研究细胞分裂作为主动塑性事件（active plastic events）对组织集体动力学的影响，发现细胞分裂虽在准静态极限下维持边缘稳定性（marginal stability），但强烈抑制了系统尺度的雪崩式重排（system-spanning avalanches），该抑制源于能量平衡：细胞分裂注入的能量在屈服应力（yield stress）以下驱动剪切流，同时为重排提供有限预算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发展中的组织（developing tissues）通过细胞分裂和重排持续重塑，同时维持力学连贯性，类似于非晶态固体（amorphous solids）。被动非晶态固体中局部重排可通过长程弹性相互作用引发系统尺度的雪崩。但细胞分裂独立于局部力学稳定性产生应力和重排事件，因此是否应预期类似的集体动力学尚不明确。

Method: 采用二维弹塑性模型（two-dimensional elastoplastic model），将细胞分裂处理为主动塑性事件（active plastic events），并研究该模型在准静态极限下的力学行为与重排动力学。

Result: 细胞分裂使组织在被动屈服应力（passive yield stress）以下流体化，但保留了准静态极限下的边缘稳定性。然而，与被动非晶态固体不同，细胞分裂强烈抑制了系统尺度的雪崩式细胞重排。该抑制源于能量平衡：细胞分裂注入的能量使组织在屈服应力以下产生剪切流，同时为重排提供了有限预算。

Conclusion: 增殖中的组织（proliferating tissues）在结构上表现出边缘非晶态固体（marginal amorphous solids）的特征，但与被动非晶态固体相比，动力学相关性（correlations in dynamics）的尺度要短得多。

Abstract: Developing tissues often maintain mechanical coherence while continuously remodeling through cellular processes such as cell divisions and rearrangements. In this way, they are an example of amorphous solids. In passive amorphous solids, local rearrangements can trigger one another through long-ranged elastic interactions, leading to system-spanning avalanches near yielding. Whether similar collective dynamics should be expected in living tissues is unclear, because cell divisions generate stress and remodeling events independently of local mechanical stability. Here, we address this question using a two-dimensional elastoplastic model in which cell divisions are treated as active plastic events. We find that while cell divisions fluidize the tissue below the passive yield stress, but preserve the marginal stability in the quasistatic limit. However, they also strongly suppress the system-spanning avalanches of cell rearrangements, in constrast with the expected behavior in passive amorphous solids. Finally, we show that the avalanche supression originates from the energy balance in the system. Namely, the energy injected by cell divisions allows for shear flow below the yield stress, but also provides a finite budget for rearrangements. These results suggest that proliferating tissues display the structural hallmarks of marginal amorphous solids while exhibiting much shorter-ranged correlations in dynamics, compared to passive amorphous solids.

### [96] [Following the thread: surface and bulk solvent migration in silicone elastomers from local volumetric swelling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12125)
*Chenzhuo Li,Tom Beyeler,Marc Antonio Chalhoub,John M. Kolinski*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过原位三维时空测量，研究了聚二甲基硅氧烷（PDMS）网络在自由溶胀和弯曲构型下的溶剂扩散动力学，发现通量受限的界面边界条件（flux-limited interfacial boundary condition）修正了标准分析中数量级级别的扩散率低估，并验证了Flory-Rehner理论需引入有效有限可扩展性修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文首先对聚二甲基硅氧烷（PDMS）网络与硅油体系进行原位三维时空测量，探测自由溶胀过程中的基线扩散动力学（diffusion kinetics）；随后在弯曲构型下研究三种材料制备状态（as-prepared、mobile-phase-free、fully swollen）中的溶剂迁移，并结合力松弛数据进行比较。

Result: 测量识别出通量受限的界面边界条件，推翻了经典的完全排液（fully drained）假设，修正了标准体相分析中扩散率（diffusivity）被低估一个数量级的问题。溶胀平衡可由经有效有限可扩展性（finite extensibility）修正的Flory-Rehner理论准确描述。弯曲实验中，as-prepared和mobile-phase-free样品无明显体积变化或力松弛，但原位测量直接分辨出拉伸侧膨胀和压缩侧收缩，有效扩散率与力松弛数据一致。

Conclusion: 这些测量严格标定了聚合物网络中的溶剂扩散率，强调了明确界面边界条件的重要性，并为多孔弹性聚合物和地质材料中的力学与工程问题提供了新的理解。

Abstract: Poroelastic materials, consisting of a permeable solid matrix infiltrated with fluid, are ubiquitous in natural and engineering contexts. In poroelastic polymer solids, the elastic matrix swells to equilibrium when immersed in a solvent bath; thus, the network elasticity couples to the solvent transport. Despite the ubiquity and importance of poroelastic theory in describing phenomena as diverse as earthquakes and biological tissues, there is a paucity of experimental data that probe the local network response to controlled stress and solvent boundary conditions. Here, we first probe the baseline diffusion kinetics of a polymeric solvent during free swelling of a polydimethylsiloxane (PDMS) network with well-characterized silicone oils. In situ 3D spatiotemporal measurements identify a flux-limited interfacial boundary condition, contradicting the canonical fully drained assumption. This correction eliminates an order-of-magnitude underestimation of diffusivity in standard bulk analysis. The swelling equilibrium is accurately captured by a Flory-Rehner theory that requires modification to include the effective finite extensibility of the filled network. Solvent migration is then studied using a bending configuration for three material preparations: as-prepared, mobile-phase-free, and fully swollen in silicone oils. The as-prepared and mobile-phase-free beams show no discernible volumetric change or force relaxation, whereas local in situ measurements directly resolve tensile-side dilation and compressive-side contraction, yielding the effective diffusivities in agreement with the force-relaxation data. These measurements rigorously benchmark solvent diffusivity in polymer networks, underscoring the importance of unambiguous interfacial boundary conditions and shedding light on mechanics and engineering across poroelastic polymers and geomaterials.

### [97] [Morphology-resolved stress contributions in sheared wet granular materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12152)
*Ahmad Awdi,Camille Chateau,Coumba Niang,Patrick Aimedieu,Jean-Noël Roux,Abdoulaye Fall*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过三维X射线显微断层成像（3D X-ray microtomography）结合流变测量，在颗粒尺度上重构了非饱和湿颗粒材料中毛细应力（capillary stress）的形态学解析。研究发现剪切局部化（shear localization）主导液相再分布：毛细桥（capillary bridges）均匀分布，而高阶液簇（higher-order morphologies）通过剪切驱动聚并机制在剪切带下边界累积；尽管存在空间局域化，简单的两颗粒桥贡献了各向同性毛细压力的绝大部分（约85%），而复杂液簇对整体内聚力贡献微弱。将形态学解析的毛细压力纳入有效应力（effective-stress）框架，无需可调参数即可定性复现整个实验液体含量范围内的宏观摩擦系数，从而在液桥形态与湿颗粒材料的流变学（rheology）之间建立了预测性的微观-宏观关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 湿颗粒材料（wet granular materials）中毛细力（capillary forces）对宏观力学行为具有决定性影响，但现有理论缺乏对液相形态（liquid morphology）空间分布及其与剪切局域化相互作用的微观定量理解。本文旨在建立液桥形态（从简单毛细桥到高阶簇团）与宏观摩擦系数之间的微观-宏观预测框架。

Method: 采用三维X射线显微断层成像（3D X-ray microtomography）耦合流变测量（rheometric measurements），在颗粒尺度上对毛细应力进行形态学解析重构。将液相域自动分类为毛细桥、二聚体（dimers）、三聚体（trimers）及更大簇团，并追踪其空间组织随剪切变形和液体含量的演变。

Result: 剪切局部化（shear localization）是液相重分布的主控机制：毛细桥保持均匀分布，而高阶液簇通过剪切驱动聚并（shear-driven coalescence）在剪切带下边界累积。在液固体积比ε=0.05时，简单两颗粒桥贡献约85%的各向同性毛细压力（isotropic capillary pressure），复杂液簇对内聚力贡献微弱。基于形态学解析毛细压力的有效应力框架，无需可调参数即可定性复现全部液体含量范围内的宏观摩擦系数。

Conclusion: 本研究在液桥形态与湿颗粒材料流变学之间建立了预测性的微观-宏观关联（micro–macro link）。形态学解析的毛细压力可有效纳入有效应力框架，为理解非饱和颗粒介质的力学行为提供了无需经验参数的定量途径。

Abstract: Three-dimensional X-ray microtomography, coupled to rheometric measurements, enables a morphology-resolved reconstruction of capillary stresses at the grain scale in unsaturated wet granular materials. Liquid domains are automatically classified into capillary bridges, dimers, trimers, and larger clusters, and their spatial organization is tracked as a function of shear deformation and liquid content. We show that shear localization governs the redistribution of the liquid phase: capillary bridges remain uniformly distributed throughout the sample, while higher-order morphologies accumulate preferentially near the lower boundary of the shear-zone through a shear-driven coalescence mechanism. Despite this spatial localization, simple two-grain bridges generate the dominant contribution to the isotropic capillary pressure, accounting for nearly 85\% of the total at liquid-to-solid volume ratio $ε= 0.05$, whereas more complex liquid clusters contribute only weakly to the overall cohesion. Incorporating the morphology-resolved capillary pressure into an effective-stress framework qualitatively reproduces the macroscopic friction coefficient across the full range of investigated liquid contents, without adjustable parameters. These results establish a predictive micro--macro link between liquid morphology and the rheology of wet granular materials.

</details>


### [98] [Variational approach to droplet motion on uneven solid surfaces, including contact line dynamics and evaporation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12393)
*Gyula I Tóth,David N Sibley,Agnes J Bokányi-Tóth,Dmitri Tseluiko,Andrew J Archer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文展示了如何将凹凸表面上液膜与液滴的动力学（含接触线动力学及蒸发/冷凝效应）纳入由Onsager变分原理（Onsager's variational principle）生成的变分动力学框架，并应用于研究接触线动力学、液滴钉扎与滑移等现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有液膜与液滴在非均匀表面上的动力学描述方法复杂，且难以统一处理接触线运动、蒸发/冷凝等关键效应；需要一个能够自然包含系统平衡性质的变分框架来生成动力学方程。

Method: 基于Onsager变分原理（Onsager's variational principle），在等温过阻尼动力学（isothermal overdamped-dynamics）极限下，将液膜与液滴的动力学方程构建为变分动力学（variational dynamics），从系统自由能（free energy）出发导出方程。

Result: 该方法成功重现了关于接触线动力学的若干已有经典结果，并应用于研究液滴在倾斜波纹表面上的钉扎（pinning）与滑移（sliding）行为。

Conclusion: 该变分方法能够自然整合系统的正确平衡性质，从而为液滴与液膜在凹凸表面上的复杂动力学提供统一的理论框架。

Abstract: We show how dynamical equations for liquid films and drops on uneven surfaces, including contact line dynamics and evaporation/condensation effects, may be formulated as a variational dynamics, generated via Onsager's variational principle. The theory applies in the isothermal overdamped-dynamics limit. We apply this general approach to obtain several well-known results on contact line dynamics and to study drops pinning and sliding on inclined corrugated surfaces. This approach constructs the dynamical equations starting from the free energy of the system and therefore has the advantage that it naturally incorporates the correct equilibrium properties.

</details>


### [99] [Fluctuation spectra of embryonic cell-cell interfaces reveal inverse-square scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12402)
*Brian Huynh,Shinuo Weng,José Alvarado*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过对非洲爪蟾（Xenopus）胚胎组织外植体进行细胞-细胞连接横向波动的谱分析，发现波动功率谱的空间和时间标度行为分别服从 ~q⁻² 和 ~f⁻² 的幂律关系，与张力主导下的Helfrich哈密顿量（Helfrich Hamiltonian）和过阻尼膜动力学（overdamped dynamics）预测一致，且降低肌动球蛋白收缩性（actomyosin contractility）未显著改变标度指数。该工作为张力承载组织的定量研究建立了基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组织尺度的形状变化由细胞内力的集合驱动，但在这些情境下测量力仍然是一个困难挑战。本研究旨在通过谱分析（spectral analysis）方法对胚胎组织中的细胞-细胞连接波动进行定量刻画，以建立一种可测量的力相关物理特性。

Method: 研究开发了一套图像分析流程，从时间序列共聚焦显微影片中提取细胞-细胞连接的横向波动振幅轮廓 u(x,t)，并计算了二维时空功率谱（spatiotemporal power spectra）。同时，通过低剂量blebbistatin或latrunculin B药理学降低肌动球蛋白收缩性，观察其对标度指数的影响。

Result: 观测到平均平方波动功率谱呈现幂律标度（power-law scaling）：空间谱 ⟨u_q²⟩ ~ q⁻²，时间谱 ⟨u_f²⟩ ~ f⁻²。空间标度与Helfrich哈密顿量的预测一致，时间标度与过阻尼膜动力学一致，两者均处于张力主导区域（tension-dominated regime）。药理学降低肌动球蛋白收缩性未显著改变任一标度指数。

Conclusion: 简单的张力主导膜模型足以描述横向连接动力学，尽管这些系统具有活性和耦合性质。该研究为张力承载组织的未来研究建立了定量基线，并推动针对多细胞系统的物理模型发展。

Abstract: Tissue-scale shape changes are driven by ensembles of intracellular forces. However measuring force in these contexts remains a difficult challenge. Here we perform spectral analysis of transverse fluctuations of cell-cell junctions in \emph{Xenopus} embryonic tissue explants undergoing convergent extension. We developed an image analysis pipeline to extract fluctuation amplitude profiles $u(x,t)$ from time-lapse confocal movies and computed two-dimensional spatiotemporal power spectra. We observe power-law scaling of mean-squared fluctuation power spectra consistent with $\langle u_q^2 \rangle \sim q^{-2}$ and $\langle u_f^2 \rangle \sim f^{-2}$. The spatial scaling agrees with predictions from the Helfrich Hamiltonian, and the temporal scaling agrees with overdamped dynamics of a fluctuating membrane, both in the tension-dominated regime. Pharmacological reduction of actomyosin contractility (via low-dose blebbistatin or latrunculin B) did not significantly alter either scaling exponent. Our results provide an early empirical characterization of junction fluctuation spectra in an actively shape-changing tissue. Simple tension-dominated membrane models appear sufficient to describe transverse junction dynamics despite their active and coupled nature. This work establishes a quantitative baseline for future studies of tension-bearing tissues and motivates the development of physical models specific to multicellular systems.

</details>


### [100] [Designing Coulombic Contact Interactions between Polarizable Particles through Asymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12489)
*Yanyu Duan,Zecheng Gan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过理论推导和数值模拟证明，通过联合调控尺寸、电荷和介电不对称性，可以消除极化粒子间的接触静电相互作用，使其退化为纯库仑形式，为可控自组装和材料设计提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极化粒子体系（如带电胶体、极化离子、生物分子组装体和软纳米材料）中，介电失配（dielectric mismatch）和几何奇点（geometric singularity）会放大极化效应（polarization effects），导致接触静电相互作用显著偏离库仑行为，增加了理解和调控这类体系的复杂性。

Method: 以带电介电球（charged dielectric spheres）为模型体系，扩展近期发展的镜像电荷公式（image-charge formula）至接触介电球情形，推导出接触相互作用退化为裸库仑形式的解析条件；通过精确两球计算验证接触设计规则（contact design rules），并利用多体分子动力学（many-body molecular dynamics）模拟检验体系的自组装行为。

Result: 解析推导给出了接触相互作用简化为裸库仑形式的条件；两球精确计算验证了设计规则，相对误差低于3%；多体分子动力学模拟表明，满足两体规则的体系自组装形成的结构与纯库仑参考体系高度吻合。

Conclusion: 不对称性（asymmetry）可作为一种将接触处的静电复杂性转化为库仑简单性的有效路径，对可控自组装和材料设计具有重要启示。

Abstract: Polarizable particle systems, including charged colloids, polarizable ions, biomolecular assemblies, and soft nanomaterials, can exhibit contact electrostatic interactions that depart strongly from Coulomb behavior when dielectric mismatch and geometric singularities amplify polarization effects. Here we use charged dielectric spheres as a model system and show that these polarization contributions can be canceled by jointly tuning size, charge, and dielectric asymmetries. By extending a recently developed image-charge formula to contacting dielectric spheres, we derive analytical conditions under which the contact interaction reduces to the bare Coulomb form. Accurate two-sphere calculations validate the resulting contact design rules with relative errors below $3\%$. Strikingly, many-body molecular dynamics simulations reveal that systems satisfying these two-body rules self-assemble into structures that closely match their pure Coulomb references. These results establish asymmetry as a route for turning electrostatic complexity into Coulombic simplicity at contact, with implications for controlled self-assembly and materials design.

</details>

### [101] [Homogenization of rod-like metamaterials as a special Cosserat rod](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10952)
*Vinayak,Ajeet Kumar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种方法，通过将杆状超材料（rod-like metamaterials）在宏观上均匀化为连续介质杆（continuum rod），利用几何精确的Cosserat杆理论（geometrically exact special Cosserat rod theory）获取其非线性本构响应（nonlinear constitutive response），并通过螺旋周期性边界条件（helically periodic boundary condition）将问题简化为微观结构单元（RVE）的分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 杆状超材料是通过在单一方向上周期性组装微结构单元（杆件网络）而获得的结构。为了准确描述这种结构在宏观尺度上的大变形非线性力学行为，需要建立有效的均匀化（homogenization）方法，将微观结构信息映射到宏观连续介质模型上。

Method: 采用几何精确的Cosserat杆理论同时在微观和宏观尺度对杆件进行建模；假设宏观尺度下超材料沿弧长均匀应变，将完整结构问题简化为微观结构单元在螺旋周期性边界条件下的边值问题；基于变分框架（variational setting）求解存在杆件关节约束的微观问题，并推导宏观均匀化杆的应力合力（internal contact force and moment）及刚度表达式。

Result: 通过多种微观结构单元（RVE）的数值算例验证了方法：简单方形和十字形RVE的结果与已有文献一致；含螺旋杆件的方形RVE可应用于人工肌肉材料；最终实现了对拉胀管状超材料（auxetic tubular metamaterials）的均匀化。

Conclusion: 所提方法能够通过调节RVE的设计参数来获得期望的宏观响应，从而为杆状超材料的力学性能设计提供理论工具。

Abstract: Rod-like metamaterials are the structures that are obtained by periodically assembling its microstructural unit (network of rods) in just one direction. In this work, we present a scheme for obtaining the nonlinear constitutive response of such structures when homogenized macroscopically as a continuum rod. To capture accurately arbitrary and large deformation, the geometrically exact special Cosserat rod theory is used for modeling the rod at both micro and macro scales. By assuming the metamaterial structure to be strained uniformly (at macroscale) along its arc length, the full structure problem is reduced to just that of its microstructural unit but subjected to helically periodic boundary condition. The microscale problem, consisting of a network of rods and formulated in a variational setting, is solved in the presence of rod joint constraints and helically periodic boundary conditions. The expressions for the macroscale/homogenized rod's stress resultants (internal contact force and moment) and stiffnesses are then obtained. Finally, several numerical examples having different microstructural units/RVEs are presented to demonstrate our method. We start with simpler square and cross RVEs to validate our results with the existing literature. We then take up more complex RVEs such as square RVEs having helical constituent rods which have application as artificial muscle material and eventually we work on the homogenization of auxetic tubular metamaterials. We show how various design parameters of these RVEs can be tuned to obtain the desired macroscopic response.

</details>


### [102] [Adamantane plasma polymers: fluorine-free vacuum-processable triboelectric thin films for all-triboelectric nanogenerator configurations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11052)
*Gloria P. Moreno-Martinez,Fernando Nunez-Galvez,Hari Krishna Mishra,Triana Czermak,Xabier Garcia-Casas,Vanda Cristina Godinho,Bernd Wicklein,Juan Carlos Sanchez-Lopez,Javier Ferrer,Isabel Montero,Juan Ramon Sanchez-Valencia,Andris Sutka,Francisco Aparicio,Angel Barranco,Ana Borras*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于金刚烷（adamantane）等离子体聚合层的双价摩擦电表面，该表面无需添加或功能化处理，仅通过调控合成条件即可同时表现出正摩擦电（tribopositive）和负摩擦电（tribonegative）特性，并在多种固-固、固-液及混合压电-摩擦电结构中展现出优异的稳定性、加工性和输出性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 摩擦纳米发电机（triboelectric nanogenerators, TENGs）是智能设备现场发电、自供能传感器及新型催化过程的重要驱动力。现有摩擦电材料通常需要添加剂或功能化处理来调控极性，亟需一种简单、可扩展且环境友好的方法制备高性能双价摩擦电表面。

Method: 采用等离子体聚合方法制备金刚烷基薄膜，通过改变等离子体沉积时的基底朝向（facing或backfacing the plasma）来调控薄膜的介电常数、杨氏模量（Young's modulus）和二次电子发射（secondary electron emission）特性，从而获得具有不同摩擦电极性的聚合物层。此外，通过屈曲（buckling）工艺进行额外纹理化处理以增强输出。

Result: 厚度2.8 μm（负摩擦电）与400 nm（正摩擦电）的组合在屈曲纹理化后实现了高达90 V cm⁻²的电压和0.6 μA的电流输出。在开关电极液滴TENG结构中，采用500 nm厚的正摩擦电金刚烷聚合物，从盐水液滴中获得了2.1 μW cm⁻²的最大功率密度。该材料在固-固纳米发电机中可稳定运行超过10⁵次循环，在固-液构型中可承受10⁴次液滴冲击。

Conclusion: 金刚烷等离子体聚合物作为一种薄膜摩擦电材料，兼具环境友好性和工业可扩展性，无需添加剂或功能化即可实现双极性摩擦电特性，为TENG领域提供了可靠且具有竞争力的解决方案。

Abstract: Triboelectric nanogenerators (TENGs) are major drivers in on-site power generation for smart devices, enable self-powered sensors, and introduce novel catalytic processes. Here, we present the advantages of adamantane plasma layers as bivalently triboelectric surfaces capable of exhibiting both tribopositive and tribonegative character through simple modification of the synthesis conditions without the need for additives or functionalization. Fabrication facing or backfacing the plasma yields thin film polymers with different dielectric constants, Young's moduli, and secondary electron emission. The conformality, stability, and processability of the polymers enable direct implementation across solid-solid, solid-liquid, and hybrid piezo-triboelectric configurations. Additional texturization by buckling is shown to provide voltage and current outputs as high as 90 V cm2 and 0.6 uA for a 2.8 um (tribonegative) vs. 400 nm (tribopositive) combination. A maximum power density of 2.1 uW cm-2 is generated from salty droplets in a switch-electrode drop-TENG configuration employing a 500 nm-thick tribopositive adamantane polymer as the triboelectric surface. These layers have demonstrated outstanding durability, enabling more than 10^5 cycles in solid-solid nanogenerators and 10^4 droplet impacts in solid-liquid configurations. The synthetic method is environmentally friendly and industrially scalable, making the adamantane plasma polymer a reliable and competitive solution for thin film triboelectric materials.

### [103] [Application of the exact-factorization density-functional perturbation approach to pentacene crystal and monolayer MoS2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11094)
*Rachel Steinitz-Eliyahu,Galit Cohen,Guy Vosco,E. K. U. Gross,Ryan Requist,Sivan Refaely-Abramson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文首次在扩展周期性材料中实现了基于精确因子化（EF）的密度泛函微扰理论（EF-DFPT），计算了由电子-声子相互作用驱动的非绝热效应对Kohn-Sham电子态的修正，并展示了该效应对静态介电响应的材料依赖性影响：在软模系统（并五苯分子晶体）中显著，在硬模系统（单层MoS₂）中可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Born-Oppenheimer（BO）近似忽略了电子-声子相互作用导致的非绝热效应，而精确因子化（EF）形式主义为超越绝热近似处理此类效应提供了严格框架。本研究旨在将此前提出的EF密度泛函微扰理论（EF-DFPT）方法首次实际应用于扩展周期性材料，以评估其可计算性并揭示非绝热效应对实验可观测量的影响。

Method: 采用基于精确因子化（EF）形式主义的密度泛函微扰理论（EF-DFPT）方案，在简谐极限下对Kohn-Sham（KS）电子态进行核位移二阶微扰展开，计算声子驱动的非绝热修正。以并五苯分子晶体（pentacene molecular crystal）和单层二硫化钼（monolayer MoS₂）分别作为软模系统和硬模系统的代表性材料进行应用。

Result: 非绝热电子-声子相互作用通过两方面机制改变静态介电响应：非绝热声子修饰的电子波函数（NA phonon-dressed electronic wavefunctions）以及二阶非绝热能量重整化（second-order NA energy renormalizations）。其效应呈现强材料依赖性：在单层MoS₂中非绝热效应可忽略，而在并五苯中则因软振动模（soft vibrational modes）和增强的电子-声子耦合导致显著的长程屏蔽效应（long-range screening effects）。

Conclusion: EF-DFPT方法能够有效计算扩展周期性材料中的非绝热电子-声子相互作用对静态介电响应的影响，且该影响具有显著的材料依赖特征，对软模系统和强电子-声子耦合体系尤为重要。

Abstract: Non-adiabatic effects arising from electron-phonon interactions are often neglected within the Born-Oppenheimer (BO) approximation, which assumes that electronic states adjust instantaneously to nuclear motion. The exact factorization (EF) formalism provides a rigorous framework for treating such effects beyond the adiabatic regime and has recently been adapted to density functional theory (DFT) in the harmonic limit. Building on these foundations, we previously introduced an EF-based perturbative scheme, the EF density-functional perturbation theory (EF-DFPT), that enables the computation of phonon-driven non-adiabatic (NA) corrections to Kohn-Sham (KS) electronic states, up to second order in nuclear displacements. Here, we present the first implementation and application of EF-DFPT to extended periodic materials, focusing on its impact on experimentally relevant observables. Using the pentacene molecular crystal and monolayer MoS2 as representative soft- and stiff-mode systems, respectively, we demonstrate how NA electron-phonon interactions modify the static dielectric response. We show that these modifications originate from the combined effect of NA phonon-dressed electronic wavefunctions and second-order NA energy renormalizations. The resulting behavior is strongly material dependent: NA effects are negligible in monolayer MoS2, whereas in pentacene they lead to pronounced long-range screening effects associated with soft vibrational modes and enhanced electron-phonon coupling.

</details>


### [104] [Synergistic doping of the grain interior and grain boundary alters deformation mechanisms and enables extreme strength in nanocrystalline Ni-Cr-Y alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11175)
*Yi Liu,Jason R. Trelewicz,Timothy J. Rupert*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过在恒晶粒尺寸的纳米晶Ni-Cr-Y溅射薄膜中系统调控Cr（固溶强化）和Y（晶界偏析）的含量，揭示了两种强化机制的协同与竞争关系。Cr在低浓度时提供固溶强化，但在高浓度下出现饱和，Y的晶界偏析通过钉扎位错抑制多种变形过程，然而高Y浓度会削弱Cr的固溶强化效果。三元合金最高硬度达11.0 GPa，为单相镍基合金中最高水平之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的研究独立证明了固溶添加（solid solution addition）和晶界偏析（grain boundary segregation）均可增强纳米晶合金（nanocrystalline alloys）的强度，但两者的协同效应尚未被系统探究。

Method: 采用纳米晶Ni-Cr-Y溅射薄膜（sputtered films），通过系统变化合金元素含量并保持晶粒尺寸（grain size）恒定；利用纳米压痕（nanoindentation）测试硬度，并结合压痕堆垛形貌（pile-up morphologies）分析变形机制。

Result: Cr添加提供纳米晶固溶强化，但在高浓度下由于晶界主导过程（grain boundary dominated processes）的显现而出现饱和。Y的晶界偏析通过钉扎位错（pinning dislocations）、抑制位错发射、晶界滑移（grain boundary sliding）和晶粒旋转（grain rotation）增强晶界介导的强化；然而随Y浓度升高，Cr的固溶强化效应减弱，归因于掺杂钉扎导致的位错弓出距离（dislocation bowing distance）减小。最强三元Ni-Cr-Y合金硬度达11.0 GPa。

Conclusion: 通过调控晶粒与晶界化学（grain and grain boundary chemistry），可有效控制位错力学（dislocation mechanics）并提高纳米晶金属的强度。

Abstract: Solid solution addition and grain boundary segregation have been independently shown to enhance the strength of nanocrystalline alloys. In the present study, the synergy between these two effects is investigated in nanocrystalline Ni-Cr-Y sputtered films through systematic variation of alloying element contents with grain size kept constant. Cr is introduced into a solid solution and serves to strengthen the lattice, while Y segregates to the grain boundaries to stabilize these features. Nanoindentation is used to probe hardness, with unexpected trends and very high values observed. Cr additions led to nanocrystalline solid solution strengthening, yet saturation was observed at higher concentrations due to the emergence of grain boundary dominated processes, as evidenced by pile-up morphologies containing slip steps and grain rotation. Y segregated to the grain boundaries, enhancing boundary-mediated strengthening by pinning the dislocations and suppressing dislocation emission, grain boundary sliding, and grain rotation processes. With increasing Y concentration, the nanocrystalline solid solution strengthening effect induced by Cr addition becomes weaker. This phenomenon can be attributed to a reduced dislocation bowing distance caused by dopant pinning. Most notably, the strongest ternary Ni-Cr-Y alloy exhibited a hardness of 11.0 GPa, among the highest hardness values reported for single-phase Ni-based alloys. These findings highlight how tuning grain and grain boundary chemistry offers a viable strategy to control dislocation mechanics and improve the strength of nanocrystalline metals.

### [105] [Symmetry Guided Band-Gap Opening via Periodic Topological Defects in Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11183)
*D. N. Garzon,Leonel Cabrera-Loor,Jacopo Gliozzi,Marco Fronzi,Catherine Stampfl,Henry P. Pinto*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理密度泛函理论（DFT）和紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）计算，证明在石墨烯中引入周期性拓扑缺陷（如Stone-Wales缺陷和花状缺陷）阵列可以可预测地打开并调控带隙，揭示了缺陷间距与晶格对称性对带隙形成的微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯缺乏本征带隙（intrinsic band-gap），严重限制了其在电子器件中的应用。因此，寻找一种可预测且可控的方式来打开石墨烯的带隙是当前研究的核心需求。

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算，并辅以紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）进行验证。研究了包含Stone-Wales缺陷和花状缺陷（flower-like defect）的石墨烯超晶格（superlattice），覆盖不同$N \times N$周期性的缺陷排列。

Result: 带隙打开仅在特定方式降低平移对称性时发生：当超胞周期数$N$为3的倍数时，布里渊区折叠（Brillouin-zone folding）将$K$和$K'$点的狄拉克锥（Dirac cone）映射到约化布里渊区中的相同动量点。花状缺陷超晶格能产生更大且可调的带隙，带隙大小随缺陷间距增大而系统性减小，并在稀缺陷极限下趋近于零。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了缺陷图案化石墨烯中能带工程（band-gap engineering）的可预测框架，阐明了周期性重构晶格中带隙形成的微观机制。

Abstract: Graphene lacks an intrinsic band-gap, which limits its use in electronic applications. Here we demonstrate that periodic arrays of topological defects can open and control a band-gap in a predictable manner governed by defect spacing and lattice symmetry. Using first-principles density functional theory calculations supported by tight-binding models, we investigate graphene superlattices containing Stone-Wales and flower-like defects over a range of $N \times N$ periodicities, where $N$ determines the defect separation. We show that band-gap opening occurs only when translation symmetry is reduced in a specific way: for supercells with $N$ a multiple of three, Brillouin-zone folding brings the Dirac cones at $K$ and $K'$ to the same momentum in the reduced Brillouin zone. In particular, flower-like defect superlattices produce larger and tunable band-gaps, whose magnitude decreases systematically with increasing defect separation and approaches zero in the dilute-defect limit. These results establish a predictive framework for band-gap engineering in defect-patterned graphene and clarify the microscopic mechanism underlying gap formation in periodically reconstructed lattices.

### [106] [$G^0W^0$ implementation based on the pseudopotential and numerical-atomic-orbital basis-set framework: Algorithms and benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11512)
*Huanjing Gong,Min-Ye Zhang,Peize Lin,Bohan Jia,Ziqing Guan,Lixin He,Xinguo Ren*

TL;DR: 本文在数值原子轨道（NAO）和赝势（PP）框架下，通过ABACUS软件与LibRPA库的接口，实现了一个高效且数值稳定的周期性$G^0W^0$计算方案，采用局域化解析恒等式（LRI）压缩技术、小q极限解析处理和势函数筛选策略，在大规模电子能带结构计算中兼顾了高精度与计算效率。

Result: 系统基准测试验证了压缩方案和实空间张量过滤策略的有效性，实现了高精度与显著的计算效率提升；与已有$G^0W^0$实现的对比在能带结构和带隙上表现出一致性，证实了ABACUS+LibRPA平台的可靠性和高效性。

Conclusion: ABACUS+LibRPA被确认为一个可靠且高效的大规模$G^0W^0$模拟平台，填补了NAO-PP框架下周期性$GW$实现的空白，为高精度电子结构计算和机器学习电子结构方法的发展提供了重要工具。

Abstract: The $GW$ method delivers substantially improved accuracy in electronic band structure calculations over conventional Kohn-Sham density functional theory (KS-DFT) by explicitly incorporating the electron self-energy effect beyond mean-field approximations. Despite many existing implementations, a periodic $GW$ implementation within the framework of numerical atomic orbitals (NAO) combined with the pseudopotential (PP) scheme has not been reported. This is urgently needed given the increasing popularity of the NAO-PP framework in KS-DFT calculations and its importance for the development of machine-learning electronic-structure approaches. In this work, we present an efficient NAO-PP-based $G^0W^0$ computational framework by interfacing the first-principles software package ABACUS with LibRPA -- a library for performing low-scaling random-phase approximation and $GW$ calculations based on NAOs. Our approach employs the localized resolution of identity (LRI) technique with a novel compression scheme, significantly improving both computational efficiency and numerical stability. In addition, an analytic treatment of the small-q limit of the microscopic dielectric function reduces the need for dense q-point sampling. Furthermore, we propose a practical strategy to select a suitable KS-DFT pseudopotential prior to $G^0W^0$ calculations by examining the frequency-dependent macroscopic dielectric function. Systematic benchmarks validate the effectiveness of our compression scheme and real-space tensor filtering strategies, demonstrating both high accuracy and significant computational efficiency gains. Comparisons with established $G^0W^0$ implementations show excellent agreement in band structures and band gaps, confirming ABACUS+LibRPA as a reliable and efficient platform for large-scale $G^0W^0$ simulations.

*Zeyu Wang,Shuya Yamazaki,Martin Hoffmann Petersen,Masato Ohnishi,Tomiya Yamamoto,Wei Nong,Jianghai Wang,Ruiming Zhu,Masatoshi Hanai,Michimasa Morita,Toyotaro Suzumura,Zekun Ren,Junichiro Shiomi,Kedar Hippalgaonkar*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成模型打开了功能材料设计中广阔的化学空间。尽管机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potentials, MLIPs）大幅加速了声子计算，但对晶格热导率（lattice thermal conductivity, κlat）的高保真预测仍需要精确处理非谐相互作用（anharmonic interactions），这在新型化学空间中仍是现有势函数的关键挑战。

Method: 利用 Phonix 数据库（6,966 条基于一阶原理推导的非谐声子特性数据），对 15 种替代模型进行基准测试。模型分为三类：物理信息特征描述符（physical-informed feature descriptors）结合机器学习模型、端到端深度神经网络（end-to-end deep neural networks）以及预训练 MLIP 嵌入（pre-trained MLIP-embeddings）结合机器学习模型。评估采用随机划分、空间群不交叠划分（space-group disjoint split，测试对未知晶格对称性的泛化能力）以及基于 κlat 的分布外划分（Out-Of-Distribution split, OOD，测试对训练范围之外性质区间的外推能力）。

Result: MLIP 嵌入模型在采样充分区域的插值（interpolation）任务上表现优异；深度神经网络模型（尤其是 ALiEGNN）在 OOD 场景下展现出最强的鲁棒性，这对发现新型低 κlat 材料至关重要。此外，降低结构表示（structural representation）的维度会导致模型性能系统性下降。替代模型的精度虽低于一阶原理直接模拟，但计算成本降低数个数量级。

Conclusion: 替代模型能够在生成设计流程（generative design workflow）中以最小精度损失实现热电材料的高通量高效筛选。不同模型类别在插值与探索（exploration）任务中各有优势，其中 MLIP 嵌入与深度神经网络分别擅长已知区域和未知区域的推断。

Abstract: The appearance of generative models has opened vast chemical spaces in the design of functional materials. Although machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) have substantially accelerated phonon calculations, high-fidelity prediction of lattice thermal conductivity \k{appa}lat still requires accurate treatment of anharmonic interactions, which remains a key challenge for existing potentials across novel chemical spaces. To address this challenge, we present a comprehensive benchmark of 15 surrogate models for predicting \k{appa}lat using the Phonix database, which contains 6,966 entries with anharmonic phonon properties derived from first-principles calculations. Firstly, We categorize these surrogate models into three distinct groups: Physical-informed feature descriptors combined with ML models, end-to-end deep neural networks, and pre-trained MLIP-embeddings combined with ML models. By evaluating model performance across random, space-group disjoint (testing generalization to unseen crystal symmetries), and Out-Of-Distribution splits (OOD dataset that testing extrapolation to property regimes beyond the training range) based on \k{appa}lat, we probe both interpolation and exploration capabilities. Our results reveal that MLIP-embedded models excel in interpolation within well-sampled regions, deep neural network models especially ALiEGNN demonstrate superior robustness in OOD regimes critical for discovering novel low-\k{appa}lat. Additionally, we find a systematic degradation in performance when the structural representation is reduced. Although surrogate models exhibit lower accuracy than direct simulations using first-principles calculation, they reduce computational costs by orders of magnitude, enabling efficient high-throughput screening of thermoelectric materials with minimal loss in generative design workflows.

### [110] [Universality of magnetic susceptibility in the conical state of kagome ferromagnet Fe$_3$Sn$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11851)
*Lilian Prodan,Donald M. Evans,Lukas Puntigam,1 István Kézsmárki,Vladimir Tsurkan*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用等消光-不变性分析（isosbestic-invariance analysis）处理DMS等温线数据，并结合互补的场依赖磁力显微镜（magnetic-force microscopy）测量，观察不同磁场下的自旋织构演化。

Abstract: We report universal behavior of the differential magnetic susceptibility (DMS) in the conical phase that mediates the spin-reorientation (SR) transition of the kagome ferromagnet Fe$_3$Sn$_2$. Within the SR temperature range, the DMS isotherms exhibit extremely narrow crossing regions, forming isosbestic points. Using an isosbestic-invariance analysis, we show that the isotherms collapse onto a single temperature-independent curve, revealing quadratic-in-temperature corrections to the susceptibility. Complementary field-dependent magnetic-force-microscopy measurements uncover evolution of spin textures from stripe-like domains at low fields to isolated bubble-like domains near the isosbestic field ($\sim 0.6$~T), a behavior not previously reported in bulk Fe$_3$Sn$_2$ within the conical state. ### [111] [Tailoring the material properties, nanostructure and grain alignment of Alnico magnets through micromagnetic simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11982)

TL;DR: 通过有限元微磁学模拟和统计方法，系统研究了Alnico永磁合金中交换退耦纳米棒的尺寸、间距和晶粒取向对磁滞性能的影响，并利用多层感知机回归器预测磁性能，揭示了纳米结构、本征材料性质和晶粒排列对提升磁性能的调控规律。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 孤立纳米棒与交换退耦系统的矫顽力对比揭示了磁静相互作用（magnetostatic interaction）的影响；矫顽力随填充分数p的标度关系通过解析计算得到验证；不同磁晶各向异性常数（magnetocrystalline anisotropy constant）和饱和极化强度（saturation polarisation）材料的对比，展示了本征材料性质对磁行为的影响。

Abstract: Alnico magnets have gained renewed interest in the search for rare-earth free permanent magnets due to their high thermal stability and magnetisation. However, the limited coercivity of these shape-anisotropy-based alloys constrains their performance. Starting from a reference Alnico sample, we realised a finite elements micromagnetic study of exchange-decoupled rods by varying their dimensions and interrod spacing across those observed experimentally. We computed the hysteresis properties by progressing from micromagnetic simulations of a small number of rods within the magnetostatic field of their neighbours to large systems treated statistically based on the distribution of orientations of the grains. We compared the coercivity of an isolated rod with that of the exchange-decoupled system to highlight the effect of magnetostatic interactions. We computed analytically the stray field acting on a single rod as a consequence of its surrounding rods in order to confirm the scaling of the coercivity with the packing fraction p. We explored how intrinsic material properties influence magnetic behaviour by examining materials with different magnetocrystalline anisotropy constants and saturation polarisation values. Results from several hundred simulations were used to train a multi-layer perceptron regressor and predict the magnetic properties as function of the dimensions of the rods, interrod spacing and orientation of the grains. With this approach, we highlight the underlying trends by which nanoscale structuring, intrinsic material properties and grain alignment can be tailored to improve the magnetic properties of Alnico alloys.

### [112] [Vacancy-Enhanced $N-N$ Bonding and Deep Level Complex Defect Formation in $β-Ga_2O_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12029)
*Asiyeh Shokri,Yevgen Melikhov,Yevgen Syryanyy,Maryna Chernyshova,Iraida N. Demchenko*

TL;DR: 基于第一性原理计算，系统分析了β-Ga₂O₃中与氮相关的缺陷复合体的形成与电子性质，发现这些复合体倾向于形成氮-氮共局域化构型，但未完全达到分子N₂特征；空位辅助的复合体在热力学上稳定，但所有构型均在带隙中引入局域电子态，表现为深能级陷阱中心，从而限制载流子输运并促进半绝缘行为。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），从能量最优的Nᵢ₉–Nₒᴵ构型出发，计算键长、电子局域化函数（electron localization function, ELF）、形成能（formation energy）、结合能（binding energy）以及态密度（density of states, DOS）和自旋密度（spin density）。

Conclusion: 这些缺陷复合体在β-Ga₂O₃中作为深能级陷阱中心（deep trapping centers），有效限制载流子输运，从而促进半绝缘行为和电流阻挡特性。

Abstract: The formation and electronic properties of nitrogen-related defect complexes in $β-Ga_2O_3$ are investigated using first-principles calculations. Starting from the energetically favorable $N_{i9}-N_{OI}$ configuration, nitrogen atoms exhibit a strong tendency toward co-localization, leading to reduced $N-N$ separation. However, analysis of bond lengths and electron localization function shows that these configurations do not fully attain molecular $N_{2}$ character. The role of intrinsic defects is further examined by introducing oxygen and gallium vacancies. Vacancy-assisted configurations enhance local lattice relaxation and further decrease the $N-N$ distance. Formation energy calculations indicate that several vacancy-assisted complexes are thermodynamically favorable, while binding energy analysis confirms their stability against dissociation. Despite this, the density of states analysis reveals that all configurations introduce localized electronic states within the band gap. These states originate primarily from hybridized $N$-$2p$ and $O$-$2p$ orbitals and remain energetically separated from the band edges. Spin density analysis further confirms strong localization. Overall, these defect complexes act as deep trapping centers, limiting carrier transport in $β-Ga_2O_3$ and thereby promoting semi-insulating behavior and current blocking characteristics.

### [113] [Discovery of High-Voltage Magnesium-Ion Cathodes using Machine Learning and First-Principles Calculations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12067)
*Jhon Rogelnor A. Florida,Edward Aris D. Fajardo*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用改进的晶体图卷积神经网络（mCGCNN）对917种含镁拓扑量子材料（TQMs）进行高通量筛选；随后对候选材料进行密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，包括形成能、凸包分析（convex-hull calculation）、电压曲线计算以及基于Wannier插值（Wannier interpolation）的电子结构分析。

Conclusion: 拓扑量子材料（TQMs）相比传统镁正极具有更高电压和竞争性容量，有望用于下一代多价电池；将机器学习与第一性原理计算相结合是发现和理解新型正极材料的高效策略。

Abstract: Developing high-performance cathode materials for magnesium-ion batteries (MIBs) remains challenging because Mg$^{2+}$ ions move slowly, and conventional materials exhibit low voltage outputs. In this study, machine learning and first-principles calculations were combined to investigate topological quantum materials (TQMs) as a new class of cathode candidates. A modified crystal graph convolutional neural network (mCGCNN) was used to screen 917 Mg-containing TQMs, identifying a small subset of materials with predicted voltages above 3 V and high volumetric capacities. Among these, Mg$_2$VO$_4$ and Mg$_6$MnO$_8$ were selected for detailed density functional theory (DFT) analysis. Formation energy and convex-hull calculations indicate that Mg$_x$VO$_4$ exhibits a fully stable magnesiation pathway, whereas Mg$_x$MnO$_8$ demonstrates minor metastability at intermediate compositions. The calculated voltage profiles yield average voltages of 3.66 V for Mg$_2$VO$_4$ and 4.06 V for Mg$_6$MnO$_8$, in good agreement with machine learning predictions. Electronic structure analysis, supported by Wannier interpolation, confirms that both materials are semiconducting, with valence bands dominated by O $2p$ states and conduction bands by transition-metal $d$ states, indicating a charge-transfer redox mechanism. Compared to conventional Mg cathodes, these TQMs exhibit higher voltages and competitive capacities, underscoring their potential for next-generation multivalent batteries. This study demonstrates that integrating machine learning with first-principles calculations offers an efficient approach for discovering and understanding novel cathode materials.

Conclusion: 该异质结构设计框架提供了一种简单可行的策略，用于调控材料的失效与抗冲击性能，可应用于从Whipple防护屏到运动装备等多种防护场景。

Abstract: The two-dimensional electron gas (2DEG) in reduced strontium titanate offers a versatile platform for oxide electronics, yet its dissipation mechanisms under field driven charge fluctuations remain poorly understood. Abstract: The liquid crystalline 4-pentylphenyl-4'-decyloxythiobenzoate is investigated in various temperature programs for determination of crystallization kinetics and glassforming properties. The Avrami model, Augis-Bennett method and isoconversional method are used. Cooling at the 25-30 K/min rate results in formation of the glass of the tilted smectic Y phase with the herring-bone order within layers. Both Cr1 and Cr2 are conformationally disordered crystal phases, which is indicated both by the melting entropy values and the dielectric spectra. The results demonstrate that the energy released during cold crystallization can be tuned by thermal history, highlighting 10OS5 as a candidate for thermal energy storage applications.

However, direct extraction of quantitative physical information from these high-dimensional, noisy fluctuation maps faces a significant challenge.
