Motivation: 硫掺杂少层石墨烯（S-doped few-layer graphene）在电池应用与氧还原反应（oxygen reduction reaction）中具有技术重要性，但目前对其基面硫掺杂如何影响电子性质的系统理解尚不充分。

Method: 采用考虑范德华（van der Waals）修正的第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），对单层、双层和四层石墨烯中不同构型的基面硫掺杂进行系统研究。

Result: 在单层中，噻吩型掺杂（2V1S）维持了狄拉克锥（Dirac cone）并在费米能级（Fermi level）以外产生局域杂质带；石墨型掺杂（1V1S）打开0.4 eV带隙并在费米能级附近出现平带（flat bands）；三硫原子吸附于四空位（4V3S）导致n型掺杂与自旋极化（spin-polarization）。在少层体系中，2V1S使狄拉克锥变为双曲接触带；1V1S与4V3S分别减少或闭合带隙并引入附加双曲接触带与平带，4V3S的自旋极化有所减弱。

Conclusion: 硫掺杂能够设计少层石墨烯的能带结构，将其电子行为从金属性调至绝缘性、从线性色散调至平带，使硫掺杂少层石墨烯成为面向多样化技术应用的前景材料。

Abstract: Motivated by the technological relevance of S-doped few-layer graphene (FLG) in battery applications and in the oxygen reduction reaction, we systematically explore the effect of basal plane S-doping on the electronic properties of mono-, bi-, and four-layer graphene, using first-principles calculations with van der Waals corrections. In the monolayer we find a variety of effects ranging from a sustained Dirac cone with localized impurity bands away from the Fermi level in thiophenic doping (2V1S) to a band gap opening of 0.4 eV and flat bands close to the Fermi-level in graphitic doping (1V1S) and an additional $n$-type doping together with spin-polarization, when three S-atoms are adsorbed in a four-site vacancy (4V3S). Incorporation in FLG leads to modification of the Dirac cone into a set of hyperbolic touching bands in 2V1S; reduction (bilayer) and closing of the band gap with additional hyperbolic touching bands in conjunction with the flat band at the Fermi level in 1V1S and 4V3S and a reduction of spin polarization in the latter. Overall, S-doping enables design of the band structure and tuning the electronic behavior of FLG from metallic to insulating and from linear dispersive to flat bands that makes S-doped FLG a promising material for versatile technological applications.

</details>


### [119] [Ordering governs magnetic tunability in FePt-based Janus particles independent of curvature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12283)
*Natalia Gonzalez-Vazquez,Eylül Suadiye,Eberhard Goering,Ruben O. Miranda-Rosales,Hilda David,Frank Thiele,Julia Unangst,Andrew K. Schulz,Gunther Richter*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和微磁学模拟，系统研究了FePt包覆的Janus颗粒（直径3-10微米）中的曲率依赖磁性，发现磁滞行为几乎不受曲率影响，而主要受材料化学有序度控制，并由此开发了开源模拟框架FunMaP。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然曲率驱动的磁性效应在纳米尺度已得到充分认识，但其在微米尺度颗粒中对磁化反转（magnetization reversal）的影响尚不明确。本文旨在填补这一认知空白，定量界定曲率效应在微米磁性颗粒中的有效性边界。

Method: 结合实验与微磁学模拟（micromagnetic simulation）：对直径3-10微米的FePt包覆Janus颗粒进行结构、晶体学表征及磁强计测量，并将模拟范围扩展至1-20微米。开发了开源模拟框架FunMaP，实现实验与理想化FePt帽层之间的直接对比。

Result: 连续FePt涂层呈近等原子比组成与部分L1₀有序化。磁强计测量显示，不同尺寸颗粒的矫顽力（coercivity）几乎恒定（μ₀Hc = 1.13 ± 0.05 T，n=8），统计检验表明矫顽力（p=0.61）与剩磁比（remanence, Mr/Ms, p=0.85）均不显著依赖于颗粒直径。模拟确认微米尺度下曲率对磁化反转影响很小，而化学有序度的差异显著影响磁滞回线形状与矫顽力。

Conclusion: 微米尺度FePt Janus颗粒的磁性行为主要由材料有序度（material ordering）而非曲率主导。该工作建立了曲率依赖磁性的定量边界，并为可编程磁性微系统提供了设计指导。

Abstract: Magnetic Janus particles enable remote actuation in biomedical, microfluidic, and materials applications. While curvature-driven magnetic effects are well known at the nanoscale, their influence on magnetization reversal in micrometer-sized particles is still unclear. In this work, we combine experiments and micromagnetic simulations to study curvature-dependent magnetism in FePt-coated Janus particles with diameters ranging from 3-10 microm, and extend the analysis to 1-20 microm through simulations. Structural and crystallographic characterization confirms continuous FePt coatings with near-equiatomic composition and partial L1_0 ordering. Magnetometry measurements show nearly unchanged hysteresis behavior across particle sizes, with coercivity remaining approximately constant m_0Hc = 1.13 +/- 0.05 T, pooled n = 8). Statistical analysis reveals no significant dependence of coercivity or remanence on particle diameter (p = 0.61 for Hc and p = 0.85 for Mr/Ms). To explain these results, we introduce FunMaP, an open-source micromagnetic simulation framework that enables direct comparison between experiments and idealized FePt caps. Simulations confirm that curvature has little effect on magnetization reversal at micrometer scales, consistent with a locally planar magnetic limit where the exchange length is much smaller than the particle radius. In contrast, differences in chemical ordering strongly affect hysteresis shape and coercivity. These findings demonstrate that magnetic behavior in micrometer-scale FePt Janus particles is governed mainly by material ordering rather than curvature. This work establishes a quantitative boundary for curvature-dependent magnetism and provides design guidelines for programmable magnetic micro-systems.

### [120] [Graphene lattice recoil in hard X-ray photoemission: Experiment and Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12330)
*Simone Ritarossi,Alice Apponi,Orlando Castellano,José Lorenzana,Domenica Convertino,Camilla Coletti,Tien-Lin Lee,Francesco Offi,Alessandro Ruocco*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过实验与建模结合，研究了硬X射线C 1s光电子能谱中原子核反冲（nuclear recoil）与固有电子不对称性对单层石墨烯（monolayer graphene）谱线形状的协同贡献，提出了一种将本征电子线形与声子反冲核（phonon recoil kernel）卷积的模型，成功再现了谱线演化与质心移动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在0.8–8 keV光子能量范围内，单层石墨烯的硬X射线C 1s光电子能谱中，原子核反冲与固有电子不对称性在可比能量尺度上共同影响谱线形状，现有Fujikawa–Takata累积量形式（cumulant formalism）无法再现测量谱中明显的不对称拖尾，因此需要建立更精确的谱线形状模型。

Method: 采用基于第一性原理声子计算（first-principles phonon calculations）约束的各向异性振动态密度（anisotropic vibrational density of states），实现石墨烯专用的Fujikawa–Takata累积量形式；同时引入显式电子卷积模型（explicit electronic convolution model），将从近无反冲（near-recoilless）0.8 keV数据中提取的光子能量无关的本征电子线形与携带全部角度与能量依赖的声子反冲核进行卷积。

Result: 该卷积模型成功再现了所有测试光子能量下的谱线形状演化与质心移动，无需在高光子能量下重新拟合谱线；而结合对称展宽（symmetric lifetime broadening）的基线处理方法则无法描述石墨烯中的反冲效应。

Conclusion: 石墨烯C 1s谱线的反冲效应必须与固有多体电子响应（intrinsic many-body electronic response）协同处理，不能仅用声子反冲核配合对称寿命展宽的基线方法描述。

Abstract: Hard-x-ray C 1s photoemission from monolayer graphene probes a regime in which nuclear recoil and intrinsic electronic asymmetry contribute on comparable energy scales to the observed spectral line shape. Here we combine experiment and modeling over the photon-energy range 0.8 keV--8 keV to resolve this interplay quantitatively. A graphene-specific implementation of the Fujikawa--Takata cumulant formalism, based on an anisotropic vibrational density of states constrained by first-principles phonon calculations, captures the expected recoil scaling with photon energy and emission geometry but fails to reproduce the pronounced asymmetric tails of the measured spectra. To overcome this limitation, we introduce an explicit electronic convolution model in which an intrinsic, photon-energy-independent electronic line shape extracted from near-recoilless 0.8 keV data is convolved with a phonon recoil kernel carrying the full dependence on photon energy and emission angle. This approach reproduces both the measured line-shape evolution and the observed centroid shifts across the explored energy range without refitting the spectra at higher photon energies. The results show that recoil in graphene cannot be described by a baseline treatment in which the phonon recoil kernel is combined only with symmetric lifetime broadening, but must be treated together with the intrinsic many-body electronic response of the C 1s line.

### [121] [Equivariant Space Group and Hamiltonian for Collinear Magnetic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12440)
*Chaoxi Cui,Zhi-Ming Yu,Yilin Han,Run-Wu Zhang,Shengyuan A. Yang,Yugui Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于等变空间群（equivariant space group）的对称性框架，用于构建显式依赖磁有序参量取向 n 的等效磁性哈密顿量（equivariant magnetic Hamiltonian, EMH），并展示了其在拓扑泵浦、第一性原理计算及非共线磁系统中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 凝聚态物理中，利用磁有序参量取向（magnetic order parameter orientation）n 作为调控共线磁性材料性质的旋钮日益重要，但目前缺乏一种通用的方法来构建显式依赖于 n 的有效哈密顿量。

Method: 提出一个基于等变空间群（equivariant space group）的对称性框架，用于构建等效磁性哈密顿量（EMH）。该 EMH 存在于高维的 k-n 空间中，展现出非常规的对称性作用和拓扑特征。方法可推广至非共线磁系统，并能融入第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）。

Result: 以一维铁磁链和三维反铁磁体为例，EMH 中显式的 n 依赖性使能研究磁动力学驱动的拓扑泵浦，包括偶数整数电荷泵浦（even-integer charge pumping）以及由第二陈数（second Chern number）诱导的表面反常霍尔电导（surface anomalous Hall conductivity）的量子化泵浦。通过结合第一性原理计算构建的从头算 EMH（ab-initio EMH）能准确捕捉真实材料中依赖 n 的能带结构。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个构建 EMH 的通用框架，为探索由磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）和磁动力学（magnetic dynamics）产生的丰富物理现象提供了基础。

Abstract: Condensed matter physics increasingly focuses on exploiting the magnetic order parameter orientation n as a tuning knob for properties of collinear magnetic materials, but a general method for constructing effective Hamiltonians with explicit n-dependence has been lacking. Here, we develop a symmetry-based framework, built on the equivariant space group, for constructing such Hamiltonians, termed equivariant magnetic Hamiltonians (EMHs). The resulting EMH lives in a higher-dimensional k-n space and exhibits unconventional symmetry actions and topological features. Using a 1D ferromagnetic chain and a 3D antiferromagnet as examples, we demonstrate that explicit n-dependence in EMHs enables the study of magnetic-dynamics-driven topological pumping, including even-integer charge pumping and a second-Chern-number-induced quantized pumping of surface anomalous Hall conductivity. Beyond model systems, we incorporate the framework into first-principles calculations to construct ab-initio EMHs that accurately capture the n-dependent band structures of real materials. The approach can also be generalized to non-collinear magnetic systems. Our work establishes a general framework for constructing EMHs and for exploring the rich physics arising from magnetic anisotropy and magnetic dynamics.

*Lalit Yadav,Yongqiang Cheng,Mathieu Doucet*

TL;DR: RADAR-PD 是一个面向X射线和中子粉末衍射（powder diffraction）的模态感知机器学习框架，结合粗粒度动量指纹上的容错神经网络、自动晶格微调（lattice nudging）和物理约束的Rietveld验证，实现了自动化物相鉴定（phase identification）与定量分析，在实验基准上优于现有方法，并填补了中子衍射自动化分析的空白。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: RADAR-PD 采用模态感知（modality-aware）机器学习框架，其核心包括：(1) 一个运行在粗粒度动量转移（momentum-transfer）指纹上的容错神经网络（mismatch-tolerant neural network）；(2) 自动晶格微调机制；以及 (3) 物理约束的Rietveld验证（physics-constrained Rietveld verification）。该方法能够从元素约束生成主要物相假设，并递归地分离次要物相。

Result: 在实验性RRUFF PXRD基准测试中，RADAR-PD 在恢复参考物相方面优于DARA方法。此外，该方法在复杂飞行时间（time-of-flight）和恒定波长（constant-wavelength）中子数据集上提供了稳健的多物相分析，解决了中子衍射自动化分析中一个重要的未满足需求。

Conclusion: RADAR-PD 被确立为一个可审计（auditable）、与仪器无关（instrument-agnostic）的框架，适用于自主结构发现，尤其在中子粉末衍射自动化分析领域展现出显著优势。

Abstract: Powder diffraction is a primary structural characterization tool in materials science, yet automated phase identification remains a major bottleneck for autonomous discovery. Existing workflows rely heavily on search--match heuristics and manual Rietveld refinement, and broadly usable end-to-end automation is especially limited for neutron powder diffraction, where comparable tools are largely absent. Here we introduce RADAR-PD, a modality-aware machine learning framework for phase identification and quantification across both X-ray and neutron powder diffraction. RADAR-PD couples a mismatch-tolerant neural network operating on coarse momentum-transfer fingerprints with automated lattice nudging and physics-constrained Rietveld verification, enabling dominant-phase hypotheses to be generated from elemental constraints and secondary phases to be isolated recursively. On an experimental RRUFF PXRD benchmark, RADAR-PD outperforms DARA in recovering the reference phase. RADAR-PD further provides robust multiphase analysis on complex time-of-flight and constant-wavelength neutron datasets, addressing an important unmet need in automated neutron diffraction analysis. These results establish RADAR-PD as an auditable, instrument-agnostic framework for autonomous structural discovery.

### [123] [Midpoint BKM Estimates and Boundary Coherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11024)
*Hassan Nasreddine*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了密度矩阵（density matrix）与其分块对角部分（block-diagonal part）之间量子相对熵（quantum relative entropy）的下界，利用Bogoliubov–Kubo–Mori（BKM）核（kernel）给出了一个非对易（noncommutative）的下界估计，并在谱间隙条件（spectral gap condition）下得到了显式的对数下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子相对熵是量子信息论中的核心量，然而在实际应用中常需要将其与分块对角近似进行比较；现有下界估计往往损失了相干项（coherence term）的联合谱结构信息，因此需要一个保留更多非对易结构的精确下界。

Method: 作者将待比较的矩阵与它的分块对角投影（block-diagonal projection）通过仿射插值（affine interpolation）连接，利用BKM Hessian（BKM Hessian）的中点估计（midpoint estimate）来推导相对熵的下界。

Result: 证明了一个保留对角线分块与相干项联合谱结构（joint spectral structure）的非对易下界；在A相对于C满足谱间隙条件时，得到与相干块的Frobenius范数（Frobenius norm）平方成正比的对数下界。

Conclusion: BKM度规（BKM metric）在该问题中自然出现，因为它恰好是量子相对熵的Hessian；所获得的下界严格优于仅依赖范数的平庸估计，在量子信息理论中具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We study lower bounds for the quantum relative entropy between a density matrix and its block-diagonal part. For a block matrix with diagonal blocks A,C>0 and off-diagonal coherence block B, we prove a lower bound expressed through the associated Bogoliubov--Kubo--Mori (BKM) kernel.
  The proof uses a midpoint estimate for the BKM Hessian along the affine interpolation between the matrix and its block-diagonal projection. The resulting estimate is genuinely noncommutative and retains information about the joint spectral structure of the diagonal blocks and the coherence term.
  As a consequence, under a spectral gap condition on A relative to C, we obtain an explicit logarithmic lower bound proportional to the squared Frobenius norm of the coherence block. The appearance of the BKM metric is natural in this setting because it coincides with the Hessian of quantum relative entropy.

</details>


### [124] [Graph-State Circuit Blocks control Entanglement and Scrambling Velocities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11076)
*Chandana Rao,Himanshu Sahu,Aranya Bhattacharya,Suhail Ahmad Rather,Mario Flory,Zahra Raissi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究发现，即使是在固定随机电路架构中，多体电路基本单元（multipartite circuit primitives）的内部结构仍能显著影响纠缠增长和算子扩散的动力学速率。通过分析基于图态（graph states）的克利福德量子电路（Clifford quantum circuits），论文展示了局部克利福德（LC）不等价的图态会生成截然不同的纠缠速度 $v_E$ 和蝴蝶速度 $v_B$，且这两种速率分别由块内二分纠缠分布和图论连通性特征所控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机电路模型通常采用通用两量子比特门描述局域动力学，成功地捕捉了多种场景下的纠缠增长与算子扩散，导致人们普遍认为精细的门结构对粗粒化纠缠诊断仅有有限影响。本文旨在挑战这一假设，揭示多体电路基本单元的内部结构——在固定电路架构和随机参数条件下——仍能显著改变动力学速率。

Method: 研究采用一族精确可模拟的克利福德量子电路，其基本构建模块为固定的 $n$ 量子比特图态制备酉操作（graph-state preparation unitaries）。具体设置为一维 $N$ 量子比特链，初始化为乘积态，逐层演化时在链上按间距参数 $α$ 随机放置不重叠的长度为 $n$ 的块。通过对比不同图态构建块（包括局部克利福德不等价的图态）下的纠缠速度 $v_E$ 和蝴蝶速度 $v_B$，分析块级特征与动力学速率之间的关联。

Result: 不同图态构建块导致显著不同的纠缠速度和蝴蝶速度，即便电路架构和随机性参数完全相同。局部克利福德不等价的图态生成速度差异尤其显著。纠缠速度 $v_E$ 与图态内部二分纠缠分布相关，而蝴蝶速度 $v_B$ 与跨越二分区的图论连通性（graph-theoretic connectivity）相关。两者由不同结构特征独立控制，且绝对最大纠缠态（AME states）在该系综中表现出最快的混扰能力。

Conclusion: 电路基本单元的详细结构对粗粒化动力学速率具有重要影响，不可被忽略。纠缠增长和算子扩散由局部块的不同结构特征分别决定，这提示在随机电路模型中应更细致地考虑基本门结构的设计与分类。

Abstract: Random circuit models often describe local dynamics using generic two-qubit gates, which have proven successful in capturing entanglement growth and operator spreading in many contexts. This approach naturally leads to the expectation that detailed gate structure plays only a limited role in coarse-grained entanglement and scrambling diagnostics. We show that the internal structure of multipartite circuit primitives can significantly influence these dynamical rates, even within a fixed random-circuit architecture. To investigate this, we study an exactly simulable family of Clifford quantum circuits built from fixed $n$-qubit graph-state preparation unitaries, which we treat as elementary building blocks. Specifically, we consider a one-dimensional chain of $N$ qubits initialized in a product state and evolved by layers in which nonoverlapping length-$n$ blocks are placed at uniformly random positions with sparsity $α$. We find that different choices of graph-state building blocks lead to strongly varying dynamical rates. Graph states that are inequivalent under local Clifford (LC) transformations generate sharply different entanglement velocities $v_E$ and butterfly velocities $v_B$, even though the circuits are drawn from the same ensemble with identical architecture and randomness parameters. We further show that this hierarchy is captured by two complementary block-level characteristics: the distribution of entanglement across internal bipartitions of the graph state, which correlates with $v_E$, and a graph-theoretic connectivity profile across bipartitions, which correlates with $v_B$. Neither descriptor alone fully determines the dynamics; rather, entanglement growth and operator spreading are controlled by distinct structural features of the local circuit blocks. Notably, AME states appear among the fastest scrambling building blocks within the ensembles studied here.

</details>


### [125] [A post-Newtonian Gravitational Collapse Model from Linearized Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12172)
*Rudi B. P. Pietsch,Luciano Petruzziello,Martin B. Plenio*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于线性化引力和引力电磁学（gravitoelectromagnetism），引入了一种与引力相关的普适塌缩机制（collapse mechanism）。通过经典-量子混合动力学方法，推导出主方程（master equation），其非幺正部分由质量分布和流决定。该模型在仅考虑引力电势耦合时恢复经典的Diósi-Penrose塌缩模型，而在引入引力磁矢势后，还能产生针对旋转自由度和质量-旋转混合贡献的额外塌缩机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的引力塌缩模型（如Diósi-Penrose模型）仅考虑了引力电（gravitoelectric）效应，忽略了引力磁（gravitomagnetic）效应。本文旨在基于线性化引力（linearized gravity）和引力电磁学，提出一个更一般的引力塌缩机制，以涵盖旋转自由度及其与质量分布的耦合。

Method: 采用经典-量子混合动力学（hybrid classical-quantum dynamics）方法，从广义相对论的弱场极限（weak-field limit）出发，利用引力电磁学建立引力电势与质量密度、引力磁矢势与质量流之间的有效耦合，进而推导出包含非幺正项的主方程。

Result: 当仅考虑引力电势耦合时，恢复Diósi-Penrose塌缩模型；当纳入引力磁矢势后，模型中出现了针对旋转自由度的塌缩机制以及质量-旋转混合贡献的塌缩机制。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于线性化引力的塌缩机制比传统模型更普适，不仅涵盖位置自由度，还自然包含了旋转自由度的量子塌缩，为将引力与量子力学结合的模型提供了新的理论扩展。

Abstract: We introduce a general gravity-related collapse mechanism based on linearized gravity. Starting from the weak-field limit of general relativity, gravitoelectromagnetism suggests an effective coupling between the gravitoelectric potential and the mass density distribution. At the same time, it provides a similar relation for the gravitomagnetic vector potential and the mass current. Following a hybrid (classical-quantum) dynamics approach, these couplings lead to a master equation whose non-unitary part is determined by the underlying mass distribution and currents. When the gravitoelectric potential coupling is considered, the well-known Diósi-Penrose collapse model acting on positional degrees of freedom is recovered. However, upon including the gravitomagnetic vector potential, additional collapse mechanisms emerge for rotational degrees of freedom as well as for mixed mass-rotation contributions.

</details>


### [126] [Permutation-symmetric quantum trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11103)
*Elliot W. Lloyd,Aleksandra A. Ziolkowska,Jonathan Keeling*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在弱置换对称性（weak permutation symmetry）下对N个发射体耦合至公共系统（如腔模）的模型进行随机展开（stochastic unraveling）的方法。对于二能级发射体，计算复杂度从O(N^5)降至O(N^2)，并可通过进一步优化降至O(N)；对于d能级系统，复杂度为O(N^{d(d-1)/2})，可实现d=3时的大规模N模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接模拟N个发射体耦合至公共系统的精确量子动力学，计算成本随N增长极快（如二能级系统为O(N^5)），严重限制了可模拟的系统规模。因此需要发展更高效的算法来突破这一瓶颈。

Method: 利用弱置换对称性（weak permutation symmetry）设计一种随机展开（stochastic unraveling）方法，通过对称性约化将发射体的自由度有效压缩，从而大幅降低计算复杂度。

Result: 对于二能级发射体，该方法将计算成本从O(N^5)降至O(N^2)，进一步优化可降至O(N)；对于d能级系统，计算复杂度为O(N^{d(d-1)/2})，且当d=3时能够实现大N模拟。

Conclusion: 该方法显著扩大了可进行精确量子动力学模拟的系统规模范围，并推广至任意d能级系统，为研究多体量子系统提供了高效的数值工具。

Abstract: We show how one may perform a stochastic unraveling which respects weak permutation symmetry for models of $N$ emitters coupled to a common system (e.g. a cavity mode). For problems involving 2-level emitters, such an unravelling reduces the computational cost from $\mathcal{O}(N^5)$ to $\mathcal{O}(N^2)$, and with additional refinements, allows reduction to $\mathcal{O}(N)$. This significantly increases the range of system sizes for which one can model exact quantum dynamics of such systems. We further show how the method can also be applied to d-level systems, with computational effort scaling as $\mathcal{O}(N^{d(d-1)/2})$, and we show it allows large-N simulations for d=3.

</details>


### [127] [Lecture Notes on Replica Tensor Networks for Random Quantum Circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11150)
*Xhek Turkeshi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文以教学为导向，系统介绍了用于随机量子电路的副本张量网络（replica tensor-network）技术。核心思想是将电路平均可观测量的计算转化为经典张量网络的缩并问题，等价于一个统计力学模型（statistical-mechanics model）的配分函数。该方法具有普适性：改变可观测量或初态仅改变副本边界条件，改变电路系综则改变体张量。文章以量子信息诊断为例展示了该方法在干净和噪声随机幺正电路中的应用，并简要说明如何推广至正交系综（orthogonal ensemble）或克利福德电路（Clifford circuit）。附带的ReplicaTN库提供了C++/Python实现及教学笔记本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机量子电路在量子信息科学中有广泛应用，但电路平均可观测量的解析或数值计算往往非常复杂。现有方法缺乏统一且直观的教学框架，限制了研究者（尤其是初学者）对该领域技术的掌握。

Method: 提出副本张量网络方法：将电路平均可观测量重新表述为经典张量网络的缩并（contraction），等价于一个统计力学模型的配分函数，其中有效自旋（effective spins）生活在门系综的交换子空间（commutant of the gate ensemble）中。该方法通过修改副本边界条件适应不同的可观测量和初态，通过修改体张量适应不同的电路系综。

Result: 在干净和噪声随机幺正电路上，成功应用该方法计算了波函数扩散度量（wavefunction spreading metrics）和纠缠量化器（entanglement quantifiers）等量子信息诊断量。并简要展示了方法可扩展至正交系综和克利福德电路等其他系综。

Conclusion: 副本张量网络技术为一类随机量子电路的平均可观测量计算提供了统一、通用的框架，具备良好的可教学性和可扩展性。附带的ReplicaTN开源库降低了该技术的使用门槛，有助于推动其在量子信息及相关领域中的更广泛应用。

Abstract: We present a pedagogical, hands-on tutorial on \emph{replica tensor-network} techniques for random quantum circuits. At its core, the method recasts circuit-averaged observables acting on multiple copies of the system as the contraction of a classical tensor network, equivalently the partition function of a statistical-mechanics model whose effective spins live in the commutant of the gate ensemble. The framework is general: changing the observable or the initial state modifies only the replica boundary conditions, while changing the ensemble modifies the bulk tensors. Focusing on quantum-information diagnostics, from metrics of wavefunction spreadings to entanglement quantifiers, we illustrate the approach in both clean and noisy random unitary circuits. We then briefly explain how the methodology extends to other ensembles, such as orthogonal or Clifford circuits. The lecture notes are accompanied by \texttt{ReplicaTN}, a self-contained C++/Python library and pedagogical notebooks.

</details>


### [128] [Quantum tunneling, global phases and the limits of classical action reconstructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11252)
*Chong Qi,Mário B. Amaro*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文检验了通过经典作用量分支（classical action branches）离散叠加精确重构薛定谔波函数（Schrödinger wave function）的方案的可行性，发现该方案在量子隧穿（quantum tunneling）和量子相位现象（quantum phase phenomena）中因缺乏实经典作用量而失效，必须引入非零量子势（quantum potential）或复值作用量（complex-valued action），且全局边界条件（global boundary conditions）提供的增长势垒分量及全局相位约束不可由局域实经典轨迹（local real classical trajectories）获得。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证近期提出的、无需半经典近似即可从经典作用量分支的离散叠加精确重建薛定谔波函数的方案在量子隧穿及量子相位现象中的有效性与局限性。

Method: 通过有限势垒量子隧穿和量子相位现象（包括α衰变与核聚变中的矩形势垒和库仑势垒隧穿、贝里相位、磁通量子化、约瑟夫森隧穿及dc SQUID干涉）对该重建方案进行理论检验。

Result: 当哈密顿-雅可比方程（Hamilton-Jacobi equation）存在全局定义的实分支时该构造在形式上成立，但在经典禁区（classically forbidden regions）中因缺乏实经典作用量而失效；波函数需要非零量子势或复值作用量；由全局边界条件决定的增长势垒分量对透射至关重要，且无法从局域实经典轨迹导出；贝里相位（Berry phase）、磁通量子化（flux quantization）、约瑟夫森隧穿（Josephson tunneling）及dc SQUID干涉均施加了局域经典作用量输运所不具备的全局相位约束。

Conclusion: 该重建方案在隧穿和量子相位现象中本质上是有限的，必须借助量子势或复值作用量，且全局边界条件和全局相位约束在这些过程中起不可或缺的作用，仅依靠局域实经典轨迹不足以描述此类量子效应。

Abstract: It was proposed recently that the Schrödinger wave function can be reconstructed exactly from a discrete superposition of classical action branches weighted by associated classical densities, without semiclassical approximations. We examine this construction for quantum tunneling through finite potential barriers and for quantum phase phenomena. Although formally consistent when the Hamilton-Jacobi equation admits globally defined real branches, the construction breaks down in classically forbidden regions where no real classical action exists. Using rectangular and Coulomb barrier tunneling in alpha decay and nuclear fusion, we show that the wave function requires either a non-vanishing quantum potential or complex-valued action. The growing barrier component fixed by global boundary conditions is essential for transmission and cannot arise from local real classical trajectories alone. Berry phase, flux quantization, Josephson tunneling, and dc SQUID interference likewise impose global phase constraints absent from local classical action transport.

</details>


### [129] [Squeezing and adiabaticity breaking in time-dependent quantum harmonic oscillators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12124)
*Mattia Orlandini,Beatrice Donelli,Lorenzo Buffoni,Stefano Gherardini*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了含时频率量子谐振子的严格求解方法，重点阐述了Lewis-Riesenfeld不变量方法、Bogoliubov变换与Ermakov-Pinney方程的统一框架，并将其与压缩（squeezing）效应和绝热性破坏相联系，覆盖了从突然淬火到平滑扫描的多种频率协议。该综述为理解二次势中的非平衡动力学提供了综合性工具，应用领域涵盖热力学、凝聚态物理和量子控制理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 含时频率量子谐振子是驱动量子动力学的典范模型，且是少数存在精确解析解的非平凡系统。现有方法较为分散，需要一份统一的综述来整合Lewis-Riesenfeld不变量方法、Bogoliubov变换和Ermakov-Pinney方程等不同工具。

Method: 本文采用综述性方法，基于Lewis-Riesenfeld不变量方法（Lewis-Riesenfeld invariant method）、Bogoliubov变换（Bogoliubov transformations）和Ermakov-Pinney方程（Ermakov-Pinney equation）构建统一处理框架，并将这些方法与压缩描述及绝热性破坏（breakdown of adiabaticity）建立自然联系。

Result: 文章详细讨论了突然淬火（sudden quenches）和平滑扫描（smooth ramps）下的精确结果，阐明了不变量方法与压缩形式（squeezing formalism）之间的显式桥梁。

Conclusion: 该综述为理解二次势中的非平衡动力学（nonequilibrium dynamics）提供了全面框架，其应用范围涵盖热力学（thermodynamics）、凝聚态物理（condensed matter）和量子控制理论（quantum control theory）。

Abstract: The quantum harmonic oscillator with time-dependent frequency is a paradigmatic model of driven quantum dynamics and one of the few nontrivial systems that admits an exact analytical solution. In this review paper, we present a unified treatment of the time-dependent oscillator based on the Lewis-Riesenfeld invariant method, Bogoliubov transformations and the Ermakov-Pinney equation. We show how these approaches naturally connect to squeezing for the description of excitations production, and to the breakdown of adiabaticity under generic frequency protocols. Exact results for sudden quenches and smooth ramps are discussed in detail. By explicitly bridging invariant methods and squeezing formalism, this review is meant to provide a comprehensive framework for understanding nonequilibrium dynamics in quadratic potentials, with applications ranging from thermodynamics and condensed matter to quantum control theory.

</details>


### [130] [Understanding oxide-thickness-dependent variability in dense Si-MOS quantum dot arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12143)
*Arne Loenders,Jacques Van Damme,Clement Godfrin,Paola Favia,Jacopo Franco,Thomas Van Caekenberghe,Bart Raes,Gulzat Jaliel,Sylvain Baudot,Luis Francisco Pinotti,Alexander Grill,George Simion,Kristof Moors,Vukan Levajac,Sofie Beyne,Sugandha Sharma,Stefan Kubicek,Yosuke Shimura,Roger Loo,Massimo Mongillo,Danny Wan,Kristiaan De Greve*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用300毫米CMOS工艺结合极紫外光刻（EUV lithography）制备7x7硅量子点阵列，在四种不同氧化物厚度下，利用基于行的并行测量方法（row based measurements）统计表征了392个量子点的阈值电压（threshold voltage）、电容（capacitance）、杠杆臂（lever arm）及充电能（charging energy）。

Result: 识别出17 nm SiO2为最优厚度，可将阈值电压标准差降至63 mV以下；观察到多种无序源（multiple sources of disorder）引入竞争的氧化物厚度依赖性（competing oxide-thickness dependencies），导致非单调变化趋势。

Conclusion: 结果为密集可扩展硅自旋量子比特架构提供了关键设计指导，表明通过优化栅极氧化物厚度可有效改善量子点阵列的均匀性。

Abstract: Achieving uniform and scalable control of semiconductor spin qubits remains a key challenge for large scale quantum computing. In this work, we investigate how gate oxide thickness influences uniformity in dense two dimensional silicon quantum dot arrays. Using a 7 x 7 array fabricated in a 300 mm CMOS-process patterned by EUV lithography, we statistically characterize 392 quantum dots across four different oxide thicknesses. The threshold voltages, capacitances, lever arms, and charging energies are extracted using parallel row based measurements and we identify an optimal SiO2 thickness of 17 nm that minimizes threshold voltage variability below 63 mV standard deviation. Our observations illustrate how multiple sources of disorder can introduce competing oxide-thickness dependencies, resulting in non-monotonic trends. These results provide key design guidelines for dense, scalable silicon spin qubit architectures.

### [131] [Scalable Measurement-Based Quantum Simulation Patterns for Benchmarking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12502)
*V. W. Scarola*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发布了QPatLib（Quantum Measurement Pattern Library）v1.0，这是一个用于测量型量子计算（measurement-based quantum computing）的量子测量模式（measurement pattern）数据集，专注于提供量子模拟中所需的Pauli字符串酉算子（Pauli-string unitary）执行模式及基准测试模式，旨在作为模式优化协议的标准测试平台，并支持直接硬件使用与未来扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量型量子计算中的模式优化受硬件与软件约束的多变量影响，具有高度依赖性与复杂性，大规模模式在现实假设下的优化仍存在障碍，亟需标准化的基准数据集来支撑优化协议开发与验证。

Method: 提出了一套生成用于量子模拟的Pauli字符串酉算子执行模式的工作流，并定义了不同的可交换Pauli字符串子集（commuting Pauli-string subsets）约定，以调控模式的规模与复杂度。

Abstract: Measurement-based quantum computing uses measurement patterns on predefined quantum resource states to execute quantum logic. Quantum simulation offers an important use case on near-term devices. However, pattern optimization depends on the multivariable interplay between hardware and software constraints and is therefore use-dependent and highly non-trivial. Optimization of large-scale patterns under realistic assumptions remains a barrier. We announce the release of the quantum measurement pattern library QPatLib, a dataset that, in v1.0, presents patterns for use in measurement-based quantum simulation. We present the workflow for generating patterns that execute Pauli-string unitaries needed for many quantum algorithms. We provide benchmark patterns for measurement-based quantum unitary evolution. The measurement patterns are defined with different conventions for commuting Pauli-string subsets to allow scaling of pattern size and complexity. The purpose of the library is to (i) serve as a standardized testbed for pattern-optimization protocols for measurement-based quantum simulation routines, (ii) offer a suite of patterns for direct use on hardware, (iii) provide data to empirically justify pattern design principles, and (iv) provide a flexible resource for future storage and use of measurement-based patterns beyond quantum simulation.

### [132] [Outer Detector of Hyper-Kamiokande](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11580)
*R. Shinoda*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文报告了Hyper-Kamiokande（HK）外层探测器（Outer Detector, OD）中8 cm光电倍增管（PMT）的选型过程，最终采用滨松（Hamamatsu）R14374型PMT，并基于全探测器模拟评估了其对宇宙线μ子本底的排除性能。单独OD切割可将μ子本底压低至$O(10^{-6})$量级，结合有效体积切割（fiducial volume cuts）后可达$O(10^{-9})$，对核子衰变和大气中微子分析的影响可忽略不计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hyper-Kamiokande作为世界最大的水切伦科夫环形成像探测器（water Cherenkov ring-imaging detector），其外层探测器（OD）需要高效排除来自外部的背景事件（尤其是宇宙线μ子），以保障内探测器（Inner Detector）中物理分析的敏感性，因此需要为OD选择性能最优的光电倍增管（PMT）。

Method: 对比了两种8 cm直径PMT候选型号——滨松R14374与NNVT N2031，并利用全探测器模拟（full detector simulation）评估了宇宙线μ子背景的压低性能。

Result: 滨松PMT因其在深紫外（deep-UV）波段具有更优的入水探测效率（in-water detection efficiency）和稳定性而被采用。仅基于OD的切割即可将宇宙线μ子排除效率压低至$O(10^{-6})$量级（即残留率），结合有效体积切割（fiducial volume cuts）后预期可达$O(10^{-9})$。

Conclusion: 所选的滨松PMT与OD方案能够将宇宙线μ子本底压低至足够低的水平，对核子衰变（nucleon decay）和大气中微子（atmospheric neutrino）分析的影响可忽略不计。

Abstract: Hyper-Kamiokande (HK) is the world's largest water Cherenkov ring-imaging detector, planning to start data taking in 2028. The Outer Detector (OD) surrounds the Inner Detector and plays a critical role in rejecting background events entering from outside, particularly cosmic-ray muons. We report on the selection of $8\,\mathrm{cm}$ diameter photomultiplier tubes (PMTs) for the OD, comparing Hamamatsu R14374 and NNVT N2031 candidates, and present the evaluation of cosmic-ray muon background reduction performance using a full detector simulation. Hamamatsu PMTs were adopted for their superior in-water detection efficiency in deep-UV and stability. The cosmic-ray muon reduction inefficiency reaches $O(10^{-6})$ with OD-based cuts alone, and $O(10^{-9})$ is expected when combined with fiducial volume cuts, which is sufficiently negligible for nucleon decay and atmospheric neutrino analyses.

</details>


### [133] [CaloArt: Large-Patch x-Prediction Diffusion Transformers for High-Granularity Calorimeter Shower Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12011)
*Zhengkun Huang,Gongxing Sun*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出 CaloArt，一种基于大块令牌化（large-patch tokenization）和 x-预测（x-prediction）的现代化 DiT 风格扩散变压器（diffusion transformer），用于高粒度量能器（calorimeter）的快速簇射模拟。在 CaloChallenge 数据集上，该方法在保持每簇射 O(10) ms 单 GPU 生成时间的同时，取得了最优的 FPD 和高层指标，证明了无需预训练潜编码器即可实现高效的高粒度簇射合成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高粒度量能器使得基于机器学习的快速簇射模拟成为一个高维生成建模问题，体素空间生成器必须在物理保真度与训练及推理成本之间取得平衡。现有方法在小体素规模下尚可，但面对大规模体素网格（如 40500 体素）时面临计算瓶颈，亟需一种无需预训练潜编码器（pretrained latent tokenizer）的高效生成方案。

Method: 提出 CaloArt 架构，采用大块令牌化（large-patch tokenization）与 x-预测（x-prediction）实现高效的原始体素生成。模型基于现代化 DiT 风格骨干网络，引入 3D 位置编码（3D positional encoding）与架构改进，通过条件流匹配（conditional flow matching）进行训练，并采用解耦的预测空间与损失空间（decoupled prediction and loss spaces）策略。

Result: 在 CaloChallenge Dataset 2 上，小块规模仍可行时 v-预测表现良好，CaloArt 取得最佳 FPD（Fréchet Physics Distance）、最强高层指标及最优 ResNet 分类器指标。在 CaloChallenge Dataset 3（40500 体素网格）上，大块成为必要，x-预测在所有指标上均优于 v-预测，使 CaloArt 处于质量-生成时间帕累托前沿（Pareto frontier）。最终模型在 CCD2 和 CCD3 上分别保持 9.71 ms 和 11.14 ms 每簇射的单 GPU 生成时间。

Conclusion: 大块体素空间扩散变压器结合 x-预测是实现高粒度量能器簇射合成的计算高效路径，能够在不依赖预训练潜编码器的情况下降低训练与推理成本。

Abstract: High-granularity calorimeters make ML-based fast shower simulation a high-dimensional generative modeling problem, where voxel-space generators must balance physics fidelity with training and inference cost. This work studies large-patch tokenization with x-prediction, enabling efficient raw voxel generation. We propose CaloArt, a modernized DiT-style backbone with 3D positional encoding and architectural refinements, trained via conditional flow matching with decoupled prediction and loss spaces. On CaloChallenge Dataset 2, where small patch size remains affordable, v-prediction performs well, and CaloArt achieves the best FPD, strongest high-level metrics, and strongest ResNet classifier metrics. On CaloChallenge Dataset 3, the 40500-voxel grid makes large patches necessary; x-prediction improves all reported metrics over v-prediction and places CaloArt on the quality-generation-time Pareto frontier. The final CCD2 and CCD3 models both retain O(10) ms single-GPU generation time, with 9.71 and 11.14 ms per shower. These results support large-patch voxel-space diffusion transformers with x-prediction as a compute-efficient route to high-granularity calorimeter shower synthesis, reducing training and inference cost without a pretrained latent tokenizer.

</details>


### [134] [Bridging the Gap between Extreme Environments and Precision Measurements: Recent Progress in Megagauss Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11379)
*Shojiro Takeyama*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本综述聚焦单匝线圈（STC）和电磁磁通压缩（EMFC）两种技术，系统回顾了在100~T至1000~T超强脉冲磁场中实现高精度材料科学测量的最新进展，包括EMFC突破千特斯拉、定制化低温测量平台建设，以及多种强关联与低维体系中的量子现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超强磁场（100~T至1000~T）只能由破坏性脉冲磁体产生，而现有多种产生方法中，需要确定哪些技术能为材料科学中的高精度测量提供最佳环境，并系统梳理其最新突破与实验基础设施。

Method: 综述以单匝线圈（Single-Turn Coil, STC）和电磁磁通压缩（Electromagnetic Flux Compression, EMFC）两种技术为核心，并描述了配套的磁光、磁化、磁输运测量基础设施，包括微型全塑料低温恒温器（miniaturized all-plastic cryostat）和定制样品架，以兼容低温与兆高斯（megagauss）场双极端条件。

Result: EMFC方法近期取得技术突破，已成功实现超过1000~T的磁场强度；利用上述平台揭示了阻挫磁体中的量子相变（quantum phase transition）、碳纳米管中的阿哈罗诺夫–玻姆效应（Aharonov–Bohm effect），以及强关联系统中的半导体–金属转变（semiconductor-to-metal transition）。

Conclusion: 在超强脉冲磁场领域，通过仪器和实验精炼（instrumentation and experimental refinements）可确保可靠的数据采集；未来应进一步关注磁致伸缩（magnetostriction）、比热（specific heat）和超声速度（ultrasound velocity）等新兴测量平台。

Abstract: Ultrastrong magnetic fields, ranging from 100~T to 1,000~T, are generated exclusively by destructive pulsed magnets. While various generation methods exist, this review focuses on the Single-Turn Coil (STC) and Electromagnetic Flux Compression (EMFC) techniques, which provide optimal environments for high-precision measurements in materials science. First, we present recent technological breakthroughs in the EMFC method that have successfully achieved fields exceeding 1,000~T. We then describe specialized measurement infrastructures for magneto-optics, magnetization, and magneto-transport, highlighting the development of miniaturized all-plastic cryostats and custom sample holders designed for the dual extremes of cryogenic temperatures and megagauss fields. Representative physical phenomena revealed through these techniques are discussed, including quantum phase transitions in frustrated magnets, Aharonov--Bohm effects in carbon nanotubes, and semiconductor-to-metal transitions in strongly correlated systems. Furthermore, we address emerging measurement platforms such as magnetostriction, specific heat, and ultrasound velocity. Throughout this review, we emphasize the instrumentation and experimental refinements that ensure reliable data acquisition in the ultrastrong pulsed field regime.

</details>

### [135] [MeVPrtl: An Event Generator for Dark Sector Particles in the Short-Baseline Neutrino Program](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11321)
*ICARUS Collaboration,SBND Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: MeVPrtl 是一个面向短基线中微子（SBN）计划开发的模块化事件生成器，用于模拟超出标准模型（BSM）的新粒子在费米实验室束流中产生、传播至探测器并衰变为标准模型（SM）粒子的过程。该工具已实现了 Higgs 门户（Higgs portal）、重中性轻子（heavy neutral lepton）和重 QCD 轴子（heavy QCD axion）等模型，并提供了与 SBN 计划基于 LArSoft 的探测器模拟相衔接的接口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超出标准模型（BSM）的新物理模型——如暗物质（dark matter）、中微子质量尺度和强 CP 问题（strong CP problem）的解决方案——预测新粒子可在费米实验室的强束流中产生、传播至 SBN 探测器并衰变。为系统模拟这些过程，需要一个模块化的事件生成器。

Method: MeVPrtl 提供了模块化接口（interface），用于实现不同 BSM 模型的重叠现象学（overlapping phenomenology），并将介子流输入（meson flux inputs）与 SBN 计划中基于 LArSoft 的探测器模拟所需的输出对象相连接。论文详细说明了接口规范，并在 MeVPrtl 中实现了 Higgs 门户、重中性轻子和重 QCD 轴子三个模型的代码及验证。

Result: 在 MeVPrtl 内完成了 Higgs 门户、重中性轻子和重 QCD 轴子模型的代码实现与验证工作。论文对这些实现及其验证结果进行了详细说明。

Conclusion: MeVPrtl 作为一个模块化事件生成器，能够有效支持 SBN 计划中 BSM 新物理信号的模拟需求，其提供的接口可灵活适配多种新物理模型。

Abstract: MeVPrtl is a modular event generator of beyond the Standard Model (BSM) physics particles developed for use in the Short-Baseline Neutrino (SBN) Program. A large class of BSM physics models predict that new particles could be produced in the intense Booster Neutrino Beam (BNB) and Neutrinos at the Main Injector (NuMI) beams at Fermilab, travel to the SBN Program detectors, and decay into Standard Model (SM) particles. These new physics models are motivated by dark matter, the neutrino mass scale, and a solution to the strong CP problem. MeVPrtl provides an interface to implement the overlapping phenomenology of these models, and to connect them with meson flux inputs and object outputs used by the SBN Program's LArSoft-based detector simulation. Implementations for the Higgs portal, heavy neutral lepton, and heavy QCD axion models exist within MeVPrtl. In this paper these implementations and their validation, as well as details of the MeVPrtl interface, are specified.

</details>

Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文首次报道了 $D^{+} \rightarrow K_{S}^{0}K_{L}^{0}\pi^{+}$ 衰变的振幅分析和分支比测量，基于 BESIII 探测器在质心能量 3.773 GeV 处收集的 20.3 $\rm fb^{-1}$ 数据。实验测得的分支比为 $(5.780\pm0.085\pm 0.052)\times10^{-3}$，并利用已知的 $D^+ \to \phi\pi^+$ 分支比，确定了 $\phi\to K_{S}^0K_{L}^0$ 与 $\phi\to K^+K^-$ 的相对分支比为 $0.628\pm0.022\pm 0.015\pm0.017$，该结果显著低于此前世界平均值，但与 $\phi$ 介子同位旋（isospin）预期一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对 $D^{+} \rightarrow K_{S}^{0}K_{L}^{0}\pi^{+}$ 衰变进行首次振幅分析和分支比测量，以检验 $\phi$ 介子衰变到中性及带电 kaon 对的同位旋关系，并澄清此前世界平均值与理论预期之间的偏差。

Method: 利用 BESIII 探测器在质心能量 3.773 GeV 处采集的 20.3 $\rm fb^{-1}$ 数据，对 $D^{+} \rightarrow K_{S}^{0}K_{L}^{0}\pi^{+}$ 衰变开展振幅分析并测量分支比。通过已知的 ${\cal B}(D^+ \to \phi\pi^+,\,\phi\to K^+K^-)$ 值，推导 $\phi\to K_{S}^0K_{L}^0$ 与 $\phi\to K^+K^-$ 的相对分支比。

Result: 测得 $D^{+} \rightarrow K_{S}^{0}K_{L}^{0}\pi^{+}$ 分支比为 $(5.780\pm0.085\pm 0.052)\times10^{-3}$，其中第一项为统计不确定度（statistical uncertainty），第二项为系统不确定度（systematic uncertainty）。相对分支比 $\mathcal{B}(D^{+} \to \phi\pi^{+}, \phi\to K_{S}^0K_{L}^0)/\mathcal{B}(D^{+} \to \phi\pi^{+}, \phi\to K^+K^-)= 0.628\pm0.022\pm 0.015\pm0.017$，第三项不确定度来源于 $\mathcal{B}(D^{+} \to \phi\pi^{+}, \phi\to K^+K^-)$。

Conclusion: 该相对分支比结果显著低于此前世界平均值（world average），但与 $\phi$ 介子耦合到带电及中性 kaon 对的同位旋预期一致，表明实验数据支持同位旋对称性（isospin symmetry）在 $\phi$ 介子衰变中的适用性。

Abstract: We present the first amplitude analysis and branching fraction measurement of $D^{+} \rightarrow K_{S}^{0}K_{L}^{0}π^{+}$ decay. The analysis uses a dataset corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 20.3~$\rm fb^{-1}$, which was recorded at a center-of-mass energy 3.773~GeV by the BESIII detector. The measured branching fraction is $\mathcal{B}(D^{+} \rightarrow K_{S}^{0}K_{L}^{0}π^{+})=(5.780\pm0.085\pm 0.052)\times10^{-3}$, where the first uncertainty is statistical and the second is systematic. Using the known value of ${\cal B}(D^+ \to φπ^+,\,φ\to K^+K^-)$, we determine the relative branching fraction between $φ\to K_{S}^0K_{L}^0$ and $φ\to K^+K^-$ to be $\mathcal{B}(D^{+} \to φπ^{+}, φ\to K_{S}^0K_{L}^0)/\mathcal{B}(D^{+} \to φπ^{+}, φ\to K^+K^-)= 0.628\pm0.022\pm 0.015\pm0.017$, where the third uncertainty is related to $\mathcal{B}(D^{+} \to φπ^{+}, φ\to K^+K^-)$. This result is significantly lower than the previous world average and is consistent with the isospin expectation for the $φ$ meson's coupling to charged and neutral kaon pairs.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CEBAF大接受谱仪CLAS12在核子与原子核结构研究中发挥了核心作用。随着实验数据精度不断提高，出现了超越CLAS12现有能力的新物理机遇，因此有必要提出新的实验方案以进一步探索核子的夸克与胶子结构。

Method: 采用μCLAS12实验装置，通过双缪子电产生（di-muon electroproduction）和光产生（photoproduction）过程进行测量。核心方法是通过测量双深虚康普顿散射（DDVCS）过程ep → e′μ+μ−p′中的束流自旋不对称性（beam-spin asymmetries），并独立改变入射与出射光子的虚度（virtualities）和动量转移。

Result: DDVCS测量可独立变化光子虚度和动量转移，因此能够获取广义部分子分布（Generalized Parton Distributions, GPDs）在全三维相空间中的信息，突破了深虚康普顿散射（DVCS）和类时康普顿散射（TCS）的动力学约束。此外，μCLAS12的大接受度和高亮度还将支持近阈值J/ψ产生的精确测量和高统计量的TCS研究。

Conclusion: 基于CLAS12升级的μCLAS12实验项目，通过DDVCS中的束流自旋不对称性测量，能够在全三维相空间提取GPDs，从而深化对核子内部夸克与胶子结构的理解，同时拓展了在近阈值J/ψ产生和TCS方面的精确测量能力。

Abstract: The CEBAF Large Acceptance Spectrometer for operation at 12 GeV (CLAS12) at the Thomas Jefferson National Accelerator Facility has played a central role in advancing the understanding of nucleon and nuclear structure. As increasingly precise data become available, new physics opportunities emerge that extend beyond the current capabilities of CLAS12. In this article, a program to explore the quark and gluon structure of the nucleon through di-muon electro- and photoproduction is presented. Its primary focus is the measurement of beam-spin asymmetries in Double Deeply Virtual Compton Scattering, $ep \rightarrow e^\prime μ^+ μ^-p^\prime $. By independently varying the incoming and outgoing photon virtualities and momentum transfer, the DDVCS measurement provides access to the Generalized Parton Distributions over their full three-dimensional phase space, extending beyond the kinematic constraints of Deeply Virtual Compton Scattering and Timelike Compton Scattering. In addition, the large acceptance and high luminosity of the $μ$CLAS12 experiment will enable precision measurements of near-threshold $J/ψ$ production and high-statistics studies of Timelike Compton Scattering.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Recent clinical evidence shows a correlation between linear energy transfer (LET) and tumor control in carbon ion radiotherapy. This prompts the direct inclusion of LET into the treatment planning. Currently, LET is mainly extracted from simulations. Good clinical practice requires adopting measurement routines that correlate with LET, such as microdosimetry. In this work, we describe an application-specific integrated circuit (ASIC) for reading out microdosimeteric sensors. The ASIC is designed for input capacitances up to 3 pF. It contains four readout channels, each with a different saturation charge ranging from 75 fC to 3.2 pC. In the 75 fC range, at 1 pF input capacitance and a shaping time of 1 microseconds, the ASIC has an equivalent noise contribution (ENC) below 15 electrons at ambient temperature. This low noise level is expected to enable new measurement possibilities, including the assessment of microdosimetric proton spectra in the low-LET region of the entrance channel, as well as studying the contribution of delta electrons.

Abstract: We present novel, ultra-thin, large-diameter silicon nitride windows for various soft X-ray applications. ### [140] [Novel Machine Learning Methods to Improve Z Pole Integrated Luminosity at Future Colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12407)
*Brendon Madison*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究针对未来Z极点正负电子对撞机（$e^+e^-$ collider）积分亮度（integrated luminosity）测量中$\frac{δL}{L}<10^{-4}$的精度需求，系统分析了双光子（diphoton/$\gamma\gamma$）道的两个主要不确定度来源：使用梯度提升决策树（BDTG）和自适应符号记忆回归（ASMR）分别处理本底和束流偏转偏差问题，结果表明升级后的亮度量能器（LumiCal）可抑制小角巴巴散射（SABS）本底，ASMR将束流偏转不确定度降至$5\times10^{-6}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来Z极点$e^+e^-$对撞机要求积分亮度测量的相对精度达到$\frac{δL}{L}<10^{-4}$，除标准的小角巴巴散射（SABS）道外，$\gamma\gamma$事件可提供互补测量手段，但需解决其主导不确定度问题。

Method: 首先，通过粒子识别对$\gamma\gamma$道的本底进行分析，识别出SABS和低不变质量（low-invariant-mass）中性强子为最重要本底，并采用梯度提升决策树（BDTG）进行事件分类。其次，针对束流偏转偏差（beam deflection bias）问题，分别使用BDTG和新提出的自适应符号记忆回归（ASMR）进行逐事件（event-by-event）求解。

Result: 分类结果表明，现有和升级版的前向径迹探测器（forward tracker）及亮度量能器（LumiCal）设计均可抑制中性强子本底，但只有升级版LumiCal能将SABS本底抑制到$\frac{δL}{L}<10^{-4}$水平。在束流偏转问题上，ASMR优于BDTG，将不确定度降至$5\times10^{-6}$。

Conclusion: 双光子道的积分亮度测量需同时处理本底和束流偏转两大不确定度来源。LumiCal的升级对抑制SABS本底至关重要，而新提出的ASMR算法在束流偏转校正方面表现出显著优势，为实现$\frac{δL}{L}<10^{-4}$的精度目标提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Future $e^+e^-$ colliders at the Z pole place strong demands of $\frac{δL}{L}<10^{-4}$ on the integrated luminosity measurement. Small angle Bhabha scattering (SABS) remains the standard channel, while diphoton ($γγ$) events provide a complementary measurement. This contribution summarizes recent work on two dominant uncertainties. First, we investigate backgrounds to the diphoton channel and find that SABS and low-invariant-mass neutral hadrons are the most significant backgrounds. A gradient boosted decision tree (BDTG) is used to classify events by particle ID. The classification results show the existing and upgraded forward tracker and luminosity calorimeter (LumiCal) designs reject neutral hadrons but only the LumiCal upgrade can reject SABS at $\frac{δL}{L}<10^{-4}$. Second, we solve the beam deflection bias problem on an event-by-event basis using two machine learning algorithms. A BDTG and the newly written Adaptive Symbolic Memetic Regression (ASMR) are trained on beam deflection data. ASMR outperforms BDTG and provides a reduced uncertainty of $5\times10^{-6}$ for beam deflection.

The data collected with a liquid hydrogen target in 2016-2017 will soon bring new information on the transverse momentum and may allow for the first time to extract the transverse polarisation of quarks within an unpolarised nucleon described by the Boer-Mulders function. The unique data collected with a transversely polarised deuteron target have already improved the knowledge of the d-quark transversity (transverse counterpart of the helicity PDF), reducing the uncertainties by a factor of 2.5 at large Bjorken x, and are yet to yield a number of interesting results.

### [143] [Sharp feature-learning transitions and Bayes-optimal neural scaling laws in extensive-width networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.10395)
*Minh-Toan Nguyen,Jean Barbier*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文研究了从带噪查询中学习具有层次特征（hierarchical features）的单隐层教师网络（teacher network）在知识蒸馏（knowledge transfer）至更小学生模型（student model）时的信息论极限。在高维教师宽度（width）$k \propto d$ 的设定下，通过启发式留一解耦（leave-one-out decoupling）论证，导出了贝叶斯最优（Bayes-optimal）泛化误差与特征重叠（feature overlap）的精确刻画。揭示了特征可学习性由一系列尖锐相变（phase transitions）控制：随着数据量增长，教师特征依次通过不连续跳跃被恢复，由此定义了有效宽度（effective width）$k_c$，统一了两种不同的标度律（scaling regimes）：特征学习区（feature-learning regime）泛化误差 $\varepsilon^{\rm BO} \sim n^{1/(2\beta)-1}$ 与精炼区（refinement regime）的 $\varepsilon^{\rm BO} \sim n^{-1}$，两者均坍缩为统一的标度关系 $\varepsilon^{\rm BO} = \Theta(k_c d/n)$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在知识蒸馏（knowledge transfer）场景下，理解从带噪查询（noisy queries）中学习具有层次结构的教师网络（teacher network）时的信息论极限，是模型压缩与迁移学习中的核心理论问题。现有研究在高维大宽度设定下分析仍有限，本文试图填补这一空白。

Method: 采用启发式的留一解耦（leave-one-out decoupling）论证方法，并通过数值实验验证其有效性。在高维教师宽度 $k \propto d$ 的设定下推导出贝叶斯最优（Bayes-optimal）泛化误差与特征重叠（feature overlap）的闭式不动点方程组（fixed-point equations），以及基于层次特征指数 $\beta>1/2$ 的幂律特征层次（power-law feature hierarchy）。

Result: 特征的可学习性由一系列不连续的相变（phase transitions）控制，特征按层次依次被恢复。贝叶斯最优泛化误差（Bayes-optimal generalization error）在特征学习区（feature-learning regime）标度律为 $n^{1/(2\beta)-1}$，在精炼区（refinement regime）为 $n^{-1}$，两者统一为 $\varepsilon^{\rm BO} = \Theta(k_c d/n)$，其中 $k_c$ 为有效宽度（effective width）。使用 Adam 优化器训练的学生模型在接近 $k_c$ 时可实现上述最优标度律（仅存在小幅算法差距）。

Conclusion: 本文为层次特征的顺序性学习提供了精确的信息论刻画，揭示了有效宽度（effective width）$k_c$ 是连接数据预算（data budget）与模型容量的关键变量，并统一了两种不同的泛化误差标度律。同时为理解实际训练中的模型尺寸缩放（model size scaling）提供了信息论基础。

Abstract: We study the information-theoretic limits of learning a one-hidden-layer teacher network with hierarchical features from noisy queries, in the context of knowledge transfer to a smaller student model. We work in the high-dimensional regime where the teacher width $k$ scales linearly with the input dimension $d$ -- a setting that captures large-but-finite-width networks and has only recently become analytically tractable. Using a heuristic leave-one-out decoupling argument, validated numerically throughout, we derive asymptotically sharp characterizations of the Bayes-optimal generalization error and individual feature overlaps via a system of closed fixed-point equations. These equations reveal that feature learnability is governed by a sequence of sharp phase transitions: as data grows, teacher features become recoverable sequentially, each through a discontinuous jump in overlap. This sequential acquisition underlies a precise notion of \textit{effective width} $k_c$ -- the number of learnable features at a given data budget $n$ -- which unifies two distinct scaling regimes: a feature-learning regime in which the Bayes-optimal generalization error $\varepsilon^{\rm BO}$ scales as $ n^{1/(2β)-1}$, and a refinement regime in which it scales as $n^{-1}$, where $β>1/2$ is the exponent of the power-law feature hierarchy. Both laws collapse to the single relation $\varepsilon^{\rm BO}=Θ(k_c d/n)$. We further show empirically that a student trained with \textsc{Adam} near the effective width $k_c$ achieves these optimal scaling laws (up to a small algorithmic gap), and provide an information-theoretic account of the associated scaling in model size.

</details>

### [144] [Enhanced Photomultiplication Effect by Synergistic Integration of Hole-Blocking Layers and Trap Engineering in PM-OPDs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11923)
*Awais Sarwar,Louis Conrad Winkler,Anncharlott Kusber,Fred Kretschmer,Karl Leo,Hans Kleemann,Johannes Benduhn*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文通过低化学计量比的分子陷阱工程（molecular trap engineering），在真空蒸镀的有机光电探测器（PM-OPD）中引入低浓度（0.5 wt%）m-MTDATA作为空穴陷阱位点，实现增益-带宽权衡的缓解，在-4 V偏压下峰值外量子效率（EQE）超过1100%，-2 V偏压下比探测率（specific detectivity）达4×10¹² Jones，截止频率（f₋₃dB）为22 kHz。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统光倍增型有机光电探测器（PM-OPD）在弱光探测中虽具备高灵敏度，但普遍存在增益-带宽权衡（gain-bandwidth trade-off）：高外量子效率（EQE）伴随大暗电流和慢响应速度。该工作旨在通过结构设计和陷阱工程克服这一矛盾。

Method: 采用全真空蒸镀工艺制备PM-OPD，集成空穴阻挡层（hole-blocking layers）与低化学计量比分子陷阱工程。在BDP-OMe:C60体异质结（bulk heterojunction）中以0.5 wt%的低浓度掺入m-MTDATA作为专用空穴陷阱位点，实现离散陷阱态，最大化正空间电荷积累，从而在低于定域渗流（localized percolation）阈值的前提下触发高效场辅助电子注入。

Result: 优化器件在-4 V反向偏压下峰值EQE超过1100%；在-2 V反向偏压下比探测率达到4×10¹² Jones，截止频率（f₋₃dB）为22 kHz。

Conclusion: 通过在分子层面工程设计离散陷阱位点，可有效解耦光电流倍增机制与陷阱介导的暗电流分流（trap-mediated dark current shunts），从而在保持高增益的同时实现低暗电流和快速响应。

Abstract: Photomultiplication-type organic photodetectors (PM-OPDs) promise exceptional sensitivity for weak-light detection but typically suffer from a gain-bandwidth trade-off where high external quantum efficiency (EQE) incurs large dark current and slow response times. Here, we demonstrate a fully vacuum-deposited PM-OPD architecture that mitigates these limitations by integrating hole-blocking layers low-stoichiometry molecular trap engineering. We isolate discrete trapping sites that maximize positive space-charge accumulation by introducing m-MTDATA as a dedicated hole-trapping site at a low concentration (0.5 wt\%) into a BDP-OMe:C60 bulk heterojunction. This engineered charge confinement triggers efficient field-assisted electron injection from the anode while remaining strictly below the threshold for localized percolation, effectively decoupling the photocurrent multiplication mechanism from trap-mediated dark current shunts. Consequently, the optimized device achieves a peak EQE exceeding 1100% at a reverse bias of -4 V. The optimized device exhibits a specific detectivity of 4x10^{12} Jones under -2 V reverse bias along with a cutoff frequency (f-3dB) of 22 kHz.

</details>

### [145] [On the dilaton gravity of analogue black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11046)
*Paolo Castorina,Alfredo Iorio,Jakub Kris,Mohaddese Shams Nejati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了哪些膨胀引力（dilaton gravity）模型能够复现超导量子电路等平台中实现的典型二维类比黑洞（analogue black holes）。研究发现，这些类比黑洞与已知的膨胀引力模型不对应，从而限制了其理论价值；但通过反转逻辑，可以从已知膨胀模型反推出实验实现所需的条件，将挑战从理论转向实验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定哪些膨胀引力模型能够复现超导量子电路等平台中实现的二维类比黑洞，并检验这些模型是否具有可开关的温度态依赖性（state-dependence）——这一特征在四维黑洞中是不存在的。

Method: 首先假设膨胀引力模型必须满足的合理条件，分析霍金温度（Hawking temperature, T）的态依赖性是否可以开关；在温度与态无关的情况下，探讨温度运动学（kinematics）与熵动力学（dynamics）之间的解耦关系。随后通过数值分析比较类比黑洞与已知膨胀引力模型的对应关系，最后反转逻辑，从已知膨胀模型推导实验室实现必须满足的条件。

Result: 所考察的类比黑洞并不对应任何已知的膨胀引力模型，这限制了其提取理论见解的效用；但结果表明，可以从已知膨胀模型出发，逆向推导出实验室实现应满足的条件。

Conclusion: 该研究将核心挑战从理论侧转移至实验实现侧：与其寻找现有类比黑洞对应的理论模型，不如从已知膨胀理论出发，引导实验构造符合理论要求的类比黑洞系统。

Abstract: We investigate which dilaton gravity models can reproduce the typical two dimensional analogue black holes realized in platforms such as superconducting quantum circuits. We identify the most reasonable assumptions these models must satisfy, and determine the dilaton models for which the state-dependence of the Hawking temperature, T, can be switched on and off, a feature that is absent in four dimensional black holes. When the analogue black hole exhibits state-independent temperature, as in the cases considered here, the kinematics governing T decouples from the dynamics underlying S. Our numerical analysis reveals that the given analogue black holes do not correspond to known dilaton gravity models, limiting their usefulness for extracting theoretical insights. We then show that the logic can be easily reversed: starting from established well known dilaton models, one can derive the conditions that laboratory implementations must satisfy. This shifts the challenge from the theoretical perspective to the experimental realization.

</details>


### [146] [CMB Birefringence from Vacuum Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11065)
*Nemanja Kaloper*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出宇宙微波背景辐射偏振旋转（$Δ\vartheta \sim 10^{-3}$ rad）并非必须由超轻轴子（ultralight axion）的晚期动力学解释，而是源于光子穿越暗扇区（dark sector）不同真空之间拓扑界面时获得的几何界面相位，该效应受低能有效理论中涌现的1-形式对称性（$1$-form symmetry）保护，使得宇宙双折射（cosmic birefringence）成为探测暗扇区真空结构的探针，而非轻场动力学的探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有解释将CMB偏振旋转归因于超轻轴子的动力学，但该方案需要极轻的标量自由度，理论动机存在争议。本文旨在论证这类超轻自由度并非必要，并提出一种基于真空拓扑界面相位的新机制。

Method: 通过分析光子跨越暗扇区拓扑不同真空之间界面时产生的几何相位（Pancharatnam phase），并引入壁支撑的电磁Chern–Simons相互作用（wall-supported electromagnetic Chern–Simons interaction），结合低能有效理论中涌现的1-形式对称性（$1$-form symmetry）来刻画该离散相移的受保护性质。

Result: 该机制可复现轻轴子畴壁（light axion domain walls）导致的绝热旋转（adiabatic rotation），但对于任意薄的畴壁（轴子很重或不存在）依然成立，此时旋转表现为与红移和光子频率无关的Pancharatnam相位，在自然紫外截断（ultraviolet cutoff）以下具有普适性。

Conclusion: 宇宙双折射（cosmic birefringence）应当被理解为对暗扇区真空结构的探针，而非对轻场动力学（light-field dynamics）的探针，从而为CMB偏振观测提供全新的理论框架。

Abstract: Hints of cosmic microwave background polarization rotation ($Δ\vartheta \sim 10^{-3}$ rad) are commonly attributed to late-time dynamics of ultralight axions. We show that such ultralight degrees of freedom are not required. Polarization rotation naturally arises as a geometric interface phase acquired when photons cross interfaces between topologically distinct dark sector vacua. The effect is a discrete phase shift fixed by the normalization of a wall-supported electromagnetic Chern--Simons interaction and protected by an emergent $1$-form symmetry of the low energy effective theory. This mechanism reproduces the familiar adiabatic rotation induced by light axion domain walls, but persists for arbitrarily thin walls where the axion is heavy or absent. In this regime the rotation manifests as a Pancharatnam phase localized at vacuum interfaces, independent of redshift and photon frequency below a natural ultraviolet cutoff. Cosmic birefringence thus emerges as a probe of vacuum structure in the dark sector, rather than of light-field dynamics.

</details>


### [147] [Towards the Realization of the Dark Dimension Scenario in Hořava-Witten Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11068)
*Ralph Blumenhagen,Antonia Paraskevopoulou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文探讨了Hořava-Witten理论作为暗维度场景（Dark Dimension Scenario）具体实现的可能性，指出在包含阿贝尔因子的通用向量丛下，E₈壁上的对称 tadpole 消去可以缓解质子衰变过快等问题。结合暗能量和标准模型规范耦合的约束，研究导向一个特殊的无穷远极限——M理论涌现提议（Emergence Proposal）在Hořava-Witten理论中的类比。通过外推BPS饱和振幅的结果，推测标量势、规范耦合和普朗克尺度的模依赖可由单圈Schwinger积分获得。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究提出Hořava-Witten理论可能为暗维度场景提供具体实现，但该实现存在质子衰变过快等问题。本文旨在通过对称tadpole消去机制改善这些问题，并探索暗能量和规范耦合约束所指向的特殊极限。

Method: 论文基于Hořava-Witten理论框架，考虑支持包含阿贝尔因子的通用向量丛（vector bundle）的Calabi-Yau流形，分析E₈壁上的对称tadpole消去。研究同时利用暗能量的层级小值（hierarchically small value）和标准模型规范耦合大小作为约束条件，并外推BPS饱和振幅的结果。

Result: 对称tadpole消去有助于缓解质子衰变过快等问题。暗能量和规范耦合的约束导向一个特殊无穷远极限，即Hořava-Witten理论中对应于M理论涌现提议的极限。研究推测标量势、规范耦合和普朗克尺度（Planck scale）的模依赖可由单圈Schwinger积分（one-loop Schwinger integral）通过状态塔（towers of states）求和得到。

Conclusion: Hořava-Witten理论中的对称tadpole消去机制为暗维度场景的实现提供了改进路径，该场景中的无穷远极限与M理论涌现提议相关联。单圈Schwinger积分可能统一描述标量势、规范耦合和普朗克尺度的模依赖行为。

Abstract: It has been suggested that Hořava-Witten theory could provide a concrete realization of the Dark Dimension Scenario. In this context, the observable Standard Model sector is naturally localized in the micron-sized large dimension, which is the interval in the eleventh direction. Considering Calabi-Yau manifolds supporting generic vector bundles including also abelian factors, we point out that symmetric tadpole cancellation on the $E_8$ walls has the potential to ameliorate some of the issues of such a realization, including too fast proton decay. By taking not only the hierarchically small value of the dark energy but also the size of the Standard Model gauge couplings into account, one is driven to a special infinite distance limit, which is the Hořava-Witten analogue of a limit recently at the focus of the M-theoretic Emergence Proposal. Extrapolating results obtained for BPS-saturated amplitudes, we speculate about the possibility of obtaining the moduli dependence of the scalar potential, the gauge couplings and the Planck scale by simple one-loop Schwinger integrals over towers of states.

</details>


### [148] [Positivity in Massive Spin-3/2 EFTs and the Planck-Suppressed Neighbourhood of Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11072)
*Jay Desai,Diptimoy Ghosh,Saurabh Pant*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于色散关系推导了有质量 Majorana 自旋-3/2 粒子有效场论中接触算符的非前向树级界（dispersive bounds），发现当质量远小于普朗克尺度时，允许的参数空间形成一个以超引力点（supergravity point）为边界的、被普朗克尺度压制的有界邻域，其体积按 m^6/M_Pl^6 标度收缩，并且在零质量极限下光滑地恢复到超引力结果；加入轻标量和赝标量自由度不会扩大该接触耦合空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知无质量自旋-3/2 粒子只能通过超引力（supergravity）一致地相互作用，而最近的 positivity 论证表明有质量 Majorana 自旋-3/2 粒子的有效场论只有在存在引力子且四费米子接触相互作用被调整到 N=1 超引力所规定的值时，才能光滑地取零质量极限。本文旨在研究该极限在有限质量下如何逼近。

Method: 本文假设可忽略引力子 t-通道极点，推导了有质量自旋-3/2 接触算符的非前向、树级色散界（non-forward, tree-level dispersive bounds），并基于幺正性（unitarity）和解析性（analyticity）确定有效耦合的允许区域。

Result: 对于足够小的质量 m，允许参数空间形成一个以超引力点为边界的有界邻域，且该区域体积按 m^6/M_Pl^6 标度，在 m→0 时收缩至零。超引力点位于该区域边界上。当质量接近普朗克尺度时，允许区域变为无界。添加类似 Polonyi 模型中的轻标量和赝标量自由度不会扩大接触耦合空间。

Conclusion: 非前向色散界确认了质量为零时只允许超引力点，有限小质量下允许区域是有界且受普朗克尺度压制的，光滑地恢复已知的无质量极限结果。引入额外轻粒子不会放宽对接触耦合的约束。

Abstract: It is well known that a strictly massless spin-$3/2$ particle can interact consistently only within supergravity. Recently, positivity arguments have shown that an effective field theory of a massive Majorana spin-$3/2$ particle admits a smooth $m \to 0$ limit only if a graviton is present and the four-fermion contact interactions are tuned to the values dictated by $\mathcal{N}=1$ supergravity. In this work, we investigate how this limit is approached at finite mass. Assuming that the graviton $t$-channel pole can be discarded, we derive non-forward, tree-level dispersive bounds on massive spin-3/2 contact operators and determine the region of effective couplings consistent with unitarity and analyticity. For sufficiently small $m$, we find that the allowed parameter space forms a bounded, Planck-suppressed neighbourhood of the supergravity point, defined by the supergravity values of the four-fermion couplings. The supergravity point lies on the boundary of this region. In the regime $m \ll M_{\rm Pl}$, the volume of the allowed region scales parametrically as \[ \mathrm{Vol} \sim \frac{m^{6}}{M_{\rm Pl}^{6}} \, , \] and shrinks to zero as $m \to 0$, smoothly reproducing the massless-limit results. The allowed region becomes unbounded when mass approaches the Planck scale. We further analyze the effect of including additional light scalar and pseudo-scalar degrees of freedom, motivated by the Polonyi model, and find that their couplings are also bounded in a way similar to the contact couplings and that it doesn't enlarge the allowed contact coupling space.

</details>


### [149] [Compact space catalysis of false vacuum decay and Schwinger effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11081)
*Saquib Hassan,John March-Russell*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了D维紧致空间中零温假真空衰变（false vacuum decay），发现当空间体积低于临界值时，存在一种不同于Coleman经典O(D)气泡的新型反弹解（bounce solution），其衰变速率呈指数级增强。该反弹解在解析延拓至洛伦兹时空后，在小体积下形成均匀场位形，在稍大体积下形成准均匀位形。论文通过涨落谱特征验证了该解具有假真空衰变的必要条件，并将其应用于标量场模型和紧致空间中(1+1)维轴子电动力学的类Schwinger效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的Coleman假真空衰变理论假设空间体积无限大，其反弹解为O(D)球对称气泡。然而在紧致空间（compacted spatial dimensions）中，空间体积有限时，原有理论是否仍然成立、是否会出现新的衰变机制，是尚未被充分探索的问题。

Method: 论文在D维紧致空间中研究零温假真空衰变的反弹解，通过分析不同空间体积下反弹解的存在性及其性质，发现当体积低于临界值时出现新型反弹解。该解在解析延拓（analytic continuation）至洛伦兹时空后，在小体积下表现为均匀场位形（homogeneous field configuration），在稍大体积下表现为准均匀位形（quasi-homogeneous configuration）。论文通过分析涨落（fluctuation）的本征值谱（eigenvalue spectrum）验证了该解满足假真空衰变的必要条件。

Result: 发现了紧致空间中体积低于临界值时存在的新型反弹解，它不同于传统的O(D)气泡解，且导致衰变速率呈指数级增强。该反弹解不是薄壁或厚壁气泡形式。论文进一步将这一方案应用于标量场模型以及紧致空间中(1+1)维轴子电动力学（axion electrodynamics）的类Schwinger效应（Schwinger effect）。

Conclusion: 紧致空间的有限体积会显著改变假真空衰变的动力学机制，出现新型反弹解并增强衰变速率。这一结果为理解有限体积效应下的真空衰变提供了新的理论框架，并可能对早期宇宙学、凝聚态物理中有限尺寸系统（finite-size systems）的亚稳态衰变具有重要启示。

Abstract: We study zero-temperature false vacuum decay in $D$ compact spatial dimensions and show that for volumes below a critical value a new bounce solution, different from Coleman's celebrated $O(D)$ bubble, mediates the decay process, and typically leads to an exponentially enhanced decay rate. The bounce, when analytically continued to Lorentzian signature, nucleates a homogeneous field configuration for spatial volumes below a critical value, and quasi-homogeneous configurations for slightly larger volumes, and is not of the form of a thin or thick-walled bubble embedded in a false vacuum background. We explicitly show that the new bounce has the necessary features associated with false vacuum decay, following from its eigenvalue spectrum of fluctuations. The cross-over from homogeneous to quasi-homogeneous solutions as the spatial volume is increased is discussed, as is a real-time interpretation of the bounce. We apply this bounce to the study of a scalar field model, as well as a close cousin of the Schwinger effect that applies to $(1+1)d$ axion electrodynamics in compact space.

</details>


### [150] [Analytic Bootstrap of the Veneziano Amplitude](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11084)
*Shi-Lin Wan,Shuang-Yong Zhou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文严格证明，基于色散求和规则（dispersive sum rules）、幺正性（unitarity）以及少量额外的弦论输入（如弦整体单值性条件或分裂与隐藏零点条件），对偶自举（dual bootstrap）将唯一地导出Veneziano振幅，且该结论对所有阶均成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弦论中振幅的唯一性长期以来依赖特定构造，缺乏从第一性原理出发的严格证明。本文旨在通过解析自举（analytic bootstrap）框架，从色散求和规则、幺正性等基本原理出发，唯一地确定Veneziano振幅，从而揭示其作为对偶自举必然结果的地位。

Method: 将色散求和规则重新解释为矩（moments）序列，并精确地将额外的弦论输入（弦整体单值性条件或分裂与隐藏零点条件）融入振幅的初始形式（ansatz），从而使解析自举具有足够的约束力。

Result: 严格证明Veneziano振幅是对偶自举在所有阶上的唯一输出结果。弦整体单值性条件（string monodromy condition）与分裂及隐藏零点条件（splitting and hidden-zero conditions）均可作为达成唯一性的额外弦论输入。

Conclusion: 对偶自举框架结合基本原理与最小量的弦论输入，能够唯一确定Veneziano振幅，为弦论振幅的唯一性提供了严格的解析证明。

Abstract: We analytically prove, to all orders, that the Veneziano amplitude is the unique outcome of a dual bootstrap based on dispersive sum rules, unitarity, and a small amount of additional stringy input. This stringy input can be either the string monodromy condition or the recently uncovered splitting and hidden-zero conditions. A key ingredient in our proofs is to interpret the dispersive sum rules as sequences of moments. Equally important is the precise incorporation of the extra stringy input into the amplitude ansatz, which makes the analytic bootstrap sufficiently rigid to fix the amplitude uniquely.

### [151] [Stochastic inflation from a non-equilibrium renormalization group](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11096)
*Sebastián Céspedes,Thomas Colas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从两个互补视角系统研究了随机暴胀（stochastic inflation）中可控修正的第一性原理计算：一是通过粗粒化描述的约化密度矩阵推导出长波长模式的有效场论（effective field theory），其中耗散与扩散算符自然出现，并在红外极限下以扩散为主；二是证明密度矩阵随粗粒化尺度的流动服从Polchinski型重整化群方程（renormalisation group equation），由此导出的广义Fokker-Planck方程系统地包含了次领头阶修正，并与开放有效场论的结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解随机暴胀并系统地从第一性原理计算受控修正仍然是一个重要的开放问题。正因如此，作者希望建立一套严格的理论框架来克服这一困难。

Method: 方法包括两部分：一是从粗粒化描述的约化密度矩阵出发，在薄壳近似（thin-shell approximation）下得到时间局域性，在超哈勃（super-Hubble）区域内恢复空间局域性，从而推导出包含耗散与扩散算符的开放有效场论（open effective field theory）；二是证明密度矩阵随粗粒化尺度的演化服从Polchinski型重整化群方程，并由此推导广义Fokker-Planck方程。

Result: 在开放有效场论框架下，领头阶重现了标准的Fokker-Planck方程，并可以计算次领头阶的随机动力学修正；扩散算符在粗粒化标度推向红外（infrared）时占主导地位。从重整化群流出发导出的广义Fokker-Planck方程系统性地包含了次领头阶修正，其结果与开放有效场论方法一致，且有效作用量（effective action）与Schwinger-Keldysh描述相匹配。

Conclusion: 本文建立了两种互补的理论框架来系统计算随机暴胀中的受控修正，且二者结果自洽。该工作为从第一性原理理解随机暴胀及其可控修正提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Understanding stochastic inflation, and in particular the systematic computation of controlled corrections from first principles, remains an important open problem. In this work, we address this problem from two complementary perspectives. First, we derive the effective field theory governing long-wavelength modes from the reduced density matrix of a coarse-grained description. In this framework, locality in time follows from the thin-shell approximation, while locality in space is recovered dynamically in the super-Hubble regime. The resulting open effective field theory contains both dissipative and diffusive operators, with diffusion dominating as the coarse-graining scale is pushed into the infrared. This construction reproduces the usual Fokker-Planck equation at leading order and allows us to compute its corrections, including subleading contributions to the stochastic dynamics. Second, we study the evolution of the density matrix under changes of the coarse-graining scale. We show that this flow is governed by a Polchinski-type renormalisation group equation formulated directly for the density matrix. Dissipative and diffusive operators are generated dynamically along the flow, and the resulting effective action matches the Schwinger-Keldysh description. We derive a generalised Fokker-Planck equation directly from the renormalisation group flow, systematically incorporating subleading corrections and recovering the results obtained in the open effective field theory approach.

### [152] [Aharonov--Casher effect from a supersymmetric N=1 D=4 model with Kalb--Ramond Lorentz-violating background: a SUSY-preserving mechanism via the Fayet--Iliopoulos term](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11493)

Method: 构造了一个N=1、D=4超对称规范模型，包含手征超场（chiral superfield）与阿贝尔规范超场（Abelian gauge superfield），通过添加Chern-Simons型相互作用和Fayet-Iliopoulos项实现。利用手征超场的对称组合S+S†与Kalb-Ramond超场强度的对偶映射（duality identification）引入反对称张量背景，并在非相对论极限下推导出AC哈密顿量。

Abstract: The Aharonov--Casher (AC) effect describes the geometric phase acquired by a neutral particle carrying a magnetic dipole moment moving in an external electric field. In supersymmetric gauge theories it is often argued that exact supersymmetry enforces the vanishing of anomalous magnetic dipole moments, suggesting that the AC interaction may be incompatible with unbroken supersymmetry in four dimensions. In this work we show that this conclusion is model-dependent. We construct an $N=1$, $D=4$ supersymmetric gauge model in which a Lorentz-violating Kalb--Ramond background induces dynamically the dipole interaction responsible for the AC effect while leaving the supersymmetry algebra intact. The model couples a chiral superfield to an Abelian gauge superfield through a Chern--Simons--type interaction supplemented by a Fayet--Iliopoulos term. A duality identification between the symmetric combination $S+S^\dagger$ of the chiral superfield and the Kalb--Ramond superfield strength allows the antisymmetric tensor background to enter the supersymmetric dynamics without breaking supersymmetry. Integrating out the auxiliary $D$ field generates dynamically an effective dipole interaction of the form $\barψσ^{μν}F_{μν}ψ$. In the nonrelativistic limit the resulting equation of motion reproduces the Aharonov--Casher Hamiltonian for a neutral fermion. The effective magnetic dipole moment is expressed in terms of the parameters of the model and can be mapped onto tensor coefficients of the fermion sector of the Standard Model Extension. Our results therefore provide an explicit realization of a four-dimensional supersymmetric theory in which the Aharonov--Casher interaction emerges dynamically while supersymmetry remains exact in the presence of Lorentz violation.

Main category: hep-th

Conclusion: 本文在弦云弯曲时空中完整求解了狄拉克振子的束缚态问题，揭示了时空曲率（通过参数 $a$ 和有效质量 $m_{\text{eff}}$）对能谱量子化的直接影响，证实了 tetrad 形式在弯曲时空狄拉克问题中的解析可行性，并为后续相关量子引力或弦理论背景下的相对论量子力学研究提供了理论依据。

However, unlike in literature, here, we work with the spacetime in two different forms/configurations, that is, both in its original form and in its modified form. To achieve our objective, we work with the curved DO in spherical coordinates, where we use the tetrad formalism. So, by defining a stationary ansatz for the spinor, we obtain two coupled first-order differential equations, and by substituting one equation into the other, we obtain a second-order differential equation. To analytically and exactly solve this differential equation, we use a change of function and of variable. From this, we obtain the well-known Whittaker equation, whose solution is the Whittaker function. Consequently, we obtain the energy spectrum, which is quantized in terms of the radial quantum number $n$ and the angular quantum number $κ$, and explicitly depends on the angular frequency $ω$ (describes the DO), curvature parameter $a$ (describes the cloud of strings), and on the effective rest mass $m_{\text{eff}}$ (describes the rest mass modified by the curvature of spacetime). Besides, we graphically analyze the behavior of the spectrum as a function of $ω$ and $a$ for three different values of $n$ and $κ$, as well as the behavior of the radial probability density for four different values of $κ$, $ω$, and $a$ (with $n=0$).

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入了一个忠实实现序参量横向约束（transverse constraint）的晶格模型；采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo）算法，结合局部Metropolis更新（保留约束）和零模（zero mode）的全局更新；在体积为48×48×48的立方晶格上执行模拟。

Abstract: The dipolar universality class describes the phase transition in 3D ferromagnets with strong dipolar interactions, as first discussed by Aharony and Fisher in the 1970s. While this universality class has been studied theoretically using renormalization group methods, as well as experimentally, little is known about it from Monte Carlo simulations. In this paper we aim to bridge this gap. We introduce a lattice model that faithfully implements the transverse constraint on the order parameter. We introduce a Markov Chain Monte Carlo algorithm which involves a combination of local Metropolis updates preserving the constraint, and a global update of the zero mode. We perform simulations on cubic lattices up to volume $48\times 48 \times 48$. We observe a continuous phase transition between the disordered and ordered phases. We obtain estimates of universal quantities such as the main critical exponents and the Binder ratio, and compare them with results from other techniques. We also investigate the emergence of rotation invariance at the critical point.

### [155] [Scaling Solutions of Matter Form Factors in Asymptotically Safe Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11805)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Wilsonian原时流方程（Wilsonian proper-time flow equation）推导形式因子 $f_\Lambda(-\Box)$ 关于紫外截断 $\Lambda$ 的闭合积分-微分方程；利用伪谱离散化（pseudospectral discretization）数值求解该方程的不动点问题。

Conclusion: 该引力-标量系统中的非局域扇区存在与渐近安全相容的非平凡重整化群标度结构，且不动点对应的裸作用量在标量两点扇区是局域的。

Abstract: We investigate the renormalization group flow of a gravity--matter system in which a scalar field is minimally coupled to Einstein gravity and its kinetic term is given by a scale-dependent form factor $f_Λ(-\Box)$. Employing the Wilsonian proper-time flow equation, we derive a closed integro-differential equation that encodes the dependence of the form factor on the UV cutoff $Λ$. We solve the resulting fixed-point problem with a pseudospectral discretization and find a non-trivial fixed point for which $f_\ast(-\Box)$ departs from the canonical $-\Box$ behavior. Linearizing the flow about this solution yields a discrete spectrum of perturbations and a corresponding set of critical exponents, indicating a non-trivial scaling structure in this non-local sector compatible with asymptotic safety. We also observe that the form factor becomes local once the UV cutoff is removed, suggesting that the bare action associated with this fixed point is local in the scalar two-point sector.
