*Gustav Uhre Jakobsen,Kathrin Stoldt*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将世界线量子场论（worldline quantum field theory, WQFT）形式推广至后闵可夫斯基（post-Minkowskian）体系下的黑洞散射事件角动量总通量计算，建立了与脉冲计算的一一对应关系，并通过引入“静态关联子”（static correlators）系统处理零频率引力子贡献，在D>4维时空下静态贡献消失，最终在引力与电磁理论中分别计算至O(G^3)和O(α^3)阶角动量通量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发展一套直接计算黑洞散射事件中角动量总通量（total flux of angular momentum）的图解方法，弥补后闵可夫斯基（post-Minkowskian）体系中该问题的形式化空缺。

Method: 扩展世界线量子场论（WQFT）形式，建立角动量通量计算与黑洞脉冲（impulse）计算之间的一一对应关系；针对零频率引力子（zero-frequency gravitons）引入“静态关联子”（static correlators）组织静态贡献，并采用积分约化（integration-by-parts）与微分方程方法（method of differential equations）计算单圈积分族。

Result: 静态贡献在时空维度D>4的情形下完全消失。在引力理论中，成功计算了O(G^3)阶的角动量总通量，复现了已知结果；在电磁理论中，计算了对应的O(α^3)阶结果。

Conclusion: 所提出的WQFT图解法可系统推广至角动量通量计算，零频率引力子的静态贡献可通过静态关联子高效组织，且高维时空下此类贡献自动消失，为后闵可夫斯基体系下的散射观测提供了统一的形式化框架。

Abstract: We extend the worldline quantum field theory formalism to include a direct diagrammatic method of computing the total flux of angular momentum from a black hole scattering event in the post-Minkowskian regime. Remarkably, except for subtle zero-frequency gravitons, the diagrammatic and integrational challenge is in a one-to-one correspondence with the analogous calculation of the black hole impulses -- and the well-developed WQFT methodologies for the impulse may thus be directly imported to this problem. Zero-frequency gravitons appear in this calculation as a "static" integration region in addition to the "dynamical" region usually encountered for the impulse. We show that a large class of static contributions can be organized systematically by introducing $n$-point functions referred to as "static correlators". They reduce to a simple one-loop integral family which we compute explicitly using integration-by-parts relations and the method of differential equations. In passing, our analysis shows that static contributions disappear in space-time dimensions $D>4$. As a concrete application of our new method, we compute explicitly the $\mathcal{O}(G^3)$ total flux of angular momentum reproducing known results. Further, we apply the same method to electromagnetism where we compute the analogous $\mathcal{O}(α^3)$ result.

</details>


### [159] [Necessary conditions for causality from linearized stability at ultra-high boosts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12291)
*Shuvayu Roy,Sukanya Mitra,Rajeev Singh*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新方法，仅通过非零动量下的线性稳定性分析来约束相对论性流体动力学系统的因果参数空间，利用洛伦兹不变稳定性与“γ-抑制”特性，在近光速极限下将因果性必要条件简化为空间均匀极限的稳定性判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对论性流体动力学（relativistic hydrodynamics）理论中，因果性与稳定性之间的内在关联尚未被充分利用来高效约束参数空间；现有的研究方法往往需要在全场动量范围内进行复杂的因果条件检验。

Method: 利用因果理论的洛伦兹不变稳定性（Lorentz-invariant stability）性质，分析增强参考系（boosted frames）中的色散关系（dispersion relation）。发现一种称为“γ-抑制”的特征，即波数展开的高阶项在大增强极限下被压制。据此，在近光速洛伦兹增强（near-luminal Lorentz boost）条件下，空间均匀极限的稳定性判据足以识别满足因果性必要条件的参数区域。

Result: 在共形 Müller-Israel-Stewart（MIS）理论中测试了该方法，结果表明该方法能够高效导出因果性的必要条件，且始终保持在流体动力学有效性的低能区域（low-energy regime）内。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种仅从线性稳定性分析出发、无需全动量扫描即可约束相对论流体系统因果参数空间的有效途径，拓宽了因果性检验在唯象流体模型中的应用方式。

Abstract: In this work, we provide a novel method to constrain the causal parameter space of a relativistic hydrodynamic system exclusively from its linear stability analysis at non-zero momenta. Our approach exploits the Lorentz-invariant stability property of causal theories. In boosted frames, the dispersion relation exhibits a feature that we call ``$γ$-suppression,'' whereby the higher-order terms in the wavenumber expansion are increasingly suppressed beyond leading order at large boosts. As a consequence, at near-luminal values of Lorentz boost, stability criteria at the spatially homogeneous limit are sufficient to identify the region of the parameter space that satisfies the necessary conditions of causality, even at non-zero momenta. After presenting the general hydrodynamic framework, we test the method in conformal Müller-Israel-Stewart theory and show that it provides an efficient way of deriving the necessary conditions of causality while remaining within the low-energy regime of hydrodynamic validity.

</details>


### [160] [Classifying double copies and multicopies in AdS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12359)
*V. E. Didenko,N. K. Dosmanbetov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在纯三维负宇宙常数引力（pure three-dimensional gravity with a negative cosmological constant）的解与四维经典双拷贝（classical double copies）之间建立了平行关系，通过等度规代数（isometry algebra）的轨道分类与Penrose型变换，系统构建并分类了各类双拷贝解，并将其推广至更高自旋（higher spins）情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示三维AdS引力中的拓扑解（如BTZ黑洞）与四维经典双拷贝结构之间的深层数学对应关系，并寻求一种统一的分类框架。

Method: 利用AdS等度规代数so(2,2)和so(2,3)的轨道（orbits）分类思想，通过Penrose型变换（Penrose-type transform）将三维解对应到四维双拷贝解；借助给定AdS等度规的中心化子（centralizer）定义与阿贝尔部分（Abelian part）相关的正则坐标（canonical coordinates），并引入两个Casimir不变量（Casimir invariants）参与度规构造。

Result: 完成了so(2,3)所有元素分类，生成了对应的双拷贝解，包括AdS黑洞（AdS black holes）、黑膜（black branes）等；证明双拷贝等度规（double-copy isometries）源于给定AdS等度规的中心化子；两个Casimir不变量出现在度规中；分类自然延伸至更高自旋，在线性化层次提供了非等价多拷贝（multicopies）。

Conclusion: 三维引力解与四维经典双拷贝之间存在一一对应的轨道分类关系，该框架可系统生成多种AdS双拷贝解，并可推广至更高自旋场景，为经典双拷贝理论提供了新的几何基础。

Abstract: In this paper, we draw a parallel between solutions of pure three-dimensional gravity with a negative cosmological constant and classical double copies in four dimensions. In the former case, topological solutions, such as the BTZ black hole, deficit angles, and naked singularities, emerge from identifying points in AdS using elements from its isometry algebra $so(2,2)$. The type of solution corresponds one-to-one with the orbits of $so(2,2)$. We demonstrate how various double copies of four-dimensional AdS gravity similarly arise from the $so(2,3)$ isometry elements, which also correspond one-to-one with their orbits through a Penrose-type transform. We classify all such elements and generate the corresponding double copies, which include AdS black holes, black branes, and many others. The double-copy isometries originate from the centralizer of a given AdS isometry, allowing us to define canonical coordinates associated with its Abelian part. Additionally, the two Casimir invariants of $so(2,3)$ feature in the metrics. Our classification naturally extends to higher spins, providing nonequivalent multicopies at the linearized level.

Conclusion: 超几何框架为系统地构建超对称理论中的高形式对称性提供了有效途径。文中给出了直接从超引力构造Chern-Weil和几何Chern-Weil对称性的超对称对称张量场论的初步原创提示，为后续研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: We review the construction of higher-form symmetries for supersymmetric theories using a supergeometry framework. This reveals an enlarged set of topological conserved supercurrents, including Chern-Weil symmetries and new geometric Chern-Weil symmetries built from invariant supermanifold forms. In N=1 super-Maxwell theory in three dimensions, we construct the corresponding operators and charged defects, with charges determined by a super-linking number between their supporting hypersurfaces. Abstract: We observe that the null string action possesses a previously overlooked local symmetry. By correctly accounting for this symmetry, we show that the number of physical propagating degrees of freedom of null strings in $D$ dimensional target space is $D-3$, in contrast to $D-2$ that one finds in the literature. Overlooking this symmetry has led to an unphysical over-counting of states, rendering the null string analyses inconsistent. Thus, our observation calls for a thorough revision of all statements and results in the null string literature.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以平坦欧氏空间（flat Euclidean space）上的度规扰动（metric perturbations）二次近似为出发点，利用周期性边界条件（periodic boundary conditions）$β=1/T$引入有效温度。通过引入一个特殊的协变矢量场$ξ^μ(x)$，将静态几何中的Killing矢量（Killing vector）推广至满足类时周期性条件的非均匀度规，从而将平坦空间结果协变化为基于时空曲率（spacetime curvature）的表达式。

Result: 得到了在度规扰动二次近似下协变形式的热核和有效作用量；推导了非局部形状因子（nonlocal formfactors）的高温渐近行为；该形式自动恢复为Tolman温度（Tolman temperature）$T/\sqrt{g_{00}(x)}$在稳态流形上的标准形式。

Conclusion: 所建立的框架可用于研究非稳态引力背景下的量子场热力学行为，其高温渐近结果可能对早期宇宙或黑洞物理等宇宙学场景具有应用价值。

Abstract: Curvature expansion for the heat kernel trace and the one-loop effective action is built for the wave operator of the theory in the quasi-thermal setup of a nonvacuum quantum state. This setup implies a non-static and non-stationary Euclidean gravitational background with periodic boundary conditions of the period $β=1/T$, where $T$ plays the role of effective global temperature to be locally rescaled by the metric gravitational potential. The results are obtained in the approximation quadratic in metric perturbations on top of flat Euclidean space and covariantized in terms of spacetime curvature. Covariantization includes a special vector field $ξ^μ(x)$ which generalizes the Killing vector of static geometries with time translation isometry to the case of a generic arbitrarily inhomogeneous metric subject to timelike periodicity condition. This vector field is obtained as a covariant metric functional to quadratic order in metric perturbations and gives rise to the local function $T/\sqrt{ξ^2(x)}$, $ξ^2(x)=g_{μν}(x)ξ^μ(x)ξ^ν(x)$, reducing to Tolman temperature $T/\sqrt{g_{00}(x)}$ on stationary manifolds with Killing symmetry. High ``temperature'' asymptotic behavior of the nonlocal formfactors -- operator coefficients of the curvature tensor structures in the heat kernel and effective action -- are obtained and possible cosmological applications of these results are discussed.

Abstract: Following Veltman's approach, we formulate and discuss a general cutting equation for QED in a plane-wave background. Our findings establish that although total rates can be reliably extracted from higher-loop by applying the cutting rules, reconstruction of differential rates requires additional care. The cutting rules apply to any loop order and may be extended to nonperturbative regimes.

### [166] [Anomalies in Neural Network Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12488)

TL;DR: 本文提出神经网络场论（neural network field theory, NN-FT），将场论以网络架构及其参数密度重新表述，并推导了Schwinger-Dyson方程与Ward恒等式，用于研究多种物理与机器学习中的对称性及其反常现象。

Method: 在神经网络场论框架下推导了Schwinger-Dyson方程与Ward恒等式；定义了一个守恒的参数空间流（parameter space current），用于刻画对称性及其破缺；通过适当的纤维方向平均（fiber-wise average），可在局部拉格朗日量情形下恢复局部流。

We derive Schwinger--Dyson equations and Ward identities in NN-FT and utilize them to study anomalies. The equations depend on a conserved parameter space current that characterizes symmetries and how they break. It is relevant even in non-local NN-FTs, but can recover local currents in the case of a local Lagrangian by an appropriate fiber-wise average. In machine learning, this formalism is applied to feedforward networks and the attention mechanism. In physics, we use this machinery to study $U(1)$ symmetry for a complex scalar, the scale anomaly in $4d$ massless $φ^4$ theory, the Weyl anomaly for the bosonic string (including a new computation of the critical dimension), and examples involving discrete topological data, such as winding numbers and T-duality. Since the results are obtained in network parameter space rather than the standard field space, they represent a new way to understand symmetries in quantum field theories.

</details>


<div id='cs.RO'></div>

### [167] [A Soft Robotic Demonstration in the Stratosphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04352)
*Codrin Tugui,Tirth Thakar,Anatol Gogoj,Alexander White,Ang Leo Li,Alexander Yin,Edward Pomianek,Mihai Duduta*

Main category: cs.RO

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 新型交联机制实现了快速紫外光加工和优异的电机械性能；对照实验证明其在-40°C、120°C及近真空环境中具有材料抗极端性优势；两次平流层气球任务（最高23.6 km，<0.05 atm，-55°C）成功验证了DEA在类空间条件下作为可行软体机器人技术的应用能力。

Conclusion: 该紫外光催化交联策略可有效提升硅酮弹性体在极端环境下的抗性，使介电弹性体致动器适用于空间等极端条件；该化学组合可进一步扩展至硅酮在粘合与增材制造（additive manufacturing）等其他领域的挑战。

Abstract: Machines designed for operation in Space, as well as other extreme environments, need to be both resilient and adaptable when mission parameters change. Soft robots offer advantages in adaptability, but most lack resilience to the pressure and temperature extremes found as close as the Stratosphere. Dielectric elastomer actuators overcome some of those limitations when built as solid state compliant capacitors capable of converting electrical energy into mechanical work, but the elastomer resilience limits the device's operating window. Here we present a crosslinking mechanism for silicone elastomers under ultraviolet light using trimethyl(methylcyclopentadienyl)platinum(IV) as a catalyst to react hydrosilane to vinyl groups. The formation of carbon-carbon bonds enables fast processing under UV light and exceptional electro-mechanical performance in dielectric elastomer actuators. The material resilience advantage is demonstrated in controlled experiments at -40° and 120° C, as well as near vacuum, in comparison with state-of-the-art acrylic and silicone chemistries. Fully autonomous systems controlling grippers made with the novel silicone were integrated into payloads for high altitude balloon testing. Two stratospheric balloon missions were carried out and demonstrated DEAs as a viable soft robotic technology under space-like conditions (as high as 23.6 km elevation, at <0.05 atm and -55° C). The combinations of chemical building blocks and catalyst can be further expanded to address other challenges for silicones, including adhesion and additive manufacturing.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（Density Matrix Renormalization Group, DMRG）模拟与基于纠缠的诊断工具，结合描述紧密束缚费米子对形成的有效模型。

Result: 囚禁与相互作用的共同作用重塑了渡越过程，导致绝缘区域与持续存在的超流关联（superfluid correlations）共存；引入的条件关联函数（conditioned correlation functions）的幂律衰减能够清晰区分BCS类与BEC类区域。

Abstract: Confined ultracold atoms in optical lattices provide a versatile platform for simulating lattice models of strongly correlated quantum systems, where pairing phenomena and superfluid phases can be explored under controlled conditions. While the crossover between the Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer (BCS) phase and the Bose-Einstein condensation (BEC) is well understood in homogeneous systems, spatial confinement breaks translational symmetry and reshapes correlation patterns, making the BCS-BEC identification in trapped geometries challenging and allowing unconventional phases to emerge with no direct analog in homogeneous systems. Here we present a characterization of the BCS-BEC crossover in harmonically confined one-dimensional Fermi-Hubbard chains. Our analysis combines Density Matrix Renormalization Group (DMRG) simulations and entanglement-based diagnostics with effective models describing the formation of tightly bound fermion pairs. This combined approach enables a detailed understanding of how the interplay between interactions and confinement reshapes the crossover, leading to insulating regions coexisting with persistent superfluid correlations. Within this framework, we further introduce conditioned correlation functions whose power-law decay allows a clear distinction between BCS-like and BEC-like regimes. The consistency between the effective descriptions and the numerical DMRG results yields a unified picture of the crossover in harmonically confined geometries.

### [169] [Giant critical response in a driven-dissipative quantum gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11230)
*Ross C. Schofield,Daniel Lim,Himadri S. Dhar,Robert A. Nyman,Akshay K. Verma,Edmund Clarke,Jon Heffernan,Florian Mintert,Rupert F. Oulton*

TL;DR: No AI summary available.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: No AI summary available.

Method: No AI summary available.

Result: No AI summary available.

Conclusion: No AI summary available.

Abstract: Systems close to a phase transition turn weak perturbations into large responses. At equilibrium, this amplification is closely linked to criticality: fluctuations grow, dynamics slow, and a common soft mode controls the response. Whether this correspondence survives in driven-dissipative quantum systems, sustained by continuous pumping and loss away from thermal equilibrium, remains an open question. Here we show experimentally that it does. In a room-temperature semiconductor photon Bose-Einstein condensate, the critical slowing of spontaneous intensity fluctuations and the amplification of weak pump perturbations are measured independently. Both peak at the same condensate population, $\bar{n}_c = 1250$, where the dimensionless slowing factor and susceptibility reach the same value, $\bar{n}_c/2 = 625$. A single weakly damped collective photon-reservoir mode governs both effects. This fluctuation-response correspondence in a finite open quantum gas establishes critical susceptibility as a measurable dynamical signature of condensation, with peak gain set by system size.

### [170] [Barnett effect in rotating spinor dipolar quantum droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11670)
*Donghao Yan,Shaoxiong Li,Hiroki Saito*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稳定偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体自束缚液滴中的涡旋态，并探索由此产生的自旋与轨道角动量耦合效应及其宏观力学表现。

Method: 释放自旋自由度（spin degree of freedom），使液滴涡旋态通过类似Barnett效应的机制实现轨道角动量向自旋角动量的转移，从而产生自发磁化（spontaneous magnetization）。

Result: 涡旋液滴产生轴向自发磁化；在外磁场下整个原子云作为宏观物体发生力学拉莫尔进动而不改变形状；手性相反的一对液滴通过自发磁化液滴间的吸引相互作用形成稳定束缚态。

Conclusion: 释放自旋自由度可有效稳定偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体液滴中的涡旋态，并产生可观测的宏观磁-力学耦合效应及束缚态结构。

Abstract: We propose releasing the spin degree of freedom to stabilize the vortex state in self-bound droplets of dipolar Bose-Einstein condensates. When a vortex is embedded into the droplet, spontaneous magnetization arises in the axial direction via a mechanism similar to the Barnett effect; that is, the orbital angular momentum is transferred to the spin angular momentum. When an external magnetic field is applied to the spontaneously magnetized droplet, the entire atomic cloud starts to rotate without changing its shape, which can be regarded as mechanical Larmor precession of a macroscopic object. A chirally different pair of droplets can form a stable bound state because of the attractive interaction between the spontaneously magnetized droplets.

### [171] [Observation of sine-Gordon-like solitons in a spinor Bose-Einstein condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11861)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在超冷原子系统中实现和调控类正弦-戈登孤子，并验证其可积系统的动力学特性，从而为非线性可积模型提供高度可控的实验平台。

Method: 采用鲁棒且可重现的局域相位印记方案，在自旋-1自旋玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中生成类正弦-戈登孤子；通过改变有效二次塞曼位移来调节孤子速度，进而研究受控孤子相互作用。

Result: 实验观察到可积正弦-戈登模型的特征弹性碰撞行为；孤子碰撞产生的空间位移（phase shift）即成对相互作用的标志，在误差范围内与数值自旋-1模拟结果定量吻合。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了自旋BEC作为高度可控的实验平台，可用于研究类正弦-戈登模型的动力学行为。

Abstract: We experimentally generate sine-Gordon-like solitons in a spin-1 spinor Bose-Einstein condensate (BEC) utilizing a robust and reproducible local phase-imprinting scheme. We find that the soliton velocity can be tuned by the effective quadratic Zeeman shift. This enables the investigation of controlled soliton interactions, in which we observe the characteristic elastic collision behavior of the integrable sine-Gordon model. The spatial displacement -- the so-called phase shift -- between incoming and outgoing solitons, the signature of their pairwise interaction, is found to be in quantitative agreement with numerical spin-1 simulations within the error bars. These results establish spinor BECs as a highly controllable experimental platform for studying aspects of the dynamics of sine-Gordon-like models.

</details>


### [172] [Universal Speed Limit in a Far-from-Equilibrium Bose Gas: Symmetry and Dynamical Decoherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11895)
*Jun-Cheng Liang,Bo Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文首次解析预测了远离平衡态量子系统中非热固定点（NTFP）的普适输运振幅C，通过揭示对称性与耗散之间的深层关联，推导出参数无关的几何基线值C=3，并与实验值C=3.4(3)在考虑对数修正后定量一致，为强关联非平衡系统输运系数的预测建立了新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 远非平衡量子系统中普适输运系数的预测是一个根本性挑战。以孤立玻色气体的非热固定点（non-thermal fixed point, NTFP）为例，尽管标度指数z=2已被充分确认，但振幅C因粒子级联n(k)~k^{-4}导致动能发散而长期无法确定。

Method: 利用非热固定点处涌现的弱U(1)对称性（weak U(1) symmetry）约束低能相位动力学服从含随机电流散度噪声的扩散型朗之万方程（diffusive Langevin equation），结合高动量模的动态退相干（dynamical decoherence），推导出正则化紫外发散的普适幂律动量分布f̃(v)~(1+v²)^{-3}，进而得到参数无关的几何基线C=3。实验值C=3.4(3)与固定点处微扰无关耦合（marginally irrelevant coupling）引起的普适对数修正定量一致。

Result: 获得了参数无关的普适振幅几何基线C=3；理论预测与Martirosyan等人的实验值C=3.4(3)在考虑对数修正后定量吻合。

Conclusion: 建立了预测强关联非平衡系统输运系数的新范式：对称性约束决定低能有效理论，动态退相干提供自然紫外截断，标度分析从标度指数走向定量振幅预测。

Abstract: Predicting universal transport coefficients in far-from-equilibrium quantum systems remains a fundamental challenge. A paradigmatic example is the non-thermal fixed point (NTFP) of isolated Bose gases, where coherence spreads as $\ell^2(t) = C\hbar t/m$ with a universal constant $C$. While the scaling exponent $z=2$ is well established, the amplitude $C$ has remained elusive because the underlying particle cascade $n(k)\sim k^{-4}$ leads to a divergent kinetic energy, threatening the very existence of a constant speed limit. Here we resolve this paradox and present the first analytical, parameter-free prediction of a universal amplitude $C$. A deep interplay between symmetry and dissipation is uncovered. The emergent weak U(1) symmetry at the NTFP enforces a conserved total current, forcing the low-energy phase dynamics to obey a diffusive Langevin equation with noise entering as the divergence of a stochastic current. This structure, combined with dynamical decoherence of high-momentum modes, yields a universal power-law momentum distribution $\tilde{f}(v)\sim(1+v^2)^{-3}$ (with $v=k\ell$) that naturally regularizes the ultraviolet divergence. From this, a parameter-free geometric baseline $C=3$ is obtained, independent of microscopic details. The experimental value $C=3.4(3)$ [Martirosyan et al., Nature 647, 608 (2025)] is then shown to be quantitatively consistent with universal logarithmic corrections arising from a marginally irrelevant coupling at the fixed point. A new paradigm is thus established for predicting transport coefficients in strongly correlated non-equilibrium systems: symmetry constraints determine the low-energy effective theory, dynamical decoherence provides a natural ultraviolet completion, and scaling analysis delivers testable predictions moving beyond scaling exponents to quantitative amplitude prediction.

</details>


### [173] [The wave nature of a Mott insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12322)
*Xudong Yu,Chengyang Wu,Wenhan Chen,Igor Zhuravlev,Zekui Wang,Yi Zeng,Sudipta Dhar,Milena Horvath,Thierry Giamarchi,Manuele Landini,Hanns-Christoph Nägerl,Hepeng Yao,Yanliang Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验和量子蒙特卡洛（QMC）模拟，证明在一维强相互作用晶格气体中，莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）态仍然可以表现出显著的干涉峰，挑战了传统上将干涉峰作为超流性标志的观点，揭示了莫特绝缘体中存在的波动性相干特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，超流-莫特绝缘体（SF-MI）相变被理解为从波动性相干到粒子性局域化的转变，干涉峰的出现与消失分别被视为超流性和绝缘性的判定标志。该研究旨在检验这一观点在一维强相互作用晶格气体中的适用性，并探索莫特绝缘体态中是否存在未被预期的相干性。

Method: 研究在一维强相互作用气体中施加浅晶格势（shallow lattice potential），通过钉扎（pinning）实现带隙的莫特绝缘体态。采用干涉图案观测和单粒子关联函数（one-body correlation function）测量，并结合量子蒙特卡洛（QMC）模拟进行定量比较。

Result: 实验发现，在莫特绝缘体区域中仍然存在显著的干涉峰，且随着莫特分数（Mott fraction）增大，干涉反而增强。单粒子关联函数测量显示，绝缘态中呈现振荡且指数衰减的相干模式，覆盖多个晶格位点，与量子蒙特卡洛模拟结果定量吻合。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，干涉现象不能唯一地诊断超流性，并揭示了一维莫特绝缘体具有出乎意料的波动性本质（wave nature），挑战了传统相变判断依据。

Abstract: Quantum phases of matter are routinely identified by coherence features, with interference patterns being one of the most directly observable quantities. In lattices, the superfluid-to-Mott-insulator (SF-MI) transition is commonly viewed as a change from wave-like coherence to particle-like localization: interference peaks are taken as a hallmark of superfluidity, whereas their disappearance is used to diagnose insulating behavior. Here, we challenge this picture for one-dimensional (1D) strongly interacting gases subject to a lattice potential. We realize a gapped Mott insulator through pinning in a shallow lattice and find that pronounced interference peaks persist deep in the insulating regime. Strikingly, the interference becomes stronger as the Mott fraction increases, demonstrating that a certain degree of coherence still exists in the insulator state. Measurements of the one-body correlation function reveal an oscillatory, exponentially decaying coherence pattern across several lattice sites, in quantitative agreement with quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) simulations. Our work shows that interference does not uniquely diagnose superfluidity and it exposes the unexpected wave nature of a 1D Mott insulator.

</details>


### [174] [Programmable Superradiance in an Interacting Qubit Array](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12442)
*Botao Du,Qihao Guo,Ruichao Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过超导量子比特阵列与微波波导耦合的实验平台，实现了对多体量子发射体集体辐射动力学（包括超辐射与亚辐射）的微观测量与控制，揭示了超越理想Dicke模型的集体衰变机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多个量子发射体耦合到共同电磁环境时，其集体辐射动力学中的干涉效应会产生超辐射（superradiance）和亚辐射（subradiance）。然而，在相干相互作用与集体耗散（collective dissipation）竞争的区域内，支撑这些现象的微观多体动力学和量子关联在理论上具有挑战性，且在实验上仍难以探测。

Method: 实验上构建了一个耦合到公共微波波导的超导量子比特阵列，利用波导介导的集体耗散，同时实现相干相互作用的访问和微观多体动力学的测量。通过可调振幅和相位的工程化量子比特-波导耦合，控制集体干涉及其产生的超辐射和亚辐射态；并利用位点分辨（site-resolved）控制与读出，直接观测多量子比特态的微观衰变动力学。

Result: 直接观测了不同激发流形（excitation manifold）下多量子比特态的微观衰变动力学，追踪了布居数和可调量子关联的演化。揭示了超越理想Dicke模型（Dicke model）的集体衰变：强量子比特-量子比特相互作用能够抑制局部退相干（dephasing）以稳定超辐射和亚辐射，并通过空间和光谱结构化的多体本征态重塑衰变路径。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个灵活的实验平台，用于探索多体量子光学（many-body quantum optics）中的集体现象，以及驱动-耗散方法（driven-dissipative approaches）在鲁棒量子信息处理中的应用。

Abstract: When multiple quantum emitters couple to a common electromagnetic environment, interference in their collective radiative dynamics gives rise to superradiance and subradiance. In regimes where coherent interactions and collective dissipation compete, the microscopic many-body dynamics and quantum correlations among the emitters that underlie superradiance and subradiance are theoretically challenging and remain experimentally elusive, even though collective emission has been observed in many physical systems. Here, we realize a superconducting qubit array coupled to a common microwave waveguide that mediates collective dissipation, with simultaneous access to coherent interactions and microscopic measurements of many-body dynamics. Engineered qubit-waveguide couplings with tunable amplitude and phase enable control of collective interference and the resulting super- and subradiant states. Leveraging site-resolved control and readout, we directly observe the microscopic decay dynamics of multi-qubit states across different excitation manifolds and track the evolution of populations and tunable quantum correlations. We reveal collective decay in regimes beyond the ideal Dicke model, where strong qubit-qubit interactions stabilize superradiance and subradiance against local dephasing and reshape decay pathways through spatially and spectrally structured many-body eigenstates. Our results establish a flexible platform for exploring collective phenomena in many-body quantum optics and driven-dissipative approaches to robust quantum information processing.

</details>

### [175] [Detection Defines Dephasing in Two-Dimensional Electronic Spectroscopy of Materials: Coherent Field Emission versus Incoherent Population Observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08708)
*Simón Paiva-Ortega,Hao Li,Eric R. Bittner,Carlos Silva-Acuña*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文讨论二维电子光谱（two-dimensional electronic spectroscopy）中同质谱线宽（homogeneous spectral linewidth）的测量取决于检测算符（detection operator）的选择，而非仅由微观相干损失决定。通过统一框架表明，发射场检测保留传统的退相时间（dephasing time）$T_2$ 定义，而种群检测模态（如光致发光、光电流）会耦合激发态种群再分布动力学，产生有效相干时间 $T_{2,\mathrm{eff}}$。检测算符部分决定了光谱作为材料探针的意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上认为同质谱线宽仅由凝聚相体系的微观量子动力学（即相干损失）决定，但实验发现不同检测方式下观测到的谱线宽度存在差异，说明需要重新审视线宽测量的操作定义（operational definition）。

Method: 采用统一理论框架，构建一个包含共同 Liouville 算符（Liouvillian）的耦合模式模型（coupled-mode model），分别模拟相干发射场检测（coherent emitted-field measurement）和种群检测（population-detected modalities，包括光致发光、光电流及其他动作检测二维光谱）两种投影途径。

Result: 在相同微观动力学条件下，发射场检测的谱线宽度保持与传统光学相干时间 $T_2$ 对应的关系，而种群检测模式下的表观线宽额外编码了激发态种群再分布动力学，产生有效相干时间 $T_{2,\mathrm{eff}}$，两者数值不同。

Conclusion: 检测算符不仅仅是测量二维光谱的手段，而是从根本上决定了光谱作为材料探针的含义。退相的定义依赖于观测算符的选择，因此解释光谱数据时必须明确考虑检测模态。

Abstract: The homogeneous spectral linewidth associated with light-matter interactions is a fundamental descriptor of the optical properties of materials, governed by the quantum dynamics of the condensed-matter system. We discuss here that the homogeneous linewidth measured by means of two-dimensional electronic spectroscopy depends not only on microscopic coherence loss, but also on the observable through which the nonequilibrium dynamics are projected onto the measurement. In this Perspective, we develop a unified framework showing that changing the detection operator changes the operational definition of dephasing. For coherent emitted-field measurements, the observed linewidth largely retains its conventional connection to the optical coherence time $(T_2$). By contrast, in population-detected modalities such as photoluminescence-, photocurrent-, and other action-detected two-dimensional spectroscopies, the apparent linewidth can additionally encode excited-state population redistribution dynamics, leading naturally to an effective coherence time \(T_{2,\mathrm{eff}}\). Using a coupled-mode model propagated under a common Liouvillian, we show that identical microscopic dynamics yield distinct apparent dephasing times when projected onto coherent-emission and population-derived observables. We posit that the detection observable is not merely how a two-dimensional spectrum is measured, but part of what the spectrum fundamentally means as a materials probe.

</details>


### [176] [Low-rank compression of two-electron reduced density matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11253)
*Kemal Atalar,Hugh G. A. Burton,Andreas Grüneis,George H. Booth*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种保持楔积结构与物理对称性的两体约化密度矩阵（2RDM）低秩压缩协议，将存储成本从四次方降至二次方，在保持化学精度的前提下实现约99%的压缩率，并成功应用于本征矢量延拓（eigenvector continuation）与非绝热分子动力学模拟中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 两体约化密度矩阵（two-body reduced density matrix, 2RDM）是电子结构计算中的核心对象，但其四次方（quartic）存储开销严重限制了实际应用的规模可扩展性，亟需开发高效的压缩策略。

Method: 研究了一种简洁的压缩协议，通过低秩分解将过渡与非过渡2RDM转化为保留楔积结构（wedge-product structure）和物理对称性的低阶表示。该分解通过一组公共低秩因子耦合库仑（Coulomb）与交换（exchange）通道，形成比单通道分解更紧凑的秩稀疏（rank-sparse）表示。

Result: 对于关联态，有效秩随系统规模线性增长，对辛烷（octane）的耦合簇（coupled-cluster）2RDM实现了约99%的压缩，同时保持化学精度。该方案将本征矢量延拓（eigenvector continuation）中的内存成本从四次方降至二次方，且每电子误差可控。在光激发H28链的非绝热分子动力学（nonadiabatic molecular dynamics）模拟中，从压缩的近精确DMRG训练数据成功解析了结构、动力学与光谱可观测量。

Conclusion: 该结构保持的压缩中间体可有效建立实用的关联电子结构工作流，在保持物理一致性的前提下大幅降低存储与计算开销。

Abstract: Two-body reduced density matrices (2RDMs) encode the essential two-electron physics of electronic states, but their quartic storage cost poses a major limitation in practical workflows. We investigate a simple protocol to compress both transition and non-transition 2RDMs into a lower-rank representation that preserves their wedge-product structure and physical symmetries under truncation. The resulting decomposition couples Coulomb and exchange channels through a common set of low-rank factors, yielding a more compact rank-sparse representation than single-channel factorizations. For correlated states, the effective rank scales linearly with system size, achieving a $\sim99$\% compression for the coupled-cluster 2RDM of octane while retaining chemical accuracy. We apply this to the recently introduced {\em ab initio} eigenvector continuation workflows, where many-body wave functions are interpolated across nuclear geometries with mean-field cost. Here, 2RDMs between training states act as projectors into a subspace but their memory scaling limits applications to larger systems. The compression scheme reduces the memory cost from quartic to quadratic for a fixed error per electron. Metrics to systematically control the decomposition are investigated, enabling statistically resolved structural, dynamical and spectroscopic observables from nonadiabatic molecular dynamics simulations of photoexcited H$_{28}$ chains, interpolating from compressed near-exact DMRG training data. This establishes these structure-preserving compressed intermediates for practical correlated electronic structure workflows.

</details>


### [177] [Gel-Chemistry-Dependent Heavy-Metal Ion Transport and Immobilization in Cementitious Nanopores: A Molecular Dynamics Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11604)
*Weiqiang Chen,Qiyao He,Kai Gong*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过经典分子动力学（classical molecular dynamics）模拟，系统比较了三种水泥凝胶（C-S-H、C-(N)-A-S-H、N-A-S-H）纳米孔道中重金属离子（Pb²⁺、Ba²²⁺、Cs⁺）的吸附控制迁移行为，揭示了凝胶表面化学与离子固定程度之间的原子尺度关联机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶凝材料（cementitious materials）广泛用于危险废物固化，但不同凝胶化学组成对重金属离子（heavy-metal ion）保留的分子机制尚不清楚。

Method: 采用经典分子动力学（classical molecular dynamics）模拟，结合孔平均扩散率、空间分辨扩散率、驻留时间分析、离子密度分布、二维吸附图、径向分布函数（radial distribution function）、配位数分析和界面结合强度描述符等多种分析方法，建立比较原子框架。

Result: 所有凝胶纳米孔中离子迁移率均显著低于体相溶液；高Al/Si比的C-(N)-A-S-H通过类离子交换（ion-exchange-like）机制表现出最强固定能力；C-S-H主要通过表面羟基氧和Ca介导键合固定离子；N-A-S-H呈现更分布化的结合环境；Pb²⁺与Ba²⁺的固定机制相似，Cs⁺则表现出与硅酸盐/铝硅酸盐氧位点不同的凝胶依赖性相互作用；新引入的相对总结合强度（relative total binding strength, rTBS）描述符与离子固定程度呈强正相关。

Conclusion: 研究阐明了不同凝胶类型和离子种类在理想化水泥纳米孔中控制重金属保留的机制，并提供了一个可用于预测和设计固化材料性能的原子框架。

Abstract: Cementitious materials are widely used for hazardous-waste encapsulation, yet the molecular mechanisms governing heavy-metal ion retention across different gel chemistries remain insufficiently resolved. Here, classical molecular dynamics simulations were employed to investigate the adsorption-controlled mobility of representative heavy-metal ions (Pb2+, Ba2+, and Cs+) within nanopores of C-S-H, C-(N)-A-S-H, and N-A-S-H gels. By combining pore-averaged diffusivity, spatially resolved diffusivity and residence-time analysis, ion-density profiles, two-dimensional adsorption maps, radial distribution functions, coordination analysis, and interfacial binding-strength descriptors, this study establishes a comparative atomistic framework linking gel surface chemistry to ion mobility suppression under nanoconfinement. Ion mobility is substantially reduced in all gel nanopores relative to bulk solutions, but the extent and mechanism of suppression vary strongly with gel chemistry. C-(N)-A-S-H with higher Al/Si ratios exhibits the strongest retention, driven by ion accumulation around Al-linked oxygen species via an ion-exchange-like mechanism with charge-balancing Na+. C-S-H immobilizes ions primarily through surface hydroxyl oxygens and Ca-mediated linkages, whereas N-A-S-H exhibits more distributed binding environments. Pb2+ and Ba2+ exhibit broadly similar immobilization mechanisms, whereas Cs+ shows more distinct, gel-dependent interactions with silicate and aluminosilicate oxygen sites. A relative total binding strength (rTBS) descriptor is introduced, showing a strong positive correlation with the extent of ion immobilization across gel types, ion species, and pore sizes examined. These results clarify gel-specific and ion-specific mechanisms controlling heavy-metal retention in idealized cementitious nanopores.

</details>

### [178] [Catching UHE Neutrinos with HERON](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12081)
*Andrew Zeolla*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: HERON（Hybrid Elevated Radio Observatory for Neutrinos）是一种新提出的超高能地球掠射τ中微子探测器，利用24个紧凑型相控射电阵列与360个独立天线的稀疏阵列结合，部署在山脉沿线，通过探测τ轻子逃逸大气引发的上行广延大气簇射的射电辐射，实现超大瞬时有效面积和高指向精度，适用于天体物理瞬变事件探测与多信使天文学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的中微子探测器在超高能（ultrahigh energy）波段对瞬变天体源（如伽马射线暴）的探测能力有限，需要更大有效面积和更高指向精度的探测方案来推进超高能中微子天文学（UHE neutrino astronomy）与多信使（multi-messenger）观测。

Method: HERON采用混合架构：24个紧凑型相控射电阵列（phased radio arrays）嵌入由360个独立天线（standalone antennas）组成的更大稀疏阵列中，整体沿山脉分布。利用地球掠射（Earth-skimming）的超高能τ中微子与地球相互作用产生的τ轻子逃逸到大气中，引发上行广延大气簇射（up-going extensive air showers），并通过探测这些簇射的射电辐射来识别中微子事件。

Result: 由于高海拔观测站点和射电信号的长传播距离，HERON在地平线方向获得了极大的瞬时有效面积（instantaneous effective area），从而在高能天体物理瞬变事件（如伽马射线暴）探测方面表现出色。稀疏阵列提供了优异的指向分辨率（pointing resolution）。

Conclusion: HERON具备开展超高能中微子天文学研究的潜力，并可被纳入更广泛的多信使仪器网络（network of multi-messenger instruments），为天体物理瞬变源的探测与定位提供新手段。

Abstract: The Hybrid Elevated Radio Observatory for Neutrinos, or HERON, is a newly proposed ultrahigh energy Earth-skimming tau neutrino detector. Ultrahigh energy tau neutrinos which skim the Earth may produce $τ$-leptons which escape into the atmosphere and initiate up-going extensive air showers. The HERON concept consists of 24 compact phased radio arrays, embedded within a larger sparse array of 360 standalone antennas, distributed along a mountain range and designed to capture the radio emission of these up-going extensive air showers. Due to the high elevation observation sites and the long propagation length of radio, HERON achieves a very large instantaneous effective area towards the horizon, and thus excels at the detection of astrophysical transient events such as gamma-ray bursts. With the excellent pointing resolution offered by the sparse array, HERON would be capable of conducting UHE neutrino astronomy and could be incorporated into the broader network of multi-messenger instruments. Here, we detail the HERON concept and describe the science which can be accomplished with it.

</details>


### [179] [Black Hole Binary Detection Landscape for the Laser Interferometer Lunar Antenna (LILA): Signal-to-Noise Calculations & Science Cases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11283)
*Tintin Nguyen,Anjali Yelikar,Ryan Nowicki,Karan Jani,Angelo Ricarte*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出月球激光干涉天线（LILA）引力波项目，通过利用月球环境探测分赫兹频带，实现对中等质量黑洞（IMBH）双星及其相关系统的观测，揭示早期宇宙大质量黑洞起源并补充现有地面引力波探测器（LIGO/Virgo/KAGRA）的观测空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力波探测器（如LIGO/Virgo/KAGRA）在分赫兹频带（deci-Hz band）存在观测盲区，而月球环境具有独特优势填补这一空白，从而探测中等质量黑洞（intermediate-mass black hole, IMBH）双星及其演化过程，推动对早期宇宙大质量黑洞种群的理解。

Method: 通过部署月球激光干涉天线（LILA）引力波项目，利用月球稳定环境实现分赫兹频带引力波观测；计划开展4年连续观测周期，针对中等质量黑洞（IMBH）双星（质量约$10^2-10^6 \, M_{\odot}$）及中等质量比旋进系统（intermediate-mass-ratio inspiral, IMRI）进行探测，并结合高信噪比（SNR $\gtrsim 100$）事件开展强场引力检验（strong-field tests of gravity）。

Result: LILA可将中等质量黑洞（IMBH）的探测范围延伸至早期宇宙（红移$z \sim 20-30$）；可探测总质量约$10^4-10^6 \, M_{\odot}$、质量比约$10^{-4}-10^{-2}$的中等质量比旋进系统（IMRI）；能在双星并合前数月到数年发现具有可测偏心率残余（eccentricity residuals）的IMBH双星；可观测到高信噪比（$\gtrsim 100$）事件；将恒星起源黑洞的质量上限扩展至$\gtrsim 250 \, M_{\odot}$。

Conclusion: LILA将为理解大质量黑洞的形成与演化、黑洞双星的天体物理环境及演化路径提供重要见解；其观测结果将补充LIGO/Virgo/KAGRA在对不稳定质量间隙事件（pair-instability mass gap events）、层级并合候选体（hierarchical merger candidates）及轻质量IMBH并合方面的探测，同时拓展已发现恒星起源黑洞的上限质量。

Abstract: The Laser Interferometer Lunar Antenna (LILA) is a proposed gravitational-wave project aiming to take full advantage of the Moon's environment to access the deci-Hz band and detect intermediate-mass black hole (IMBH) binaries of mass $\sim 10^2-10^6 \, M_{\odot}$ (arXiv:2508.11631). With an observational period of 4 years, LILA can extend its IMBH detection horizon to the very early Universe, directly probing the first population of massive black holes ($z \sim 20-30$). LILA could also detect intermediate-mass-ratio inspiral systems with a total mass of $\sim 10^4 - 10^6 \, M_{\odot}$ and a mass ratio of $\sim 10^{-4} - 10^{-2}$. LILA can discover IMBH binaries months to years before merger with measurable eccentricity residuals retained from their formation, providing crucial early warning for multi-messenger and multi-band follow-up. The high SNR ($\gtrsim 100$) events detectable with LILA would enable strong-field tests of gravity. With these capabilities, LILA will provide important insights into the formation and evolution of massive black holes, as well as the astrophysical environments and evolutionary pathways of black hole binaries. LILA will also complement current LIGO/Virgo/KAGRA detections of pair-instability mass gap events, hierarchical merger candidates, and light IMBH mergers, while expanding the upper envelope of discovered black holes with stellar origin to masses of $\gtrsim 250 \, M_{\odot}$.

</details>


### [180] [Precessing Black Hole Jets and Galactic Fossils](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12448)
*Maria J. Rodriguez*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出银河系中心伽马射线超出（GCE）与费米/eROSITA气泡（FEB）均源自同一历史时期人马座A*（SgrA*）的活动：一个倾斜磁抑制盘驱动的进动抛物面Blandford-Znajek喷流，在约7.5百万年前的活跃期结束后，既吹出了千秒差距尺度的FEB，又注入了强子宇宙射线贡献GCE通量。对于EHT偏好的自旋参数a* = 0.9，强子成分占GCE面亮度的约3–14%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 银河系中心伽马射线超出（GCE）——即费米卫星在大约2–5 GeV能量范围内探测到的来自SgrA*周围的异常信号——已存在超过十五年而无共识解释。暗物质湮灭与未分解毫秒脉冲星种群是两大主要候选机制，但二者均未考虑SgrA*过去活动的化石记录，即费米气泡与eROSITA气泡（FEB）。因此有必要提出一个能够统一解释GCE与FEB的物理框架。

Method: 模型基于三个独立验证的输入：EHT提出SgrA*自旋轴相对于银河系旋转轴存在约35°倾斜；活跃期内盘通过Lense-Thirring进动完成约5个方位角周期；采用双区宇宙线输运模型，结合银河系内区标准扩散系数描述宇宙线在中央分子区（CMZ）和核球中的传播。通过验证质子拉莫尔半径将宇宙线约束在喷流柱内、以及指向银心的伽马射线光学深度可忽略，确保模型内部自洽性。

Result: 与当前GCE观测的比较表明，强子贡献依赖于黑洞自旋：对于EHT偏好的SgrA*自旋参数a* = 0.9，强子成分不可约地贡献了内10度范围内观测GCE面亮度的约3–14%。这揭示了一个此前未被探索的GCE组成部分，对构建完整GCE模型具有意义。

Conclusion: GCE和FEB可以统一解释为SgrA*过去一次喷流活动的化石印记，其中强子宇宙线贡献构成GCE通量的一个不可忽略且此前未被考虑的组分。该结果为理解银河系中心高能现象及其与星系核历史活动的关联提供了新视角，并强调了自旋参数在定量预测中的关键作用。

Abstract: The Galactic Centre gamma-ray excess (GCE) - an anomalous ~ 2-5 GeV Fermi-LAT signal around SgrA$^{\star}$ - has remained without a consensus interpretation for more than fifteen years. Dark-matter annihilation and unresolved millisecond-pulsar populations remain the leading candidates, yet neither incorporates the past activity of SgrA$^{\star}$ recorded by the Fermi and eROSITA bubbles (FEB). We propose a unified scenario in which both the GCE and the FEB are fossil imprints of a single past episode of SgrA$^{\star}$ activity: a precessing parabolic Blandford-Znajek jet launched from a tilted, magnetically arrested disc during a ~7.5 Myr active phase ending ~ 2.6 Myr ago. The jet both inflated the kpc-scale FEB and injected hadronic cosmic rays contributing to the GCE flux. The model rests on three independently motivated inputs: the EHT-proposed ~ $35^{\circ}$ tilt of the SgrA$^{\star}$ spin axis from the Galactic rotation axis, Lense-Thirring precession of the disc through ~5 azimuthal cycles during the active phase, and a two-zone cosmic-ray transport prescription through the CMZ and bulge with standard inner-Galaxy diffusion coefficients. Internal consistency is verified by checking that the proton Larmor radius confines cosmic rays to the jet column and that the gamma-ray optical depth toward the Galactic Centre is negligible. Comparison with current GCE observations yields a spin-dependent hadronic contribution: for the EHT-favoured SgrA$^{\star}$ spin a$^{\star}$ = 0.9, we find an irreducible hadronic floor of ~ 3-14% of the observed GCE surface brightness across the inner ten degrees, highlighting a previously unexplored component relevant for comprehensive models of the GCE.

</details>


### [181] [Black Hole Ringdown Seen in Photon Polarization Swings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11499)
*Jiewei Huang,Yehui Hou,Zhen Zhong,Minyong Guo,Bin Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个协变微扰框架，用于描述极化光子在弯曲时空中的传播，并推导出克尔黑洞铃宕（ringdown）过程中可观测偏振角摆动的紧凑表达式。结果表明，偏振角摆动与准正则模（quasi-normal modes）在时域上锁定，振幅可达约10度，为黑洞并合与铃宕过程提供了新的偏振测量窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索扰动时空中的光传播能否将引力波波形直接印刻在电磁可观测量的偏振信号上，从而建立引力波与电磁波之间的直接关联。

Method: 采用协变微扰框架处理一般弯曲时空中的极化光子传播，推导出克尔黑洞铃宕过程中偏振角的解析表达式，并通过动力学射线追踪（dynamical ray-tracing）数值验证结果的普适性。

Result: 发现擦过强场区域的光子呈现出消色差（achromatic）的阻尼偏振角振荡，该振荡与铃宕过程同步，相位由准正则模的角结构决定，摆动振幅可达约10度，并在空间分辨的自相关中留下独特特征。

Conclusion: 该研究为黑洞并合与铃宕过程的观测开辟了一个新的偏振测量窗口（polarimetric window），使得通过电磁偏振信号直接探测引力波波形成为可能。

Abstract: Light propagating through a perturbed spacetime could imprint the underlying gravitational waveform directly onto electromagnetic observables. In this Letter, we develop a covariant perturbative framework for polarized photon propagation in generic curved spacetimes, and derive a compact expression for the observable polarization-angle (PA) swing during Kerr ringdown, explicitly demonstrating its time-domain locking to the quasi-normal modes. We confirm this behavior using dynamical ray-tracing calculations for a broad class of photon trajectories. Photons grazing the strong-field region exhibit an achromatic, damped PA oscillation that tracks the ringdown, with a phase set by the mode's angular structure. The swing amplitude can reach $\sim 10^{\circ}$ and leaves distinctive signatures in spatially resolved autocorrelations. These results open a new polarimetric window onto black hole mergers and ringdown.

</details>


### [182] [A New Timing Signature of Black Hole Spin: Time-Delay Asymmetry in Kerr Accretion Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11734)
*Shakibul Chowdhury*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的广义相对论时间观测量（timing observable），用于测量黑洞自旋（spin）导致的光子到达时间反射对称性破缺（reflection symmetry breaking）。通过克尔（Kerr）时空中的反向光线追踪（backward ray tracing）构建时延图（time-delay maps），定义镜面对称不对称性（mirror-paired asymmetry）$A_t$，并证明其随自旋增加而增大，且与观测者倾角和辐射半径密切相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统时域分析（timing analysis）基于空间积分信号，无法提取黑洞自旋在光子传播过程中编码的方向信息。本文旨在构造一种能够直接测量克尔度规（Kerr metric）中光子顺行与逆行轨迹系统差异的时域观测量，以提供黑洞旋转的物理驱动定时特征。

Method: 在克尔时空下执行反向光线追踪，构建观测者像平面上的时延图；定义基于光子从投影自旋轴两侧到达的镜面对称不对称性；通过施瓦西（Schwarzschild）极限（$a=0$）验证数值精度。

Result: 施瓦西黑洞下不对称性在数值精度内为零，验证方法有效性；旋转黑洞中，克尔旋转破坏零测地线（null geodesics）的左右传播对称性，产生非零的镜面时延不对称性$A_t$；$A_t$值随自旋增大而增大，并强烈依赖于观测者倾角和发射半径，最大信号出现在靠近黑洞的发射区域和中高倾角情形；转换为物理单位后，代表性超大质量黑洞系统的时间偏移为秒至小时量级。

Conclusion: 所提出的观测量能够从时间域提取克尔光子传播中的方向信息，为强引力定时研究和X射线回响映射（X-ray reverberation mapping）提供了黑洞旋转的物理驱动定时特征。

Abstract: We introduce a new general-relativistic timing observable that measures the breaking of reflection symmetry in photon arrival times caused by black hole spin. Using backward ray tracing in the Kerr spacetime, we construct time-delay maps across the observer image plane and define a mirror-paired asymmetry based on photons arriving from opposite sides of the projected spin axis. In the Schwarzschild limit ($a=0$), the asymmetry vanishes to numerical precision, providing a stringent validation test of the method. For rotating black holes, Kerr rotation breaks the left-right propagation symmetry of null geodesics, producing systematic differences between prograde and retrograde photon trajectories and resulting in a nonzero mirror-paired timing asymmetry, $A_t$. We find that $A_t$ increases with spin and depends strongly on observer inclination and emission radius, with the largest signals arising from emission close to the black hole and from intermediate to high inclinations. Converting the dimensionless asymmetry into physical units yields timing offsets ranging from seconds to hours for representative supermassive black hole systems. Unlike traditional timing analyses based on spatially integrated signals, the observable introduced here isolates directional information encoded in Kerr photon propagation and provides a physically motivated timing signature of black hole rotation. We discuss the implications of this effect for strong-gravity timing studies and X-ray reverberation mapping.

</details>


### [183] [Inferring host environment properties and gravitational-wave decay time from the eccentricity measurement of dynamically captured binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11947)
*A. Vincent Paul,Parthapratim Mahapatra,Marc Favata,K. G. Arun*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用偏心率和质量后验概率来识别动态引力波俘获事件宿主环境的诊断方法，并将其应用于GW200105和GW190521事件，结果表明GW200105有71%概率源自核星团（NSC）、29%概率源自球状星团（GC）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 致密恒星环境中的动态俘获（dynamical capture）是产生偏心致密双星并合（eccentric compact binary mergers）的重要渠道，但目前尚无确定性的偏心并合探测事件。若未来探测到偏心引力波事件，需要一种方法从单次事件中识别其宿主天体物理环境。

Method: 假设观测到的偏心事件源自动态引力波俘获（dynamical gravitational wave capture），将偏心率后验概率（eccentricity posterior）映射到关键俘获参数的后验概率，包括无穷远相对速度（relative velocity at infinity）和碰撞参数（impact parameter）。将这些参数与不同天体物理环境预期的速度分布进行比较，从而对宿主环境施加约束。

Result: 将该框架应用于中子星-黑洞并合事件GW200105，通过与球状星团（GC）和核星团（NSC）核心中子星的速度弥散分布比较，得到GW200105在GC中并合的概率为29%，在NSC中为71%。该方法对GW190521的约束较弱。此外，推断GW200105从俘获到并合的引力波衰变时间（GW decay time）为11–156天。

Conclusion: 该方法可为单次偏心并合事件提供宿主环境的宝贵天体物理诊断，并可推广至偏心双星群体。随着未来探测到更多偏心并合事件，该方法将具有重要的应用价值。

Abstract: Dynamical capture in dense stellar environments is a promising channel for producing eccentric compact binary mergers. Although there have been no confident detections of eccentric mergers to date, a few candidates show indications of non-negligible in-band eccentricity upon re-analysis of the data. By assuming an observed eccentric event originates from a dynamical gravitational wave (GW) capture, we show that it is possible to identify the host environment using the eccentricity and mass posteriors. In particular, the eccentricity posterior can be mapped to posteriors on key capture parameters, such as the relative velocity at infinity and the impact parameter. By comparing these with the expected velocity distributions of different astrophysical environments, we can place constraints on the likely host. Assuming that it originated from a GW capture, we applied this framework to the neutron star-black hole merger GW200105. By comparing with the velocity dispersion distributions of neutron stars in the cores of globular clusters (GCs) and nuclear star clusters (NSCs), we find the probability that GW200105 merged in a GC (NSC) to be 29% (71%). As we anticipate detecting several eccentric mergers in the future, this method can provide a valuable astrophysical diagnostic of their host environments on a single-event basis; this can be straightforwardly generalized to a population of eccentric binaries. The formalism we develop is also applied to GW190521, but is less constraining for that event. Lastly, we infer a GW decay time from capture to merger of 11-156 days for GW200105.

</details>

### [184] [Contrasting structural reversibility and magnetic correlations in isostructural honeycomb magnets CrCl$_3$ and $α$-RuCl$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11106)
*Zachary Morgan,Iris Ye,Jiasen Guo,Michael A McGuire,Jiaqiang Yan*

TL;DR: 通过中子单晶衍射对比研究了层状卤化物 CrCl₃ 和 α-RuCl₃ 的结构与磁性，发现两者在高温 C2/m 到低温 R$\bar{3}$ 的一级结构相变中面内晶格响应截然不同，且表现出差异显著的磁散射行为，源于层间滑移能与不同电子构型（electronic configurations）的协同作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究具有蜂窝状（honeycomb）过渡金属离子排列但电子构型不同的两种层状卤化物 CrCl₃ 和 α-RuCl₃ 在结构相变与磁性行为上的异同，揭示层间滑移动力学与电子构型的关联。

Method: 采用中子单晶衍射（neutron single crystal diffraction）对比研究两种化合物的结构相变、晶格响应和磁有序（magnetic ordering）特性。

Result: 两者在 c 轴晶格均表现出阶梯状变化，反映层间堆叠重组；但面内晶格响应迥异：α-RuCl₃ 呈现突变滞后变化且伴随热循环下的渐进晶格退化，CrCl₃ 则呈现平滑演变且结构稳定。CrCl₃ 在 TN=14 K 形成 A 型反铁磁（A-type antiferromagnetic）结构，漫散射延伸至约 40 K；α-RuCl₃ 在 TN=7.6 K 出现之字形反铁磁（zig-zag antiferromagnetic）有序，但无明显的磁漫散射。

Conclusion: 对比的结构与磁行为源于层间滑移（interlayer sliding）能量学与两种化合物根本不同的电子构型之间的相互作用。

Abstract: We report a comparative neutron single crystal diffraction study of the structural and magnetic properties of layered halides CrCl$_3$ and $α$-RuCl$_3$, which host a honeycomb arrangement of transition metal ions with distinct electronic configurations and undergo a first-order structural transition between high-temperature \textit{C}2/\textit{m} and low-temperature \textit{R}$\bar{3}$. Both compounds show a step-like change in the $c$-lattice, consistent with an expected stacking rearrangement. In contrast, the in-plane lattice response is quite different: $α$-RuCl$_3$ exhibits an abrupt hysteretic change across the transition accompanied by progressive crystalline degradation upon thermal cycling, whereas CrCl$_3$ shows a smooth in-plane lattice evolution and remains structurally robust. Magnetically, CrCl$_3$ orders into an A-type antiferromagnetic structure at T$_N$=14\,K and exhibits pronounced diffuse magnetic scattering extending up to about 40\,K. $α$-RuCl$_3$ shows no observable magnetic diffuse scattering above its zig-zag antiferromagnetic ordering temperature T$_N$=7.6\,K. These results suggest that the contrasting structural and magnetic behaviors arise from an interplay between interlayer sliding energetics and the fundamentally different electronic configurations of the two compounds.

### [185] [Unbiased large-$N$ approach to competing vestigial orders of density-wave and superconducting instabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11281)
*Grgur Palle,Rafael M. Fernandes*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文揭示了大$N$方法在处理残余序（vestigial orders）时存在的内在歧义性——该歧义源于不同复合序参量（composite OP）之间的冗余关系（如Fierz恒等式）。作者提出了一种无偏的大$N$方法，该方案尊重冗余关系和对称群结构，能唯一确定所有残余通道的有效相互作用。分析表明，在四阶朗道系数的参数空间中普遍存在残余序不稳定的区域，并通过电荷密度波、自旋密度波和多组分超导体等系统验证了该结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多分量主序参量（primary order parameter）支持多个残余通道（vestigial channels），每个通道由二次或更高阶的复合序参量描述。但标准的大$N$方法在解耦复合序参量时存在内在歧义性，可能导致人为增强或完全消除残余不稳定性（vestigial instability），需要建立一种无偏且自洽的处理方案。

Method: 作者证明标准大$N$方法中的歧义源于复合序参量之间的冗余关系（redundancy relations），即Fierz恒等式（Fierz identities），这些关系反映了不同残余通道之间的相互干扰，不能单独处理。为此提出一种无偏的大$N$方法（unbiased large-$N$ approach），该方法同时尊重冗余关系和底层对称群结构（underlying symmetry-group structure），从而为所有残余通道给出唯一的有效相互作用值。

Result: 分析揭示了在四阶朗道系数（quartic Landau coefficients）的参数空间中普遍存在残余序不稳定的区域，这与标准大$N$方法的结果相悖，但与弱耦合方法（weak-coupling approach）和变分方法（variational approach）一致。通过分析四方晶系中的电荷密度波（charge-density waves）、六方晶系中的自旋密度波（spin-density waves）以及立方晶系中的多组分超导体（multi-component superconductors）等系统中的残余序，验证了该方法的有效性，并发现了描述自旋四极（spin-quadrupolar）、电荷$4e$超导（charge-$4e$ superconducting）和交替磁性（altermagnetic orders）等奇异残余相。

Conclusion: 复合序参量之间的Fierz恒等式导致的冗余关系是标准大$N$方法歧义性的根本原因；所提出的无偏大$N$方法能够在尊重对称性和冗余关系的框架下唯一确定残余通道的有效相互作用，从而正确预测残余序的稳定区域。

Abstract: When a primary order breaks multiple symmetries, partially ordered phases that only break a subset of those symmetries, known as vestigial phases, may onset at a higher temperature. This concept has been applied to a wide range of systems, including iron pnictides, cuprates, van der Waals antiferromagnets, doped topological insulators, and twisted bilayer graphene. In general, a multi-component primary order parameter (OP) supports multiple vestigial channels, each described by a quadratic (or higher-order) composite OP. However, the standard large-$N$ approach to the Ginzburg-Landau action of the primary OP has an intrinsic ambiguity in how one decouples the composite OPs, leading to situations in which one can seemingly enhance or eliminate altogether any vestigial instability. Here, we show that this ambiguity is a direct consequence of redundancy relations, such as Fierz identities, that relate different composite OPs, reflecting the fact that different vestigial channels interfere with each other and thus cannot be treated separately. To resolve this ambiguity, we propose an unbiased large-$N$ approach that respects both the redundancy relations and the underlying symmetry-group structure, and that gives unique values for the effective interactions of all vestigial channels. Our analysis reveals the generic existence of regions in the parameter space of quartic Landau coefficients where no vestigial order is stable, in contrast to the standard large-$N$ approach, but in agreement with weak-coupling and variational approaches. We illustrate our results by analyzing the vestigial orders of charge-density waves, spin-density waves, and multi-component superconductors in tetragonal, hexagonal, and cubic systems, respectively, revealing the presence of exotic vestigial phases describing spin-quadrupolar, charge-$4e$ superconducting, and altermagnetic orders.

Abstract: By means of slave-boson theory for the Hubbard model on the checkerboard lattice, we calculate dynamical altermagnetic spin susceptibilities from the metallic to the Mott-insulating regime. We track magnon dispersion and lifetime renormalization, allowing us to uncover a crossover from a chirality-selective dissipation of magnon modes to coherent yet strongly deformed chiral magnon branches across the metal insulator transition. Our formalism lends itself to a quantitative description of collective spin dynamics in correlated altermagnets.

### [187] [CERTIFY-ED: A Multi-Layer Verification Framework for Exact Diagonalization of Quantum Many-Body Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11787)
*Sarang Vehale,Ritu Goel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出并实现了一个名为 certify-ed 的验证框架，旨在为精确对角化（ED）计算结果提供可机器验证的正确性证明，弥补该领域长期缺乏数值验证实践的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确对角化（exact diagonalization, ED）是计算量子多体物理（quantum many-body physics）的核心技术，但发表的ED结果极少附带机器可验证的正确性证据，社区仅依赖隐式的信任链（LAPACK → 用户代码 → 结果），这种做法不足以支撑基于ED结果的理论主张。

Method: certify-ed 框架包含三个核心组件：(i) 多参考（multi-oracle）特征求解器，运行三条独立的 LAPACK 路径并报告两两不一致程度；(ii) 13个逻辑独立的验证层，涵盖代数不变量、解析极限、替代算法、任意精度参考计算、守恒律、动力学一致性以及有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）；(iii) 防篡改的 SHA-256 哈希证书，供下游消费者验证。此外还附带错误注入层，用于确认整个流程能检测六类注入错误。

Result: 在从一维自旋链到二维 Kitaev 蜂巢团簇的16个物理模型上，参考实现通过了全部53个单元测试和81个独立验证测试，耗时不到30秒。与 QuSpin 的320个特征值比较中，最大不一致程度为 $1.6\times 10^{-14}$，与50位 mpmath 参考值的一致程度达到 $1.6\times 10^{-15}$。

Conclusion: certify-ed 作为与现有ED软件包（QuSpin、XDiag、ALPS）并行的验证框架，而非替代品，能够高效、系统地验证ED计算结果的数值正确性，显著提升了该领域结果的可信度与可复现性。

Abstract: Exact diagonalization (ED) is a workhorse technique in computational quantum many-body physics, but published ED results are rarely accompanied by machine-checkable evidence of their numerical correctness. The community typically relies on the implicit trust chain LAPACK $\to$ user code $\to$ result, with at most informal agreement against another package treated as confirmation. We argue that this practice is inadequate for a method whose output frequently underpins theoretical claims, and we present \textsc{certify-ed}, a verification framework designed to be used \emph{alongside} existing ED packages (QuSpin, XDiag, ALPS) rather than as a replacement for them. The framework consists of (i) a multi-oracle eigensolver that runs three independent LAPACK paths and reports their pairwise disagreement, (ii) thirteen logically independent validation layers covering algebraic invariants, analytic limits, alternative algorithms, arbitrary-precision reference computation, conservation laws, dynamical consistency, and finite-size scaling, and (iii) tamper-evident SHA-256 hashed certificates that downstream consumers can verify. The framework also ships an error-injection layer that confirms the entire pipeline detects six injected error classes. Running on sixteen physics models from one-dimensional spin chains to two-dimensional Kitaev honeycomb clusters, our reference implementation passes 53 of 53 unit tests and 81 of 81 individual validation tests in under thirty seconds, with maximum disagreement against QuSpin of $1.6\times 10^{-14}$ across 320 eigenvalue comparisons, and agreement with 50-digit \texttt{mpmath} reference values to $1.6\times 10^{-15}$. The package is released under the MIT license on Zenodo and Github

### [188] [Exciton-roton mode in moiré fractional Chern insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11794)
*Xiaoyang Shen,Zijian Zhou,Ruiping Guo,Renqi Wang,Wenhui Duan,Chong Wang,Yong Xu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和变分贝特-萨佩特方程（Bethe-Salpeter equation）方法对扭曲二碲化钼（twisted MoTe₂）体系进行理论计算，分析磁旋子-莫尔é能带间激发的杂化行为。

Result: 磁旋子与莫尔é能带间激发的杂化由量子几何（quantum geometry）调控，产生了兼具激子光学响应和FCI旋子极小值特征的激子-旋子模；该模式保持在低能位置，激发能量低于能带间跃迁，并具有光学活性，导致双峰光谱特征。

Conclusion: 这些结果将光学光谱学（optical spectroscopy）确定为直接探测莫尔é FCIs中集体激发的有效方法。

Abstract: Moiré fractional Chern insulators (FCIs) are a novel class of quantum matter that realizes fractional quantum Hall (FQH) physics in zero magnetic field and provides a platform for exploring unconventional collective excitations. Here we show that hybridization between the magneto-roton and moiré interband excitations gives rise to an exciton-roton mode absent in continuum FQH systems in the long-wavelength limit. Using exact diagonalization and a variational Bethe-Salpeter equation for twisted MoTe$_2$, we demonstrate that this hybridization is controlled by the quantum geometry and yields a mode that combines excitonic optical response with the characteristic FCI roton minimum. The resulting exciton-roton remains low-lying, with excitation energy below the interband transition, and acquires optical activity, leading to a double-peak spectroscopic signature. These results identify optical spectroscopy as a direct probe of collective excitations in moiré FCIs.

### [189] [Relationship between doping-induced in-gap states and spin excitations in Kitaev-Hubbard models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11830)
*Si-Qi Hou,Shun-Li Yu,Zhao-Yang Dong,Jian-Xin Li*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过团簇微扰理论（cluster perturbation theory）研究一维和准一维Kitaev-Hubbard模型，揭示了掺杂Mott绝缘体中由掺杂诱导的带内态（in-gap states）与自旋激发（spin excitations）之间的直接对应关系。带内态的色散与自旋激发谱高度一致，可反映从海森堡模型到伊辛模型的转变、Kitaev极限下的Jordan-Wigner费米子谱，以及自旋激发分数化和拓扑Z₂涡旋（vison）等现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究掺杂Mott绝缘体（Mott insulators）中由掺杂诱导的带内态（in-gap states）与底层自旋激发（spin excitations）之间的内在联系，以期为通过电荷激发谱学手段探测量子自旋现象（如分数化和拓扑激发）提供新的实验途径。

Method: 在一维（one-dimensional, 1D）和准一维Kitaev-Hubbard模型上应用团簇微扰理论（cluster perturbation theory），通过调节类Kitaev跳跃项（$t^{\prime}$）在强耦合极限下选择性控制自旋各向异性（spin anisotropies），从而对比分析带内态与自旋激发谱的对应关系。

Result: 在Z链中，带内态从无能隙色散演变为有能隙平带，能隙标度为$2t^{\prime 2}/U$，与伊辛自旋能隙（Ising spin gap）一致；在XY链的Kitaev极限下，带内态分裂为一个色散支和一个平带支，完美对应Jordan-Wigner费米子谱（Jordan-Wigner fermionic spectrum）；在两腿梯子模型中，出现宽连续谱带内态，反映自旋激发分数化（fractionalization），并伴随体现拓扑Z₂涡旋（topological $Z_2$ visons）的能隙。

Conclusion: 掺杂Mott绝缘体中电荷动力学与自旋动力学之间建立了稳健的对应关系，带内态可作为探测分数化和拓扑激发等奇异量子自旋现象的有效探针，为通过电荷激发谱学手段研究自旋液体（spin liquids）提供了新途径。

Abstract: We investigate the connection between doping-induced in-gap states and underlying spin excitations in Mott insulators by employing cluster perturbation theory on one-dimensional (1D) and quasi-1D Kitaev-Hubbard models. By manipulating Kitaev-like hopping terms ($t^{\prime}$) that selectively control spin anisotropies in the strong-coupling limit, we establish a direct correspondence between the kinetic dispersion of the in-gap states and the spin excitation spectra. Specifically, in the Z chain, in-gap states evolve from a gapless dispersion to a gapped flat band as the system transitions from the Heisenberg to the Ising model, exhibiting a gap scaling of $2t^{\prime 2}/U$ that matches the Ising spin gap. In the XY chain, the in-gap states split into a dispersive and a flat branch at the Kitaev limit, perfectly mirroring the Jordan-Wigner fermionic spectrum. For the two-leg ladder, we observe an emergent broad continuum of in-gap states that reflects the fractionalization of spin excitations, accompanied by a gap manifesting the presence of topological $Z_2$ visons. Our results establish a robust correspondence between charge and spin dynamics in doped Mott insulators and demonstrate that in-gap states can serve as a probe of exotic quantum spin phenomena, including fractionalization and topological excitations, offering a new pathway to investigate spin liquids via spectroscopic probes of charge excitations.

</details>


### [190] [Staggered spin susceptibility at a two-dimensional antiferromagnetic quantum critical point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11965)
*Y. Itoh*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文通过自洽重整化理论，在量子临界点（quantum critical point）处研究二维反铁磁自旋涨落（antiferromagnetic spin fluctuations）的有限温度交错自旋磁化率χ(Q)与模-模耦合常数y₁的关系，发现y₁=0.1可作为划分弱耦合区居里定律（Curie law）与强耦合区居里-外斯型（Curie-Weiss type）或幂律型温度依赖关系的判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子临界点附近，零点半经典量子涨落（zero-point quantum fluctuations）对有限温度自旋磁化率的温度依赖行为的影响尚不完全清楚，需要建立一个定量的分类判据。

Method: 采用自洽重整化理论（self-consistent renormalization theory），设定零点半经典量子涨落参数y₀=0，将模-模耦合常数y₁作为关键控制参数，系统计算有限温度交错自旋磁化率χ(Q)的温度依赖关系。

Result: 发现y₁=0.1是一个临界阈值：当y₁ < 0.1时，χ(Q)的温度依赖服从居里定律；当y₁ > 0.1时，则表现为居里-外斯型或幂律型温度依赖行为。

Conclusion: 模-模耦合常数y₁的强弱决定了零点自旋涨落对交错磁化率温度依赖性的影响模式，y₁=0.1可作为区分两种不同标度行为的临界值。

Abstract: We report on the finite temperature staggered spin susceptibility $χ(Q)$ as a function of the mode-mode coupling constant $y_1$ in the self-consistent renormalization theory of two-dimensional antiferromagnetic spin fluctuations with zero-point quantum fluctuations just at the quantum critical point ($y_0$ = 0). We find that the value $y_1$ = 0.1 is a criterion to classify the effect of the zero-point spin fluctuations on the temperature dependence of $χ(Q)$ into a Curie law for weak $y_1 < $ 0.1 and a Curie-Weiss type or a power law type for strong $y_1 > $ 0.1.

</details>


### [191] [Emergent Vortex Ordering in a Multiflavor Pyrochlore-Lattice Compound GeCo$_2$O$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12042)

TL;DR: 本研究通过中子散射实验与正则化回归框架相结合，在烧绿石晶格化合物GeCo₂O₄中发现了由纠缠的自旋与轨道自由度产生的涡旋晶格（vortex lattice），并识别出Kitaev相互作用（Kitaev interaction）是稳定该有序态的关键因素。

Motivation: 纠缠的自旋与轨道自由度（spin and orbital degrees of freedom）为产生传统自旋系统中无法实现的新型磁态提供了多自由度途径。然而，在三维材料中实现涡旋晶格（vortex lattice）的途径尚不明确，亟需实验验证。

Method: 研究结合了全面中子散射实验（neutron scattering experiments）与正则化回归框架（regularized regression framework），对烧绿石晶格（pyrochlore-lattice）化合物GeCo₂O₄中的磁有序结构进行表征与哈密顿量确定。

Result: 识别出最近邻Co²⁺赝自旋（pseudospin）之间存在显著的Kitaev相互作用（Kitaev interactions），该相互作用与几何阻挫（geometric frustration）协同作用，稳定了涡旋晶格（vortex lattice）有序态。

Conclusion: 该结果揭示了在三维Kitaev阻挫磁体（Kitaev-frustrated magnet）中实现涡旋晶格有序的意外途径，并展示了一种用于阻挫量子材料（frustrated quantum materials）哈密顿量确定的正则化实验协议。

Abstract: Entangled spin and orbital degrees of freedom provide a multiflavor route to novel magnetic states inaccessible in conventional spin systems. Here, we report the experimental identification of an emergent vortex lattice in the multiflavor pyrochlore-lattice compound GeCo$_2$O$_4$. By combining comprehensive neutron scattering experiments with a regularized regression framework, we identify substantial Kitaev interactions among the nearest-neighboring Co$^{2+}$ pseudospins, which cooperate with geometric frustration to stabilize the vortex order. These results reveal an unexpected route to vortex-lattice order in a three-dimensional Kitaev-frustrated magnet and demonstrate a regularized protocol for Hamiltonian determination in frustrated quantum materials.

### [192] [Magnetism and spin dynamics of Na\textsubscript{5}Yb(MoO\textsubscript{4})\textsubscript{4}: A weakly interacting rare-earth stretched diamond lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12045)
*N. Rajeesh Kumar,J. Khatua,Changhyun Koo,Izumi Umegaki,C. -E. Yin,C. -W. Wang,A. M. Strydom,H. -T. Jeng,Kwang-Yong Choi,R. Sankar,W. -T. Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文系统研究了Na₅Yb(MoO₄)₄的结构与磁性，确认其属于拉伸金刚石磁晶格（stretched diamond magnetic lattice）家族，在低至60 mK的温度下未发现长程磁有序（long-range magnetic order），表现为一种罕见的偶极量子顺磁体（dipolar quantum paramagnet），其中单离子物理与长程偶极相互作用占主导，而交换相互作用（exchange interactions）被抑制至毫开尔文能量尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索拉伸金刚石磁晶格家族中Na₅Yb(MoO₄)₄的结构与磁性，特别是研究在交换相互作用极弱的情况下，偶极相互作用能否稳定形成长程磁有序，并寻找可能存在的量子顺磁体（quantum paramagnet）新范例。

Method: 采用中子粉末衍射（neutron powder diffraction）在3.3 K下确定晶体结构；使用磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）和比热（specific heat）测量表征低温磁行为；利用密度泛函理论+U（DFT+U）计算评估交换相互作用；进行μ子自旋弛豫（muon spin relaxation）测量探测低能自旋动力学。

Result: 化合物在四方I4₁/a空间群中结晶，Yb离子间距为6.33 Å，形成三维拉伸金刚石框架。低至60 mK未发现长程磁有序。低温行为由J_eff = 1/2 Kramers双重基态（Kramers doublet ground state）主导，受畸变十二面体氧配位影响。DFT+U计算表明交换相互作用可忽略。比热显示有能隙的自旋激发（gapped spin excitations）特征，可能源于长程偶极关联。μ子自旋弛豫揭示持续的低能自旋动力学，偶极关联保持动态，无法在50 mK以下稳定静态磁有序。

Conclusion: Na₅Yb(MoO₄)₄被确认为一种罕见的偶极量子顺磁体，其磁性行为由单离子物理和长程偶极相互作用主导，交换相互作用被抑制至毫开尔文尺度，为研究偶极主导的量子磁体提供了重要平台。

Abstract: We report a comprehensive investigation of the structural and magnetic properties of Na$_5$Yb(MoO$_4$)$_4$, a member of the stretched diamond magnetic lattice family. Neutron powder diffraction at 3.3~K confirms that the compound crystallizes in the tetragonal \textit{I4$_1$/a} space group, with a large interatomic separation of 6.33~Å between magnetic Yb ions forming a three-dimensional stretched diamond framework. Magnetic susceptibility and specific heat measurements reveal no evidence of long-range magnetic order down to 60~mK. The low-temperature magnetic behavior is governed by an effective $J_{\mathrm{eff}} = 1/2$ Kramers doublet ground state, well separated from excited crystal-field levels, arising from the distorted dodecahedral oxygen coordination of Yb$^{3+}$. Density functional theory calculations within the DFT+$U$ framework indicate that exchange interactions between Yb ions are negligibly small, consistent with the long O--Mo--O super-superexchange pathways. The temperature dependence of the specific heat exhibits signatures of gapped spin excitations, most likely originating from long-range dipolar correlations and further shaped by weak exchange interactions together with the strong single-ion anisotropy of the Yb moments. Muon spin relaxation measurements reveal persistent low-energy spin dynamics, indicating that dipolar correlations remain dynamic and are insufficient to stabilize static magnetic order down to 50~mK. These results identify Na$_5$Yb(MoO$_4$)$_4$ as a rare example of a dipolar quantum paramagnet in which single-ion physics and long-range dipolar interactions dominate, while exchange interactions are suppressed to the millikelvin energy scale.

</details>


### [193] [$H$-linear magnetoresistance in NbSe$_2$ due to impeded cyclotron motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12048)
*A. Kool,D. Pizzirani,P. Tinnemans,S. Wiedmann,F. Flicker,J. van Wezel,N. E. Hussey,R. D. H. Hinlopen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过分析电荷密度波（CDW）化合物2H-NbSe₂中无序对磁电阻的影响，发现其线性磁电阻（LMR）与受阻回旋运动（ICM）的玻尔兹曼输运分析高度吻合，并将ICM的源头归因于CDW序连接高温费米圆柱体所形成的强散射“热点”，从而解释了LMR的成因以及电荷序态中量子振荡缺失的长期谜题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性磁电阻（LMR）在从半导体纳米结构到量子临界和奇异金属等多种量子材料中普遍存在，但尽管有多种理论解释，其完整物理机制仍不明确，且很可能依赖于具体的电子态。因此，需要针对特定体系（如电荷密度波化合物）深入研究LMR的起源。

Method: 本文以原型电荷密度波（CDW）化合物2H-NbSe₂为研究对象，通过实验测量无序对磁电阻形态的影响，并将实验结果与基于受阻回旋运动（ICM）的玻尔兹曼输运（Boltzmann transport）分析进行定性和定量比较。

Result: 实验测量的磁电阻与ICM的玻尔兹曼输运分析在定性和定量上均表现出高度一致。ICM的源头被识别为CDW序连接高温费米圆柱体所形成的强散射“热点”（hotspots），这些热点同时解释了LMR的产生以及2H-NbSe₂在电荷序态中量子振荡（quantum oscillations）长期缺失的现象。

Conclusion: 这些发现提供了强有力的证据，表明受阻回旋运动（ICM）在某些关联金属中是产生线性磁电阻（LMR）的机制。

Abstract: Linear magnetoresistance (LMR) is a widespread phenomenon observed in a host of quantum materials ranging from semiconductor nanostructures to quantum critical and strange metals. While multiple scenarios to explain LMR have been proposed, a complete understanding of the phenomenon remains elusive. Indeed, it is highly likely that the origin of LMR depends on the specific electronic state. Here, we report a study of the impact of disorder on the form of the magnetoresistance of the prototypical charge-density-wave (CDW) compound 2$H$-NbSe$_2$. The magnetoresistance is shown to exhibit strong qualitative and quantitative agreement with Boltzmann transport analysis incorporating impeded cyclotron motion (ICM). We identify the source of ICM in 2$H$-NbSe$_2$ as strong scattering sinks where the CDW order connects the high temperature Fermi cylinders. Such unusual "hotspots" provide an explanation for the observed LMR as well as for the long-unexplained absence of quantum oscillations inside the charge ordered state in 2$H$-NbSe$_2$. These findings provide strong evidence that ICM generates LMR in certain correlated metals.

</details>

### [194] [General and concise operator approach to the dyadic Green's function of layered media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12346)
*Aliaksandr Arlouski,Lei Gao,Dongliang Gao,Andrey Novitsky*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于算符方法（operator approach）推导各向异性平面分层介质（anisotropic planarly-layered medium）中电与磁场的并矢格林函数（dyadic Green's function）的新途径，将格林函数表示为各层演化算子（evolution operators）与表面阻抗张量（surface impedance tensors）的组合，并自然分离出奇异项（singular term）。该方法简化了物理理解与实际应用，并可推广至球面与柱面分层情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 并矢格林函数是计算光子学（computational photonics）中的重要工具，能够深入揭示光与物质相互作用（light-matter interaction）的物理机制。然而，对于各向异性分层介质，格林函数的推导通常较为复杂，亟需一种更简洁、概念更清晰的推导框架。

Method: 采用算符方法，将各向异性平面分层介质中电与磁场的并矢格林函数表达为各层演化算子（一种转移矩阵（transfer matrices）形式）与表面阻抗张量的函数，并从中自然分离出奇异项。

Result: 所得格林函数表达式结构清晰，奇异项与非奇异项分离；该方法同时适用于电场与磁场。此外，文中展示了若干实际应用示例，并指出该方法可轻松推广至球面与柱面分层介质。

Conclusion: 该算符方法简化了各向异性分层介质格林函数的推导与理解，为纳米光子学（nanophotonics）工程问题的求解提供了一种通用且可扩展的分析工具。

Abstract: Dyadic Green's function is an important tool of computational photonics, giving deeper insights into light-matter interaction. We present an operator approach to the derivation of the dyadic Green's function of a generic anisotropic planarly-layered medium for both electric and magnetic fields. The resulting Green's function is expressed through the evolution operators (a kind of transfer matrices) of the comprising layers and the surface impedance tensors, the singular term being naturally separated from other terms. The operator approach to the Green's function simplifies both the conceptual understanding of the problem and the subsequent practical applications, some of which are demonstrated here. The proposed approach can be easily generalized to the case of spherical and cylindrical layers. The obtained results can be applied in nanophotonics engineering problems.

</details>


### [195] [Plasmon exciton coupling enhances second order nonlinear response in borophene ZnO hybrid structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11173)
*Maximilian Black,Yaser Abdi,Prabhdeep Singh,Bharti Garg,Zahra Alavi,Mohammadreza Alikhanim,Mohammad Hossein Salemi Seresht,Fatemeh Chahshouri,Masoud Taleb,Nahid Talebi*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本研究通过在低维材料异质结构中结合各向异性硼烯（anisotropic borophene）和激子氧化锌（excitonic zinc oxide），实现了增强且共振的非线性光学响应，揭示了非线性等离激元-激子耦合（nonlinear plasmon-exciton coupling）作为调控频率转换的新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维材料中的非线性光学过程通常较弱或受对称性禁阻（symmetry forbidden），限制了其在纳米级光源和片上频率转换中的应用。因此，需要寻找增强低维材料非线性响应的方法。

Method: 构建硼烯-氧化锌异质结构（borophene-ZnO heterostructures），利用阴极发光（cathodoluminescence）和可调谐近红外激发下的二次谐波产生（second harmonic generation, SHG）测量非线性光学特性。

Result: 在400 nm和800 nm处观察到阴极发光强度提升了两个数量级，归因于增强的双光子吸收（two photon absorption, TPA）过程。在可调谐近红外激发下，出现清晰的二次谐波信号，具有二次功率依赖性和在800 nm附近的强共振行为。

Conclusion: 非线性等离激元-激子耦合重塑了激子响应，实现了高效的混合频率转换路径。各向异性等离激元-激子杂化（anisotropic plasmon-exciton hybridization）可作为控制低维异质结构中非线性光学响应的有效策略。

Abstract: Nonlinear optical processes in low dimensional materials are often weak or symmetry forbidden, limiting their use in nanoscale light sources and on chip frequency conversion. Here, we show that combining two weakly nonlinear systems, anisotropic borophene and excitonic zinc oxide, yields an enhanced and resonant nonlinear response. In borophene ZnO heterostructures, cathodoluminescence reveals a two orders of magnitude enhancement at 400 nm and 800 nm, due to an enhanced two photon absorption process. Under tunable near infrared excitation, a clear second harmonic signal emerges with quadratic power dependence and strong resonance near 800 nm. We attribute this to nonlinear plasmon exciton coupling, which reshapes the excitonic response and enables efficient hybrid pathways for frequency conversion. These results establish anisotropic plasmon exciton hybridization as a route to controlling nonlinear optical responses in low dimensional heterostructures.

### [196] [Theory of Supercritical Coupling And Generalized Bound States in the Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11741)
*Sergio Balestrieri,Bruno Miranda,Silvia Romano,Gianluigi Zito*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过亮-暗超模（bright-dark supermode）分解建立了连续谱束缚态（BIC）的干涉机制、狄拉克拓扑（Dirac topology）与非厄米物理（non-Hermitian physics）的统一理论框架，揭示了超临界耦合（supercritical coupling）与广义连续谱束缚态（gBIC）的概念，为开放光子系统中超高品质因子增强与损耗工程提供了完整理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续谱束缚态（bound states in the continuum, BICs）源于相消干涉抑制辐射，但其内在的干涉机制与非厄米耦合过程缺乏统一的基矢描述。本文旨在通过亮-暗超模分解（bright-dark supermode decomposition）建立BIC干涉、狄拉克拓扑与非厄米物理之间的联系，并阐明超临界耦合（supercritical coupling）的物理起源。

Method: 通过亮-暗超模分解将共振耦合到共享辐射通道的 Friedrich-Wintgen 干涉自然呈现为基矢构建；利用四波哈密顿量（four-wave Hamiltonian）进行定量分析，并与严格耦合波分析（rigorous coupled-wave analysis, RCWA）对标验证；扩展到光子晶体平板（photonic crystal slabs）中的狄拉克型色散（Dirac-like dispersions），识别开放狄拉克奇点（open-Dirac singularity）。

Result: 准BIC（quasi-BIC）的有限泄漏诱导因果驱动的反应耦合（reactive coupling），实现暗区非厄米泵浦（non-Hermitian pumping）；推导出最优条件对应于此前发现的超临界耦合区间，并自然恢复准BIC通用不对称性标度律（universal quasi-BIC asymmetry scaling）；发现狄拉克隙（Dirac gap）与超临界区间匹配的开放狄拉克奇点；揭示传统临界耦合（critical coupling）的失效，并发现吸收交叉耦合可抑制有效耗散损耗至低于传统材料极限。

Conclusion: 提出广义连续谱束缚态（generalized bound state in the continuum, gBIC）概念，将其定义为辐射与有效增益补偿的极限非厄米态，此时总品质因子（quality factor）发散。本工作建立了BIC干涉、狄拉克拓扑与非厄米物理的统一框架，为开放光子系统的超高Q值增强与损耗工程奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Bound states in the continuum (BICs) arise from destructive interference suppressing radiation despite spectral overlap with the continuum. Here we show that Friedrich--Wintgen interference naturally emerges from a bright--dark supermode decomposition of resonances coupled through a shared radiation channel. In this basis, any finite leakage of a quasi-BIC induces a causality-driven reactive coupling enabling non-Hermitian pumping of the dark sector. We derive the optimal condition for this process and show that it corresponds to the supercritical coupling regime previously identified in [Nature 626, 765 (2024)], while naturally recovering universal quasi-BIC asymmetry scaling. Extending the theory to Dirac-like dispersions in photonic crystal slabs, we identify an open-Dirac singularity where the Dirac gap matches the supercritical regime. A four-wave Hamiltonian quantitatively reproduces rigorous coupled-wave analysis, revealing the breakdown of conventional critical coupling. Near this regime, absorptive cross-coupling induces coherent absorption interference and enables suppression of effective dissipative losses beyond conventional material limits. These results motivate the concept of a generalized bound state in the continuum (gBIC) as a limiting non-Hermitian state where radiative and effective gain compensate, producing a true divergence of the total quality factor. Overall, this work establishes a unified framework connecting BIC interference, Dirac topology, and non-Hermitian physics for ultra-high-Q enhancement and loss engineering in open photonic systems.

</details>

### [197] [Computed Tomography Reconstruction Algorithm Using Markov Random Field Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11637)
*Taiga Shimomiya,Taichi Kusumi,Yuichi Yokoyama,Masayuki Uesugi,Akihisa Takeuchi,Yuki Sada,Hayaru Shouno,Masato Okada*

Main category: physics.med-ph

TL;DR: 本研究评估了一种基于马尔可夫随机场（Markov random field）模型的贝叶斯CT重建算法，在低剂量和稀疏视角条件下表现优于传统的滤波反投影（FBP）方法，并通过最小化贝叶斯自由能（Bayesian free energy）自适应估计超参数，提升了重建图像质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的滤波反投影（FBP）算法虽然计算成本低，但在低剂量或稀疏视角条件下会放大噪声，导致重建图像质量严重下降。因此，需要一种在有限观测数据下仍能保持高重建性能的CT重建算法。

Method: 提出了一种基于马尔可夫随机场（Markov random field）模型的贝叶斯CT重建算法，通过最小化贝叶斯自由能（Bayesian free energy）来估计超参数，从而自适应地反映观测投影数据的噪声特性。

Result: 通过仿真实验证明，在低剂量和稀疏视角两种不良条件下，所提出的贝叶斯重建算法均表现出比滤波反投影（FBP）更高的重建性能。

Conclusion: 该算法有望拓展CT在对剂量敏感的应用以及时间受限的测量场景中的适用性，这些场景通常只能获得有限的观测投影数据。

Abstract: X-ray computed tomography (CT) reveals the materials' internal structures non-destructively from a tilt series of projected images. Filtered back projection (FBP) is a widely-adopted reconstruction algorithm in CT owing to its small computational cost. Under low-dose or sparse-view conditions, however, FBP often amplifies noise, severely degrading the reconstructed images. In this study, we evaluated the performance of a Bayesian CT reconstruction algorithm based on the Markov random field model under such adverse conditions. Through simulations, we demonstrated that the proposed algorithm shows higher reconstruction performance than FBP under both low-dose and sparse-view conditions. The hyperparameters are estimated by minimizing the Bayesian free energy, enabling adaptive reconstruction that reflects the noise characteristics of the observed projection data. These results suggest that the proposed algorithm can broaden the applicability of CT to dose-sensitive applications and time-constrained measurements, where only limited observed projection data are available.

### [198] [Capturing many-body effects in electrical conductivity of warm dense matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11308)
*Brian P. Robinson,Alina Kononov,Lucas J. Stanek,Andrew D. Baczewski,André Schleife,Stephanie B. Hansen*
