  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory，DFT）的电导率模型近似了多体物理效应，且忽略了电子-电子散射寿命。为提高温稠密物质电导率计算的精度，需要引入更完善的多体理论框架。

Method: 采用电子自能的GW近似（GW approximation）构建电导率的多体框架，用于计算铍（beryllium）材料的电导率。

Result: 对于铍材料，改进的跃迁能量在低温下导致直流电导率出现显著降低；而电子-电子散射主要在高温下降低直流电导率。

Conclusion: GW近似的多体框架能更准确地描述温稠密物质的电导率行为，揭示了跃迁能量修正和电子-电子散射在不同温度区间对直流电导率的不同影响机制。

Abstract: Conductivity models for warm dense matter inform simulations of planetary structure and fusion experiments. State-of-the-art conductivity calculations based on density functional theory approximate many-body physics and neglect electron-electron scattering lifetimes. We introduce a many-body framework for electrical conductivity using the GW approximation of the electronic self-energy. For beryllium, improved transition energies yield a surprisingly large reduction in low-temperature DC conductivity, while electron-electron scattering primarily reduces high-temperature DC conductivity.

### [199] [Field Theory of Data: Anomaly Detection via the Functional Renormalization Group. The 2D Ising Model as a Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11138)
*Riccardo Finotello,Vincent Lahoche,Parham Radpay,Dine Ousmane Samary*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文建立了高噪声条件下异常检测（anomaly detection）与非平衡场论重整化群流（renormalization group flow）之间的对应关系，证明非平衡系统中的相变检测可映射为平衡场论在 Gaussian 不动点附近的有效理论，并利用泛函重整化群（Functional Renormalization Group）在二维 Model A 上展示了噪声-信号比作为物理温度的作用，最终以 Onsager 精确解为基准实现了低于 4% 的临界阈值识别误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高噪声条件下，传统信息论指标（如 Kullback-Leibler 散度）难以有效识别复杂数据集中的结构或相变临界点，缺乏统一的理论框架将统计力学（statistical mechanics）与统计推断（statistical inference）联系起来。

Method: 首先建立异常检测与非平衡场论重整化群流之间的数学对应关系；然后证明该问题可映射为以 Marchenko-Pastur 分布为标识的 Gaussian 不动点附近的平衡场论；最后应用泛函重整化群求解二维 Model A，并利用 Onsager 精确解作为基准进行误差验证。

Result: 噪声-信号比（noise-to-signal ratio）可作为物理温度（physical temperature），信号表现为热化涨落背景中的有序畴（ordered domains）；该方法检测临界阈值的误差低于 4%，显著优于标准的 Kullback-Leibler 散度指标。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种在临界条件（criticality）附近从复杂数据集中解析结构的通用策略，弥合了统计力学与统计推断之间的理论鸿沟。

Abstract: We establish a correspondence between anomaly detection in high-noise regimes and the renormalization group flow of non-equilibrium field theories. We provide a physical grounding for this framework by proving that the detection of phase transitions in interacting non-equilibrium systems maps to the study of an effective equilibrium field theory near its Gaussian fixed point, which we identify with the universal Marchenko-Pastur distribution. Applying the Functional Renormalization Group to the two-dimensional Model A, we demonstrate that the noise-to-signal ratio acts as a physical temperature, where the signal emerges as ordered domains within a thermalized background of fluctuations. Using the exact Onsager solution as a benchmark, we show that this approach identifies critical thresholds with an error below 4%, significantly outperforming standard information-theoretic metrics such as the Kullback-Leibler divergence. Our results provide a universal strategy for resolving structures in complex datasets near criticality, bridging the gap between statistical mechanics and statistical inference.

### [200] [Random-h Fractional-Dimensional Lattices Reveal Endpoint-Compressed Percolation Activation between Two and Three Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11310)
*Ran Huang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出随机-h 分维（random-h fractional dimension, RhFD）晶格框架，通过随机激活局域连接性生成分数维度环境，并利用淬火位点逾渗模拟展示了从二维到三维的维度交叉行为，揭示了质量维度、局域配位与临界连通性在交叉过程中的解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非整数维度（non-integer dimensionality）对分形与复杂系统至关重要，但现有框架极少提供显式晶格，使得经典统计力学（statistical mechanics）模型无法直接在分数维度晶格上模拟。本文旨在构建一种可显式生成的分数维度晶格框架。

Method: 引入随机-h 分维（RhFD）框架：通过在正方基底上以概率 ρh 递归生长面外（out-of-plane）位点来生成分数维度晶格，覆盖从二维到三维的区间；采用淬火位点逾渗（quenched site-percolation）模拟进行验证。

Result: RhFD 构造恢复了整数维端点，并展现出稳健的交叉（crossover）行为，逾渗阈值从二维区间向三维区间递减；高分辨率扫描显示出端点压缩激活（endpoint-compressed activation）现象，即 -dpc/dρh 随 ρh→1 递增。质量维度（mass dimension）随 ρh 增加，配位描述符（coordination descriptor）先因稀疏突起形成而下降，后在密集三维骨架出现时急剧上升。

Conclusion: RhFD 为分数维度统计力学提供了显式晶格基底，并表明在维度交叉过程中，几何质量、局域配位与临界连通性（critical connectivity）可以解耦（decouple）。

Abstract: Non-integer dimensionality is central to fractal and complex systems, yet it is rarely represented as an explicit lattice on which classical statistical-mechanical models can be directly simulated. Here we introduce random-h fractional dimension (RhFD), a constructive lattice framework in which fractional-dimensional environments are generated by stochastic activation of local connectivity, h. In the 2D-to-3D interval, RhFD lattices are formed by recursively growing out-of-plane sites from a square base with probability \r{ho}h. Using quenched site-percolation simulations, we show that the construction recovers the integer-dimensional endpoints and yields a robust crossover in which the percolation threshold decreases from the 2D regime toward the 3D regime. The crossover is not a uniform interpolation: high-resolution scans reveal endpoint-compressed activation, with -dpc/d\r{ho}h increasing toward \r{ho}h = 1. Mass dimension increases with \r{ho}h, whereas the coordination descriptor first decreases as sparse protrusions form and then rises sharply when a dense 3D backbone emerges. RhFD provides an explicit lattice substrate for fractional-dimensional statistical mechanics and shows that geometric mass, local coordination, and critical connectivity can decouple during dimensional crossover.

### [201] [Critical Dynamics of Non-Reciprocally Coupled Conserved Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11892)
*Emir Sezik,Gunnar Pruessner*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过场论重整化群（renormalization group）方法，研究了非互易耦合自旋系统中的临界守恒动力学，发现非互易性仅通过非线性相互作用引入时，临界行为依赖于微观参数值；对于 n ≥ 4，存在一个固定点，其临界动力学渐近满足细致平衡（detailed-balance），表明大尺度下微观非互易性被抹除；守恒动力学减少了独立标度指数的数量，类似于标准涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relation）的效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非互易（non-reciprocal）系统可产生行波等时间依赖模式，但不同模型中的时空模式及标度行为存在差异。为更好地理解不同非互易相互作用的影响，本文研究非互易耦合自旋系统的临界守恒动力学。

Method: 采用场论重整化群（field-theoretic renormalisation group）程序，对两个 n 分量序参量场（order parameter fields）的非互易耦合动力学进行单圈（one-loop）分析。

Result: 在单圈水平上，临界行为依赖于某些微观参数值；对于 n ≥ 4，存在一个固定点（fixed point），其临界动力学渐近满足细致平衡（detailed-balance），表明大尺度上动力学对微观非互易性不敏感；守恒动力学减少了独立标度指数（scaling exponents）的数量。

Conclusion: 非互易性通过非线性相互作用引入时，临界行为表现出对微观参数的依赖性；但在 n ≥ 4 条件下，大尺度涌现动力学可恢复细致平衡，且守恒动力学使得标度行为受到类似涨落-耗散关系的约束。

Abstract: Non-reciprocal systems have been shown to sustain time-dependent patterns, most prominently travelling waves. The transition into these time-dependent states generally breaks time-translational invariance, representing a clear deviation from equilibrium dynamics. Though common implementations of non-reciprocity lead to such phenomenology, these spatio-temporal patterns are absent in other models. In the same vein, the ensuing scaling behaviour also depends on the precise way non-reciprocity is implemented. To better understand the effects of different non-reciprocal interactions, we study the critical conserved dynamics of non-reciprocally coupled spin systems. Specifically, we consider the dynamics of two $n$-component order parameter fields $\boldsymbolφ_i$ with $i \in\{1,2\}$. Unlike the common implementations of non-reciprocal interactions, we introduce the non-reciprocity solely through the non-linear interaction between the distinct species. Using the field-theoretic renormalisation group (RG) procedure, we perform a one-loop analysis and show that at one-loop level, the critical behaviour depends on the microscopic value of certain quantities. Using the flow functions, we elucidate the behaviour of the fixed points for different bare microscopic values. We also show that for $n \geq 4$, there is a fixed point where the ensuing critical dynamics asymptotically obey detailed-balance, implying the emergent dynamics are agnostic to the microscopic non-reciprocity on large scales. Finally, we show that the conserved dynamics reduces the number of independent scaling exponents, mimicking the effect of a standard fluctuation-dissipation relation.

</details>


### [202] [Statistical Potential for Identical Fermions: Emergent Attraction and Pauli Crystal Formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12043)
*Kawon Lee,Sangeun Oh,Young Woo Choi,Jeong-Hyuck Park*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明了 N 个全同费米子的热力学可以映射为受集体统计势（collective statistical potential）支配的可区分粒子的热力学，该势是简并压（degeneracy pressure）的微观起源。对于 N≥3，该势出现吸引成分，其最小值对应泡利晶体（Pauli crystal）构型。在大 N 极限下，内壳层以吸引力为主，外壳层以排斥力为主，且该势非两体起源；全局最小值在特定温度下经历离散熔化转变（discrete melting transitions）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示全同费米子简并压的微观起源，以及由此生成的泡利晶体结构的能量学基础；澄清多体费米子系统中集体统计相互作用（collective statistical interaction）的本质及其非两体特性。

Method: 通过将 N 个全同费米子的热力学映射到可区分粒子系统，引入一个集体统计势（collective statistical potential）来描述简并压的微观来源；分析该势在 N=2、N≥3 及大 N 极限下的性质，并考察其最小值与泡利晶体（Pauli crystal）构型的对应关系。

Result: 该统计势在 N=2 时纯粹排斥，在 N≥3 时出现吸引成分；势的最小值与泡利晶体构型一致；在大 N 下，内壳层受力以吸引力为主，外壳层以排斥力为主，且该力非两体相互作用（non-two-body interaction）所致；全局最小值在特定温度下发生离散熔化转变。

Conclusion: 全同费米子的统计效应可通过集体统计势统一描述，该势为简并压和泡利晶体结构提供了微观能量学解释；其非两体特性和离散熔化转变揭示了费米子系统统计力学（statistical mechanics）中新的相行为。

Abstract: We show that the thermodynamics of $N$ identical fermions maps onto that of distinguishable particles governed by a collective statistical potential -- the microscopic origin of degeneracy pressure. Known to be purely repulsive for ${N=2}$, this potential develops attractive contributions for ${N\geq 3}$. Its minima coincide with Pauli crystal configurations, providing the energetic origin of these structures. For large $N$, the dominant force is attractive on inner shells and repulsive on outer ones -- not of two-body origin. The global minimum undergoes discrete melting transitions at specific temperatures.

### [203] [Identifying the relevant parameters in design strategies for stable glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12127)
*Leonardo Galliano,Ludovic Berthier*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过新计算方法的实验表明，玻璃稳定性的增强并非由超均匀性（hyperuniformity）或局部有序性（local ordering）等物理量的优化所导致，而更可能是由粒子直径动态变化（diameter dynamics）这一动力学过程所引起，从而挑战了当前关于超稳定玻璃（ultrastable glass）设计规则的主流因果解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理气相沉积（physical vapor deposition）可制备超稳定玻璃，且已有多种数值算法通过优化特定物理性质提升玻璃稳定性，但究竟哪些参数是稳定性增强的根本原因尚不清楚。本文旨在检验这些物理量是否是玻璃稳定性的因果驱动因素。

Method: 作者提出了不改变粒子直径即可优化物理量的计算方法；分别在大尺度上增强超均匀性、在小尺度上增强局部有序性，以此构建玻璃构型（glass configurations），并与体平衡态（bulk equilibrium states）进行对比。

Result: 尽管设计的玻璃在超均匀性和局部有序性上显著优于体平衡态，但这些玻璃并未展现出增强的稳定性。所优化的物理量与玻璃稳定性存在相关性，但并非超稳定性的因果因素。

Conclusion: 玻璃稳定性的设计规则应重新理解为由生成稳定性的动力学过程（dynamical processes）所主导，而非仅仅关注所优化的目标物理量。粒子直径动态变化可能是增强稳定性的主要来源。

Abstract: A glass is conventionally obtained by cooling a bulk supercooled liquid through its glass transition temperature. The discovery of ultrastable glasses prepared using physical vapor deposition, together with the recent multiplication of numerical algorithms created to increase the stability of glasses, demonstrates the existence of a variety of strategies for designing glasses with different physical properties. This raises a broader question: which parameters most strongly govern the enhancement of glass stability? Existing computational strategies often produce highly stable glasses by optimizing certain physical properties through dynamical changes in particle diameters. We challenge the idea that these physical quantities are causally responsible for glass stability and suggest instead that diameter dynamics is the principal source of enhanced stability. To support our view, we introduce computational methods to optimize physical quantities without changing the particle diameters. Using the examples of enhanced hyperuniformity at large scale and local ordering at small scale, we design glass configurations with highly optimized values compared to bulk equilibrium states. However, these glasses do not show enhanced stability. The proposed physical quantities are correlated with glass stability, but are not causally responsible for ultrastability. These findings indicate that design rules for stable glasses should be reinterpreted in terms of the dynamical processes that generate stability, rather than the optimized physical quantities they target.

</details>


### [204] [Link length and energy fluctuations in extensible freely jointed chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12333)
*Michael R. Buche*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在可扩展自由连接链（extensible freely jointed chain）模型框架下，系统分析了施加外力下聚合物单链中键长和键能的统计涨落，给出了渐近精确的解析关系及其精确表达式，并通过误差分析验证了其正确性，揭示了特定条件下涨落近似服从正态分布的特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的自由连接链（freely jointed chain）模型缺乏键拉伸导致的内能变化，无法捕捉键长与键能的热涨落。由于许多聚合物链与网络模型将链解离视为键长或键能的函数，理解和量化这些涨落对于完善模型至关重要。

Method: 在施加外力的可扩展自由连接链模型中，对键长和键能的涨落进行分析，计算其平均值、标准差和概率分布；引入渐近正确的解析关系及其精确（但形式较繁琐）对应式，并通过直接比较和超越小项（transcendentally small terms）误差分析验证渐近关系的准确性。

Result: 给出了键长和键能涨落的平均值、标准差和概率分布；渐近解析关系与精确解直接比较结果一致，误差分析表明其正确性可达超越小项量级；在特定条件下，涨落近似服从正态分布。

Conclusion: 基于键长或键能的模型组件应当考虑这些涨落的影响，以确保模型在热力学框架下的完整性和准确性。

Abstract: The freely jointed chain is often applied to model the thermodynamics of single polymer chains, but the traditional formulation of the model lacks internal energy changes due to bond stretching. For this reason, the extensible freely jointed chain model includes a potential energy function, typically harmonic, that governs the length of each link in the chain. Among the other quantities of interest that are subject to thermal fluctuations, these link lengths and energies too fluctuate about their ensemble average values. Since a plethora of models for polymer chains and networks incorporate chain dissociation as a function of either link length or energy, these fluctuations are crucial to understand and quantify. Motivated by this fact, fluctuations in link length and energy are analyzed within a freely jointed chain under an applied force. These fluctuations are quantified through their average values, standard deviations, and probability distributions. Across all values, asymptotically correct analytic relations and their less ergonomic exact counterparts are introduced. The asymptotic relations are verified to be accurate through direct comparison and to be correct within transcendentally small terms through error analysis. In certain cases, the fluctuations are shown to be approximately normally distributed. Hereafter, model components predicated on link length or energy ought to account for these fluctuations.

</details>
